Matthew1:1 Ala lalis bann anset Zezi Kris, desandan David ek Abraam."
Matthew1:2 Abraam ti papa Izaak. Izaak ti papa Zakob. Zakob ti papa Zida ek so bann frer.
Matthew1:3 Zida ti papa Perez ek Zera, zot mama ti apel Tamar. Perez ti papa Esron. Esron ti papa Ram."
Matthew1:4 Ram ti papa Aminadab. Aminadab ti papa Nason. Nason ti papa Salma.
Matthew1:5 Salma ti papa Boaz, so mama ti apel Raab. Boaz ti papa Obed, so mama ti apel Rit. Obed ti papa Zese."
Matthew1:6 Zese ti papa lerwa David. David ti papa Salomon. Mama Salomon ti marye avek Iri.
Matthew1:7 Salomon ti papa Roboam. Roboam ti papa Abia. Abia ti papa Asa.
Matthew1:8 Asa ti papa Zozafat. Zozafat ti papa Zoram. Zoram ti papa Ozias.
Matthew1:9 Ozias ti papa Yotam. Yotam ti papa Akaz. Akaz ti papa Ezekias.
Matthew1:10 Ezekias ti papa Manase. Manase ti papa Amon. Amon ti papa Zozias.
Matthew1:11 Zozias ti papa Yekonia ek so bann frer. Sa lepok la, bann Izraelit ti exile dan Babilonn."
Matthew1:12 Apre sa letan lexil, Yekonia ti papa Salatiel. Salatiel ti papa Zorobabel."
Matthew1:13 Zorobabel ti papa Abioud. Abioud ti papa Eliakim. Eliakim ti papa Azor.
Matthew1:14 Azor ti papa Sadok. Sadok ti papa Akim. Akim ti papa Elioud.
Matthew1:15 Elioud ti papa Eleazer. Eleazer ti papa Matann. Matann ti papa Zakob.
Matthew1:16 Zakob ti papa Zozef. Zozef ti marye avek Marie, e Marie finn donn nesans Zezi ki nou apel Lemesi."
Matthew1:17 Antou ti ena katorz zenerasion depi Abraam ziska David, Katorz depi David ziska lepok lexil dan Babilonn e katorz depi lexil ziska Lekris."
Matthew1:18 Ala kouma Zezi Kris ti ne. So mama Marie ti fianse avek Zozef. Avan ki zot ti koumans viv ansam Marie finn trouv li ansint par laksion Lespri Sin.
Matthew1:19 So fianse, Zozef ti enn zom drwat. Li pa ti anvi fer Marie perdi loner devan dimoun, alor li desid divorse san ki personn kone."
Matthew1:20 Letan Zozef pe kalkil tousala, anz Lesegner paret devan li dan enn rev. Anz la dir li, “Zozef, garson David, pa per pou pran Marie kouma to fam. Zanfan ki dan so vant li sorti depi Lespri Sin."
Matthew1:21 Li pou donn nesans enn garson e to pou apel li Zezi. Avredir limem pou sov so lepep ki dan pese.”
Matthew1:22 Tousala ti arive pouki parol ki nou Segner finn dir par so profet realize:
Matthew1:23 “Enn zennfi pou ansint, li pou donn nesans enn garson. Li pou apel Emaniel,” ki vedir, ‘Bondie avek nou.’"
Matthew1:24 Ler Zozef leve, li fer saki anz la finn komann li. Li pran so fam kot li,"
Matthew1:25 me li pa ti gagn okenn relasion avek li ziska nesans so garson. E li apel li Zezi.
Matthew2:1 Zezi ti ne dan Betleem dan Galile, lepok lerwa Erod. Apre so nesans, enn bann savan sorti kote soley levan, ariv dan Zerizalem."
Matthew2:2 Zot dimande, “Kot lerwa bann Zwif ki finn fek ne?” “Nou finn trouv so zetwal leve dan les e nou finn vini pou ador li.”"
Matthew2:3 Kan lerwa Erod tann sa, so latet fatige e tou bann abitan Zerizalem osi ti trakase."
Matthew2:4 Li ti apel tou bann sef pret ek bann dokter lalwa ki travay pou lepep, e li dimann zot ki kote Lemesi pou ne."
Matthew2:5 Zot reponn li, “Betleem dan Zide. Ala seki profet finn ekrir:"
Matthew2:6 Betleem, twa ki lor later Zide to napa pli dernie parmi bann lavil prinsipal, parski kot tomem pou sorti enn berze ki pou diriz mo lepep Izrael.”"
Matthew2:7 Alor Erod apel bann savan la san ki personn kone e li dimann zot ki dat exak sa zetwal la ti paret.
Matthew2:8 Apre sa, li avoy zot Betleem e li dir zot: “Al rod tou linformasion lor sa zanfan la, e kan zot trouv li, fer mwa kone pouki mo osi mo al ador li.”"
Matthew2:9 Apre ki zot finn tande saki lerwa ti ena pou dir zot, zot ale. Sa zetwal ki zot finn trouve dan les ti pe avanse devan zot, li ti aret zis lao landrwa kot zanfan la ti ete."
Matthew2:10 Zot ti dan enn gran lazwa kan zot trouv zetwal la.
Matthew2:11 Ler zot rant dan lakaz la, zot trouv Zezi ek so mama Marie. Zot tom azenou pou ador li; zot ouver zot kof bizou e zot ofer li lor, lansan ek lamir;"
Matthew2:12 me dan enn rev Bondie ti averti zot pa retourn kot Erod; zot pran enn lot sime pou retourn dan zot pei.
Matthew2:13 Apre ki bann savan finn fini ale, enn anz Lesegner paret devan Zozef dan enn rev e li dir li, “Leve, pran sa zanfan la ek so mama, sove al dan Lezip; res laba ziska ki mo dir twa retourne, parski Erod pou rod sa zanfan la pou touy li.”"
Matthew2:14 Dan lanwit, Zozef leve li pran zanfan la ek so mama, li al Lezip."
Matthew2:15 Li res laba ziska lamor Erod. Tousala finn arive pouki parol ki Lesegner finn dir atraver so profet realize “Mo finn apel mo garson depi Lezip.”
Matthew2:16 Ler Erod realize ki sa bann savan la finn tronp li, li ankoler. Li donn lord touy tou bann garson ki ena de-zan ou mwins e ki abit dan rezion Betleem. Li finn azir dapre lanket ki li finn pran avek bann savan lor dat exak ki zetwal ti paret."
Matthew2:17 Alor seki profet Zeremi ti deklare ti finn realize,"
Matthew2:18 “Enn lavwa leve dan Rama. Ena plore, ena plegne, Rasel pe plor so bann zanfan. Li pale konsolasion parski zot nepli la.”"
Matthew2:19 Apre lamor Erod anz Lesegner paret devan Zozef dan enn rev kan li ti ankor Lezip.
Matthew2:20 Li dir li, “Leve, pran zanfan la ek so mama avek twa e retourn lor later Izrael parski bann seki ti pe rod touy li finn fini mor.”"
Matthew2:21 Alor Zozef leve, li pran zanfan la ek so mama e li retourn lor later Izrael."
Matthew2:22 Ler li aprann ki Arkelais ti finn ranplas so papa Erod kouma lerwa Zide, li gagn per pou al laba. Apre ki enn anz finn averti li dan enn rev, li ti al dan rezion Galile."
Matthew2:23 Li instal li laba, dan enn lavil ki apel Nazaret. Tousala finn realize dapre seki bann profet ti anonse: “Li pou apel Nazareen.”"
Matthew3:1 Sa mem lepok la, Zan Batis ti pe proklame dan dezer Zide."
Matthew3:2 Li ti pe dir, “Sanz zot leker, Rwayom Bondie finn aprose.”"
Matthew3:3 Profet Izai finn koz lor Zan e li finn dir: ‘Enn lavwa ape kriye dan dezer: prepar sime Lesegner, ouver enn sime kler pou li.’"
Matthew3:4 Zan ti met enn linz pwal samo ek enn sang lapo dan so lerin. Li ti manz sotrel ek dimiel sovaz.
Matthew3:5 Dimoun Zerizalem, tou Zide ek rezion larivier Zourdin ti vinn kot Zan."
Matthew3:6 Li ti batiz zot letan zot ti pe konfes zot pese anpiblik.
Matthew3:7 Ler li trouv enn kantite Farizien ek Sadisein vinn kot li pou pran batem, li dir zot, “Bann espes serpan, kisannla finn dir zot ki zot pou kapav evit lakoler Bondie.?"
Matthew3:8 Prodwir bon fri ki montre ki zot finn sanz zot leker.
Matthew3:9 Pa nek dir dan zotmem, ‘Abraam nou papa!’ Parski les mo dir zot ki avek sa bann ros la, Bondie kapav fer bann desandan Abraam leve."
Matthew3:10 Asterlamem laserp finn fini pare pou koup bann pie depi zot rasinn. Tou bann pie ki pa raport bon fri pou koupe zet dan dife.
Matthew3:11 Mwa, mo pe batiz zot dan dilo pou zot repanti. Me Sa-Enn ki pe vini apre mwa, li pli for ki mwa; mo pa ase bon, pou mo kourbe devan li pou larg so sandalet."
Matthew3:12 Li, li pou batiz zot ar Lespri Sin ek dife. Ena enn gro fours dan so lame pou separ lagrin dible ek lapay. Lagrin dible, li ramas dan stor, lapay, li bril li dan dife ki zame pou tegn.”"
Matthew3:13 Letan Zezi sorti Galile, li al dan Zourdin, pou resevwar batem ar Zan."
Matthew3:14 Zan ti refiz li, e li dir, “Mwa ki bizin resevwar batem ar twa.”"
Matthew3:15 Zezi reponn li, “Les ale asterla, parski koumsamem ki nou pou akonpli lazistis Bondie.”"
Matthew3:16 Alor Zan aksepte. Zis kouma Zezi fini batize, li sorti dan dilo; lesiel fann an-de e Lespri Sin parey kouma enn kolonb desann lor li."
Matthew3:17 Enn lavwa dan lesiel dir, “limem mo Garson ki mo bien kontan; li donn mwa boukou lazwa.”"
Matthew4:1 Zis apre sa, Lespri ti ris Zezi dan dezer kot diab ti tant li."
Matthew4:2 Apre ki li finn pas karant zour ek karant nwit san manze, Zezi gagn fin."
Matthew4:3 Diab vinn ar li e dir li, “Si tomem Garson Bondie, donn lord sa bann ros la vinn dipin.”"
Matthew4:4 Zezi reponn, “Dan liv finn ekrir: ‘Dimoun pa viv zis ar dipin me ar tou bann parol ki sorti dan labous Bondie.’ ”"
Matthew4:5 Alor diab amenn li dan lavil sint e fer li dibout net lao lor tanp e dir li,"
Matthew4:6 “Si tomem Garson Bondie, zet to lekor dan vid, parski dan liv finn ekrir: ‘Li pou donn lord so bann anz pou tini twa dan zot lame, pouki okenn ros pa bles to lipie.’ ”"
Matthew4:7 Zezi dir li, “Finn osi ekrir: ‘Fode pa to tant Lesegner to Bondie.’ ”"
Matthew4:8 Apre sa, diab amenn Zezi lor enn montagn bien-bien ot, li montre li tou bann rwayom lor later"
Matthew4:9 e li dir li, “Mo pou donn twa tousala, si to tom azenou pou ador mwa.”"
Matthew4:10 Zezi reponn, “Sorti la ale Satan, parski finn ekrir: ‘To pou ador Lesegner to Bondie, li tousel to bizin servi.’ ”"
Matthew4:11 Alor diab kit li ale, e bann anz vinn servi li."
Matthew4:12 Ler li tann dir ki bannla finn aret Zan, Zezi ti retir li dan Galile"
Matthew4:13 Li kit Nazaret pou al res dan Kafarnaom, dan borlamer, dan teritwar Zabilon ek Neftali."
Matthew4:14 Sa finn arive, pouki parol Profet Izai realize:"
Matthew4:15 “Teritwar Zabilon ek Neftali, lor sime lakot, lot kote Zourdin, Galile, pei payin;"
Matthew4:16 lepep ki ti dan teneb finn trouv enn gran lalimier e bann ki ti finn mor dan zot pese, enn lalimier finn leve pou zot.”"
Matthew4:17 Depi sa letan la Zezi koumans proklame, “Sanz zot leker, parski Rwayom Bondie pe aprose.”"
Matthew4:18 Letan Zezi pe mars-marse dan borlamer Galile, li trouv de peser: Simon, ki ti apel Pier ek so frer Andre; zot ti pe lapes lasenn."
Matthew4:19 Zezi dir zot, “Vini, swiv mwa, mo pou montre zot lapes dimoun.”"
Matthew4:20 Lor vites, zot kit zot file, zot swiv Zezi"
Matthew4:21 Inpe pli lwin, li trouv de garson Zebede: Zak ek so frer Zan. Toulede avek zot papa ti dan pirog pe demay zot file; li apel zot."
Matthew4:22 Lor vites zot kit zot papa anplan dan bato e zot swiv li.
Matthew4:23 Zezi finn al partou dan Galile, li ti pe ansegne dan zot sinagog, li ti pe proklam Bonn Nouvel lor size Rwayom Bondie. Li ti geri bann dimoun avek toutsort kalite malad."
Matthew4:24 So repitasion finn al partou dan Lasiri. Zot amenn kot li tou bann ki pe soufer ek aflize par tou kalite maladi; bann ki posede.
Matthew4:25 Enn gran lafoul sorti Galile, Dekapol, Zerizalem, Zide ek lot kote larivier Zourdin ti swiv li."
Matthew5:1 Ler Zezi trouv sa lafoul dimoun la, li mont lor montagn e li asize. So bann disip rasanble otour li."
Matthew5:2 Li pran laparol e li koumans ansegn zot.
Matthew5:3 “Bienere zot ki pov dan zot lespri, Rwayom Bondie li pou zot."
Matthew5:4 Bienere zot ki andey, zot pou gagn konsolasion."
Matthew5:5 Bienere zot ki dou e ranpli avek imilite, zot pou erit later promiz."
Matthew5:6 Bienere zot ki fin ek swaf lazistis, zot dezir pou exose."
Matthew5:7 Bienere zot ki montre konpasion pou lezot, Bondie pou pitie zot."
Matthew5:8 Bienere zot ki ena leker san tas, zot pou ar Bondie e zot pou trouv li."
Matthew5:9 Bienere zot ki met lape, Bondie pou apel zot so bann zanfan."
Matthew5:10 Bienere zot ki dimoun pe persekite akoz zot fer dibien, Rwayom Bondie li pou zot."
Matthew5:11 Zot pou Bienere kan dimoun insilte zot, persekit zot ek malparl zot parski zot krwar dan mwa."
Matthew5:12 Zot bizin dan lazwa e santi zot ere parski zot ena enn rekonpans dan lesiel; koumsamem zot ti persekit bann ansien profet.
Matthew5:13 Zotmem disel pou lemonn. Me si disel perdi so gou sale, kouma pou kapav refer li vinn sale? Li nepli bon pou nanye, apar zet dan bwa e bann dimoun mars lor li."
Matthew5:14 Zotmem lalimier pou lemonn. Enn lavil ki finn konstrir lor enn montagn pa kapav kasiet.
Matthew5:15 Nou pa alim enn lalanp pou met li anba bake. Okontrer nou met li lor enn stenn, e li donn lalimier pou tou dimoun dan lakaz."
Matthew5:16 Dan samem fason, les to lalimier briye devan tou dimoun, pouki zot kapav trouv to bann bienfe e loue to Papa dan lesiel."
Matthew5:17 Pa panse ki mo finn vini pou aboli lalwa ek bann profet; mo pa finn vini pou aboli me pou akonpli zot.
Matthew5:18 Laverite mo dir zot, osi lontan ki later ek lesiel existe, nanye pa pou retire dan lalwa, pa mem sa ti pwin lor i, ziska tou akonpli."
Matthew5:19 Si kikenn kas enn pli tipti sa bann komannman la e ansegn lezot pou fer parey, li pou konsidere kouma pli piti dan lesiel, me kikenn ki pratik e ansegn sa bann komannman la li pou konsidere kouma gran dan lesiel."
Matthew5:20 Les mo dir zot ki si zot pa montre zot pli fidel anver volonte Bondie ki sa bann Farizien ek dokter lalwa la, zot pa pou rant dan lesiel."
Matthew5:21 Zot finn tande seki finn dir ar nou bann anset, ‘Pa fer krim e si kikenn touy enn lot dimoun, li merit santans.’"
Matthew5:22 Me mwa mo dir zot, si kikenn ankoler avek so frer ou so ser, li merit zizman. Kikenn ki dir so frer ou so ser ‘fatra’, li merit zize par konsey bann ansien; kikenn ki dir so frer ‘fou’ li merit dife lanfer."
Matthew5:23 Akoz samem si to vinn devan lotel pou ofer enn sakrifis e to rapel ki to pa bien ar to frer,"
Matthew5:24 les to ofrand lamem, rekonsilie ar to frer, apre to va prezant to ofrand Bondie."
Matthew5:25 Si to ena enn zafer lakour kont kikenn, tom enn laranzman ar li dan sime mem letan pe al lakour. Sa pou evit to adverser amenn twa devan mazistra, e anpes mazistra remet twa lapolis."
Matthew5:26 Laverite mo dir twa, to pa pou sape tanki to pa ranbours to det ziska dernie sou."
Matthew5:27 Zot finn tande ki finn dir, ‘Pa komet adilter.’"
Matthew5:28 Me mwa, mo dir zot, tou dimoun ki get enn fam e anvi li, finn deza komet adilter dan so leker."
Matthew5:29 Si to lizie drwat antrenn twa dan lemal, tir li, zet li; li preferab ki to perdi enn parti to lekor, ki antie to lekor al dan lanfer."
Matthew5:30 Si to lame drwat antrenn twa dan lemal, koup li, zete, li preferab ki to perdi enn parti to lekor ki antie to lekor al dan lanfer."
Matthew5:31 Finn osi dir, ‘Si kikenn divors ar so fam, li bizin servi li enn papie divors.’"
Matthew5:32 Me mwa, mo dir zot, ninport kisannla divorse ar so fam, exsepte dan ka enn maryaz ilezitim, fer fam la komet adilter, e kikenn ki marye ar enn fam divorse li osi komet adilter"
Matthew5:33 Zot finn osi tande ki finn dir zot gran dimoun, ‘Fode pa kas enn promes, me to bizin fer saki to finn promet Lesegner pou fer.’"
Matthew5:34 Me mo dir zot, pa fer okenn serman, ni par lesiel parski samem tronn Bondie"
Matthew5:35 ou par later, parski samem so marspie, ou par Zerizalem parski samem lavil gran Lerwa,"
Matthew5:36 e pa fer serman lor to latet, parski to pa kapav fer enn sel brin to seve vinn nwar ou blan;"
Matthew5:37 zot ena zis pou dir wi ou non, tou seki zot dir anplis li sorti kot diab."
Matthew5:38 Zot finn tande ki finn dir, ‘Enn lizie pou enn lizie, enn ledan pou enn ledan.’ Me mwa, mo dir zot pa bizin zot fer rezistans kont move dimoun."
Matthew5:39 Si kikenn kalot twa lor to lazou drwat, donn li osi to lazou gos."
Matthew5:40 Si kikenn pourswiv twa pou to triko, donn li osi to palto."
Matthew5:41 Si kikenn fors twa pou fer enn kilomet ar li, fer de kilomet."
Matthew5:42 Done kan dimoun dimann twa, e pa tourn to ledo ar dimoun ki anvi pran prete ar twa."
Matthew5:43 Zot finn tande ki finn dir, ‘Kontan to prosin e air to lennmi.’"
Matthew5:44 Me mwa, mo dir zot: kontan zot lennmi e priye pou bann ki persekit zot."
Matthew5:45 E zot pou vinn zanfan zot Papa ki dan lesiel, parski li fer so soley lev lor bann bon kouma lor bann move e li fer lapli tom lor bann zis kouma lor bann inzis."
Matthew5:46 Avredir, si zot kontan bann ki kontan zot, ki rekonpans zot pou gagne. Bann kolekter tax osi pa fer parey?"
Matthew5:47 E si zot frekant selman zotmem, ki ena extraordiner ladan? Bann payin osi pa fer parey?"
Matthew5:48 Zot bizin parfe parey kouma zot Papa ki dan lesiel li parfe.”
Matthew6:1 “Tansion zot pratik zot devwar relizie devan lezot, zis pou lizie lezot; sinon zot pa pou gagn rekonpans ki sorti kot zot Papa dan lesiel."
Matthew6:2 Kan to fer lasarite, pa bizin sonn tronpet kouma bann ipokrit fer dan bann sinagog ek dan lari, pouki dimoun aplodi zot. Laverite, mo dir zot, zot finn fini resevwar zot rekonpans."
Matthew6:3 Me twa, kan to fer lasarite fodre to lame gos ignor seki to lame drwat fer,"
Matthew6:4 fodre ki to bonaksion res sekre; to Papa ki trouv tou saki to fer pou rekonpans twa.
Matthew6:5 Kan zot fer lapriyer, pa fer kouma bann ipokrit ki kontan vinn devan pou priye dan sinagog e dan kat kwin lari pouki dimoun trouv zot. Laverite mo dir zot, sa bann la finn deza gagn zot rekonpans."
Matthew6:6 Me twa, kan to priye, rant dan to lasam, ferm twa andan e priye to Papa ki la dan sekre avek twa; to Papa ki trouv tou saki to fer, li pou rekonpans twa."
Matthew6:7 Kan to priye pa bizin rabase kouma bann payin, ki panse ki plis zot koze, plis zot lapriyer pou exose."
Matthew6:8 Pa fer kouma bannla, parski twa, to Papa deza fini kone ki bon pou twa avan mem ki to dimann li."
Matthew6:9 Gete kouma zot bizin priye: ‘Nou Papa lao dan lesiel, ki to nom sanktifie."
Matthew6:10 Fer to regn vini realiz to volonte lor later kouma dan lesiel.
Matthew6:11 Donn nou azordi dipin ki nou bizin.
Matthew6:12 Pardonn nou nou bann pese, parey kouma nou pardonn bann ki finn ofans nou."
Matthew6:13 Pa les nou tom dan tantasion Me tir nou dan lemal.’
Matthew6:14 Si zot pardonn lezot zot fot, zot Papa dan lesiel pou pardonn zot osi,"
Matthew6:15 me si zot pa pardonn lezot, zot Papa osi pa pou pardonn zot fot."
Matthew6:16 Kan zot fer karem, pa bizin fer lakagn, kouma bann ipokrit, zot fer long-long figir pou montre lezot ki zot pe karem. Laverite mo dir zot, zot finn fini gagn zot rekonpans;"
Matthew6:17 me twa, kan to zene, parfim to latet, lav to figir bien prop,"
Matthew6:18 pouki lezot pa rekonet si to pe fer karem, me to Papa ki invizib, li trouv tou saki to fer anprive e li pou rekonpans twa."
Matthew6:19 Pa ramas trezor lor later, la kot lever ek larouy kapav detrir li, e kot voler kapav defonse pou kokin."
Matthew6:20 Ramas zot trezor plito dan lesiel, la kot ni lever, ni larouy pa kapav detrir li, e kot voler pa kapav defonse pou kokin,"
Matthew6:21 parski la kot to trezor ete, to leker osi li lamem."
Matthew6:22 Lizie, li lalanp nou lekor. Si to lizie li bon, tou to lekor pou eklere,"
Matthew6:23 me si to lizie li malad, tou to lekor pou dan teneb. Alor, si lalimier ki sipoze dan twa finn vinn teneb, be ki kalite marenwar sa!"
Matthew6:24 Personn pa kapav vinn servi de met. Swa li air enn e kontan lot la, oubien li atas li ar enn e mepriz lot la. Zot pa kapav servi de met."
Matthew6:25 Akoz samem mo dir zot: pa fatig zot ar zot lavi, ar seki zot pou manze ou bwar, ar labiyman zot lekor. Eski lavi pa pli inportan ki manze, e lekor pa pli inportan ki linz?"
Matthew6:26 Get bann zwazo dan lezer, zot pa ni seme, ni rekolte, ni ramase dan grenie, e pourtan Bondie Papa ki dan lesiel nouri zot. Eski zot pena plis valer ki zwazo?"
Matthew6:27 E kisannla parmi zot, dan so linkietid, kapav prolonz so lavi."
Matthew6:28 E kifer zot trakase ar linz? Get bann fler lis dan karo, kouma zot pouse. Zot pa ni travay ni koud,"
Matthew6:29 me mo dir zot, mem Salomon dan tou sa laglwar pa finn zame abiye kouma sa bann fler la."
Matthew6:30 Si Bondie abiy enn karo lerb parey, ki zordi pe pouse e dime pou brile dan dife, eski li pa pou abiy zot ankor pli zoli ki sa? Ala zot lafwa mins la!"
Matthew6:31 Alor, pa bizin zot trakase pou dimann zotmem, ‘Ki nou bizin manze?’ ou ‘Ki nou bizin bwar?’ oubien ‘Ki nou bizin met lor nou?’"
Matthew6:32 Parski bann payin ki rod tousala; me zot Papa ki dan lesiel, li kone ki sa bann kiksoz ki neseser pou zot."
Matthew6:33 Rod plito Rwayom Bondie ek so lazistis, e tou lezot kiksoz li pou donn zot anplis."
Matthew6:34 Alor, pa bizin trakase pou dime, les dime get so zafer. Traka enn zour li ase pou zordi.”"
Matthew7:1 “Pa ziz lezot e Bondie pa pou ziz zot.
Matthew7:2 Parski Bondie pou ziz zot parey kouma zot ziz lezot e mezir ki zot servi pou lezot, samem li pou servi pou zot."
Matthew7:3 Ki manier to trouv lapay ki dan lizie to frer, me poto ki dan to lizie to pa remarke."
Matthew7:4 Kouma to kapav dir ar to frer, les mo retir lapay ki dan to lizie me poto ki dan pou twa, to pa trouve?"
Matthew7:5 Zot bann ipokrit, retir anpremie poto ki dan zot lizie, lerla zot pou trouv bien kler pou retir lapay ki dan lizie zot frer."
Matthew7:6 Pa donn lisien seki sakre, e pa zet zot perl ar koson ki kapav kraz li e revire pou atak zot."
Matthew7:7 Dimande, e to pou gagne, rode e to pou trouve, tape e laport pou ouver pou twa."
Matthew7:8 Parski tou dimoun ki dimande pou resevwar, seki rode pou trouve, e laport pou ouver pou seki tape."
Matthew7:9 Kisannla parmi zot, ki si so garson dimann dipin, li donn li enn ros;"
Matthew7:10 si li dimann pwason, pou donn li enn serpan?"
Matthew7:11 Move kouma zot move, zot kone kouma donn bon kado zot zanfan, alor ki kantite bon kiksoz anplis zot Papa ki dan lesiel pou donn zot kan zot dimann li."
Matthew7:12 Alor tou seki zot anvi ki lezot fer pou zot, fer parey pou lezot osi, samem lansegnman lalwa ek bann profet."
Matthew7:13 Pas par laport etrwat, parski laport lanfer li bien larz e sime perdision li fasil. Finn ena boukou ki prefer sa sime la."
Matthew7:14 Parski laport etrwat ek sime lavi li dir, e tigit dimoun pran sa sime la."
Matthew7:15 Fer atansion bann fos profet ki vini kouma bann mouton me ki anverite zot bann loulou feros.
Matthew7:16 Zot pou rekonet li par so fri. To pa rekolte rezin oubien fig lor pie pikan.
Matthew7:17 Tou zarb ki bon raport bon fri, zarb ki pa bon raport move fri."
Matthew7:18 Enn zarb bon pa kapav prodwir move fri, ni enn zarb malad bann bon fri."
Matthew7:19 Tou bann zarb ki pa donn bon fri, pou koupe e zet dan dife."
Matthew7:20 Koumsamem zot pou rekonet bann fos profet, par zot kondwit.”"
Matthew7:21 “Pa tou dimoun ki dir mwa, ‘Segner, Segner’ ki pou rant dan rwayom lesiel, me zis bann ki fer volonte mo papa ki dan lesiel."
Matthew7:22 Zour zizman, pou ena boukou ki pou dir mwa ‘Segner, Segner, lor to nom nou finn azir kouma profet, lor to nom nou finn sas bann move lespri, lor to nom ki nou finn akonpli boukou mirak.’"
Matthew7:23 Lerla li pou dir zot, ‘Zame mo pa finn konn zot; sorti la ale, zot ki komet lemal.’"
Matthew7:24 Koumsamem, tou dimoun ki ekout saki mo fek dir e met li anpratik, li parey enn zom ki finn ranz so lakaz lor fondasion solid."
Matthew7:25 Lapli tonbe, linondasion vini, divan soufle lor lakaz la, li pa kraze, akoz li finn konstrir lor ros."
Matthew7:26 E tou dimoun ki ekout mo parol e pa met li anpratik, zot pou parey enn fou ki konstrir so lakaz lor disab."
Matthew7:27 Lapli tonbe, linondasion vini, divan soufle lor lakaz la, li kraze.”"
Matthew7:28 Ler Zezi fini dir sa bann zafer la, lafoul ti etone par so lansegnman,"
Matthew7:29 parski li ti ansegn zot parey enn kikenn ki ena lotorite, pa parey kouma bann dokter lalwa."
Matthew8:1 Ler Zezi sorti lor montagn pe desann anba, enn gran lafoul swiv li."
Matthew8:2 Enn lepre vinn kot li, tom azenou devan li e dir, “Si sa to volonte, to kapav geri mwa.”"
Matthew8:3 Zezi poz lame lor li, tous li, e dir li, “Samem mo volonte, aster to pou pirifie.” Deswit li vinn prop."
Matthew8:4 Zezi dir li, “Ekout bien, pa rakont sa personn, me al get enn pret, donn seki Moiz finn dir pou pirifikasion; sa pou enn temwagnaz pou lezot.”"
Matthew8:5 Kouma Zezi ariv Kafarnaom, enn ofisie Romin vinn get li e sipliy li,"
Matthew8:6 “Segner, mo serviter finn paralize lakaz, li dan move soufrans.”"
Matthew8:7 Zezi dir ofisie la, “Mwa, mo pou al ar twa, pou geri li.”"
Matthew8:8 Me ofisie la reponn, “Segner, mo pa dign pou resevwar twa kot mwa, me dir selma enn parol e mo serviter pou geri."
Matthew8:9 Momem, mo anba lotorite mo bann siperyer, e mo ena enn bann solda anba mo lotorite; si mo dir enn, ‘Ale’ li ale, enn lot ‘Vini’ li vini e avek mo esklav ‘Fer sa’ e li fer li.”"
Matthew8:10 Zezi ti etone ler li tann sa, e li dir bann ki ti swiv li, “Laverite mo dir zot, zame mo pa finn trouv kikenn avek enn lafwa parey dan Izrael.”"
Matthew8:11 Ala mo dir zot: boukou pou sorti dan les ek dan lwes e pou asiz atab avek Abraam, Izaak, ek Zakob dan rwayom lesiel."
Matthew8:12 Me bann ki sipoze dan rwayom, pou gagn zet deor dan nwar kot zot pou plore ek grins zot ledan."
Matthew8:13 Zezi dir ofisie la, “Ale, ki tou kiksoz ariv dapre to lafwa.” E sa mem moman la serviter la finn geri."
Matthew8:14 Zezi al dan lakaz Pier, li rantre e li trouv belmer Pier lor lili avek enn move lafiev"
Matthew8:15 Zezi trap so lame, lafiev la kit li, li dibout li koumans servi Zezi."
Matthew8:16 Sa swar la, zot ti amenn kot li boukou ki ti posede ar move lespri; Zezi ti sas bann lespri la avek so parol e li geri tou seki ti malad."
Matthew8:17 Tousala ti arive dapre seki profet Izai ti dir, “Li pran lor li tou nou bann infirmite ek nou bann maladi.”"
Matthew8:18 Ler Zezi trouv sa gran lafoul la otour li, li donn lord pou travers lot kote larivier."
Matthew8:19 Enn dokter lalwa apros ar li e dir li, “Met, mo pou swiv twa ninport ki kote to ale.”"
Matthew8:20 Zezi dir li, “Bann renar ena zot lakav, zwazo lesiel ena zot nik, me Garson Limanite pena okenn landrwa pou poz so latet.”"
Matthew8:21 Enn lot disip dir li, “Segner, les mwa al anter mo papa avan.”"
Matthew8:22 Zezi dir li, “Swiv mwa, e les bann mor anter zot mor.”"
Matthew8:23 Zezi mont dan bato, e so bann disip swiv li."
Matthew8:24 Enn gro divan soufle lor lamer, zot bato ti pre pou savire, me Zezi ti pe dormi."
Matthew8:25 Zot al lev li, zot dir li, “Sov nou, Segner, nou pe mor.”"
Matthew8:26 Li dir zot, “Kifer zot per? Ala zot lafwa feb la.” Apre li leve, li menas divan ek vag e ti ena enn gran akalmi."
Matthew8:27 Tou dimoun etone, zot dir, “Kisannla sa? Mem divan ek lamer obeir li.”"
Matthew8:28 Ler li ariv lot kote, lor teritwar Gadarenien, de posede vinn ar li; zot sorti dan simitier. Zot ti telman feros ki personn pa ti kapav pas dan sa sime la."
Matthew8:29 Zot kriye for-for, “Ki to le ar nou, Garson Bondie? Eski to finn vinn isi pou fatig nou avan ler?”"
Matthew8:30 Ti ena enn troupo koson ki ti pe manze dan lezanviron.
Matthew8:31 Bann posede la sipliy li, “Si to sas nou, avoy nou dan sa troupo koson la”"
Matthew8:32 Zezi dir zot, “Ale!” Alor zot sorti e zot rant dan troupo koson. Troupo la degringol depi lao, tom dan lamer e zot tou nwaye."
Matthew8:33 Bann gardien koson sove, zot al dan lavil e zot rakont tou seki finn pase avek sa de posede la."
Matthew8:34 Alor tou dimoun dan lavil sorti pou vinn zwenn Zezi; ler zot trouv li, zot sipliy li kit zot teritwar."
Matthew9:1 Zezi mont dan bato, li travers larivier, li al dan so lavil."
Matthew9:2 Zot amenn ar li enn paralize alonze lor enn brankar. Ler Zezi trouv grander zot lafwa, li dir paralize la, “Pran kouraz mo garson; to bann pese finn pardone.”"
Matthew9:3 Detrwa dokter lalwa ti pe dir dan zotmem, “Sa boug la pe blasfeme.”"
Matthew9:4 Me Zezi ti konn zot panse, li dir zot, “Kifer zot ena move panse dan zot leker?"
Matthew9:5 Ki pli fasil pou dir, ‘To pese finn pardone,’ oubien ‘Leve, marse’?"
Matthew9:6 Me pou zot kone ki Garson Limanite ena lotorite lor later pou pardonn pese,” Li dir paralize la, “Leve, pran to lili retourn kot twa.”"
Matthew9:7 Li leve, li al kot li."
Matthew9:8 Letan lafoul trouv sa, laper trap zot, e zot glorifie Bondie ki finn donn limanite enn lotorite parey."
Matthew9:9 Letan Zezi kite li ale, li trouv enn boug ki ti apel Matie, li ti pe asiz dan biro tax. Zezi dir li, “Swiv mwa.” Matie leve swiv li."
Matthew9:10 Letan Zezi ti atab dan lakaz, boukou komi tax ek dimoun move lavi ti vinn asiz atab avek Zezi ek so bann disip"
Matthew9:11 Letan bann Farizien trouv sa, zot dir ar bann disip Zezi, “Kifer zot Met, li manz avek bann komi tax ek dimoun move lavi?”"
Matthew9:12 Me ler Zezi tann sa li dir, “Bann dimoun ki bien pa bizin dokter, zis bann seki malad."
Matthew9:13 Ale, al aprann seki sa parol la vedir, ‘Mo dezir mizerikord, pa sakrifis zanimo. Parski mo pa finn vini pou apel bann zis me bann peser.’ ”"
Matthew9:14 Apre sa, bann disip Zan vinn get Zezi e dimann li, “Kifer nou ek bann Farizien, nou fer karem, me to disip pa fer karem ditou?”"
Matthew9:15 Zezi dir zot, “Eski zot panse ki bann invite dan maryaz kapav andey pandan ki nouvo marye ankor avek zot? Enn zour pou arive kot nouvo marye pou ale, lerla zot pou fer karem."
Matthew9:16 Personn pa rakomod enn vie linz avek enn tisi nef; parski latwal tisi nef la pou retresi e pou desir ankor plis sa vie linz la.
Matthew9:17 E personn pa met nouvo divin dan bann vie damzann, sinon zot pou kase, divin pou fane e damzann la pou nepli bon. Nou met nouvo divin dan damzann nef e koumsa toulede pou konserve.”"
Matthew9:18 Letan li ankor pe koz ar zot, enn sef Zwif arive e tom azenou devan Zezi, li dir, “Mo tifi fek mor, me vinn poz to lame lor li e li pou viv.”"
Matthew9:19 Zezi leve, li swiv li avek so bann disip."
Matthew9:20 Lerla enn madam ki pe soufer avek enn lemorazi pandan douz-an, vinn deryer Zezi e tous bor so linz,"
Matthew9:21 parski li ti finn dir dan limem, “Si selman mo kapav tous so linz, mo pou geri.”"
Matthew9:22 Zezi vire, e ler li trouv madam la, li dir, “Pran kouraz mo tifi, to lafwa finn geri twa.” Deswit madam la geri."
Matthew9:23 Ler Zezi ariv kot lakaz sa sef Zwif la, li trouv bann mizisien pe zwe laflit e lafoul ki pe fer enn pake tapaz."
Matthew9:24 Li dir, “Sorti la tou dimoun, tifi la pa finn mor, li pe dormi”. Zot tou zot riy li."
Matthew9:25 Me ler tou dimoun finn sorti, Zezi rant dan lakaz, li pran li par so lame e tifi la leve."
Matthew9:26 Sa nouvel la ti fane dan tou landrwa.
Matthew9:27 E ler Zezi al inpe pli lwin, de aveg swiv li, zot kriye bien for, “Pitie nou, garson David”"
Matthew9:28 Ler li rant dan lakaz, bann aveg la vinn kot li e Zezi dir zot, “Eski zot krwar ki mo kapav fer sa?” Zot dir, “Wi Segner.”"
Matthew9:29 Apre li tous zot lizie, e dir, “Sa pou arive dapre zot lafwa.”"
Matthew9:30 Zot lizie ouver. Zezi donn zot enn warning pou pa rakont sa personn.
Matthew9:31 Me apenn zot ale, zot fann sa nouvel la dan tou landrwa."
Matthew9:32 Ler zot ti pe sorti pou ale, dimoun ti amenn devan Zezi enn boug ki pa koze e ki ti posede."
Matthew9:33 Kouma li fini sas demon la, boug la koumans koze e lafoul ti etone, zot dir, “Zame zot finn trouv kiksoz parey dan Izrael.”"
Matthew9:34 Me bann Farizien ti pe dir, “Li servi prins demon pou sas demon.”"
Matthew9:35 Zezi ti al partou dan Galile, li ti pe ansegne dan zot sinagog, li ti pe proklam Bonn Nouvel Rwayom Bondie. Li ti geri bann dimoun ki ti ena tousort kalite malad."
Matthew9:36 Ler Zezi get lafoul, li ti ranpli ar konpasion pou zot, parski zot ti pe plegne e zot ti abat kouma bann mouton ki pena berze."
Matthew9:37 Lerla li dir so bann disip, “Ena enn gran rekolt, me pena ase travayer."
Matthew9:38 Alor, priye met larekolt pou avoy travayer”"
Matthew10:1 Zezi apel so douz disip e li donn zot pouvwar pou sas bann move lespri ek geri tou sort kalite maladi ek infirmite
Matthew10:2 Ala nom bann apot: premie se Simon, so ti-nom Pier, so frer Andre; Zak garson Zebede, ek so frer Zan;"
Matthew10:3 Filip ek Bartime; Toma ek Matie ramaser tax; Zak ti garson Alfe, e Tade,"
Matthew10:4 Simon ki sorti Kana, e Zida Iskaryot, limem ki pou trair Zezi."
Matthew10:5 Zezi ti avoy Ledouz anmision avek sa bann instriksion la, “Pa bizin al dan rezion bann payin, pa rant dan okenn lavil bann Samaritin,"
Matthew10:6 al plito kot bann brebi perdi dan Izrael.
Matthew10:7 Lor zot sime, anons, ‘Rwayom Bondie pe aprose.’"
Matthew10:8 Geri bann malad, resisit bann mor, pirifie bann lepre, sas bann demon. Zot finn resevwar tou kado, donn tou kado."
Matthew10:9 Pa pran ni lor, ni larzan, ni pies kwiv dan zot pos,"
Matthew10:10 okenn sak vwayaz, okenn semiz resanz, pa pran sandalet ek baton, parski enn travayer merit so saler."
Matthew10:11 Ninport ki lavil ou vilaz ki zot rantre, rod kisannla ki pare pou akeyir zot, res kot li ziska zot depar."
Matthew10:12 Letan zot rant dan enn lakaz, souet lape tou dimoun,"
Matthew10:13 si sa bann dimoun la tret zot bien, zot lape res lor zot, me si pa bien resevwar zot, repran zot lape."
Matthew10:14 Si personn pa resevwar zot oubien refiz ekout zot parol, tap zot lipie e tir tou lapousier letan zot kit lakaz la ou lavil la."
Matthew10:15 Laverite mo dir zot, bann dimoun dan Sodom ek Gomor pou gagn pli bon tretman ki sa bann dimoun la."
Matthew10:16 Get bien, mo pe avoy zot kouma bann mouton parmi bann loulou; zot bizin bien malin kouma serpan e inosan kouma kolonb."
Matthew10:17 Fer bien atansion, akoz ena pou amenn zot devan tribinal e pou fwet zot dan zot sinagog;"
Matthew10:18 akoz mwa, zot pou pas devan bann gouverner ek bann lerwa, sa pou servi bann la ek lezot kouma enn temwagnaz."
Matthew10:19 Kan pou amenn zot devan tribinal, pa trakase ki zot pou dir e kouma zot pou dir sa; parol la pou vinn par limem dan zot labous;"
Matthew10:20 pa zot ki pou koze, me Lespri Bondie ki pou koz atraver zot."
Matthew10:21 Frer pou trair frer, papa pou kont so zanfan, zanfan pou lev kont zot fami e pou kondann zot amor."
Matthew10:22 Tou dimoun pou air zot akoz mwa, me seki tini ferm ziska dan bout, li pou sove."
Matthew10:23 Letan zot gagn persekite dan enn lavil, sove al dan enn lot; laverite mo dir zot, avan ki zot reysi al dan tou lavil Izrael Garson Limanite pou finn fini vini."
Matthew10:24 Enn disip, pa pli siperyer ki so met; ni enn esklav ki so patron;"
Matthew10:25 Enn disip bizin zis resanble so met ek esklav la so patron. Si zot apel sef enn lakaz Belzeboul, mazine aster ki nom zot pou donn so fami."
Matthew10:26 Pa per personn. Tou saki kasiet pou vinn dan kler, tou saki sekre pou devwale;"
Matthew10:27 seki mo dir zot dan marenwar, dir li dan lalimier lizour; seki zot finn tann dir dousman dan zot zorey, mont lor lakaz, dir li bien for."
Matthew10:28 Pa per bann ki touy lekor imin, me ki pa kapav touy so nam; okontrer per saki kapav detrir toulede, nam ek lekor dan lanfer."
Matthew10:29 Eski zot pa vann de mwano pou enn sou? Pourtan, pa enn sel tom anba san ki Bondie nou Papa kone."
Matthew10:30 Zot osi, sak brin zot seve konte."
Matthew10:31 Alor, pa bizin per, zot ena plis valer ki enn mwano.”"
Matthew10:32 “Si kikenn rekonet mwa anpiblik ki mo ete, mwa osi mo pou rekonet li devan mo Papa dan lesiel;"
Matthew10:33 me si kikenn dir anpiblik ki li pa konn mwa, mwa osi mo pou dir ki mo pa konn li devan mo Papa dan lesiel.”"
Matthew10:34 “Pa panse ki mo finn vini pou amenn lape lor later; mo pa finn vini pou amenn lape, me lepe."
Matthew10:35 Mo finn vinn separ enn garson avek so papa, tifi ek so mama, belfi ek belmer."
Matthew10:36 To lennmi pou dan to prop fami.
Matthew10:37 Seki kontan so papa oubien so mama plis ki mwa, li pa dign pou vinn mo disip."
Matthew10:38 Seki pa pran so lakrwa pou swiv mwa, li pa dign pou vinn mo disip."
Matthew10:39 Seki anvi sov so lavi, pou perdi li; me seki perdi so lavi akoz mwa, pou gagn li.”"
Matthew10:40 “Dimoun ki akeyir zot, akeyir mwa, dimoun ki akeyir mwa, pe akeyir sa enn ki finn avoy mwa la."
Matthew10:41 Dimoun ki akeyir enn profet akoz li enn profet pou gagn rekonpans enn profet; dimoun ki akeyir enn fidel akoz li enn fidel, li pou gagn rekonpans enn fidel."
Matthew10:42 Laverite mo dir zot, si kikenn donn enn ver dilo enn sa bann pli tipti parmi zot, akoz li mo disip, les mo dir zot, li pou gagn so rekonpans.”"
Matthew11:1 Ler Zezi fini donn instriksion so douz disip, li kit sa landrwa la pou al prese ek ansegne dan lavil kot zot reste."
Matthew11:2 Dan prizon, ler Zan tann travay ki Zezi pe fer, li avoy detrwa disip,"
Matthew11:3 pou dimann Zezi, “Eski tomem Sa-Enn ki sipoze vini la, oubien nou bizin atann enn lot?”"
Matthew11:4 Zezi reponn zot, “Al rakont Zan seki zot finn tande ek trouve:"
Matthew11:5 bann aveg pe trouv kler, bann andikape pe marse, bann lepre pe pirifie, bann sourd pe tande, bann mor pe resisite e bann pov pe tann Bonn Nouvel ki pe anonse."
Matthew11:6 Bienere, sa dimoun ki pa tom dan pese akoz mwa.”"
Matthew11:7 Apre ki bann disip Zan finn ale, Zezi koz ar lafoul lor size Zan, e li dir: “Ki zot finn al gete dan dezer? Enn fatak balanse dan divan?"
Matthew11:8 Ki zot finn al gete? Enn zom bien abiye? Me bann ki met zoli linz, res dan pale lerwa."
Matthew11:9 Abe ki zot finn al gete? Enn profet? Wi, les mo dir zot, li plis ki enn profet."
Matthew11:10 Parski lor Zan mem ki finn ekrir: ‘Gete, mo pe avoy mo mesaze avan twa pou prepar to sime.’"
Matthew11:11 Laverite mo dir zot, parmi tou dimoun ki finn ne lor later, pena enn pli gran ki Zan Batis; pourtan sa ki pli tipti dan rwayom lesiel, pli gran ki li."
Matthew11:12 Depi lepok Zan Batis ziska zordi, rwayom lesiel finn toultan sibir violans e bann dimoun violan finn akapar li."
Matthew11:13 Tou bann profet ek lalwa Moiz finn anons sa rwayom la ziska lepok Zan.
Matthew11:14 E si zot anvi kone, ala mo dir zot. Zan, limem Eli ki sipoze vini."
Matthew11:15 Seki ena zorey, ava tande."
Matthew11:16 Koman mo pou konpar sa zenerasion la? Li parey kouma bann zanfan ki pe asize lor laplas piblik ki pe koze ant zot,"
Matthew11:17 ‘Nou finn zwe zoli lamizik pou zot e zot pa finn danse; nou finn zwe kantik lanterman e zot pa finn plore.’
Matthew11:18 Zan finn vini, li pa finn manze ni bwar, e zot finn dir, ‘Li enn posede!’"
Matthew11:19 Garson Limanite finn vini, li manze, li bwar e zot dir, ‘Li enn gourman, li soular, li frekant bann ramaser tax ek bann move dimoun.’ Pourtan li finn demontre lasazes Bondie par so bann bonaksion.”"
Matthew11:20 Alor Zezi koumans fer repros ar sa bann lavil kot li finn fer boukou mirak parski dimoun pa finn konverti.
Matthew11:21 “Maler pou tom lor twa, lavil Korazin! Maler pou twa, lavil Betsaida! Parski si bann mirak ki finn arive kot zot, ti ariv dan Tir ek Sidon, depi lontan sa bann lavil la ti pou finn montre piblikman ki zot finn sanz zot leker."
Matthew11:22 Les mo dir zot, zour zizman, Tir ek Sidon pou gagn enn meyer tretman ki zot."
Matthew11:23 Twa Kafarnaom, eski to krwar to pou mont drwat dan lesiel? To pou desann ziska dan lanfer parski si sa bann mirak ki finn arive kot twa la, ti deroul dan Sodom, ziska zordi sa lavil la ti pou ankor existe."
Matthew11:24 Akoz samem, mo dir zot, zour zizman li pou pli dir pou zot ki pou Sodom.”"
Matthew11:25 Samem lepok la Zezi dir “Mo remersie twa, Papa, Segner lesiel ek later, parski to pa finn montre sa bann kiksoz la bann saz ek bann intelizan, me to finn revel zot ar bann pli tipti."
Matthew11:26 Wi, Papa samem ti to volonte."
Matthew11:27 Mo Papa finn donn mwa tou e personn pa kapav konn so garson exsepte so Papa, personn pa kapav konn so Papa exsepte so Garson ek dimoun ar ki so garson anvi revel li."
Matthew11:28 Vinn kot mwa zot tou ki fatige, ki pe sarye enn fardo bien lour, mo pou donn zot repo."
Matthew11:29 Met mo fardo lor zot ledo, e vinn aprann ar mwa parski mo karakter li dou e mo leker ranpli ar imilite"
Matthew11:30 Mo zoug li fasil sarye e mo fardo li leze.”
Matthew12:1 Sa mem lepok la, enn zour saba, Zezi ti pe travers enn karo dible; so bann disip ti gagn fin, e zot koumans kas bann zepi dible pou manze."
Matthew12:2 Ler bann Farizien trouv sa, zot dir li, “Get sa, to bann disip pe fer kiksoz ki pena drwa fer zour saba.”"
Matthew12:3 Me Zezi reponn zot, li dir, “Eski zot pa finn lir seki David ti fer kan li ek so bann kamarad ti gagn fin?"
Matthew12:4 Koman li ti rant dan lakaz Bondie e kouma li ti manz dipin ki ti finn ofer Bondie? Pourtan ni li, ni so bann kamarad pa ti sipoze fer sa, parski dapre lalwa, zis bann pret gagn drwa manz sa."
Matthew12:5 Zot pa finn lir osi dan lalwa, ki zour saba, bann pret kas lalwa saba dan tanp san ki zot rann zot koupab?"
Matthew12:6 Les mo dir zot, isi ena kiksoz pli gran ki tanp."
Matthew12:7 Me si zot ti konpran sinifikasion sa bann mo Lekritir la, ‘mo dezir mizerikord, pa sakrifis,’ zot pa ti pou kondann bann inosan."
Matthew12:8 Parski Garson Limanite, limem propriyeter saba.”"
Matthew12:9 Zezi kit sa landrwa la e rant dan zot sinagog;
Matthew12:10 ti ena la enn boug; so lame ti paralize. Bann Farizien ti anvi piez Zezi; zot dir li, “Eski lalwa permet fer gerizon zour saba?”"
Matthew12:11 Li dir zot, “Sipoze enn parmi zot ena enn sel mouton e zour saba mouton la tom dan enn gran trou; eski li pa pou fer enn demars pou tir so mouton depi dan trou la?"
Matthew12:12 Dimoun ena san fwa plis valer ki enn mouton. Alor lalwa li permet fer dibien zour saba.”
Matthew12:13 Li dir paralize la; “Donn to lame.” Li tann so lame, e sa revinn parey kouma lot lame la."
Matthew12:14 Bann Farizien sorti e zot koumans konplote, pou gete kouma pou fer li disparet."
Matthew12:15 Ler Zezi aprann sa, li kit sa landrwa la. Enn gran lafoul swiv li e li geri zot tou,"
Matthew12:16 li warning zot pou pa dir nanye lor li ar dimoun.
Matthew12:17 Sa ti arive pouki seki profet Izai ti dir akonpli:
Matthew12:18 “Ala mo serviter, ki mo finn swazir, mo bieneme, dan ki mo finn met tou mo lazwa. Mo pou met mo Lespri lor li, e li pou pres lazistis ar bann payin"
Matthew12:19 Li pa pou lager ar personn, li pa pou kriye, pa pou tann so lavwa lor gran sime"
Matthew12:20 li pa pou kas okenn baton rozo ki ti finn deza pliye, li pa pou soufle lor enn lames ki deza pe al tegn. Me li pou persiste ziska li fer lazistis triyonfe,"
Matthew12:21 e tou dimoun pou fer li konfians.”
Matthew12:22 Zot amenn ar Zezi enn aveg ki ti mie parski ti ena enn demon dan li. Zezi geri boug la e lerla li koze ek li trouv kler.
Matthew12:23 Lafoul ti etone e zot dir, “Pa limem Garson David?”"
Matthew12:24 Ler bann Farizien tann sa, zot dir, “Li sas demon par Belzeboul, sef demon.”"
Matthew12:25 Zezi ki konn zot panse dir zot, “Enn rwayom ki divize kont limem, li enn rwayom fini, e okenn lavil ou lakaz ki divize kont limem kapav tini."
Matthew12:26 Si Satan sas Satan, li diviz limem; kouma so rwayom pou kapav tini?"
Matthew12:27 E si mwa, mo sas demon par Belzeboul, par ki zot prop disip sas demon? Bann la mem pou ziz zot."
Matthew12:28 Me si mwa, mo sas demon par Lespri Bondie, savedir ki regn Bondie finn deza vinn kot zot."
Matthew12:29 Kouma kikenn kapav rant dan lakaz enn zom for pou pran so bann dibien si li pa atas li avan? Lerla li kapav kokin.
Matthew12:30 Dimoun ki pa avek mwa, li kont mwa, dimoun ki pa rasanble ar mwa, fer divizion."
Matthew12:31 Akoz samem mo dir zot, tou bann pese, tou bann blasfem pou pardone, me blasfem kont Lespri Sin pa pou pardone."
Matthew12:32 Si kikenn koz kont Garson Limanite, li pou pardone, me si kikenn koz kont Lespri Sin, li pa pou pardone, ni lor later ni dan lemonn ki pe vini."
Matthew12:33 Swa fer enn pie vinn bon lerla so fri osi pou bon, swa enn pie malad lerla so fri osi pou malad, parski nou rekonet pie la dapre so fri."
Matthew12:34 Bann espes serpan! Kouma bon kiksoz kapav sorti dan zot labous, kan zotmem zot move? Parski labous exprim seki ena dan fon leker."
Matthew12:35 Enn bon dimoun tir dan so bon trezor bann bon kiksoz, e enn dimoun move tir move kiksoz dan so move trezor."
Matthew12:36 Les mo dir zot, zour zizman zot pou zize lor tou sa bann parol initil ki zot dir;"
Matthew12:37 parski pou deklar zot drwat par zot parol, e zot pou kondane par zot parol.”"
Matthew12:38 Detrwa dokter lalwa ek Farizien dir ar Zezi, “Met, nou ti anvi to donn nou enn sign.”"
Matthew12:39 Li reponn zot, “Zenerasion move ek adilter, zot pe rod enn sign, okenn sign pa pou donn zot anplis ki sign profet Zonas."
Matthew12:40 Parey Zonas ti pas trwa zour ek trwa nwit dan vant enn gro pwason, koumsamem Garson Limanite pou pas trwa zour ek trwa nwit anba later."
Matthew12:41 Bann abitan Niniv pou leve zour zizman e zot pou kondann sa zenerasion la, parski zot, zot ti konverti ler Zonas ti pres zot la parol. Ena isi pli gran ki Zonas!"
Matthew12:42 Larenn Seba pou leve zour zizman kont sa zenerasion la e li pou kondann li parski li finn sorti dan fin-fon later pou ekout lasazes Salomon. Me ena isi pli gran ki Salomon!”
Matthew12:43 “Ler enn lespri inpir sorti dan enn dimoun, li vwayaz dan bann landrwa dezer pou rod enn plas pou repoze, me li pa trouv nanye."
Matthew12:44 Alor li dir dan limem, ‘Mo pou retourn dan mo lakaz, la kot mo sorti.’ Ler li retourne, li trouv lakaz la vid, bien netwaye e bien dan lord."
Matthew12:45 Lerla li al rod set lespri pli for ki li, zot rant dan lakaz la zot tou e zot instal zot; alafin, sa dimoun la li finn vinn pir ki avan. Li pou parey avek sa zenerasion la.”"
Matthew12:46 Letan li ti ankor pe koz ar lafoul, so mama ek so bann frer vini. Zot ti pe dibout deor e zot ti pe anvi koz ar li."
Matthew12:47 Kikenn dir li, “To mama ek to bann frer deor, zot anvi koz ar twa.”"
Matthew12:48 Zezi reponn li, “Kisannla mo mama? Kisannla mo bann frer?”"
Matthew12:49 Lerla li montre zot so bann disip e li dir, “Ala mo mama ek mo bann frer!"
Matthew12:50 Parski dimoun kifer dapre volonte mo Papa ki dan lesiel, limem mo frer, mo ser ek mo mama.”"
Matthew13:1 Sa mem zour la Zezi sorti deor, li al asiz dan borlamer."
Matthew13:2 Enn gran lafoul ti finn antour li; lafoul ti telman gran ki li ti finn bizin mont dan pirog e li asize; lafoul finn res ater dan bor dilo.
Matthew13:3 Alor Zezi koz ar zot an parabol, li dir, “Tann sa: enn planter sorti pou al seme;"
Matthew13:4 letan li seme, enn parti lagrin tom dan bor sime; bann zwazo vini, manz tou."
Matthew13:5 Enn lot parti tom dan landrwa inpe ros-ros kot pena boukou later; zot pouse vit-vit parski later ti bien mins.
Matthew13:6 Me kan soley tape, zot griye, zot fletri parski zot pa ti ena ase rasinn."
Matthew13:7 Enn lot parti tom dan pikan; pikan la monte, grandi e touf zot."
Matthew13:8 Enn lot parti tom dan bon later, zot pouse e raport boukou fri, enn raport san, enn lot swasant, enn lot trant."
Matthew13:9 Saki ena zorey pou tande, ava tande.”"
Matthew13:10 So bann disip vinn ar li e dimann li, “Kifer to koz an parabol?”"
Matthew13:11 Li reponn zot, “Parski zot, finn donn zot kapasite resevwar don pou konn sekre Rwayom Bondie, me lezot pa finn resevwar sa."
Matthew13:12 Parski seki ena, pou gagn ankor plis e li pou gagn plis ki bizin; me seki pena la, mem sa tigit ki li ena, sa osi pou pran ar li."
Matthew13:13 Ala kifer mo koz ar zot an parabol, parski zot pe gete san trouve e zot pe ekoute san tande e san konpran."
Matthew13:14 Sa parol ki profet Izai ti dir pou zot la, pe akonpli: ‘Zot pou bon ekoute me zot pa pou konpran zot pou bon gete e zot pa pou trouve."
Matthew13:15 parski leker sa pep la finn vinn dir; zot zorey bouse, zot finn ferm zot lizie, pouki zot pa get ar zot lizie, pouki zot pa ekout ar zot zorey, pouki zot pa konpran ar zot leker, e ki zot pa konverti; e mo ti pou geri zot.’"
Matthew13:16 Me zot, zot bienere, parski zot lizie trouve e zot zorey tande."
Matthew13:17 Laverite, mo dir zot, boukou profet ek dimoun ki viv drwat devan Bondie ti anvi trouv seki zot finn trouve, me zot pa finn trouve; e ti anvi tann seki zot finn tande, me zot pa finn tande.”"
Matthew13:18 “Ekout bien sinifikasion parabol planter.
Matthew13:19 Kan kikenn tann koze lor Rwayom Bondie e li pa konpran, diab vini, ras tou saki finn seme dan so leker. Li resanble sa sime kot lagrin finn tonbe la."
Matthew13:20 Saki finn seme dan terin ros li resanble sa dimoun letan li tann laparol, toutswit li resevwar li dan lazwa."
Matthew13:21 Me pena rasinn dan li e laparol res dan li pou enn ti moman; me ler persekision ek lezot problem vini akoz laparol, so lafwa tom enn sel kout."
Matthew13:22 Saki finn seme dan pikan, li resanble sa dimoun ki tann laparol, me bann problem lavi tou lezour, lamour dibien materyel touf tou e li pa raport okenn fri."
Matthew13:23 Me saki finn seme dan bon later, li resanble sa dimoun ki tann laparol, konpran li bien e ki raport bann fri; ena raport san, enn lot swasant e enn lot bann trant.”"
Matthew13:24 Zezi rakont lafoul enn lot parabol: “Kapav konpar Rwayom Bondie ar enn dimoun ki finn sem enn bon lagrin dan so karo;
Matthew13:25 me ler tou dimoun pe dormi, enn lennmi vini e sem move lerb dan karo dible la, apre li ale."
Matthew13:26 Alor letan bann pie dible pouse e donn bann zepi, move lerb la osi pouse."
Matthew13:27 Bann serviter propriyeter vinn dimann li, ‘Met, eski to pa finn sem bon lagrin dan to karo? Kot sa bann move lerb la sorti alor?’"
Matthew13:28 Li reponn zot, ‘Enn lennmi ki finn fer sa.’ Bann serviter dir li, ‘Eski to oule ki nou al ras zot?’"
Matthew13:29 Li reponn, ‘Non, parski letan zot ras move lerb la, zot kapav derasinn osi bann pie dible."
Matthew13:30 Les toulede grandi ansam ziska rekolt; lerla mo pou dimann bann travayer ramas move lerb avan, atas zot ansam, fer bann pake pou bril zot, me ramas dible dan mo grenie.’ ”"
Matthew13:31 Zezi rakont zot enn lot parabol, li dir, “Rwayom lesiel, parey kouma lagrin moutard ki kikenn pran pou sem dan so karo;"
Matthew13:32 limem pli tipti lagrin dan tou bann lagrin, me kan li grandi li vinn pli gran touf. Apre li vinn enn pie kot bann zwazo vinn fer zot nik dan so brans.”"
Matthew13:33 Li rakont zot enn lot parabol, “Rwayom Lesiel, parey kouma levin ki enn madam pran pou melanz avek trwa goble lafarinn ziska tou lapat la monte.”"
Matthew13:34 Zezi ti koz an parabol avek lafoul; li pa ti dir nanye san servi parabol.
Matthew13:35 Li fer sa pouki parol profet realize: “Mo pou koz an parabol, mo pou anons bann kiksoz ki finn res kasiet depi kreasion lemonn.”"
Matthew13:36 Zezi kit lafoul e rant lakaz. So bann disip vinn kot li, e dir li, “Explik nou parabol move lerb dan karo.”"
Matthew13:37 Li reponn, “Sa dimoun ki sem bon lagrin la limem Garson Limanite."
Matthew13:38 Karo la samem lemonn; e bann bon lagrin la zotmem bann zanfan Rwayom Bondie; move lerb reprezant bann zanfan lennmi Bondie,"
Matthew13:39 sa lennmi ki sem move lerb limem Satan, rekolt reprezant lafin-dimonn, e bann travayer zotmem bann anz."
Matthew13:40 Parey kouma nou ramas bann move lerb pou brile, koumsamem li pou ete ler lafin-dimonn arive."
Matthew13:41 Garson Limanite pou avoy so bann anz; zot pou ramas tou bann ki finn antrenn lezot dan lemal pou met zot andeor so rwayom e li pou fer parey ar bann ki finn komet lemal.
Matthew13:42 Li pou zet zot dan enn gran dife, kot pou ena plore, kriye ek grinsman ledan."
Matthew13:43 Lerla, bann ki finn res fidel pou briye kouma lalimier soley dan rwayom zot Papa. Seki ena zorey ava tande.”"
Matthew13:44 “Rwayom lesiel, parey kouma enn trezor ki finn kasiet dan enn karo. Ler kikenn dekouver li, li rekasiet li; li telman kontan ki li vann tou seki li ena e li al aste sa karo la.”"
Matthew13:45 “Rwayom lesiel, parey kouma enn marsan ki pe rod bann perl rar;"
Matthew13:46 ler li trouv enn ki ena enn bel valer, li al vann tou seki li ena pou al aste sa perl la.”"
Matthew13:47 “Rwayom lesiel, parey kouma enn file ki zot avoy dan lamer. File la may tou sort kalite pwason;"
Matthew13:48 kan li finn bien ranpli, zot amenn li ater, zot asize, zot met bann bon pwason dan enn panie e zet bann seki pa bon."
Matthew13:49 Koumsamem li pou ete ler lafin-dimonn arive. Bann anz pou vini, pou separ bann ki move avek bann ki finn res fidel."
Matthew13:50 Seki move pou zet zot dan sa gran dife la, kot pou ena boukou plore ek kriye e grinsman ledan.”"
Matthew13:51 “Eski zot finn konpran tousala?” Zot reponn, “Wi.”"
Matthew13:52 Lerla li dir zot, “Tou dokter lalwa ki finn vinn disip rwayom lesiel, li kouma enn propriyeter lakaz ki separ dan so trezor saki nef ek saki vie.”"
Matthew13:53 Ler Zezi fini rakont sa bann parabol la, li kit sa landrwa la, li ale."
Matthew13:54 Li al dan vilaz kot li ti grandi e li koumans ansegn dimoun dan zot sinagog. Sa bann dimoun la ti etone e zot dir, “Kot li finn gagn sa kalite sazes la? Kouma li kapav fer bel-bel mirak koumsa?"
Matthew13:55 Pa limem garson sarpantie? So mama, pa Marie? So bann frer pa Zak, Zozef, Simon ek Zida?"
Matthew13:56 Tou so bann ser pa res isi avek nou? Be kot li finn gagn tou sa pouvwar la, li?”"
Matthew13:57 Zot refiz aksepte li. Me Zezi dir zot tou, “Enn profet, li onore partou, exsepte dan so prop pei e dan so fami.”"
Matthew13:58 E li pa ti kapav fer okenn mirak dan sa landrwa la, parski zot lafwa ti feb."
Matthew14:1 Sa mem lepok la Erod Tetrark ti tann koz Zezi.
Matthew14:2 Li dir so bann serviter, “Sa Zan Batis sa; li finn leve parmi bann mor e samem li ena pouvwar pou fer bann mirak.”"
Matthew14:3 Parski Erod ti finn fer aret Zan, li ti fer atas li e met li dan prizon akoz Erodiad fam so frer, Filip."
Matthew14:4 Ofet, Zan ti dir li, “Li pa korek ki to pran Erodiad pou fam.”"
Matthew14:5 Erod ti anvi touy li, me li ti per lafoul ki ti finn pran li pou enn profet."
Matthew14:6 Alor, pou laniverser nesans Erod, tifi Erodiad ti dans omilie bann invite e li ti sitan pler Erod"
Matthew14:7 ki li ti pran langazman solanel pou donn li seki li dimande.
Matthew14:8 Lor konsey so mama, li ti fer sa demann la: “Donn mwa, asterlamem latet Zan Batis lor enn plato.”"
Matthew14:9 Lerwa, ki ti finn fer serman devan tou bann invite, ti bien sagrin me li ti donn lord pou akord so demann."
Matthew14:10 Li donn lord koup latet Zan dan prizon.
Matthew14:11 Zot amenn so latet lor enn plato, zot donn tifi la e li donn li so mama."
Matthew14:12 Bann disip Zan ti pran so lekor e zot anter li. Apre sa zot al anons nouvel la Zezi.
Matthew14:13 Ler Zezi tann sa nouvel la, li pran enn bato, li al dan enn landrwa retire li tousel. Me ler lafoul aprann sa, zot kit lavil e swiv li apie."
Matthew14:14 Ler li debark ater, li trouv enn gran lafoul; li pitie zot e li geri tou zot bann maladi."
Matthew14:15 Ler koumans fer nwar, bann disip vinn dir Zezi, “Sa landrwa la li dezer e li deza tar, ranvway sa lafoul la pou zot kapav al aste manze pou zotmem dan vilaz.”"
Matthew14:16 Me Zezi reponn zot, “Kifer zot bizin ale? Donn zot manze zotmem.”"
Matthew14:17 Zot dir li, “Nou ena la zis sink dipin ek de pwason.”"
Matthew14:18 Li dir zot, “Amenn zot kot mwa”"
Matthew14:19 Li ordonn lafoul pou instal zotmem lor lerb, li pran sa sink dipin ek sa de pwason la, li lev so lizie ver lesiel e li beni zot. Apre sa li kas bann dipin la, li donn bann disip pou distribie avek lafoul."
Matthew14:20 Tou dimoun manze vant plin e zot amenn douz panie bann bout ki finn reste.
Matthew14:21 Bann ki ti manze ti anviron sink mil zom san kont bann fam ek bann zanfan.
Matthew14:22 Zis apre sa, Zezi fer bann disip mont dan pirog ale pouki zot ariv avan li lot kote lak, letan sa li fer lafoul al zot lakaz."
Matthew14:23 Apre ki li finn fini fer lafoul ale, li mont lor enn montagn li tousel pou priye. Ler ariv aswar, li ti la li tousel,"
Matthew14:24 me pirog ti finn ariv omilie lamer. Bann gro vag ti pe fwet ar pirog parski ti ena enn divan kontrer.
Matthew14:25 Boner gramatin, Zezi mars lor lamer vinn ar zot."
Matthew14:26 Me ler bann disip trouv li pe mars lor dilo, zot panike e zot dir, “Enn fantom sa!” E zot kriye, zot tranble kouma fey."
Matthew14:27 Me Zezi rasir zot toutswit e li dir, “Kouraz, mwa sa; pa bizin per.”"
Matthew14:28 Pier reponn, “Segner, si tomem sa, donn lord ki mo mars lor dilo pou vinn kot twa.”"
Matthew14:29 Zezi reponn, “Vini.” Alor Pier desann dan pirog e li koumans mars lor dilo dan direksion Zezi."
Matthew14:30 Me letan li remark lafors divan, li gagn per e li koumans koule; li kriye “Segner, sov mwa!”"
Matthew14:31 Zezi nek avoy lame, trap li, tir li e dir li, “To lafwa feb, kifer to finn doute?”"
Matthew14:32 Ler zot rant dan pirog, divan la tonbe."
Matthew14:33 Bann ki ti dan pirog, zot tom azenou, zot loue li, zot dir, “Vremem to Garson Bondie.”"
Matthew14:34 Ler zot finn fini travers lak, zot ariv dan rezion Zenezaret."
Matthew14:35 Letan bann dimoun dan landrwa rekonet Zezi, zot avoy nouvel partou e zot amenn tou bann malad kot li."
Matthew14:36 Zot sipliy li pouki li les zot tous omwin rebor so linz. Tou seki ti reysi touse, li ti geri."
Matthew15:1 Bann Farizien ek bann dokter lalwa ki sorti depi Zerizalem koste ar Zezi e zot dir,"
Matthew15:2 “Kifer to disip pa respekte tradision nou bann gran dimoun? Zot pa lav lame avan manze.”
Matthew15:3 Li reponn zot, “Be zot, kifer zot kas komannman Bondie akoz zot tradision?"
Matthew15:4 Bondie finn dir, ‘Onor to papa ek to mama; e osi, ninport kisannla ki modi so papa ek so mama, li merit lamor.’"
Matthew15:5 Me zot, zot dir si enn dimoun dir ar so papa ou so mama, ‘Seki mo ti kapav donn twa, mo rezerv li pou Bondie’ lerla sa dimoun la nepli bizin onor so papa ou so mama."
Matthew15:6 Me zot, akoz zot tradision, zot pa respekte parol Bondie."
Matthew15:7 Ipokrit, Izai ti ena rezon kan li ti profetiz lor zot, kan li ti dir,"
Matthew15:8 ‘Sa pep la onor mwa zis avek so labous, me so leker lwin ar mwa;"
Matthew15:9 Zot lapriyer pena valer, parski zot ansegn doktrinn bann imin.’ ”"
Matthew15:10 Zezi apel lafoul e li dir, “Tande e konpran bien,"
Matthew15:11 seki enn dimoun met dan so labous pa kapav rann li inpir, me seki sorti dan so labous, samem ki rann li inpir.”"
Matthew15:12 Lerla so bann disip aprose e dir li, “Eski to kone ki bann Farizien ofanse kan zot tann twa koz koumsa?”"
Matthew15:13 Li reponn, “Tou bann plant ki mo papa pa finn plante pou derasine."
Matthew15:14 Les zot trankil; zot kouma enn lider aveg ki pe diriz bann aveg. E si enn aveg diriz enn lot aveg, toulede pou tom dan trou.”"
Matthew15:15 Me Pier dir li, “Explik nou sa parabol la.”"
Matthew15:16 Li dir, “Eski zot pankor konpran zot osi?"
Matthew15:17 Zot pa trouve ki seki rant dan labous, li al dan vant e apre sa li sorti deor, li elimine?"
Matthew15:18 Me seki sorti dan labous sorti dan leker, samem ki rann nou inpir."
Matthew15:19 Parski dan leker sorti bann move lintansion, kouma fer krim, adilter, move lavi, kokin, mansonz ek palab."
Matthew15:20 Sa bann kiksoz la ki rann dimoun inpir, me manz avek lame pa lave pa rann enn dimoun inpir.”"
Matthew15:21 Zezi kit sa landrwa la e li al dan rezion Tir ek Sidon.
Matthew15:22 Enn fam Kananeenn ki sorti dan sa rezion la koumans kriye, “Pitie mwa Segner, Garson David! Mo tifi, li extra posede par enn demon.”"
Matthew15:23 Me Zezi pa dir nanye; so bann disip vinn sipliy li, zot dir li, “Pous li, li pe swiv nou, li pe fatig nou.”"
Matthew15:24 Zezi reponn, li dir, “Bondie finn avoy mwa zis pou bann brebi perdi pep Izrael.”"
Matthew15:25 Me, fam la tom azenou devan Zezi e li dir, “Segner vinn sekour mwa!”"
Matthew15:26 Zezi reponn li, “Li pa bon pran dipin bann zanfan pou zet ar bann tilisien.”"
Matthew15:27 Fam la reponn, “Vremem, Segner, pourtan bann lisien manz bann bout dipin ki tom anba latab zot met.”"
Matthew15:28 Alor Zezi dir li, “Fam, to ena enn gran lafwa; to demann pou exose.” E deswit so tifi geri."
Matthew15:29 Zezi kit sa landrwa la, li mars dan borlamer Galile, li mont lor montagn e li asize."
Matthew15:30 Enn gran lafoul vinn kot li, zot amenn bann bwate, andikape, aveg, sour-miye ek dimoun ar boukou lezot maladi ankor. Zot depoz zot devan Zezi e li geri zot tou."
Matthew15:31 Lafoul ti emerveye ler zot trouv bann mie koze, bann andikape geri, bwate marse e bann aveg trouv kler; lerla zot koumans glorifie Bondie Izrael."
Matthew15:32 Zezi apel so bann disip e li dir, “Mo ranpli ar konpasion pou sa lafoul la. Sa fer trwa zour depi zot avek mwa e zot pa finn manz nanye. Mo pa anvi ranvway zot vant vid, mo per zot gagn febles lor sime.”"
Matthew15:33 Bann disip dir li, “Dan sa landrwa dezer la, kot nou pou gagn ase dipin pou enn lafoul parey?”"
Matthew15:34 Zezi dir zot, “Komie dipin zot ena?” Zot reponn, “Set, avek detrwa tipwason”"
Matthew15:35 Alor li donn lord lafoul asiz anba.
Matthew15:36 Li pran sa set dipin la ek bann pwason la, ler li fini remersi Bondie, li kas zot, li donn so bann disip e bann la partaz avek lafoul."
Matthew15:37 Tou dimoun manze vant plin e zot retourn set korbey ranpli avek bann bout ki reste.
Matthew15:38 Ti ena kat mil zom ki ti manze, san kont bann fam ek bann zanfan."
Matthew15:39 Apre ki li finn ranvway lafoul, li mont dan pirog pou al dan teritwar Magadan."
Matthew16:1 Bann Farizien ek Sadisein avans ver Zezi pou piez li. Zot dimann li enn sign depi lesiel.
Matthew16:2 Li reponn zot, “Ler soley kouse, zot dir, ‘Pou ena botan parski lesiel rouz.’"
Matthew16:3 Boner gramatin zot dir, ‘Lapli pou tonbe zordi parski lesiel kouver.’ Zot kone kouma pou interpret sign lesiel, me zot pa kapav interpret sign letan zordi."
Matthew16:4 Zenerasion move ek adilter pe dimann enn sign, me okenn sign pa pou donn li exsepte sign Zonas.” Apre sa li kit zot li ale."
Matthew16:5 Ler bann disip ariv lot kote lak, zot ti finn bliye amenn dipin avek zot."
Matthew16:6 Zezi dir zot, “Get bien, fer atansion ar levin bann Farizien ek Sadisein.”"
Matthew16:7 Zot dir ant zot, “Sirman parski nou pa finn amenn dipin.”"
Matthew16:8 Ler Zezi aprann tousala, li dir, “Get zot lafwa kouma feb, kifer zot panse ki zot pena dipin?"
Matthew16:9 Eski zot ankor san konpran? Zot pa rapel sa sink dipin ki ti nouri sink mil zom la e kantite panie plin zot ti ramase?
Matthew16:10 Zot pa rapel sa set dipin ki ti nouri sa kat mil zom la ek sa kantite panie plin ki zot ti ramase la?
Matthew16:11 Kouma zot pa konpran ki mo pa pe koz lor dipin? Fer atansion ar levin bann Farizien ek bann Sadisein!”
Matthew16:12 Lerla zot konpran ki li pa ti pe dir zot fer atansion ar levin dipin, me lansegnman ki bann Farizien ek Sadisein ti pe done."
Matthew16:13 Ler Zezi ariv dan distrik Sezare-Filip, li dir so bann disip, “Ki dimoun pe dir lor Garson Limanite?”"
Matthew16:14 Zot dir li, “Enn bann dir Zan Batis, enn lot bann dir Eli e enn lot bann ankor dir Zeremi oubien enn lot profet.”"
Matthew16:15 Li dir zot, “Me zot, ki zot dir mo ete?”"
Matthew16:16 Simon Pier reponn, “To Lemesi, Garson Bondie Vivan.”"
Matthew16:17 Zezi reponn li, “Bienere Simon, garson Zan! Pa to natir imin ki finn revel twa sa, me mo Papa ki dan lesiel."
Matthew16:18 E mo dir twa Pier, to enn ros, e lor sa ros la mo pou konstrir mo Legliz, e pwisans lamor pa pou kapav dominn li."
Matthew16:19 Mo pou donn twa lakle rwayom lesiel, e tou seki to atase lor later pou atase dan lesiel e tou seki to large lor later pou large dan lesiel.”"
Matthew16:20 Lerla li donn lord so bann disip pou pa dir personn ki limem Lemesi.
Matthew16:21 Depi sa, Zezi koumans montre so bann disip ki li bizin al Zerizalem, soufer boukou dan lame bann ansien, bann sef pret ek dokter lalwa e ki zot pou touy li me li pou resisite lor trwaziem zour."
Matthew16:22 Pier amenn li enn kote e fer li bann repros; li dir, “Tou pou pas bien, Segner! Sa pa pou zame ariv twa.”"
Matthew16:23 Me li vire e li dir Pier, “Pas deryer mwa, Satan! To enn gro ros lor mo sime parski to pa pans kouma Bondie me kouma imin.”"
Matthew16:24 Apre sa Zezi dir ar so bann disip, “Si kikenn oule vinn ar mwa, fodre pa li mazinn zis limem, me fodre li pran so lakrwa pou swiv mwa."
Matthew16:25 Seki oule sov so lavi pou perdi li, e seki perdi so lavi akoz mwa pou sov li."
Matthew16:26 Ki serti enn dimoun gagn lemonn antie me li perdi so lavi? Ki enn dimoun kapav done pou aste lavi?
Matthew16:27 Garson Limanite pou vini avek so bann anz dan laglwar so Papa, e lerla li pou tret sak dimoun dapre seki li finn fer."
Matthew16:28 Laverite mo dir zot, ena parmi zot ki pa pou konn lamor avan ki zot trouv Garson Limanite revini dan so Rwayom.”"
Matthew17:1 Sis zour apre, Zezi pran Pier, Zak ek so frer Zan e li amenn zot lor enn montagn bien ot. Zot ti tousel avek li."
Matthew17:2 Li transfigire devan zot e so figir briye kouma soley, so linz vinn blan kouma lalimier."
Matthew17:3 So trwa disip trouv Moiz ek Eli paret enn kout e zot ti pe koz ar Zezi.
Matthew17:4 Alor Pier dir Zezi, “Segner, li bien bon nou la avek twa! Si to oule, mo ranz trwa latant, enn pou twa, enn pou Moiz e enn pou Eli.”"
Matthew17:5 Letan li ti ankor pe koze, enn niaz bien blan kouver zot e enn lavwa dan niaz la ti pe dir, “Samem mo Garson ki mo bien kontan, li donn mwa boukou lazwa, ekout li!”"
Matthew17:6 Ler bann disip tann sa lavwa la, zot ti telman efreye ki zot tom anplan lor later."
Matthew17:7 Me Zezi apros zot e tous zot, li dir, “Leve, pa gagn per.”"
Matthew17:8 Zot lev zot lizie e zot trouv Zezi tousel.
Matthew17:9 Letan zot pe desann montagn, Zezi donn zot enn lord, “Pa rakont personn seki zot finn trouve tanki Garson Limanite pa resisite parmi bann mor.”"
Matthew17:10 Lerla bann disip dimann li, “Kifer bann dokter lalwa dir fodre ki Eli revini avan?”"
Matthew17:11 Li reponn zot, “Zisteman Eli pou revini e met tou dan lord."
Matthew17:12 Me les mo dir zot ki Eli finn fini vini e bann la pa finn rekonet li, me zot finn tret li kouma zot anvi. Koumsamem Garson Limanite pou soufer ar zot.”"
Matthew17:13 Lerla bann disip konpran ki li ti pe koz ar zot lor Zan Batis.
Matthew17:14 Ler zot ariv kot lafoul ti ete, enn boug vini, tom azenou devan Zezi,"
Matthew17:15 e li dir, “Segner, pitie mo garson ki gagn kriz epileptik e li soufer boukou. Souvan li gagn kriz e li tom dan dilo ek dan dife."
Matthew17:16 Mo finn amenn li ar to bann disip me zot pa finn kapav geri li.”
Matthew17:17 Zezi reponn, “Zenerasion san lafwa ranpli ar mesanste. Komie letan ankor mo pou res ar zot? Ziska kan mo bizin siport zot? Amenn li ar mwa.”"
Matthew17:18 Zezi menas demon la, li sorti dan garson la e enn sel kout li geri."
Matthew17:19 Apre sa bann disip al get Zezi anprive, zot dir li, “Kifer nou pa finn kapav sas sa demon la?”"
Matthew17:20 Zezi reponn zot, “Parski zot lafwa tro feb. Laverite mo dir zot, si zot ena lafwa groser enn lagrin moutard e ki zot dir montagn, ‘Bouze al laba,’ li pou bouze; nanye pa inposib pou zot."
Matthew17:21 Zis ar lapriyer ki sa kalite lespri la kapav sorti.”
Matthew17:22 Letan Zezi ek so bann disip ti ansam dan Galile, li dir zot, “Zot pre pou livre Garson Limanite dan lame bann dimoun,"
Matthew17:23 zot pou touy li e li pou resisite lor trwaziem zour.” Bann disip ti bien sagrin kan zot tann sa parol la.
Matthew17:24 Ler zot ariv Kafarnaom, bann komi tax tanp vinn ar Pier e zot dir li, “Zot met, pa pey tax li?”"
Matthew17:25 Pier reponn, “Wi, li peye.” E ler li rant lakaz, Zezi koz avek Pier e li dimann li, “Ki to panse Simon, bann lerwa lor later, kisannla zot fer pey tax? Bann sitwayin oubien bann etranze?”"
Matthew17:26 Letan Pier reponn “Bann etranze,” Zezi dir li, “Savedir bann sitwayin lib, pena pou peye."
Matthew17:27 Me pou nou pa ofans zot, al lamer zet lamson e premie pwason ki morde, get dan so lagel e to pou trouv enn pies larzan; pran li e pey tax pou twa ek pou mwa.”"
Matthew18:1 Sa letan la, bann disip vinn ar Zezi e dimann li, “Kisannla pli gran dan rwayom lesiel?”"
Matthew18:2 Li apel enn ti zanfan, li met li omilie zot,"
Matthew18:3 e li dir, “Laverite mo dir zot, si zot pa sanze e vinn kouma zanfan, zot pa pou rant dan rwayom lesiel."
Matthew18:4 Dimoun ki pli gran dan rwayom lesiel li kikenn ki abes li e fer li vinn tipti kouma sa zanfan la.
Matthew18:5 Dimoun ki akeyir enn zanfan lor mo nom, li pe akeyir mwa osi."
Matthew18:6 Si kikenn fer enn sa bann ti zanfan ki krwar dan mwa la tonbe, ti pou preferab atas enn gro ros dan so likou e zet li dan fon lamer."
Matthew18:7 Maler pou lemonn akoz bann kiksoz kifer dimoun tom dan pese. Sa bann kiksoz la zot inevitab, me malere sa dimoun ki responsab tousala."
Matthew18:8 Si to lame oubien to lipie fer twa tonbe, koup li zete, preferab to rant dan lavi avek enn sel lame ek enn sel lipie ki to ena toulede lame ek lipie dan dife lanfer."
Matthew18:9 Si to lizie fer twa tonbe, aras li zete; preferab to rant dan lavi avek enn sel kote lizie ki to al dan dife lanfer avek toulede."
Matthew18:10 Fer sir ki zot pa mepriz enn sa bann ti zanfan la; parski les mo dir zot, ki zot bann anz toultan dan prezans mo Papa dan lesiel."
Matthew18:11 
Matthew18:12 Ki zot panse? Sipoze enn dimoun ena san mouton, e enn parmi perdi, eski li pa pou les sa katrovin-diznef mouton la lor montagn pou al rod sa enn ki finn perdi la?"
Matthew18:13 Si li retrouv li, mo sir li pou pli kontan pou sa sel mouton la ki sa lezot katrovin-diznef ki pa finn perdi."
Matthew18:14 Koumsamem zot Papa ki dan lesiel, li pa anvi ki okenn sa bann ti dimoun la perdi."
Matthew18:15 Si to frer krwayan ofans twa, al get li e montre li so fot kan zis zot de tousel. Si li ekoute, to pou finn regagn li kouma to frer."
Matthew18:16 Me si li pa ekout twa, pran enn ou de lezot dimoun avek twa kouma temwin."
Matthew18:17 Si li refiz ekout zot, dir tou ar legliz; e si li refiz ekout legliz, konsider li kouma enn payin oubien enn komi tax."
Matthew18:18 Laverite, mo dir zot, tou saki zot atase lor later pou atase dan lesiel, e tou saki zot delarge lor later pou delarge dan lesiel."
Matthew18:19 Laverite mo dir zot ankor enn fwa, si de ant zot tom dakor lor later pou dimann ninport kwa, mo Papa dan lesiel pou akord zot."
Matthew18:20 Parski la kot de ou trwa finn rasanble lor mo nom mo pou la omilie zot.”
Matthew18:21 Lerla Pier vinn kot Zezi e li dimann li, “Segner, si enn frer krwayan ofans mwa, konbien fwa mo bizin pardonn li? Ziska set fwa?”"
Matthew18:22 Zezi reponn li, “Non pa set fwa, me swasann-dis fwa set fwa."
Matthew18:23 Se pou sa rezon la ki rwayom lesiel li parey enn lerwa ki deside pou regle so kont avek so bann serviter.
Matthew18:24 Ler li koumans fer sa, zot amenn li kikenn ki ti dwa dis mil talan."
Matthew18:25 Kouma li pa ti kapav pey so det, so met ti finn donn lord pou vann li, so fam, so bann zanfan ek tou so dibien, pouki li ranbours so det."
Matthew18:26 Serviter la tom azenou devan lerwa, li dir, ‘Pran pasians Segner, mo pou rann twa tou saki mo dwa.’"
Matthew18:27 Dan so mizerikord, lerwa la larg li e rey tou so det."
Matthew18:28 Me samem serviter la, kouma li sorti deor, li zwenn enn so kamarad serviter ki ti dwa li san pies larzan. Li may li par likou, li dir li, ‘Pey mwa tou saki to dwa mwa.’"
Matthew18:29 Lerla so kamarad serviter tom azenou e sipliy li, ‘Ena pasians avek mwa, mo pou rann twa to larzan.’"
Matthew18:30 Me li refize; li fer met li dan prizon ziska li fini ranbours so det.
Matthew18:31 Kan bann lezot kamarad serviter trouv saki pe pase, zot ti bien tris, e zot al rakont zot met tou saki ti finn pase."
Matthew18:32 Alor lerwa apel li e dir li, ‘To move! Mo finn rey tou to det parski to finn sipliy mwa."
Matthew18:33 To pa panse to ti bizin ena pitie pou to kamarad serviter parey kouma mo finn ena pitie pou twa?’
Matthew18:34 Dan so koler, lerwa avoy li al fer travo forse ziska li fini ranbours tou so det."
Matthew18:35 Koumsamem mo Papa ki dan lesiel pou fer avek sakenn parmi zot, si zot pa pardonn zot bann frer ek ser avek tou zot leker.”"
Matthew19:1 Ler Zezi fini koze, li kit Galile e li al dan rezion Zide lot kote Zourdin."
Matthew19:2 Enn gran lafoul ti pe swiv li e li ti pe geri zot tou.
Matthew19:3 Enn bann Farizien koste ar li pou teste li. Zot dir, “Eski lalwa permet enn mari kit so fam san okenn rezon?”"
Matthew19:4 Li reponn, “Zot pa finn lir ki dan komansman Bondie Kreater finn kre dimoun zom ek fam?"
Matthew19:5 Bondie ti dir, ‘Akoz samem enn zom pou kit so papa ek so mama, li pou al atas li ar so fam e toulede pou vinn enn sel.’"
Matthew19:6 Alor zot nepli pou de, me enn sel. Fode pa dimoun separ seki Bondie finn met ansam.”"
Matthew19:7 Zot dir li, “Be pou kifer Moiz finn donn nou lord donn enn papie divors pou divorse?”"
Matthew19:8 Li dir zot, “Parski zot leker dir ki Moiz finn permet zot divors ar zot fam; me dan komansman li pa ti koumsa."
Matthew19:9 Mo dir zot, si kikenn divors ar so fam, exsepte dan ka infidelite, e marye avek enn lot dimoun, li komet adilter.”"
Matthew19:10 So bann disip dir li, “Si li koumsa ant enn zom avek so fam, vomie pa marye.”"
Matthew19:11 Me li dir zot, “Pa tou dimoun kapav aksepte sa lansegnman la, me zis bann dimoun ki finn resevwar don pou konpran sa."
Matthew19:12 Parski ena plizir rezon kifer zom pa marye, ena parski zot finn ne inpwisan, ena parski dimoun finn rann zot koumsa e lezot pa marye akoz Rwayom Lesiel. Seki kapav aksepte sa lansegnman la, li ava konpran.”"
Matthew19:13 Alor bann dimoun amenn bann tizanfan pouki Zezi inpoz lame lor zot e priye pou zot; me so bann disip farous zot.
Matthew19:14 Me Zezi dir, “Les bann ti zanfan vinn ar mwa, pa anpes zot parski Rwayom Lesiel pou dimoun ki parey kouma zot.”"
Matthew19:15 Li inpoz lame lor zot, apre li kit zot, li ale."
Matthew19:16 Ala enn dimoun vinn kot Zezi e dir li, “Met, ki bon kiksoz mo bizin fer pou gagn lavi eternel?”"
Matthew19:17 Zezi dir li, “Kifer to poz mwa kestion lor seki bon? Zis Enn Sel ki bon. Si to anvi rant dan lavi, swiv bann komannman.”"
Matthew19:18 Li dir li, “Ki sa bann komannman la?” Zezi dir li, “Pa touye, pa komet adilter, pa kokin, pa fer fos temwagnaz,"
Matthew19:19 onor to papa ek to mama, e kontan to prosin parey kouma tomem.”"
Matthew19:20 Zenes la dir li, “Tousala mo finn swiv, ki mo manke ankor?”"
Matthew19:21 Zezi dir li, “Si to anvi vinn parfe, ale, vann tou to dibien, donn bann pov e to pou gagn enn trezor dan lesiel; apre sa vini, swiv mwa.”"
Matthew19:22 Ler zenes la tann sa, li ale bien tris parski li ti ena boukou dibien."
Matthew19:23 Lerla Zezi dir so bann disip, “Laverite, mo dir zot, bien difisil pou enn ris rant dan Rwayom lesiel."
Matthew19:24 Mo redir zot, li pli fasil pou enn samo pas dan enn trou zegwi ki pou enn ris rant dan Rwayom Bondie.”"
Matthew19:25 Ler bann disip tann sa, zot etone e zot dir, “Kisannla pou kapav sape alor?”"
Matthew19:26 Zezi get zot fran-fran e dir zot, “Pou dimoun, li inposib, me pou Bondie tou kiksoz posib.”"
Matthew19:27 Pier dir li, “Get nou, nou finn kit tou pou swiv twa. Alor ki pou ariv nou?”"
Matthew19:28 Zezi dir zot, “Laverite mo dir zot, dan sa nouvo lemonn la, kan Garson Limanite pou asiz lor so tronn dan laglwar, zot ki finn swiv mwa, zot osi zot pou asiz lor douz tronn pou ziz douz tribi Izrael."
Matthew19:29 Dimoun ki finn kit lakaz, frer, ser, papa, mama, zanfan ek zot later akoz mwa, pou resevwar san fwa plis e zot pou erit lavi eternel."
Matthew19:30 Boukou premie pou vinn dernie, e bann dernie pou vinn premie.”"
Matthew20:1 “Rwayom lesiel resanble enn propriyeter ki sorti gramatin pou anplway bann travayer dan so karo rezin.
Matthew20:2 Apre ki li finn tom dakor ar zot lor lapey enn zourne travay, li avoy zot dan so karo."
Matthew20:3 Ver nev-er li resorti, e trouv lezot lor laplas piblik pe dibout san travay."
Matthew20:4 Li dir zot, ‘Al dan mo karo e mo pou pey zot enn saler rezonab.’ E zot al travay."
Matthew20:5 Ler li resorti ver midi ek ver trwa-zer, li fer parey."
Matthew20:6 Ver sink-er li sorti e trouv ankor ki pe dibout lor laplas; e li dir zot, ‘Kifer zot res la enn zourne san fer nanye?’"
Matthew20:7 Zot dir li, ‘Parski personn pa finn anplway nou.’ Li dir zot, ‘Al dan mo karo zot osi.’"
Matthew20:8 Kan finn ariv aswar, propriyeter la dir so formenn, ‘Apel bann travayer e donn sakenn zot lapey. Komans ar bann dernie pou fini par bann premie.’"
Matthew20:9 Bann ki ti pran travay ver sink-er prezant zot, e sakenn resevwar valer enn zourne travay."
Matthew20:10 Ler ariv tour bann ki finn pran travay anpremie, zot ti panse ki zot ti pou gagn plis; me sakenn resevwar valer enn zourne travay."
Matthew20:11 Letan zot resevwar zot lapey zot mirmire kont propriyeter la.
Matthew20:12 Zot dir li, ‘Sa bann dernie la finn travay enn-ertan selman, e to tret zot parey kouma nou ki finn trime tout lazourne anba enn soley diplon.’"
Matthew20:13 Propriyeter la reponn enn ladan, ‘Kamarad, mo pa finn fer twa ditor. Eski to pa ti dakor ar mwa lor sa lapey la?"
Matthew20:14 Pran to kas, ale. Mo anvi donn dernie la parey kouma mo finn donn twa."
Matthew20:15 Eski mo pena drwa fer seki mo anvi ar mo dibien? Oubien, eski to zalou parski mo zenere?’"
Matthew20:16 Koumsamem, bann dernie pou vinn premie, e bann premie pou dernie.”"
Matthew20:17 Ler Zezi pe mont Zerizalem, li pran Ledouz enn kote anprive e li koz avek zot ler zot pe marse."
Matthew20:18 Li dir, “Ekout bien, nou pe mont Zerizalem, Garson Limanite pou livre dan lame bann sef pret ek dokter lalwa e zot pou kondann li amor,"
Matthew20:19 apre sa zot pou met li dan lame bann payin, zot pou boufonn li, fwet li, krisifie li, me lor trwaziem zour li pou resisite.”"
Matthew20:20 Lerla mama bann garson Zebede vinn get Zezi avek so de garson, li tom azenou devan li pou dimann li enn faver."
Matthew20:21 Zezi dir li, “Ki to oule?” Li reponn, “Promet mwa ki mo de garson ki la, zot pou asiz enn dan to kote drwat e lot dan to kote gos dan to Rwayom.”"
Matthew20:22 Me Zezi reponn, “Zot pa kone ki zot pe dimande. Eski zot kapav bwar koup ki mo pe al bwar?” Zot dir li, “Wi, nou kapav”"
Matthew20:23 Li reponn zot, “Koup ki mo pou bwar, zot pou bwar, me pou kone kisannla pou asiz dan mo kote drwat ek gos, sa li pa depann lor mwa. Bondie, mo papa finn rezerv sa bann plas la pou sertin dimoun ki li anvi.”"
Matthew20:24 Kan lezot dis disip tann sa, zot ankoler avek de frer la."
Matthew20:25 Me Zezi apel zot e li dir, “Zot kone ki bann lerwa payin diriz e dominn lezot."
Matthew20:26 Sa bizin pa arive parmi zot; saki anvi pran grander parmi zot, li bizin okip plas serviter,"
Matthew20:27 e saki anvi vinn premie, li bizin vinn esklav tou dimoun;"
Matthew20:28 parey kouma Garson Limanite pa finn vini pouki dimoun servi li, me pou servi dimoun e donn so lavi kouma enn ranson pou boukou dimoun.”"
Matthew20:29 Letan zot pe kit Zeriko, enn gran lafoul swiv Zezi."
Matthew20:30 Ti ena de aveg pe asize lor bor sime. Letan zot tande ki Zezi pe pas par la, zot kriye for-for, “Segner, Garson David, pitie nou!”"
Matthew20:31 Lafoul pa kontan, dir zot res trankil; me zot kriye ankor pli for, “Pitie nou, Segner, Garson David!”"
Matthew20:32 Zezi arete, li apel zot, li dir, “Ki zot anvi mo fer pou zot?”"
Matthew20:33 Zot reponn, “Segner, fer nou trouv kler.”"
Matthew20:34 Zezi ranpli ar konpasion, li tous zot lizie. Enn sel kout, zot retrouv kler e zot swiv li."
Matthew21:1 Kan zot ariv pre ar Zerizalem, dan vilaz Betfaze, koste ar kolinn Pie Zoliv, Zezi avoy de disip,"
Matthew21:2 e li dir zot, “Al dan prosin vilaz; kouma zot ariv laba, zot pou trouv enn bourik ki atase e so piti avek li. Delarg zot, amenn zot kot mwa."
Matthew21:3 Si kikenn dimann zot ninport kwa, zis dir, ‘Lesegner bien bizin zot.’ Toutswit, dimoun la pou les zot ale.”"
Matthew21:4 Sa finn arive pouki parol ki bann Profet ti dir realize:
Matthew21:5 “Dir popilasion Zerizalem: gete, zot lerwa pe vini li lor enn ti bourik, e li ranpli ar imilite.”"
Matthew21:6 Bann disip ale e fer parey kouma Zezi ti finn dir zot;
Matthew21:7 zot amenn bourik la ek so piti, e zot met zot linz lor bann la e Zezi asiz lor linz la."
Matthew21:8 Enn lafoul dimoun tal zot linz lor sime, lezot koup bann brans e fann lor sime."
Matthew21:9 Lafoul ki ti devan Zezi e bann ki ti pe swiv li par deryer, ti pe kriye; “Ozana garson David! Ki Bondie beni sa dimoun ki vinn lor nom Lesegner!”"
Matthew21:10 Ler li rant dan lavil Zerizalem, tou dimoun ti azite, zot pe dimande, “Kisannla sa?”"
Matthew21:11 Lafoul reponn, “Limem profet Zezi ki sorti Nazaret dan Galile.”"
Matthew21:12 Ler Zezi rant dan tanp, li farous tou bann ki ti pe vande ek aste, li devir anba lao latab bann sanzer larzan ek sez bann vander pizon."
Matthew21:13 Li dir zot, “Finn ekrir, ‘Pou apel mo lakaz, enn lakaz lapriyer.’ Me zot finn fer li vinn enn kavern voler.”"
Matthew21:14 Bann aveg ek bann bwate vinn kot li dan tanp, e li geri zot."
Matthew21:15 Me kan bann sef pret ek dokter lalwa trouv sa bann mirak la e tann bann zanfan pe kriye, ‘Ozana Garson David,’ zot ankoler."
Matthew21:16 Lerla zot dir Zezi, “To tande ki zot pe dir?” Zezi reponn, “Wi. Eski zot pa finn lir: ‘Mem bann zanfan ek bann ti baba pou sant louanz ki finn prepare pou li.’ ”"
Matthew21:17 Zezi kit zot, li al andeor lavil Betani, e li pas lanwit laba."
Matthew21:18 Landime gramatin, ler Zezi retourn dan lavil, li gagn fin."
Matthew21:19 Li trouv enn pie fig dan bor sime e li al pre ar li, me li pa trouv okenn fri, me zis bann fey. Alor li dir pie fig la: “To nepli pou donn fri ankor” Enn sel kou pie fig sek."
Matthew21:20 Ler bann disip trouv sa, zot ti etone, e zot dir: “Kouma sa pie la kapav sek enn sel kou?”"
Matthew21:21 Zezi reponn zot, “Laverite, mo dir zot, si zot ena lafwa e zot pa doute, pa zis seki mo finn fer avek pie fig ki zot pou kapav fer; me si zot dir sa montagn la, ‘leve al zet twa dan lamer,’ sa pou arive."
