Matthew21:22 Tou seki zot dimande dan lafwa, zot pou resevwar.”"
Matthew21:23 Ler Zezi rant dan tanp, bann sef pret ek bann ansien vinn kot li, e zot dimann li, “Par ki lotorite to pe fer sa bann kiksoz la, kisannla finn donn twa sa lotorite la?”"
Matthew21:24 Zezi dir zot, “Mo pou poz zot enn ti kestion mwa osi; si zot dir mwa so repons, lerla mo pou dir zot par ki lotorite mo fer sa bann kiksoz la."
Matthew21:25 Eski batem Zan sorti depi dan lesiel ouswa dimoun ki finn invant sa?” Zot koumans diskit ant zot, “Si nou reponn ‘depi dan lesiel’, li pou dir, be kifer alor zot pa finn krwar dan li?"
Matthew21:26 Si nou reponn, ‘Dimoun,’ nou per lafoul parski tou dimoun ti konsider Zan kouma enn profet.”"
Matthew21:27 Alor zot reponn Zezi, “Nou pa kone.” Lerla Zezi reponn zot, “Mo osi mo pa pou dir zot kot mo pouvwar sorti.”"
Matthew21:28 Zezi kontigne, li dir “Ki zot panse lor la? Enn papa ena de garson. Li al get premie la, li dir li, ‘Mo garson, al travay dan mo lavign zordi.’"
Matthew21:29 Li reponn, ‘Mo pa pou ale.’ Me plitar li sanz lide li ale."
Matthew21:30 Papa la vinn ar deziem la e li dir li mem zafer; e li reponn ‘Wi papa,’ me li pa ale."
Matthew21:31 Kisannla ant sa de garson la finn fer volonte so papa?” Zot dir, “Premie la.” Alor Zezi dir zot, “Laverite, mo dir zot, bann ramaser tax ek bann prostitie pou ariv dan Rwayom Bondie avan zot tou."
Matthew21:32 Ofet, Zan Batis finn vinn kot zot pou montre zot sime lazistis zot pa finn krwar dan li, me bann ramaser tax ek bann prostitie finn krwar dan li. Me zot, mem apre zot finn trouv sa, zot pa finn sanze pou krwar dan li.”"
Matthew21:33 “Ekout enn lot parabol,” Zezi dir, “Ti ena enn propriyeter ki ti plant enn karo rezin, li antour li avek enn baraz, li fouy enn trou pou instal enn preswar, e li aranz enn mirador. Li lwe li ar bann travayer e li al dan enn lot pei."
Matthew21:34 Letan finn ariv ler pou rekolte, li avoy so bann serviter kot bann travayer la pou al sers so par."
Matthew21:35 Bann travayer trap bann serviter la, bat enn ladan, touy enn lot e avoy kout ros lor trwaziem la."
Matthew21:36 Li avoy ankor lezot serviter, plis ki premie fwa, me bann travayer la tret zot parey."
Matthew21:37 Andernie li avoy so garson. Li dir ar limem, ‘Zot pou respekte mo garson.’"
Matthew21:38 Me ler bann travayer trouv garson la, zot dir ant zot, ‘Ala leritie; vini, anou touy li e pran so leritaz.’"
Matthew21:39 Alor zot trap li, zet li andeor karo e touy li."
Matthew21:40 Asterla kan propriyeter karo rezin vini, ki li pou fer avek sa bann travayer la?”"
Matthew21:41 Zot dir li, “Li pou masakre sa bann kriminel la e lwe so karo ar enn lot bann travayer ki pou donn li so par apre rekolt.”"
Matthew21:42 Zezi dir zot, “Zame zot finn lir dan Lekritir ki dir: ‘Ros ki bann mason finn zete finn vinn ros ki tini tou, Sa travay Lesegner, Sa li enn gran mervey pou nou lizie."
Matthew21:43 Ala, mo dir zot, pou ras Rwayom Bondie ar zot e pou donn sa enn pep ki pou prodwir vre fri.” ["
Matthew21:44 Dimoun ki tom lor sa ros la pou kas-kase e si ros la ki tom lor kikenn, li pou vinn lapousier ]"
Matthew21:45 Letan bann sef pret ek bann Farizien tann sa bann parabol la, zot konpran ki li ti pe koz kont zot."
Matthew21:46 Alor zot rod trap li me selman zot ti gagn per lafoul parski bann la ti konsider li kouma enn profet.
Matthew22:1 Ankor enn fwa Zezi servi parabol pou ansegne, li dir,"
Matthew22:2 “Rwayom lesiel parey kouma enn lerwa ki organiz enn lanos pou maryaz so garson.
Matthew22:3 Li avoy so bann serviter pou apel bann invite, me zot refiz vini."
Matthew22:4 Li avoy lot serviter ankor e li donn zot sa mesaz la: ‘Dir mo bann invite, “Ala mo repa finn pare, mo finn fini touy mo bann toro ek mo bann zanimo bien gra, tou finn pare. Vinn dan lanos.”"
Matthew22:5 Me bann invite pa interese, ena al dan zot karo, ena al okip zot komers,"
Matthew22:6 ena mem ki tom lor bann serviter, maltret zot e touy zot."
Matthew22:7 Lerwa bien ankoler; li avoy so bann solda al touy sa bann asasin la e bril zot lavil.
Matthew22:8 Apre sa, li dir so bann serviter, ‘Lanos finn pare, me mo bann invite pa dign."
Matthew22:9 Al dan bann lakrwaze sime e tou dimoun ki zot trouve invit zot dan lanos.’
Matthew22:10 Bann serviter sorti, al lor lari e rasanble tou seki zot trouve, bon kouma pa bon; e lasal ranpli ar invite."
Matthew22:11 Me kan lerwa vini pou get bann invite, li remark kikenn ki pa ti ena kostim maryaz,"
Matthew22:12 e li dir li, ‘Kamarad, kouma to finn rant la san enn kostim maryaz?’ Boug la perdi laparol."
Matthew22:13 Lerla lerwa dir so bann serviter, ‘Atas so lame ek so lipie, zet li deor dan teneb, la kot pou ena boukou plore, kriye ek grinsman ledan.’"
Matthew22:14 Parski boukou pou apele, me tigit pou eli.”"
Matthew22:15 Bann Farizien fer enn konplo pou piez Zezi lor bann parol ki li finn dir.
Matthew22:16 Alor, zot avoy zot bann disip, ansam avek bann Erodien pou al get Zezi. Bann la dir li, “Met, nou kone ki to sinser, seki to ansegne lor lalwa Bondie li vre, e to pa les twa inflianse par personn parski to tret to dimoun parey."
Matthew22:17 Dir nou alor, ki to panse: Eski nou lalwa permet nou pey tax lanperer ou non?”"
Matthew22:18 Me Zezi, ki konn zot mesanste, reponn zot, “Bann ipokrit, kifer zot anvi met mwa dan lak?"
Matthew22:19 Montre mwa enn pies avek ki zot pey tax.” Zot amenn li enn pies larzan.
Matthew22:20 Apre li dir zot: “Ki figir ena lor la e ki finn ekrir?”
Matthew22:21 Zot reponn, “Lanperer.” Li dir zot, “Rann lanperer seki pou lanperer e rann Bondie seki pou Bondie.”"
Matthew22:22 Kan zot tann sa, zot dekonserte, zot kit li, zot ale."
Matthew22:23 Sa mem zour la, detrwa Sadisein vinn kot Zezi pou dir ki pena rezireksion e zot poz li enn kestion:"
Matthew22:24 “Met, Moiz ti dir, ‘Si enn zom mor san zanfan, so frer bizin marye ar so fam pou donn li enn desandan."
Matthew22:25 Enn fwa ti ena set frer ki ti viv isi. Premie la marye e mor san zanfan e li kit vev la ar so frer.
Matthew22:26 Deziem la fer parey, e mem zafer ariv trwaziem la ek tou lezot."
Matthew22:27 Apre sa, fam la osi mor."
Matthew22:28 Zour rezireksion, kisannla pou vinn so mari, parski li finn pran touleset kouma mari?”"
Matthew22:29 Zezi reponn li, “Zot fer erer, parski zot pa konn Lekritir e pwisans Bondie."
Matthew22:30 Kan bann mor pou releve, bann dimoun pa pou pran ni zom ni fam, me zot pou viv kouma bann anz dan lesiel."
Matthew22:31 Pou seki konsern rezireksion bann mor, eski zot pa finn lir seki Bondie finn dir,"
Matthew22:32 ‘Momem Bondie Abraam, Bondie Izaak, ek Bondie Zakob?’ Li pa Bondie bann mor me Bondie bann vivan.”"
Matthew22:33 Tou dimoun letan zot tann sa, zot ti inpresione par so lansegnman."
Matthew22:34 Letan bann Farizien tande ki li finn ferm labous bann Sadisein, zot rasanble zot,"
Matthew22:35 e enn parmi zot ki ti enn dokter lalwa, dimann Zezi enn kestion pou piez li."
Matthew22:36 “Met, ki pli gran komannman dan lalwa? “"
Matthew22:37 Zezi dir li, “‘To bizin kontan to Segner, to Bondie avek tou to leker, avek tou to nam e avek tou to lespri.’"
Matthew22:38 Samem komannman pli gran e pli inportan.
Matthew22:39 Deziem pli inportan ‘To kontan to prosin kouma tomem’
Matthew22:40 Tou bann lalwa ek bann profet depann lor sa de komannman la.”
Matthew22:41 Ler bann Farizien ti finn rasanble, Zezi dimann zot:"
Matthew22:42 “Ki zot panse lor Lemesi? Ki so desandan?” Zot reponn, “Desandan David”."
Matthew22:43 Zezi dir zot, “Be kouma David ki ti anba gid Lespri Sin, finn kapav apel li ‘Segner’? Parski David limem finn dir:"
Matthew22:44 ‘Lesegner finn dir mo Segner, asiz twa dan mo kote drwat ziska mo kraz mo bann lennmi anba mo lipie.’ ”"
Matthew22:45 “Si David apel li Segner, kouma li kapav so garson?”"
Matthew22:46 Personn pa ti kapav donn li enn repons, e depi sa zour la, personn pa ti oze poz li kestion ankor."
Matthew23:1 Zezi koz ar lafoul ek so bann disip, li dir,"
Matthew23:2 “Bann dokter lalwa ek Farizien, asiz lor tronn Moiz;"
Matthew23:3 alor zot bizin pratik ek swiv tou saki zot dir; me zot, pa imit sa bann la, parski zot pa pratik seki zot ansegne."
Matthew23:4 Parski zot atas bann gro fardo difisil pou amene lor zepol lezot, me ki zot, mem zot ti ledwa, zot pale bouze."
Matthew23:5 Me zot kontan fer kiksoz pou lizie dimoun, zot bann filakter bien-bien gran e franz zot manto bien long."
Matthew23:6 Zot kontan bann premie plas dan bann fet e bann meyer plas dan sinagog.
Matthew23:7 Zot kontan kan dimoun salye zot dan bann plas piblik e dimoun apel zot Rabi.
Matthew23:8 Me zot, fode pa ki zot fer apel zot Rabi, parski zot ena enn sel met e zot tou so zelev."
Matthew23:9 Pa apel ninport ki lor later papa, parski Li tousel zot papa ki dan lesiel."
Matthew23:10 Pa fer apel zot met parski zot ena enn sel met, Lemesi."
Matthew23:11 Dimoun ki pli gran parmi zot, li pou zot serviter."
Matthew23:12 Dimoun ki anvi gagn laglwar pou imilie li, dimoun ki imilie li pou gagn laglwar."
Matthew23:13 Maler lor tou bann dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit! Zot finn ferm laport lesiel pou dimoun. Zotmem zot pa rantre e kan lezot anvi rantre, zot blok laport."
Matthew23:14 Maler lor zot dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit, zot manz tou manze bann vev, zot fer long-long lapriyer pou lizie dimoun. Akoz samem zot pou gagn enn pli gran kondanasion."
Matthew23:15 Maler lor tou bann dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit. Zot vwayaz partou lor lamer ek lor later pou konverti enn sel dimoun e zot fer li al dan lanfer de fwa pli vit ki zot.
Matthew23:16 Maler lor zot, bann gid aveg. Zot dir, ‘Si kikenn fer serman lor tanp, li pa angaz nanye; me si kikenn fer serman lor tanp, la li bizin tini so serman.’"
Matthew23:17 Bann fou ek aveg! Ki pli inportan? Lor oubien tanp ki rann lor la sakre?
Matthew23:18 Zot dir osi: ‘Si kikenn fer serman lor lotel, li pa angaz nanye; me si li fer serman lor ofrand ki lor lotel, la li bizin tini so serman.’"
Matthew23:19 Bann fou ek aveg! Ki pli inportan? Ofrand oubien lotel ki rann ofrand la sakre?
Matthew23:20 Alor dimoun kifer serman lor lotel, fer serman lor lotel e lor tou saki lor li."
Matthew23:21 Dimoun kifer serman lor tanp, fer li lor tanp e lor tou saki res dan tanp."
Matthew23:22 Dimoun ki fer serman lor lesiel, fer li lor tronn Bondie e lor sa Enn ki asiz lor tronn la."
Matthew23:23 Maler lor zot, dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit. Zotmem pey ladim lor bann zepis kouma lamant, ditin ek fenouy, me zot negliz seki pli inportan dan lalwa, lazistis e mizerikord ek fidelite."
Matthew23:24 Bann gid aveg! Zot pas zot bwar dan paste pou tir enn moustik, me zot aval enn samo."
Matthew23:25 Maler lor zot, dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit! Zot netway andeor tas ek pla, me andan zot ranpli ar vis ek move dezir."
Matthew23:26 Farizien aveg! Avan tou netway andan tas pouki so andeor osi kapav prop.
Matthew23:27 Maler lor zot, dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit. Zot parey bann tonbo ki finn bien blansi, ki paret bien zoli, me ranpli ar lekor mor ek tou kalite salte."
Matthew23:28 Koumsamem zot paret korek e zis pou lizie dimoun, me dan zotmem zot ranpli ar ipokrizi ek malonete."
Matthew23:29 Maler lor zot, dokter lalwa ek Farizien ipokrit! Zot ranz tom bann profet ek dekor moniman bann zom zis,"
Matthew23:30 lerla zot dir: ‘Si nou ti viv dan lepok nou bann gran dimoun, nou pa ti pou partisip dan zot krim kont profet.’"
Matthew23:31 Alor zotmem, zot rekonet ki zot desandan bann kriminel ki finn touy bann profet."
Matthew23:32 Kontigne alor, fer saki zot bann gran dimoun finn koumanse."
Matthew23:33 Bann espes serpan! Zot panse zot pou kapav sov kondanasion Bondie?
Matthew23:34 Akoz samem, mo pou avoy zot bann profet, bann saz ek bann vre dokter lalwa. Ena ladan zot pou touye ek krisifie, lezot zot pou trangle dan zot sinagog ek persekit lezot dan bann lavil."
Matthew23:35 Alor, disan tou sa bann inosan depi Abel ziska Zakari garson Baraki ki zot ti touye devan lotel, pou tom lor zot."
Matthew23:36 Laverite, mo dir zot, tousala pou tom lor sa zenerasion la.”"
Matthew23:37 “Zerizalem, Zerizalem, twa ki touy to bann profet kout ros! Konbien fwa mo finn anvi rasanble to bann zanfan kouma enn mama poul rasanble so bann piti anba so lezel, me to pa finn anvi!"
Matthew23:38 Gete, to lakaz pou abandone."
Matthew23:39 Les mo dir twa, to pa pou trouv mwa ankor ziska to dir, ‘Ki Bondie beni sa dimoun ki vinn lor nom Lesegner.’ ”"
Matthew24:1 Letan Zezi sorti dan tanp li pe ale, so bann disip vinn kot li pou fer li remark konstriksion tanp."
Matthew24:2 Li dimann zot, “Zot trouv tousala? Laverite, mo dir zot, pa mem enn sel ros pou reste enn lor lot; tou pou grene.”"
Matthew24:3 Plitar ler li pe asize lor montagn Pie Zoliv, bann disip vinn get li anprive, zot dimann li, “Dir nou kan sa pou arive, e ki sign pou ena pou anons lafin-dimonn.”"
Matthew24:4 Zezi reponn zot, “Fer atansion ki personn pa antrenn zot dan perdision"
Matthew24:5 Pou ena boukou ki pou vini lor mo nom pou dir ‘Momem Lemesi!’
Matthew24:6 E zot pou tann tapaz lager; asire ki zot pa gagn per, parski tousala pou arive, me lafin pa ankor arive."
Matthew24:7 Nasion pou lev kont nasion, rwayom kont rwayom, e pou ena lafaminn."
Matthew24:8 Tousala zis komansman douler lanfantman.
Matthew24:9 Dimoun pou livre zot, pou touy zot e tou bann nasion pou air zot akoz mo nom."
Matthew24:10 Boukou pou abandonn zot lafwa, dimoun pou trayir e air zot kamarad."
Matthew24:11 Boukou fos profet pou leve e pou anbet dimoun.
Matthew24:12 E lemal pou ogmante, dimoun pou nepli kontan zot kamarad."
Matthew24:13 Me dimoun ki persevere ziska lafin pou sove.
Matthew24:14 Bonn Nouvel Rwayom Bondie pou anonse partou dan lemonn, kouma enn temwagnaz pou tou bann nasion; lerla lafin pou vini."
Matthew24:15 “Alor ler zot trouv bann sakrilez abominab parey kouma Profet Daniel ti anonse - seki lir sa pou konpran! -
Matthew24:16 bann ki res dan Zide pou bizin sove al lor montagn,"
Matthew24:17 dimoun ki lor lakaz fode pa desann pou pran seki li ena dan lakaz,"
Matthew24:18 dimoun ki dan karo fode pa get deryer pou pran enn triko.
Matthew24:19 Maler lor bann madam ansint e bann ki pe donn zot zanfan tete.
Matthew24:20 Priye ki zot pa sove dan liver oubien zour saba.
Matthew24:21 Parski dan sa letan la pou ena pli boukou soufrans ki lemonn finn deza kone depi so lexistans, e pa pou zame ena ankor parey."
Matthew24:22 E si Bondie pa ti finn rakoursi sa peryod letan la, personn pa ti pou viv. Me li finn fer sa pou bann ki li finn swazir."
Matthew24:23 Si kikenn dir zot, ‘Get Lemesi, li la!’ oubien ‘Ala li la.’ Pa krwar li."
Matthew24:24 Parski bann fos mesi ek fos profet pou vini; zot pou fer bann gran-gran sign ek mirak pou tronp mem bann ki Bondie finn swazir.
Matthew24:25 Ekout bien! Mo finn deza averti zot davans.
Matthew24:26 Alor, si zot dir, ‘Gete, li dan dezer,’ pa ale. Oubien si zot dir, ‘Gete, li pe kasiet isi,’ pa bizin krwar."
Matthew24:27 Parey kouma zekler briye dan lesiel depi dan les ziska lwes, koumsamem Garson Limanite pou vini."
Matthew24:28 Kot ena lekor mor, ena osi bann votour."
Matthew24:29 Vit-vit apre sa bann moman soufrans, soley pou asonbri lalinn pa pou donn lalimier zetwal pou tom depi lesiel bann pwisans lesiel pou sakouye."
Matthew24:30 Lerla sign Garson Limanite pou paret dan lesiel; tou bann tribi lor later pou fer dey e zot pou trouv Garson Limanite vini dan niaz avek boukou pwisans ek laglwar.
Matthew24:31 Avek son tronpet, li pou avoy so bann anz ki pou rasanble tou bann ki li finn swazir dan kat kwin later.”"
Matthew24:32 “Konpran bien lansegnman lor pie fig; dimoman ki so brans vinn tann e koumans donn fey, zot kone ki lete pe aprose."
Matthew24:33 Letan zot trouv tousala, kone ki Garson Limanite pre pou vini e li deryer laport."
Matthew24:34 Laverite mo dir zot, avan ki sa zenerasion la disparet, tousala pou arive."
Matthew24:35 Lesiel ek later pou disparet me mo parol pa pou disparet.
Matthew24:36 Ki zour, ki ler, personn pa kone, ni bann anz dan lesiel, ni mem Garson Limanite, zis papa la tousel kone."
Matthew24:37 Kouma sa ti pase lepok Noe, koumsamem sa pou ete kan Garson Limanite pou vini."
Matthew24:38 Parski avan inondasion vini, dimoun ti pe manze-bwar, zot ti pe marye ek aranz maryaz, ziska ki Noe rant dan lars."
Matthew24:39 Personn pa ti pe dout nanye ziska ki deliz vini e balye zot tou. Koumsamem pou ete kan Garson Limanite vini.
Matthew24:40 La kot de zom pe travay dan karo, pou pran enn ale, lot pou res deryer."
Matthew24:41 Kot de fam pe kraz dible dan moulin, pou pran enn ale, lot pou res deryer."
Matthew24:42 Alor, mo dir zot pran kont, parski personn pa kone ki zour zot Segner pou vini."
Matthew24:43 Zot konn bien, si enn propriyeter ti kone ki ler dan lanwit voler pou pas kot li, li pa ti pou dormi pouki so lakaz pa defonse."
Matthew24:44 Ala kifer, zot osi, zot bizin pare, parski Garson Limanite pou vinn enn ler ki zot pa kone.”"
Matthew24:45 “Ki sa serviter fidel ek bien serye, lor ki so patron kapav konte pou servi manze tou so bann travayer dan ler ki bizin?"
Matthew24:46 Ere sa serviter ki so met pou trouv li pe travay kan li arive.
Matthew24:47 Laverite mo dir zot, li pou met sa dimoun la ansarz tou so dibien."
Matthew24:48 Me si li enn move serviter e li dir dan limem, ‘Mo met pe tarde,’"
Matthew24:49 e li koumans bat so bann kamarad serviter, e manze, bwar avek bann soular."
Matthew24:50 So met pou retourne enn zour kot li pa pe atann li e enn ler kot li pa pou kone.
Matthew24:51 Li pou koup-koup li, e met li ansam avek bann ipokrit, la kot pou ena boukou plore ek kriye e boukou grinsman ledan.”"
Matthew25:1 “Alor rwayom lesiel pou parey kouma zistwar sa dis zennfi ki pran zot lalanp pou al zwenn nouvo marye.
Matthew25:2 Sink ladan ti insousian, e sink ti bien saz."
Matthew25:3 Ler bann insousian la pran zot lalanp, zot pa pran ase delwil avek zot;"
Matthew25:4 me bann saz la ti pran plizir flakon delwil anplis pou zot lalanp.
Matthew25:5 Nouvo marye tarde pou arive; bann zennfi la koumans kaskou e zot gagn somey.
Matthew25:6 Ler minwi sone, kikenn kriye: ‘Gete! Ala nouvo marye! Sorti pou al zwenn li!’"
Matthew25:7 Alor, bann fidoner leve e koumans prepar zot lalanp."
Matthew25:8 Bann insousian la dimann bann seki bien saz la: ‘Fer nou gagn inpe delwil ar zot, parski nou lalanp pe tegn.’"
Matthew25:9 Bann saz la reponn: ‘Non, li pa posib, parski pa pou ena ase pou nou e pou zot. Pli fasil zot al laboutik e aste inpe delwil pou zotmem.’"
Matthew25:10 Bann insousian la al aste delwil; zis dan sa lerla, nouvo marye arive. Sa sink zennfi ki ti pare la rant ansam avek nouvo marye dan lasal e bann la met lakle dan laport."
Matthew25:11 Plitar, sa sink insousian la arive, e zot kriye: ‘Misie, misie, ouver laport!’"
Matthew25:12 Me li reponn zot: ‘Laverite, mo dir zot, mo pa konn zot.’ ”"
Matthew25:13 Zezi kontigne, li dir: “Pran kont, parski zot pa konn ni zour, ni ler.”"
Matthew25:14 “Rwayom lesiel parey kouma enn dimoun ki pe al anvwayaz, li apel so bann serviter pou konfie zot so dibien."
Matthew25:15 Li donn enn sink talan, enn lot de talan e enn lot enn sel talan, sakenn dapre so kapasite, lerla li ale."
Matthew25:16 Serviter ki ti resevwar sink talan la, vitvit li finn al fer komers avek sa larzan la e sa finn raport li ankor sink talan."
Matthew25:17 Serviter ki ti resevwar de talan la fer parey li osi, e li gagn ankor de talan."
Matthew25:18 Me seki ti resevwar enn sel talan la, li fouy enn trou dan later e li kasiet larzan so patron."
Matthew25:19 Enn bon letan apre, zot patron retourne e li koumans regle so kont ar zot."
Matthew25:20 Seki ti resevwar sink talan la aprose e prezant so patron sa sink talan ki li ti finn gagne anplis, e li dir li: ‘Met, ou finn donn mwa sink talan, ala mo finn gagn ankor sink.’"
Matthew25:21 So met dir li: ‘To finn bien fer, bon serviter fidel. To finn fidel pou enn ti zafer, mo pou met twa ansarz pli gran zafer ankor. Vinn partaz lazwa to met.’"
Matthew25:22 Serviter ki ti resevwar de talan la aprose li osi, li dir: ‘Met, ou finn donn mwa de talan, ala mo finn gagn ankor de.’"
Matthew25:23 So met dir li: ‘To finn bien fer, bon serviter fidel. To finn fidel pou enn ti zafer, mo pou met twa ansarz pli gran zafer ankor. Vinn partaz lazwa to met.’"
Matthew25:24 Apre sa, serviter ki ti resevwar enn sel talan la aprose e li dir: ‘Met, mo kone kouma enn dimoun bien ti dir: ou rekolte kot ou pa finn plante, ou ramase kot ou pa finn seme."
Matthew25:25 Mo finn gagn per, e mo finn al kasiet talan la anba later. Ala, mo rann ou li.’"
Matthew25:26 Patron la reponn li, ‘Eta move serviter pares! To bien kone ki mo rekolte kot mo pa finn plante, e mo ramas kot mo pa finn seme?"
Matthew25:27 Alor to ti bien kapav met mo larzan dan labank, koumsa ler mo retourne mo ti va regagn li avek lintere."
Matthew25:28 Repran sa talan la ar li e donn li sa dimoun ki ena dis la.
Matthew25:29 Parski tou dimoun ki ena, pou gagn plis ankor, e zot pou dan labondans; me dimoun ki pena nanye, mem sa tigit ki zot ena la, pou ras sa ar zot."
Matthew25:30 Sa serviter ki pa vo nanye la, pran li zet li deor dan nwar, kot pou ena boukou plore, kriye ek grinsman ledan.’ ”"
Matthew25:31 “Kan Garson Limanite vini dan so laglwar avek tou bann anz, li pou asiz lor so tronn rwayal."
Matthew25:32 Tou bann nasion pou rasanble devan li, e li pou separ bann dimoun sakenn so kote, parey enn berze separ mouton ek kabri."
Matthew25:33 Li pou met bann mouton dan so kote drwat e bann kabri dan so gos.
Matthew25:34 Alor lerwa pou dir ar bann ki dan kote drwat, ‘Vini, zot ki mo papa finn beni. Resevwar rwayom ki Bondie finn prepare pou zot depi kreasion lemonn."
Matthew25:35 Avredir mo ti fin e zot finn donn mwa manze. Mo ti swaf e zot finn donn mwa bwar. Mo ti enn etranze e zot finn akeyir mwa.
Matthew25:36 Mo ti touni, e zot finn donn mwa linz. Mo ti malad, e zot finn vizit mwa. Mo ti dan prizon e zot finn vinn get mwa.’"
Matthew25:37 Alor bann ki finn obeir Bondie, zot dir lerwa: ‘Segner, kan nou finn trouv twa pe mordefin e nou finn donn twa manze? Oubien to ti swaf e nou finn donn twa bwar?"
Matthew25:38 Kan nou finn trouv twa enn etranze e nou finn akeyir twa, oubien touni nou finn donn twa linz?"
Matthew25:39 E kan nou finn trouv twa malad oubien dan prizon e nou finn vizit twa?’
Matthew25:40 Lerla lerwa reponn zot: ‘Laverite, mo dir zot, sak fwa ki zot finn fer sa ar enn sa bann pli tipti la ki dan mo fami, ar momem ki zot ti fer sa.’"
Matthew25:41 Apre lerwa pou dir bann ki dan so kote gos: ‘Al lwin ar mwa zot modi! Al dan dife eternel ki pa pou zame tegn e ki finn prepare pou Satan ek so bann asosie.
Matthew25:42 Parski mo ti fin e zot pa finn donn mwa manze. Mo ti swaf e zot pa finn donn mwa bwar.
Matthew25:43 Mo ti enn etranze e zot pa finn akeyir mwa, touni zot pa finn donn mwa linz, malad ek dan prizon, zot pa finn pran mwa swin?’"
Matthew25:44 Alor zot osi, zot pou dir lerwa: ‘Segner, kan eski nou finn trouv twa, to ti gagn fin ek swaf, etranze, touni, malad e dan prizon e nou pa finn ed twa?’"
Matthew25:45 Alor li pou reponn zot: ‘Laverite mo dir zot, letan zot pa finn fer sa pou enn sa bann pli tipti parmi zot, ar mwa osi zot pa finn fer li.’"
Matthew25:46 E sa bann la pou pini pou toultan, me bann zis, zot pou gagn lavi eternel.”"
Matthew26:1 Kan Zezi fini so lansegnman, li dir so bann disip,"
Matthew26:2 “Zot kone ki fet Pak pe vini dan de zour e bann la pou livre Garson Limanite e pou koulout li lor enn lakrwa.”
Matthew26:3 Apre sa, bann sef pret ek bann ansien dan pep Zwif fer enn reynion dan pale Kaif, ki ti gran pret."
Matthew26:4 Zot pran desizion ansam pou aret Zezi san ki personn kone e pou al touy li.
Matthew26:5 Zot ti pe dir, “Fodre pa ki nou aret li letan fet pe deroule parski dimoun pou kapav revolte.”"
Matthew26:6 Zezi ti dan Betani kot Simon ki ti ena lalep.
Matthew26:7 Enn fam vinn pre ar Zezi avek enn flakon an albat ki ti ranpli avek enn parfin ki ti ena gran valer; li vers sa parfin la lor latet Zezi, letan Zezi ti atab."
Matthew26:8 Letan bann disip trouv sa, zot mekontan. Zot dir, “Kifer bizin fer gaspiyaz?"
Matthew26:9 Ti kapav vann sa parfin la pou enn gro som larzan e donn kas la bann pov!”
Matthew26:10 Zezi ti kone ki zot ti pe dir, alor li dir zot, “Kifer zot met sa fam la dan lanbara; li pe fer enn bonaksion pou mwa."
Matthew26:11 Parski zot, zot pou touzour gagn bann pov parmi zot me mwa, mo pa pou toultan parmi zot."
Matthew26:12 Li finn met sa parfin la lor mo lekor pou prepar mo lanterman.
Matthew26:13 Laverite mo dir zot, partou kot Bonn Nouvel pou anonse dan lemonn antie, pou koz lor seki sa fam la finn fer e pou gard so souvenir.”"
Matthew26:14 Apre sa, enn parmi Ledouz, Zida Iskaryot, al zwenn bann sef pret"
Matthew26:15 e li dir zot, “Ki zot pou donn mwa si mo livre zot Zezi?” Zot pey li trant pies larzan."
Matthew26:16 Depi sa moman la, Zida ti pe rod enn bon lokazion pou livre zot Zezi."
Matthew26:17 Premie zour fet dipin san levin, bann disip vinn get Zezi e zot dimann li, “Kot to anvi nou prepar repa Pak pou to manze?”"
Matthew26:18 Li dir, “Al dan lavil kot intel, e dir li, ‘Lemet dir, mo letan pe aprose; mo pou manz Pak kot twa avek mo bann disip.’ ”"
Matthew26:19 Bann disip fer dapre seki Zezi finn dir zot e zot al prepar repa Pak.
Matthew26:20 Aswar, li asiz omilie Ledouz,"
Matthew26:21 e pandan repa li dir zot, “Laverite mo dir zot, enn parmi zot pou trair mwa.”"
Matthew26:22 Zot ti bien tris e sakenn so tour koumans dir li, “Mwa sa Segner?”"
Matthew26:23 Zezi reponn, “Dimoun ki finn tranp so dipin dan pla avek mwa, limem pou trair mwa."
Matthew26:24 Garson Limanite pe al mor dapre seki finn ekrir lor li, me maler pou sa dimoun ki pe trair Garson Limanite! Pou limem vomie, li pa ti ne.”"
Matthew26:25 Zida ki ti pe trair Zezi dimann li, “Mwa sa Met?” Zezi reponn li, “To finn dir tou tomem.”"
Matthew26:26 Letan pe manze, Zezi pran dipin, donn benediksion, kas dipin la e li donn so bann disip. Li dir, “Pran, manze, samem mo lekor.”"
Matthew26:27 Apre Zezi pran koup divin, li rann gras e li donn so bann disip, li dir, “Bwar sa zot tou,"
Matthew26:28 parski samem mo disan, disan lalians ki mo verse pou tou dimoun e pouki zot pese pardone."
Matthew26:29 Mo dir zot, mo nepli pou bwar fri pie rezin ziska sa zour ki mo pou bwar divin nouvo avek zot dan Rwayom mo Papa.”"
Matthew26:30 Letan zot finn fini sant bann Psom, zot al lor kolinn Pie Zoliv."
Matthew26:31 Zezi dir ar so bann disip, “Lanwit kot zot tou pou tonbe akoz mwa finn arive. Dan Lekritir finn ekrir, ‘Mo pou touy berze, e bann mouton pou fane partou kote.’ ”"
Matthew26:32 Me Zezi dir ankor, “Kan mo pou resisite, mo pou atann zot Galile.”"
Matthew26:33 Lerla Pier dir li, “Mem si arive ki tou dimoun abandonn twa, mwa, mo pa pou abandonn twa.”"
Matthew26:34 Zezi reponn li, “Laverite mo dir twa, aswar mem, avan ki kok sante, to pou renie mwa trwa fwa.”"
Matthew26:35 Pier dir li, “Mem si bizin mor avek twa, zame mo pou renie twa.” Lerla tou bann disip dir parey."
Matthew26:36 Apre sa, Zezi al avek so bann disip dan enn landrwa ki ti apel Zetsemani e li dir zot, “Res la, mwa mo pe al inpe pli lwin pou priye.”"
Matthew26:37 Li pran Pier ek de garson Zebede ar li e li koumans santi enn gran tristes ek langwas.
Matthew26:38 Li dir zot, “Mo ranpli ar enn gran tristes ki pe fini mwa. Res la avek mwa, pa dormi.”"
Matthew26:39 Li al inpe pli lwin, li tom azenou, so fron tous later e li priye, “Papa, si li posib, met sa koup la lwin ar mwa, selman pa kouma mo oule me fer kouma twa to oule.”"
Matthew26:40 Apre sa, li vinn ar so trwa disip e li trouv zot pe dormi. Li dir Pier, “To pa finn gagn lafors pou res avek mwa enn-ertan selman?"
Matthew26:41 Veye, priye pouki zot pa rant dan tantasion. Lespri anvi mem, me laser feb.”"
Matthew26:42 Enn deziem fwa, li al pli lwin e li priye, “Papa, si li pa posib ki sa koup la res lwin ar mwa e ki mo bizin bwar li, mo pou touzour fer dapre to volonte.”"
Matthew26:43 Li revinn ar so bann disip e li trouv zot pe dormi, somey dan lizie."
Matthew26:44 Li kit zot ankor e li al priye enn trwaziem fwa. Li ti pe dir toultan mem parol.
Matthew26:45 Apre sa, li revinn ar so bann disip e li dir zot, “Zot ankor pe dormi e zot pe repoze. Ala ler finn arive kot Garson Limanite pou livre dan lame bann peser."
Matthew26:46 Leve, anou ale! Gete, li pe vini, sa dimoun ki pou livre mwa la.”"
Matthew26:47 Zezi ti pe koze, kan Zida, enn parmi Ledouz, vini avek enn lafoul dimoun ki ti arme ar lepe ek gourdin. Bann sef pret ek ansien parmi bann lepep finn avoy zot."
Matthew26:48 Tret la finn donn zot enn sign; li finn dir zot, “Dimoun ki mo pou anbrase la, limem sa, trap li.”"
Matthew26:49 Zida koste ar Zezi e li dir li, “Shalom Met.” E li anbras Zezi."
Matthew26:50 Zezi dir li, “Kamarad, fer seki to ena pou fer.” Lerla bann la vini trap Zezi e zot aret li."
Matthew26:51 Anplas, enn dan group Zezi tir so lepe e donn serviter gran pret enn gran kout e li koup so zorey."
Matthew26:52 Me Zezi dir li, “Met to lepe dan to fouro parski seki servi lepe pou mor ar lepe."
Matthew26:53 Eski to pa kone ki mo kapav apel mo Papa e li ti pou avoy mwa plis ki douz larme anz?
Matthew26:54 Kimanier seki finn ekrir pou realize? Eski sa pa bizin arive?”
Matthew26:55 Lerla Zezi dir ar lafoul, “Eski zot ti bizin vinn ar lepe ek gourdin pou aret mwa kouma dir mo enn voler? Toulezour mo ti pe asize dan tanp e mo ti pe ansegne e zame zot finn aret mwa."
Matthew26:56 Tousala finn arive pouki parol bann profet realize.” Lerla tou disip kit li sove.
Matthew26:57 Bann seki finn aret Zezi amenn li devan gran pret Kaif. Bann dokter lalwa ek bann ansien ti finn zwenn.
Matthew26:58 Pier ti pe swiv enn distans e li aret devan lakour gran pret. Li rant dan lakour, li asiz avek bann gard pou gete kouma tousala pou fini."
Matthew26:59 Bann sef pret ek Gran Tribinal Zwif ti pe rod met enn fos sarz lor Zezi pou kapav kondann li amor,"
Matthew26:60 me zot pa trouv nanye, mem si boukou fos temwin ti vinn fer zot depozision. Finalman de boug aprose"
Matthew26:61 e zot dir, “Li finn dir, ‘Mo kapav detrir tanp Bondie e rekonstrir li dan trwa zour.’ ”"
Matthew26:62 Gran pret leve e dir, “To pa reponn? Ki to ena pou dir lor sa bann akizasion la?”"
Matthew26:63 Me Zezi pa dir nanye. Alor gran pret dir li, “Fer serman lor nom Bondie Vivan e dir nou si vremem to Lekris, Garson Bondie.”"
Matthew26:64 Zezi reponn, “Tomem to pe dir; me mwa, mo dir zot, asterla zot pou trouv Garson Limanite pe asiz kote drwat Bondie Toupwisan, e li pe vinn lor bann niaz dan lesiel.”"
Matthew26:65 Lerla gran pret desir so linz e dir, “Li finn blasfeme. Ki lot temwagnaz nou bizin ankor? Zot fek tann so blasfem."
Matthew26:66 Ki zot ena pou dir?” Bann la reponn, “Li koupab e li merit lamor.”"
Matthew26:67 Zot kras dan so figir, zot donn li koutpwin, ena donn li kalot."
Matthew26:68 Zot dir li, “Twa ki deklar Lekris, fer to profet ar nou, kisannla finn bat twa?”"
Matthew26:69 Pier ti pe asiz deor dan lakour e enn servant koste ar li e dir, “Twa osi to ti avek Zezi ki sorti Galile.”"
Matthew26:70 Devan zot tou, li nie ki li ti ar Zezi e li dir, “Mo pa kone ki to pe koze.”"
Matthew26:71 Apre sa li sorti, li al devan laport. Enn lot servant trouv li e li dir, “Li ti avek Zezi Nazaret.”"
Matthew26:72 Ankor enn fwa li nie e li fer serman, “Mo pa konn sa boug la mwa.”"
Matthew26:73 Zis apre, bann ki ti la, vini e dir Pier, “Pena bare, twa osi to dan sa group la; fini kone par to manier koze.”"
Matthew26:74 Alor li fer serman e li dir, “Bondie pini mwa si mo pe koz manti, mo pa konn sa boug la.” Lerlamem, kok sante."
Matthew26:75 Lerla Pier rapel parol Zezi, ‘Avan ki kok sante, to pou finn renie mwa trwa fwa,’ - e li sorti deor, li al plore ar enn gro sagrin dan leker."
Matthew27:1 Boner gramatin, tou bann sef pret ek bann ansien parmi lepep pran desizion ansam pou touy Zezi."
Matthew27:2 Zot atas li, zot amenn li e zot livre li ar gouverner Pilat."
Matthew27:3 Letan Zida ki ti trair Zezi aprann ki Zezi finn kondane, li gagn remor e li retourn trant pies larzan la bann sef pret ek bann ansien."
Matthew27:4 Li dir, “Mo finn fer pese parski mo finn livre disan enn inosan.” Zot reponn, “Ki to oule nou fer? Sa to problem.”"
Matthew27:5 Zida zet larzan la dan tanp. Li sorti e li al met li pandi.
Matthew27:6 Bann sef pret ramas larzan la e dir, “Nou lalwa pa permet nou depoz sa larzan la dan lakes tanp parski ena disan ladan.”"
Matthew27:7 Zot tom dakor pou aste terin sa dimoun kifer potri la, pou zot fer enn simitier pou bann etranze."
Matthew27:8 Akoz samem apel sa later la “Later disan” ziska zordi.
Matthew27:9 Lerla parol profet Zeremi finn realize. Li ti dir, “Zot finn pran trant pies larzan, samem valer ki bann zanfan Izrael finn estim li,"
Matthew27:10 e zot finn servi sa kas la pou aste later potie kouma Lesegner finn donn lord.”
Matthew27:11 Zezi konparet devan gouverner ki ti interoz li, “Tomem lerwa Zwif?” Zezi reponn, “Tomem to pe dir.”"
Matthew27:12 Kan bann sef pret ek bann ansien akiz li, li pa reponn nanye."
Matthew27:13 Lerla Pilat dir li, “Eski to pa tann tou bann akizasion kont twa?”"
Matthew27:14 Zezi pa reponn lor okenn pwin e so silans ti bien inpresionn gouverner.
Matthew27:15 Pou sak fet Pak, gouverner ti ena labitid larg enn prizonie ki lafoul dimande."
Matthew27:16 Be, ti ena enn prizonie ki tou dimoun kone. Li ti apel Barabas."
Matthew27:17 Lerla Pilat dimann lafoul, “Kisannla zot anvi mo large - Barabas oubien Zezi ki zot apel Lekris?”"
Matthew27:18 Pilat ti kone ki zot finn livre Zezi par zalouzi.
Matthew27:19 Letan Pilat ti pe siez dan tribinal, so fam avoy li enn mesaz, “Pa mel twa dan zizman sa inosan la parski dan lanwit, mo finn bien azite dan mo rev akoz li.”"
Matthew27:20 Bann sef pret konvink lafoul pouki liber Barabas e kondann Zezi amor.
Matthew27:21 Gouverner redimann zot, “Kisannla zot ti anvi mo large ant sa de la?” Zot reponn, “Barabas.”"
Matthew27:22 “Ki mo pou fer ar Zezi ki zot apel Lekris?” Zot tou reponn, “Krisifie li.”"
Matthew27:23 Pilat dimann zot, “Ki li finn fer demal?” Zot tou kriye, “Krisifie li.”"
Matthew27:24 Letan Pilat trouve ki li nepli kapav fer nanye me ki bann la pe pli revolte, li pran dilo e li lav so lame devan lafoul; li dir, “Mo pa responsab disan sa dimoun la; get zot zafer.”"
Matthew27:25 Lafoul antie reponn, “Disan sa boug la ava tom lor nou e lor nou bann zanfan.”"
Matthew27:26 Apre sa, Pilat larg Barabas, li fer fwet Zezi e li livre li ar lafoul pouki bann la krisifie li."
Matthew27:27 Bann solda amenn Zezi dan pale gouverner e boukou solda ti pe eskort li.
Matthew27:28 Zot dezabiy li e zot met enn manto rouz vif lor li.
Matthew27:29 Apre zot tres enn kouronn pikan, zot met sa lor so latet e zot met enn bout baton dan so lame drwat. Apre zot met zot azenou devan li e zot boufonn li, “Aksepte nou respe, Lerwa Zwif.”"
Matthew27:30 Zot kras lor li e zot servi samem baton la pou bat li lor so latet.
Matthew27:31 Kan zot finn bien boufonn li, zot tir manto la, zot remet so linz e apre zot amenn li pou koulout li lor lakrwa."
Matthew27:32 Letan zot pe ale, zot trouv Simon, enn abitan Sirenn; bann solda obliz li sarye lakrwa Zezi."
Matthew27:33 Zot ariv enn landrwa ki ti apel Golgota, sakivedir, “Landrwa Krann.”"
Matthew27:34 Zot donn li bwar enn divin melanze avek enn kiksoz amer; letan li gout sa, li pale bwar."
Matthew27:35 Zot krisifie li e apre zot tir osor pou partaz so linz.
Matthew27:36 Apre zot asize pou vey li.
Matthew27:37 Lao lor latet Zezi finn ekrir pouki rezon finn kondann li, “Limem Zezi Lerwa bann Zwif.”"
Matthew27:38 De bandi ti kouloute lor lakrwa ansam ar li. Enn adrwat, lot la agos."
Matthew27:39 Bann seki ti pe pas par la ti pe insilte li e ti pe bouz zot latet
Matthew27:40 pou dir li, “Pa tomem ki ti anvi detrir tanp pou rekonstrir enn lot dan trwa zour; sov twa tomem; si vremem to Garson Bondie, desann lor sa lakrwa la!”"
Matthew27:41 Bann sef pret, bann dokter lalwa ek bann ansien osi ti pe boufonn li. Zot ti pe dir,"
Matthew27:42 “Li finn sov lezot me li pa pe kapav sov limem! Si limem lerwa Izrael, ki li desann lor lakrwa asterlamem, nou ava krwar dan li."
Matthew27:43 Li finn met so konfians dan Bondie e li finn dir, ‘Mo Garson Bondie.’ Si vremem Bondie oule, dir li vinn delivre li asterlamem.”"
Matthew27:44 Bann bandi ki ti avek li, zot osi zot ti pe insilte li."
Matthew27:45 Depi midi teneb partou kote lor pei ziska trwa-zer tanto.
Matthew27:46 Ver trwa-zer, Zezi kriye bien-bien for, “Eli, Eli, lema sabaktani” - sakivedir, “Bondie, Bondie, kifer to finn abandonn mwa?”"
Matthew27:47 Detrwa ki ti la tann sa e zot dir, “Li pe apel Eli!”"
Matthew27:48 Toutswit enn parmi zot galoupe, al pran enn leponz, tranp li dan vineg, met li dan bout enn long baton e donn li pou bwar."
Matthew27:49 Bann lezot dir, “Atann, nou gete si Eli pou vinn sap li.”"
Matthew27:50 Zezi kriye bien for enn dernie kout e li rann so dernie soupir.
Matthew27:51 Salerla, rido tanp desire depi lao ziska anba; later tranble e bann ros fann an-de."
Matthew27:52 Bann tom ouver e boukou lekor bann krwayan ki ti pe dormi leve.
Matthew27:53 Zot sorti dan zot tom e apre rezireksion Zezi, zot rant dan lavil sint kot boukou dimoun finn trouv zot."
Matthew27:54 Santiryon Romin ek bann solda ki ti pe vey Zezi trouv later tranble e zot temwin tou seki ti pe arive. Alor zot gagn per e zot dir, “Vremem li ti Garson Bondie.”"
Matthew27:55 Ti ena boukou fam ki ti pe get delwin seki ti pe pase. Zot ti finn swiv Zezi depi Galile e zot ti so bann disip osi.
Matthew27:56 Parmi zot, ti ena Marie Magdalenn, Marie, mama Zak ek Zozef e mama bann garson Zebede."
Matthew27:57 Kan koumans fer nwar, Zozef, enn zom ris ki sorti Arimate e ki ti osi enn disip Zezi,"
Matthew27:58 al get Pilat pou gagn lekor Zezi. Pilat donn lord pou donn lekor la Zozef.
Matthew27:59 Zozef pran lekor la, anvlop li dan enn dra nef an lin."
Matthew27:60 Li depoz lekor Zezi dan so prop tonbo nef ki ti finn taye dan ros. Apre sa li pous enn ros devan lantre tonbo la e li ale.
Matthew27:61 Marie-Madlenn ek lot Marie, ti la osi. Zot ti pe asiz vizavi tonbo."
Matthew27:62 Lelandime, enn zour apre saba, bann sef pret ek bann Farizien al get Pilat ansam."
Matthew27:63 Zot dir, “Vot oner, nou rapel ki sa fos profet la ti pe dir kan li ti ankor vivan ki li pou resisite lor trwaziem zour."
Matthew27:64 Nou dimann ou permision pouki met gard devan sa tonbo la ziska trwaziem zour; parski kapav arive ki so bann disip vinn kokin so lekor pou fer lepep krwar, ‘Li finn resisite parmi bann mor.’ Sa mansonz la pou pli pir ki premie la.”"
Matthew27:65 Pilat dir zot, “Zot ena zot bann solda. Al vey tonbo la kouma zot anvi.”"
Matthew27:66 Lerla zot sorti e zot al met zot gard devan tonbo; zot met sele lor ros ki ti blok lantre tonbo.
Matthew28:1 Lelandime saba, premie zour lasemenn, kan soley pe leve, Marie-Madlenn ek lot Marie al kot tonbo."
Matthew28:2 Enn sel kout ti ena enn gran tranblemandeter parski enn anz Lesegner ki ti desann depi lesiel, ti pous sa gro ros la e li ti asiz lor la."
Matthew28:3 Li ti kouma enn zekler e so linz ti blan kouma lanez.
Matthew28:4 Bann gard ti telman per ki zot koumans tranble e zot ti vinn parey kouma dimoun mor.
Matthew28:5 Anz la dir bann madam la, “Pa gagn per. Mo kone ki zot pe rod Zezi, limem ki bann la finn krisifie;"
Matthew28:6 li nepli la, li finn resisite parey kouma li finn dir. Rantre, gete kot ti met so lekor."
Matthew28:7 Degaze al dir so bann disip, ‘Li finn resisite parmi bann mor e li pe atann zot Galile.’ Zot pou trouv li laba. Ala seki mo ti ena pou dir zot.”"
Matthew28:8 Zot sorti toutswit dan tonbo leker ranpli ar lafreyer e zot ti dan enn gran lazwa anmemtan. Zot galoupe pou al anons sa nouvel la bann disip.
Matthew28:9 Ala ki Zezi vinn devan zot e li dir zot, “Shalom.” Zot koste ar li, zot atrap so lipie e zot ador li."
Matthew28:10 Zezi dir zot, “Pa gagn per; al dir mo bann frer ek mo bann ser, al Galile; laba zot pou trouv mwa.”"
Matthew28:11 Letan bann fam la ti pe ale lor sime, detrwa gard retourn dan lavil e rakont bann sef pret tou seki finn pase."
Matthew28:12 Bann sef pret la ek bann ansien tom dakor pou donn enn gro som lamone bann gard la,"
Matthew28:13 e dir zot, “Zot bizin dir ki bann disip sa boug la finn vinn kokin so lekor dan lanwit letan zot ti pe dormi."
Matthew28:14 Si gouverner aprann sa, nou pou kapav konvink li pouki zot pa gagn problem.”"
Matthew28:15 Bann gard pran larzan la e fer exakteman dapre bann instriksion ki zot finn gagne. Koumsamem sa zistwar la finn fane parmi bann Zwif ziska zordi.
Matthew28:16 Onz disip Zezi al Galile, lor kolinn kot li finn donn zot randevou."
Matthew28:17 Letan bann la trouv li, zot ador li me enn-de parmi zot ti ankor pe doute."
Matthew28:18 Zezi vinn pre ar zot e dir zot, “Finn donn mwa tou pouvwar dan lesiel ek lor later,"
Matthew28:19 Al dan tou bann pep ki ena e fer zot vinn mo bann disip; batiz zot lor nom mo Papa, lor nom so Garson e lor nom Lespri Sin."
Matthew28:20 Montre zot met anpratik tou seki mo finn komann zot. Pa bliye, mo avek zot toulezour ziska lafin-dimonn.”"
Mark1:1 Premie komansman Bonn Nouvel Zezi Kris Garson Bondie.
Mark1:2 Dan liv profet Izai finn ekrir: “Gete, mo pe avoy mo mesaze devan twa, Limem pou tras enn sime pou twa."
Mark1:3 Enn lavwa ape kriye dan dezer, prepar sime Nou Segner, ouver enn sime kler pou li.”"
Mark1:4 Zan Batis paret dan dezer; li proklam enn batem pouki bann dimoun sanz zot leker e ki zot pese pardone.
Mark1:5 Tou dimoun ki res Zide ek Zerizalem ti pe vinn get Zan. Li ti pe batiz zot dan larivier Zourdin letan zot tou ti pe konfes zot pese anpiblik.
Mark1:6 Zan ti met enn linz pwal samo ek enn sang lapo dan so lerin. Li ti manz sotrel ek dimiel sovaz.
Mark1:7 Li ti pe proklame, “Ena enn ki pli for ki mwa, li pe vinn apre mwa; mo pa ase bon, pou mo kourbe devan li, pou larg so sandalet."
Mark1:8 Mwa, mo finn batiz zot ar dilo, me li, li pou batiz zot ar Lespri Sin.”"
Mark1:9 Samem lepok la, Zezi sorti depi Nazaret, ki trouv dan Galile; lerla Zan finn batiz li dan larivier Zourdin."
Mark1:10 Zis kouma li pe sorti dan dilo, Zezi trouv lesiel fann an-de. Lespri Sin, parey kouma enn kolonb, desann lor li."
Mark1:11 Enn lavwa, dan lesiel dir, “Tomem mo Garson, ki mo bien kontan; sa fer mwa enn gran lazwa pou swazir twa.”"
Mark1:12 Zis apre sa, Lespri pous li dan dezer."
Mark1:13 Dan dezer, Satan finn tant li, pandan karant zour. Li ti avek bann bebet sovaz e bann anz ti pe servi li."
Mark1:14 Letan bannla finn aret Zan, Zezi rant dan Galile. Li koumans proklam Bonn Nouvel Bondie."
Mark1:15 Li dir: “Ler finn arive, Rwayom Bondie pe koste. Sanz zot leker, krwar dan Bonn Nouvel.”"
Mark1:16 Letan li ti pe mars-marse dan borlamer Galile, li trouv de peser, Simon, avek so frer Andre ki ti pe lapes lasenn."
Mark1:17 Zezi dir zot, “Vini, swiv mwa; mo pou montre zot lapes dimoun.”"
Mark1:18 Lor vites, zot kit zot file, zot swiv Zezi."
Mark1:19 Inpe pli lwin, li trouv de garson Zebede: Zak ek so frer Zan. Toulede ti dan pirog; zot ti pe demay zot file."
Mark1:20 Enn sel kout, li apel zot; zot kit zot papa Zebede anplan dan bato avek bann travayer. Zot swiv Zezi."
Mark1:21 Zezi ek so bann disip al Kafarnaom. Zour saba, Zezi rant dan sinagog e li koumans donn lansegnman."
Mark1:22 So parol ti inpresionn dimoun. So koze, so lansegnman ti ena pwa parski li pa ti parey kouma bann dokter lalwa."
Mark1:23 Zisteman dan zot sinagog, ti ena enn boug posede par enn move lespri. Li ape kriye for-for:"
Mark1:24 “Zezi Nazaret, ki to oule, ki to vinn rode ar nou? To finn vini pou fini nou? Mo kone ki to ete: tomem Sin, tomem sorti kot Bondie.”"
Mark1:25 Zezi menas li. Li dir li: “Ferm to labous; sorti la, ale.”"
Mark1:26 Move lespri la sakouy-sakouy dimoun la. Li irle letan li larg dimoun la.
Mark1:27 Lasistans gagn sok; sakenn dimann ar so kamarad, “Ki pe arive, ki sa vedir? Ala enn nouvo manier koze ki ena pwa. Mem move lespri la ekout li.”"
Mark1:28 Lerlamem so koze fane partou kote dan Galile.
Mark1:29 Kouma bannla kit sinagog, zot rant dan lakaz Simon ek Andre, ansam avek Zak ek Zan."
Mark1:30 Belmer Simon ti lor lili ar enn move lafiev. Bannla raport sa Zezi.
Mark1:31 Zezi koste, li trap so lame, li lev li. So lafiev kit li ale. Lerla belmer la koumans servi zot."
Mark1:32 Aswar vini, soley ti pe al dormi, zot sarye devan Zezi tou seki ti malad, tou seki ti ena demon lor zot."
Mark1:33 Tou dimoun dan landrwa finn rasanble devan laport.
Mark1:34 Zezi geri boukou dimoun ki ti ena tout sort kalite maladi; Li sas demon lor bann ki ti posede. Li ferm labous bann demon parski zot ti kone ki Zezi ete.
Mark1:35 Gramatin boner, kan ti ankor fer nwar, Zezi leve, li kit lakaz, li al dan enn landrwa retire pou priye."
Mark1:36 Simon ek so bann kamarad ti pe rod li partou.
Mark1:37 Ler zot retrouv li, zot dir li, “Tou dimoun pe rod twa.”"
Mark1:38 Li dir zot, “Anou al inpe pli lwin dan bann lezot landrwa; laba osi, mo bizin proklam Bonn Nouvel. Akoz samem mo finn vini.”"
Mark1:39 Koumsamem li ti al partou dan Galile, li ti pe proklam Bonn Nouvel dan zot sinagog e li ti pe sas demon."
Mark1:40 Enn dimoun ki ti ena lalep vinn get li. Li ti tom azenou devan Zezi, li sipliye li, “Si sa to volonte, to kapav pirifie mwa.”"
Mark1:41 Sa fer Zezi enn gran lapenn; Zezi avans so lame e li tous li. Zezi dir li, “Samem mo volonte, aster to pou pirifie.”"
Mark1:42 Deswit lalep kit li, ek li ti pirifie."
Mark1:43 Apre ki Zezi ti warn li severman, li fer li ale."
Mark1:44 Li dir li: “Sirtou pa al rakont sa personn; ale, al get enn pret; donn seki Moiz finn dir pou pirifikasion; sa pou enn temwagnaz pou lezot.”"
Mark1:45 Kouma li sorti deor, li koumans rakonte, li fann nouvel partou. Akoz samem Zezi ti bizin kasiet-kasiet e pa ti kapav rant dan lavil; li ti oblize al dan bann landrwa retire; kanmem sa, dimoun ti sorti partou pou vinn get li."
Mark2:1 Detrwa zour apre, Zezi retourn dan Kafarnaom. Nouvel fane ki li dan lakaz enn dimoun."
Mark2:2 Lakaz ti telman ranpli ar dimoun, ki mem deor devan laport pa ti ena plas. Li ti pe explik laparol."
Mark2:3 Enn bann dimoun ti vinn get li. Kat parmi zot, ti pe sarye enn paralize."
Mark2:4 Kouma zot pa ti kapav koste kot Zezi, akoz ti ena enn gran lafoul, zot retir twa lakaz la, zot fer enn trou. Lerla, zot fer paralize la desann avek so brankar."
Mark2:5 Letan Zezi trouve ki kantite lafwa zot ti ena, li dir paralize la, “Mo garson, to pese finn pardone.”"
Mark2:6 Ti ena detrwa dokter lalwa ki ti la; zot ti pe asize. Zot ti pe panse dan zot mem,"
Mark2:7 “Pou ki li pran li pou li koz koumsa? Zot pa trouve li pe blasfeme! Kisannla kapav pardonn bann pese apart Bondie tousel?”
Mark2:8 Deswit dan so lespri, Zezi ti fini kone ki ti ena dan zot leker. Li dir zot, “Kifer zot pans koumsa?"
Mark2:9 Ki pli fasil pou dir paralize la, ‘To pese finn pardone’ ou bien, ‘Debout, ramas to brankar, marse’?"
Mark2:10 Ala mo dir zot, pouki zot trouve ki Garson Limanite ena lotorite pou pardonn bann pese lor later,” - li dir paralize la,"
Mark2:11 “Ekout mwa, leve, ramas to brankar, al to lakaz.”"
Mark2:12 Lerla paralize la leve, li ramas so brankar, li sorti devan tou dimoun. Bann dimoun emerveye. Zot glorifie Bondie, zot dir, “Zame nou finn trouv sa kalite kiksoz la ar nou lizie.”"
Mark2:13 Zezi re-al ankor enn fwa dan borlamer. Enn gran lafoul antour li; li ti pe ansegn zot.
Mark2:14 Letan li ti pe pase, li trouv Levi, garson Alfe. Li ti pe asize devan biro tax. Zezi dir li, “Swiv mwa.” Lerla, li leve, li swiv Zezi."
Mark2:15 Apre sa, li al lakaz Levi. Li asize atab. Ti ena enn kantite kolekter tax ek bann peser ki ti pe manze avek Zezi ek so bann disip. Ti ena boukou-boukou dimoun. Zot tou ti pe swiv li."
Mark2:16 Letan bann dokter lalwa ek bann Farizien trouv li pe manze avek bann peser ek bann ramaser tax, zot dir so bann disip, “Kifer li manz avek bann kolekter tax ek bann ki fer pese?”"
Mark2:17 Letan Zezi tann sa, li dir, “Dimoun ki bien pa bizin dokter me dimoun ki malad, wi; mo pa finn vini pou dimoun korek me pou bann peser.”"
Mark2:18 Bann disip Zan ek bann Farizien ti gard karem. Dimoun vini, zot poz Zezi enn kestion, “Pou kifer bann disip Zan ek disip Farizien gard karem alor ki to bann disip pa fer li?”"
Mark2:19 Zezi reponn, “Eski bann invite dan maryaz kapav gard karem kan nouvo marye ankor avek zot? Tanki nouvo marye avek zot, zot napa pou kapav gard karem."
Mark2:20 Enn zour pou arive, kot nouvo marye nepli pou la avek zot, lerla zot va gard karem."
Mark2:21 Personn pa pran enn bout latwal ki pankor retresi pou rakomod enn vie linz; si fer sa, bout latwal nef la pou ris sa vie linz la kat kote, li pou plis desire."
Mark2:22 Personn pa met divin ki fek fer dan vie barik; si fer sa, divin la pou eklat barik la, lerla nou pou perdi divin ansam ar barik. Bizin met divin nouvo dan barik nef.”"
Mark2:23 Enn zour saba, Zezi ti pe travers enn karo dible. Letan zot ti pe marse, so bann disip ti pe grenn bann zepi dible."
Mark2:24 Bann Farizien dir li, “Dir nou pou kifer to bann disip fer kiksoz ki pa gagn drwa fer zour saba?”"
Mark2:25 Li reponn zot, “Zame zot pa finn lir saki David avek so bann kamarad ti fer, letan zot vant ti vid e ki zot ti pe gagn fin?"
Mark2:26 Zot pa rapel kouma li ti rant dan lakaz Bondie letan Abiatar ti gran pret? Zot pa rapel kouma li ti manz dipin konsakre ki personn pa ti gagn drwa manze, exsepte bann pret? Kouma li ti partaz sa dipin la avek so bann kamarad?”"
Mark2:27 Zezi kontigne ankor, “Saba finn fer pou dimoun, pa dimoun pou saba."
Mark2:28 Ala mo fer zot kone, Garson Limanite ki propriyeter saba.”"
Mark3:1 Ankor enn fwa, Zezi rant dan sinagog; enn boug ek lame mognon ti la."
Mark3:2 Bannla ti pe vey Zezi, pou gete si li ti pou geri sa boug la zour saba; koumsa zot ti pou kapav met enn sarz lor li."
Mark3:3 Li dir ar sa boug lame mognon la, “Leve, vinn devan.”"
Mark3:4 Lerla li dir bannla, “Dapre lord, ki gagn drwa fer zour saba? Fer bon kiksoz, fer move kiksoz? Sov enn lavi, tir enn lavi?” Zot tou res trankil."
Mark3:5 Li get zot ar lakoler, anmemtan, li sagrin ki zot leker dir. Li dir boug la, “Dres to lame.” Mognon la dres so lame; so lame revinn normal."
Mark3:6 Kouma bann Farizien tom deor, zot fer enn konplo avek bann Erodien pou touy Zezi."
Mark3:7 Zezi retir li dan borlamer avek so bann disip. Enn pake dimoun ti pe swiv li. Zot sorti partou kote dan Galile, Zide,"
Mark3:8 Zerizalem, Idoume, lot kote larivier Zourdin, dan rezion Tir ek Sidon. Nouvel ti finn fane komie kiksoz li ti pe fer; akoz samem zot ti pe vinn get li."
Mark3:9 Zezi ti bizin dir so bann disip pare enn pirog pou li, tansion lafoul kraz li."
Mark3:10 Li ti finn geri boukou dimoun; tou saki ti malad, ti pe pouse pou tous li."
Mark3:11 Sak fwa bann move lespri trouv li, zot tonbe, zot kriye, “Tomem Garson Bondie.”"
Mark3:12 Zezi menas zot pouki zot pa fer dimoun kone ki li ete.
Mark3:13 Li mont lor montagn. Li apel dimoun ki li ti oule. Bannla vini.
Mark3:14 Li swazir douz parmi zot, (li donn zot nom apot), pou bannla res avek li e pouki li avoy zot proklame avek"
Mark3:15 lotorite sas demon.
Mark3:16 Alors li nom Ledouz. Li donn Simon enn lot nom, li apel li Pier;"
Mark3:17 apre ti ena Zak ek so frer Zan, toulede garson Zebede. Li sanz zot nom, li apel zot Boanerzes, savedir zanfan loraz ek zekler;"
Mark3:18 ti ena osi Andre, Filip, Bartelmi, Matie, Toma, Zak garson Alfe, Tade, Simon ki ti res Kana"
Mark3:19 ek Zida Iskaryot, limem ki ti vann Zezi."
Mark3:20 Apre sa Zezi rant dan lakaz. Lafoul rekomans rasanble; telman dimoun ti pe ale-vini, ki zot pa ti kapav manz enn bout dipin."
Mark3:21 Kan fami Zezi aprann sa, zot ale pou trap li. Zot ti pe dir li ti finn perdi latet."
Mark3:22 Bann dokter lalwa ki ti finn desann depi Zerizalem ti pe dir ki ena Belzeboul lor Zezi, ki li sas demon par lafors sef bann demon."
Mark3:23 Li apel zot, li koz ar zot an parabol. Li dir zot, “Ki manier Satan kapav sas Satan?"
Mark3:24 Si enn Rwayom divize kont limem, Rwayom la pa kapav tini dibout."
Mark3:25 Si enn fami divize kont limem, fami la pa pou kapav tini dibout."
Mark3:26 Si Satan lev lager ar limem, savedir li divize, li pa pou kapav tini, li pou fini limem."
Mark3:27 Ou pa kapav rant dan lakaz enn dimoun for pou kokin so bann dibien san ki ou atas li avan; lerla ou pou kapav kokin kouma ou anvi.
Mark3:28 Mo dir zot enn zafer: laverite, laverite mo dir zot, tou pese, tou blasfem, ki dimoun fer pou pardone;"
Mark3:29 enn sel blasfem pa pou pardone, blasfem kont Lespri Sin. Li enn pese ki zame pou efase.”"
Mark3:30 Zezi ti pe koz koumsa parski bannla ti pe dir ki li ena enn move lespri lor li.
Mark3:31 So mama ek so bann frer vini. Zot res deor zot fer kriye li.
Mark3:32 Enn kantite dimoun ti pe asize; zot tou ti pe antour li; zot dir li, “Gete, to mama ek to bann frer inn vinn rod twa.”"
Mark3:33 Li reponn zot, “Kisannla mo mama, kisannla mo frer?”"
Mark3:34 Li lev so latet, li promne so regar lor sak dimoun ki ti pe asize. “Ala mo mama, ala mo bann frer."
Mark3:35 Dimoun ki fer volonte Bondie, limem mo frer, limem mo ser, limem mo mama.”"
Mark4:1 Ankor enn fwa, Zezi ti pe ansegne dan borlamer. Telman ti ena enn gro lafoul ki ti pe antour li, li monte, li al asiz dan enn pirog ki ti lor lamer. Lafoul ti lor laplaz dan bor dilo."
Mark4:2 Tou so koze ti an parabol; dan so lansegnman li ti pe dir,"
Mark4:3 “Ekout sa. Ala zistwar enn planter ki pe al seme.
Mark4:4 Letan li pe seme, enn parti lagrin tom lor sime. Zwazo vini, manz tou."
Mark4:5 Enn lot parti tom dan enn landrwa inpe ros-ros kot pa ti ena boukou later. Lagrin la pous vit parski later ti mins.
Mark4:6 Kouma soley tape, li griye, li mor, parski pa ti ena ase rasinn."
Mark4:7 Enn lot parti tom dan pikan. Letan pikan pouse, grandi, li touf li; li pa kapav raporte."
Mark4:8 Enn lot parti tom dan bon later. Li pouse, li vinn gran, li raport bien-bien mem: ena donn trant, ena swasant, ena donn ziska san fwa plis.”"
Mark4:9 Zezi dir zot, “Saki ena zorey pou tande, li pou tande.”"
Mark4:10 Letan li ti tousel, bann ki ti pros ar li ek so group Douz dimann li explikasion lor bann parabol. Li dir zot,"
Mark4:11 “Zot, finn fer zot konn sekre Rwayom Bondie. Pou bann saki andeor, tou pou res enn mister."
Mark4:12 Koumsa zot kapav gete, me zot pa pou trouv nanye, Zot kapav tande me zot pa pou konpran nanye, Lerla zot pa pou kapav sanz zot leker e zot pa pou gagn okenn pardon.”"
Mark4:13 Li dir zot, “Si zot pa konpran sa parabol la, kouma zot pou konpran lezot parabol?”"
Mark4:14 “Planter la, li sem laparol."
Mark4:15 Lagrin ki tom dan bor sime, savedir bann dimoun ki tann parol Bondie. Kouma zot tande, Satan vini, aras parol ki finn seme dan zot."
Mark4:16 Lagrin ki tom dan enn landrwa inpe ros-ros, vedir bann dimoun ki resevwar laparol dan lazwa kan zot tann li."
Mark4:17 Me kouma zot rasinn lao-lao, tou zafer zis pou enn letan; kouma zot gagn difikilte, persekision akoz parol Bondie, zot tonbe."
Mark4:18 Lagrin ki tom dan pikan, vedir bann dimoun ki zot ousi tann sa parol la."
Mark4:19 Me bann traka lavi, lanvi gagn touzour plis, tou sort kalite tantasion, tousala touf la parol. Li pa raport okenn fri."
Mark4:20 Saki tom lor bon later, vedir bann ki ekout parol Bondie, ki akey li. Zot finn raport trant, swasant ziska san fwa plis.”"
Mark4:21 Li koz ar bannla ankor. “Eski nou alim enn lalanp pou met li anba seo, anba lili ouswa nou met li anler lor enn stenn?"
Mark4:22 Pena okenn sekre ki pa pou dekouver; tou saki finn kasiet pou devwale.
Mark4:23 Saki ena zorey pou tande, li pou tande.”"
Mark4:24 Li dir zot ankor, “Pran kont saki zot pe tande. Mezir ki zot servi pou lezot, samem mezir pou servi pou zot; e pou zot, li pou inpe plis."
Mark4:25 Saki ena, pou gagn ankor; saki pena, mem sa tigit ki li ena la, pou repran.”"
Mark4:26 Li kontigne ankor, li dir, “Rwayom Bondie li parey kouma enn dimoun ki zet enn lagrin dan later."
Mark4:27 Ki li dormi, ki li leve, lanwit, lizour, lagrin la pou zerme, pou grandi san mem ki li kone kouma."
Mark4:28 Par limem, later fer so travay; premie dabor nou gagn lerb, apre li vinn enn zepi, anfin dible plin-plin dan zepi;"
Mark4:29 letan so fri finn pare, nek pas enn sinp kout fosi kan sezon lakoup finn arive.”"
Mark4:30 Li kontign koze, li dir, “Ar ki zafer nou konpar Rwayom Bondie? Ki kalite parabol nou kapav servi ankor?"
Mark4:31 Li parey kouma enn lagrin moutard. Kan nou finn sem li, limem pli tipti semans ki existe lor later."
Mark4:32 Me selman, kouma ou sem li, li monte. Li vinn pli gran ki tou bann plant dan zardin. So bann brans telman gran ki bann zwazo partou kote kapav vinn fer zot nik dan so lonbraz.”"
Mark4:33 Ar boukou parabol sa zar la, li ti pe anons laparol, dapre seki zot ti pe kapav konpran."
Mark4:34 Li ti koz ar zot zis an parabol, apre kan li ti tousel ar so bann disip, li ti explik zot tou kiksoz."
Mark4:35 Sa zour la, letan aswar finn arive, Zezi dir zot, “Anou travers lot kote.”"
Mark4:36 Zot kit lafoul, zot rant dan bato kot Zezi ti ete. Lezot bato al ansam ar li."
Mark4:37 Enn gran koudvan leve; gro-gro vag vinn kraz lor bato. Enn timama, bato koumans pran dilo."
Mark4:38 Zezi limem, li ti pe dormi par deryer lor enn kousin. Zot lev li, zot dir li, “Met, sa pa fer twa nanye ki nou pe koule?”"
Mark4:39 Li nek leve, li menas divan e li koz ar lamer, “Res trankil, kalme twa.” Labriz tonbe, letan kalme net."
Mark4:40 Lerla li dir zot, “Kifer zot kapon koumsa? Zot touzour pena lafwa?”"
Mark4:41 Enn gran lafreyer pran zot. Sakenn dir ar so kamarad, “Kisannla sa? Mem divan ek lamer obeir li?”"
Mark5:1 Apre sa, zot ariv lot kote lamer, dan landrwa bann Zerazenien."
Mark5:2 Kouma Zezi debarke, enn boug posede par enn move lespri, sorti dan bann tom, vinn zwenn li."
Mark5:3 Simitier ti so lakaz. Personn pa ti reysi atas li, mem pa avek enn lasenn."
Mark5:4 Souvan defwa, bannla ti atas so lipie avek rwayar ek lasenn; sak fwa li kas rwayar, li voltiz lasenn. Personn pa ti ase for pou dont li."
Mark5:5 Lanwit-lizour li irle dan simitier, lor montagn. Li ti koup-koup limem ar ros."
Mark5:6 Letan li trouv Zezi pe vini depi lwin, li galoupe, li tom azenou devan Zezi."
Mark5:7 Li koumans kriye bien-bien for, “Ki to oule ar mwa, Zezi Garson Bondie Treo? Mo pran Bondie pou temwin, mo sipliy twa, pa fatig mwa.”"
Mark5:8 Parski Zezi ti finn dir li, “Twa, move lespri, sort dan sa boug la.”"
Mark5:9 Zezi dimann li, “Twa ki to ete?” Li reponn, “Mo enn lezion parski nou boukou.”"
Mark5:10 Li sipliy Zezi pa avoy zot dan enn lot landrwa.
Mark5:11 Lor flan montagn, ti ena enn gran troupo koson ki ti pe manze."
Mark5:12 Bann move lespri la sipliy Zezi, “Avoy nou dan bann koson, permet nou rant dan zot.”"
Mark5:13 Li donn bannla permision. Zot sorti, zot rant dan bann koson la. Troupo la deval lapant, tom direk dan lamer. Ti ena apepre demil koson, zot tou ti mor nwaye."
Mark5:14 Bann gardien koson sove-ale; zot fann nouvel dan lavil ek lakanpagn lor saki finn pase. Dimoun galoupe, vinn gete saki finn arive."
Mark5:15 Ler zot ariv kot Zezi, zot trouv sa dimoun ki ti posede la. Samem boug ki ti ena enn larme lespri lor li; li ti pe asize, so linz lor li, so lespri normal; dimoun gagn per, zot gagn sok."
Mark5:16 Bann ki finn trouve, finn rakont zistwar sa posede la ek saki finn ariv bann koson."
Mark5:17 Zot sipliy Zezi kit zot landrwa.
Mark5:18 Letan li pe mont dan bato, boug ki ti posede la, inplor Zezi pou li kapav swiv li."
Mark5:19 Zezi pa les li; li dir li, “Al to lakaz kot to bann fami; rakont zot tou saki Lesegner inn fer pou twa, kouma li finn pitie twa.”"
Mark5:20 Letan li ale, li koumans proklame dan Dekapol tou saki Zezi finn fer pou li. Tou dimoun ti plin ar admirasion."
Mark5:21 Ankor enn fwa, Zezi travers lamer pou al lot kote, enn gro lafoul ti antour li. Li ti dan borlamer."
Mark5:22 Lerla enn sef sinagog ki ti apel Zair vini. Letan li trouv Zezi, li tom azenou devan li."
Mark5:23 Li sipliy Zezi, li inplor li, “Ayo, Zezi, mo tifi pre pou mor; vini, poz lame lor li, sa pou sov li, li pou viv.”"
Mark5:24 Zezi al avek li. Enn gran lafoul ti pe swiv li. Dimoun ti pe pouse.
Mark5:25 Ti ena la enn fam ki ti ena enn lemorazi depi douz-an.
Mark5:26 Li finn soufer anba lame boukou dokter ki finn fer li depans tou so kas dan vid; letansa so maladi ti vinn pli grav.
Mark5:27 Repitasion Zezi ti finn ariv ziska madam la. Li rant dan lafoul, li pas par deryer Zezi, li tous so linz."
Mark5:28 Dan so latet li ti pe dir, “Si selman mo reysi tous so linz, mo pou geri.”"
Mark5:29 Enn sel kout, so lemorazi arete. Li santi klerman dan so lekor ki so maladi finn kit li."
Mark5:30 Anmemtan Zezi santi enn lafors ki finn sort dan so lekor. Li vire, li demande, “Kisannla finn tous mo linz?”"
Mark5:31 So bann disip dir li, “To pa trouve lafoul pe pouse, to demande, kisannla finn tous twa?”"
Mark5:32 Li vire, li gete pou kone kisannla finn fer sa?"
Mark5:33 Madam la gagn per, li tranble; li kone ki finn ariv li; li vini, li tom azenou devan Zezi, li dir li tou laverite."
Mark5:34 Zezi dir li, “Mo tifi, to lafwa finn sov twa; al anpe; to finn gagn to gerizon.”"
Mark5:35 Li ti ankor pe koze, kan dimoun ki sorti lakaz sef sinagog la vinn donn nouvel, “To tifi finn mor; pou kifer bizin kontigne deranz Met la?”"
Mark5:36 Zezi pa pran kont zot koze; li dir sef sinagog, “Pa trakase, nek krwar.”"
Mark5:37 Li pa les personn swiv li apart Pier, Zak ek so frer Zan."
Mark5:38 Zot rant dan lakaz sef sinagog; Zezi trouv enn gran deboulman, ena pe plore, ena pe gagn kriz."
Mark5:39 Letan li rantre, li dir bann dimoun, “Kifer zot azite koumsa? Kifer zot plore? Zanfan la pa finn mor, li pe dormi.”"
Mark5:40 Bannla riy li. Zezi met zot tou deor; li gard zis papa ek mama zanfan la ek sa trwa ki ti vinn ar li la; li rant dan lasam kot zanfan la ti ete.
Mark5:41 Li trap lame zanfan la, li dir li, “Talita koum,” - kivedir, “Zennfi, mo dir twa, leve.”"
Mark5:42 Deswit tifi la leve, li koumans marse (li ti ena douz-an). Tou dimoun res bet."
Mark5:43 Zezi donn zot lord pa les personn kone. Li dir zot, “Donn tifi la manze.”"
Mark6:1 Zezi kit sa landrwa la, li retourn dan vilaz kot li ti grandi; so bann disip ti pe swiv li."
Mark6:2 Zour saba li koumans ansegne dan sinagog. Tou seki ti pe ekout li, ti inpresione. Zot dir, “Kot li finn aprann tou sa bann koze la? Kot li finn gagn sa kalite sazes la? Kot li finn gagn pouvwar pou fer sa kalite mirak la ar so lame?"
Mark6:3 Pa limem sarpantie, garson Marie, frer Zak, Zoze, Zid ek Simon? Pa so bann ser mem ki res isi dan landrwa?” Zot ti skandalize par so manier."
Mark6:4 Zezi dir zot, “Enn profet pou gagn rekonesans partou exsepte dan landrwa kot li finn ne, dan so fami ek dan so prop lakaz.”"
Mark6:5 Akoz samem, li pa ti kapav fer okenn mirak dan sa landrwa la; li ti zis kapav poz so lame lor detrwa malad, e li ti geri zot."
Mark6:6 Zezi ti soke ki zot pa ti ena lafwa. Apre sa, li ti fer enn letour bann vilaz dan lezanviron, li ti kontigne ansegne."
Mark6:7 Li apel Ledouz; li koumans avoy zot de par de. Li donn zot pouvwar lor bann move lespri.
Mark6:8 Li ordonn zot pa sarye nanye kan zot ale, apar enn baton, pa pran dipin, ni sak, ni kas dan pos."
Mark6:9 Met sandalet, me pa pran okenn linz resanz."
Mark6:10 Li dir zot, “Kan zot rant dan enn lakaz, res labamem ziska zot kit landrwa la."
Mark6:11 Si dan enn landrwa dimoun refiz resevwar zot ek refiz ekout zot, sakouy bien lapousier anba zot lipie, kan zot kit bannla, sa pou enn temwagnaz kont sa bann dimoun la.”"
Mark6:12 Bann disip ale, zot proklame ki dimoun bizin sanz zot leker."
Mark6:13 Zot sas boukou demon, zot fer lonksion delwil lor bann malad e bannla ti trouv zot gerizon."
Mark6:14 Lerwa Erod finn tann koz Zezi, parski so nom ti bien popiler, bannla ti pe dir, limem Zan Batis ki finn resisite parmi bann mor, akoz samem li ena sa bann pouvwar la."
Mark6:15 Ena ti pe dir “Eli, sa.” Lezot ti pe dir, “Li enn profet kouma bann profet letan lontan.”"
Mark6:16 Letan Erod finn tann sa, li dir, “Mo finn sot likou Zan, ala li finn resisite.”"
Mark6:17 Anrealite, Erod limem finn avoy dimoun trap Zan; zot atas li, zot met li dan prizon. Sa ti arive parski Erod ti finn marye avek Erodiad ki ti fam so frer Filip."
Mark6:18 Zan ti dir Erod, “To pa gagn drwa pran fam to frer.”"
Mark6:19 Akoz samem Erodiad ti deteste Zan e li ti anvi touy li. Selman li pa ti gagn lokazion,"
Mark6:20 parski Erod ti per Zan. Li ti kone Zan ti enn dimoun drwat e sin. Erod ti pe protez li; sak fwa kan Erod ti tann li koze, li ti anbarase me selman li ti kontan ekout li."
Mark6:21 Enn zour, enn bon lokazion prezante. Zour so laniverser, Erod ti donn enn gran festin pou so bann konseye, so bann sef militer ek bann gran misie dan Galile."
Mark6:22 Tifi Erodiad rantre, danse. Erod ek tou so bann invite ti bien kontan. Lerwa dir tifi la, “Demann mwa saki to anvi, mo pou donn twa.”"
Mark6:23 Li fer enn serman ar tifi la, “Tou saki to demande, mo pou donn twa, mem ziska lamwatie mo rwayom.”"
Mark6:24 Tifi la ale, li dir ar so mama, “Ki mo pou demande?” So mama reponn, “Latet Zan Batis.”"
Mark6:25 Li galoupe, li al get lerwa, li dir li, “Mo anvi to donn mwa asterlamem, latet Zan Batis lor enn plato.”"
Mark6:26 Lerwa bien sagrin. Akoz serman li finn fer devan so bann invite, li pa ti anvi perdi fas."
Mark6:27 Deswit, lerwa avoy enn gard. Li donn li lord amenn latet Zan Batis. Gard la ale, li sot latet Zan Batis dan kaso,"
Mark6:28 e li amenn latet la lor enn plato; li donn li tifi la; tifi la donn latet la so mama.
Mark6:29 Kan so bann disip tann sa, zot vini, zot pran so lekor, zot met li dan tonbo."
Mark6:30 Bann apot rasanble otour Zezi. Zot rakont li tou saki zot finn fer e tou saki zot finn ansegne.
Mark6:31 Li dir zot, “Vinn avek mwa dan enn landrwa trankil kot nou pou tousel; repoz zot inpe.” Anfet, ti ena boukou dimoun ti pe ale-vini; zot pa ti mem gagn letan pou manz enn bouse manze."
Mark6:32 Zot pran bato pou al dan enn landrwa retire kot zot pou tousel.
Mark6:33 Boukou dimoun ki ti trouv zot ale, ti rekonet zot; depi boukou lavil, dimoun galoupe pou al bar zot avan zot arive."
Mark6:34 Letan Zezi debarke, li trouv enn gran lafoul; so leker kase parski zot ti kouma bann mouton san berze. Li koumans ansegn zot boukou kiksoz."
Mark6:35 Letan ti pe pase, bann disip koste pre ar Zezi, zot dir li, “Nou dan enn landrwa retire e li deza bien tar."
Mark6:36 Les zot ale, koumsa zot va kapav al dan bann vilaz lakanpagn pou aste kiksoz pou manze.”"
Mark6:37 Li reponn zot, “Donn bannla manze, zotmem.” Zot dir li, “Kot nou pou al gagn dipin valer de-san zourne travay pou donn zot manze?”"
Mark6:38 Li dir zot, “Komie dipin zot ena? Al gete.” Bannla pran linformasion, zot reponn li, zis sink dipin ek de pwason."
Mark6:39 Apre sa li donn zot lord fer bann dimoun la asiz angroup lor gazon.
Mark6:40 Zot asiz anba par group san ek sinkant.
Mark6:41 Zezi pran sink dipin ek de pwason la; li lev so lizie ver lesiel, li fer enn benediksion, li kas dipin la, li donn so bann disip pouki bannla fer distribision dan lafoul; li partaz de pwason la osi ar zot tou."
Mark6:42 Tou dimoun finn rasazie ar manze.
Mark6:43 Ar bout dipin ek pwason ki finn reste, zot ranpli douz panie."
Mark6:44 Antou sink-mil zom ti manze.
Mark6:45 Apre sa, Zezi obliz bann disip pran bato pou al lot kote dan Betsaida; letan sa, li pou fer lafoul ale."
Mark6:46 Kan li finn fini fer zot tou ale, li mont lor montagn, li al priye."
Mark6:47 Aswar vini, bato ti omilie lamer, Zezi ti tou sel ater."
Mark6:48 Letan li trouv zot pe rame avek boukou difikilte parski divan ti kontrer, ver kat-rer sink-er dimatin, li mars lor lamer, li vini. Li ti anvi pas devan zot."
Mark6:49 Ler bannla trouv li pe mars lor lamer, zot ti krwar enn fantom; zot koumans kriye."
Mark6:50 Zot tou ti trouv li; enn lafreyer pran zot. Lerla li pran laparol, li dir zot, “Pa traka, momem sa, pa gagn per.”"
Mark6:51 Kouma li mont dan bato avek zot, divan tonbe; zot res bet."
Mark6:52 Avredir, zot pa ti finn konpran nanye lor mirak dipin; zot leker ti kouma ros."
Mark6:53 Kan zot finn fini traverse, zot ariv pre lor rivaz Zenezaret, zot amar zot bato."
Mark6:54 Kouma zot sorti dan bato, deswit dimoun fini rekonet Zezi."
Mark6:55 Zot sorti partou kote, zot galoupe, zot koumans sarye bann malad lor brankar; zot al zwenn Zezi kot zot ti tann dir li ete."
Mark6:56 Partou kot li ale, dan vilaz, dan lavil, dan lakanpagn, zot ti amenn bann malad lor laplas piblik; zot sipliy li pouki zot kapav tous zis bout so linz; tou dimoun ki ti tous li, ti gagn zot gerizon."
Mark7:1 Bann Farizien ek detrwa dokter lalwa ki sorti depi Zerizalem antour Zezi.
Mark7:2 Zot remarke ki detrwa so bann disip ti pe manz dipin avek lame sal, savedir, zot pa finn lav zot lame."
Mark7:3 Anefe, bann Farizien parey kouma tou Zwif, ti bizin bien lav lame avan manze, pou respekte tradision zot gran dimoun."
Mark7:4 Kan zot sorti dan enn landrwa piblik, zot bizin lav zot, apre zot manze. Ena enn pake tradision koumsa ki zot finn resevwar e ki zot bien respekte, par exanp zot lav bann koup, brok, deksi."
Mark7:5 Alors bann Farizien ek bann dokter lalwa dimann li, “Pou ki rezon to bann disip pa mars dapre tradision nou bann gran dimoun? Pou kifer zot manz dipin ar lame sal?”"
Mark7:6 Zezi reponn zot, “Izai ti ena rezon kan li ti profetiz lor zot, bann ipokrit, kan li ti ekrir dan so liv, ‘Sa lepep la ador mwa zis ar so labous me so leker bien-bien lwin ar mwa."
Mark7:7 Pou nanye zot ador mwa parski zot fer zot lalwa pas pou lalwa Bondie.’
Mark7:8 Zot met lalwa Bondie dan enn kwin me zot gard tradision bann imin.”
Mark7:9 Zezi kontigne, “Zot bien malin kan bizin detourn lalwa Bondie pou favoriz zot tradision."
Mark7:10 Moiz ti bien dir, ‘Respekte to papa, respekte to mama,’ e ‘Dimoun ki maltret so papa, ek so mama, li merit lamor.’"
Mark7:11 Me zot, zot dir, si enn dimoun deklar ar so papa ek so mama, koudme ki li ti pou kapav donn zot, li Korbann - savedir li enn ofrand sakre,"
Mark7:12 alors li gagn drwa pa donn okenn led so papa, so mama."
Mark7:13 Zot diminie pwa Parol Bondie zis pou kapav transmet zot bann tradision; zot fer boukou kiksoz dan sa manier la.”
Mark7:14 Li apel lafoul ankor, li dir zot, “Ekout mwa bien zot tou, sey konpran sa ki mo pe dir."
Mark7:15 Tou seki dan lanatir e ki rant dan lekor enn dimoun, pa kapav fer li vinn inpir, selman seki sorti dan so lekor, sa kapav fer li vinn inpir. ["
Mark7:16 Si zot ena zorey pou ekoute, ekout bien! ]”"
Mark7:17 Letan li kit lafoul, li rant lakaz, so bann disip pe poz li kestion lor sa parabol la."
Mark7:18 Li dir zot, “Kouma zot ousi, zot kapav bet koumsa? Kouma zot pa konpran ki tou seki dan lanatir e rant dan enn dimoun pa kapav fer li vinn inpir,"
Mark7:19 parski li pa rant dan so leker me dan so vant apre so lekor eliminn li?” Par sa parol la Zezi ti deklare ki tou manze prop.
Mark7:20 Li kontigne, “Seki sorti depi andan, samem ki fer dimoun vinn inpir."
Mark7:21 Andan, dan leker, lamem tousort kalite move lide sorti: move lavi, kokin, touye,"
Mark7:22 adilter, groker, fer vis, zwe malin, lamizman, met lizie, zoure, vantar, divage."
Mark7:23 Tou seki move sort dan leker dimoun; samem ki fer li vinn inpir.”
Mark7:24 Kan Zezi sorti la, li al dan rezion Tir. Li rant dan enn lakaz, li pa ti anvi personn kone, me li pa ti kapav kontign kasiet."
Mark7:25 Me kouma enn madam ki so tifi ti ena move lespri lor li tann koz Zezi, li vini, li tom azenou devan li."
Mark7:26 Sa madam la pa ti dan larelizion Zwif; li ti enn Siro-Fenisyenn. Li dimann Zezi tir demon lor so tifi.
Mark7:27 Zezi reponn li, “Les bann zanfan manze avan, parski li pa bon pran dipin zanfan pou zet ar tilisien.”"
Mark7:28 Madam la reponn, “Wi Segner, me selman tilisien anba latab, manz bout dipin ki bann zanfan les tonbe.”"
Mark7:29 Alor Zezi dir li, “Akoz sa parol to finn koze la, ale, demon finn kit to tifi.”"
Mark7:30 Kan li ariv kot li, li trouv so zanfan alonze lor lili, demon finn fini kit li."
Mark7:31 Apre sa, Zezi kit rezion Tir ankor enn fwa, li pas par Sidon; li pran direksion lamer Galile, li travers Dekapol."
Mark7:32 Zot amenn enn sourd devan li, li ti osi gagn difikilte pou koze; zot sipliy Zezi poz lame lor li."
Mark7:33 Zezi pran li, amenn li dan enn kwin, lwin ar lafoul. Li met so ledwa dan so zorey; li tous so lalang ar so lakras."
Mark7:34 Li lev so lizie ver lesiel li pous enn soupir, li dir li “Efata!” -sakivedir, “Ouver-twa!”"
Mark7:35 Deswit so zorey ouver, so lalang delarge, li koz normal."
Mark7:36 Zezi donn zot lord pa dir nanye personn; me plis li donn zot lord, plis zot fann nouvel lor li partou."
Mark7:37 Zot ti bien-bien inpresione; zot tou ti pe dir, “Li finn fer boukou mervey! Mem bann sourd tande, bann miye koze.”"
Mark8:1 Enn lot fwa, ti ena ankor enn gro lafoul. Zot pa ti ena nanye pou manze. Zezi apel so bann disip, li dir zot,"
Mark8:2 “Mo leker fermal kan mo get sa lafoul la. Sa fer trwa zour ki zot ar mwa e zot pena nanye pou manze.
Mark8:3 Si mo dir zot al zot lakaz lestoma vid, zot pou gagn febles dan sime parski ena ki sorti bien lwin.”"
Mark8:4 So bann disip dir li, “Kot pou kapav gagn dipin pou ranpli zot vant dan enn landrwa dezer koumsa?”"
Mark8:5 Li dimann zot, “Komie dipin zot ena?” Zot dir li, “Set.”"
Mark8:6 Li fer lafoul asiz anba; li pran touleset dipin, li rann gras, li kas bann dipin la, li donn so bann disip pouki bannla fer lapartaz e bannla partaz avek lafoul."
Mark8:7 Ti ena osi detrwa tipwason; li beni zot e li dimann bannla partaz sa osi.
Mark8:8 Bannla manze ziska zot vant plin; apre zot ti ramas set korbey ranpli ar tibout dipin.
Mark8:9 Ti ena apepre kat mil dimoun. Apre li dir zot al lakaz.
Mark8:10 Zis apre li mont lor bato avek so bann disip e li al paraz Dalmanouta.
Mark8:11 Bann Farizien vini; zot koumans diskit ar Zezi; pou teste li, zot dimann li enn sign ki sorti depi lao dan lesiel."
Mark8:12 Li pous enn gran soupir, apre li reponn, “Kifer sa zenerasion la pe rod enn sign? Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, sa zenerasion la pa pou gagn okenn sign.”"
Mark8:13 Lerla li kit zot, li remont dan bato, li al lot kote."
Mark8:14 Bann disip ti bliye amenn dipin. Ti ena zis enn sel dipin avek zot dan bato.
Mark8:15 Zezi averti zot, “Get bien, fer atansion ar levin bann Farizien ek levin Erod.”"
Mark8:16 Bann disip ti pe diskite ant zot parski zot pa ti ena dipin.
Mark8:17 Zezi ti remarke seki ti pe pase. Li dir zot, “Kifer zot pe diskite akoz zot pena dipin? Zot lizie pankor ouver? Zot pankor konpran? Koumsa zot leker dir?"
Mark8:18 Zot ena lizie, selman zot pa trouv kler; zot ena zorey, selman zot pa tande? Zot pa rapel?"
Mark8:19 Kan mo ti kas sink dipin pou sink mil dimoun, komie panie ranpli ar bout dipin zot ti ramase?” Zot dir li, “Douz.”"
Mark8:20 “Kan mo ti kas set dipin pou kat mil dimoun, komie panie ranpli ar bout dipin zot ti ramase?” Bannla reponn, “Set.”"
Mark8:21 Li dir zot, “Zot pankor konpran mem?”"
Mark8:22 Zot ariv Betsaida. Dimoun amenn enn aveg ar Zezi; zot sipliy Zezi tous li.
Mark8:23 Zezi trap so lame, li amenn li andeor vilaz. Li met inpe lakras lor so lizie, li poz lame lor li apre li dimann li, “Eski to trouv kiksoz?”"
Mark8:24 Areg la lev so latet, li dir, “Mo trouv dimoun me zot koumadir bann pie ki pe marse.”"
Mark8:25 Zezi poz lame ankor enn fwa lor so lizie. Lerla li arive trouv bien, so lizie revinn normal e li trouv tou bien kler."
Mark8:26 Zezi fer li al so lakaz, e li dir li, “Pa pas par sa vilaz la.”"
Mark8:27 Zezi pran direksion bann vilaz Sezare-Filip avek so bann disip. Dan sime, li dimann so bann disip, “Ki bann dimoun pe dir lor mwa?”"
Mark8:28 Zot reponn li, “Ena dir to Zan Batis, ena dir tomem Eli, lezot pe dir to enn parmi bann profet.”"
Mark8:29 Me li dir zot, “E zot, ki zot dir mo ete?” Pier reponn li, “Tomem Lemesi.”"
Mark8:30 Li komann zot pa dir sa personn.
Mark8:31 Apre sa li koumans ansegn zot, fode ki Garson Limanite soufer boukou, ki bann ansien, bann pret, bann dokter lalwa rezet li, touy li, apre sa li pou resisite lor so trwaziem zour."
Mark8:32 Li ti pe koz fran-fran ar zot. Pier amenn li dan enn kwin e koumans menas li.
Mark8:33 Zezi vire, li get so bann disip, li menas Pier; li dir li, “Sorti devan mwa, Satan, parski to pena lespri Bondie me lespri dimoun.”"
Mark8:34 Li apel lafoul ek so bann disip e li dir zot, “Si kikenn anvi mars lor mo sime pou swiv mwa, li bizin bliye limem, pran so lakrwa, swiv mwa."
Mark8:35 Dimoun ki anvi sov so lavi, pou perdi li; saki perdi so lavi akoz mwa ek Bonn Nouvel, pou sov li."
Mark8:36 Kiserti enn dimoun gagn lemonn antie si li ariv perdi so lavi?
Mark8:37 Ki kiksoz enn dimoun pa pou fer pou sap so lavi?
Mark8:38 Si kikenn, dan sa zenerasion adilter ek peser la, gagn onte akoz mwa ek mo parol, Garson Limanite, li osi pou ont li, kan li pou vinn dan laglwar so Papa ek bann anz ki sin.”"
Mark9:1 Zezi dir zot ankor, “Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, ena detrwa isi ki pa pou konn lamor tanki zot pa trouv Rwayom Bondie desann avek pwisans.”"
Mark9:2 Sis zour apre, Zezi pran zis Pier, Zak ek Zan tousel avek li e li amenn zot lao lor montagn. Li transfigire devan zot."
Mark9:3 So linz vinn blan-blan-blan, enn kalite blan ki okenn dobi lor later pankor kapav reysi ariv fer."
Mark9:4 Zot trouv Eli ek Moiz paret devan zot. Bannla ti pe koz ar Zezi.
Mark9:5 Alor Pier rant dan konversasion, li dir ar Zezi, “Rabi, li bien bon ki nou isi avek twa; anou ranz trwa latant, enn pou twa, enn pou Moiz ek enn pou Eli.”"
Mark9:6 Li pa ti kone ki pou dir telman zot ti finn sezi.
Mark9:7 Lerla enn niaz rekouver zot e enn lavwa dan niaz dir, “Samem mo Garson ki mo bien kontan, ekout li.”"
Mark9:8 Enn ti moman apre, kan zot get kat kote, zot pa trouv personn, res zis Zezi tousel."
Mark9:9 Ler zot pe desann lor montagn, Zezi rekomann zot pa rakont personn seki zot finn trouve tanki Garson Limanite pa ankor resisite parmi bann mor."
Mark9:10 Zot gard sa parol la dan zot leker, mem si zot ti pe dimann zotmem, “Ki savedir ‘Resisite parmi bann mor’?”"
Mark9:11 Apre bann disip dimann li, “Kifer bann dokter lalwa dir fode Eli revini avan?”"
Mark9:12 Li reponn zot, “Premie dabor, Eli pe vini pou dres tou e met tou dan lord; alor kifer finn ekrir ki Garson Limanite pou soufer boukou e pou gagn maltrete?”"
Mark9:13 Li kontigne, “Eli finn vini, zot finn fer tou saki zot ti anvi avek li, dapre seki ti finn ekrir lor li.”"
Mark9:14 Kan zot rezwenn lezot disip, zot trouv enn gro lafoul pe antour bannla; bann dokter lalwa ti pe diskit ar zot."
Mark9:15 Kouma lafoul trouv Zezi, zot exsite. Zot galoupe pou akeyir li."
Mark9:16 Li dimann zot, “Ki zot pe diskite ar bannla?”"
Mark9:17 Enn boug dan lafoul reponn li, “Met, mo finn amenn mo garson ar ou, li posede par enn lespri ki anpes li koze."
Mark9:18 Sak fwa lespri la trap li, li fwet li anba, zanfan la kime, li grins so ledan, li redi. Mo finn dimann ou disip pous sa lespri la, selman zot pa ase for.”"
Mark9:19 Zezi reponn zot, “Sa zenerasion la, enn zenerasion ki pena lafwa; ziska kan mo pou res ar zot? Ziska kan mo pou siport zot? Amenn li ar mwa.”"
Mark9:20 Zot amenn li ar Zezi; kouma lespri la trouv li, li fer zanfan la rant antrans, li tom anba, li fer li roule, li kime."
Mark9:21 Zezi dimann so papa, “Depi komie letan li gagn sa?” Li reponn, “Depi li zanfan."
Mark9:22 Plizir fwa, lespri la finn zet li dan dife ek dan dilo pou fini li; si ou kapav fer kiksoz pou nou, sap nou, pran par dan nou maler.”"
Mark9:23 Zezi dir li, “To pe dir si ou kapav? Be tou kiksoz posib pou dimoun ki ena lafwa.”"
Mark9:24 Deswit papa garson la kriye, “Mo krwar; ed mwa, mo lafwa pa ase gran.”"
Mark9:25 Kan Zezi trouv enn latroupman, li menas move lespri la, li dir li, “Twa, lespri ki anpes koze, ki anpes tande, mo komann twa, sort dan sa zanfan la, pa revinn ankor ar li.”"
Mark9:26 Lespri la kriye, li sakouy-sakouy zanfan la, li sorti, li ale. Zanfan la pa bouze, li ti parey kouma enn dimoun mor. Dimoun dir li finn fini mor."
Mark9:27 Zezi trap so lame, fer li leve, li deboute."
Mark9:28 Letan Zezi finn rant lakaz, bann disip ris li enn kote, zot dimann li, “Kifer nou pa finn kapav pous sa lespri la, nou?”"
Mark9:29 Li dir zot, “Zis ar lapriyer ki sa kalite lespri la kapav sorti.”"
Mark9:30 Zot sorti landrwa kot zot ti ete, zot travers Galile. Zezi pa ti anvi ki dimoun konn sa."
Mark9:31 Li ti pe kontigne ansegn so bann disip e li ti pe dir zot, “Zot pou trap Garson Limanite, zot pou livre li dan lame bann dimoun; zot pou touy li, me trwa zour apre so lamor, li pou resisite.”"
