Mark9:32 Zot pa ti konpran saki li ti pe rod dir; zot ti gagn per poz li kestion.
Mark9:33 Zot ariv Kafarnaom; kouma zot rant lakaz, Zezi dimann zot, “Ki zot ti pe diskite lor sime?”"
Mark9:34 Zot tou, zot res trankil parski lor sime, zot ti pe diskite for-for pou kone kisannla pli gran."
Mark9:35 Li asize, li apel Ledouz, li dir zot, “Si kikenn anvi vinn premie, fode li vinn dernie e li bizin vinn serviter tou dimoun.”"
Mark9:36 Lerla li pran enn ti zanfan, li met li dan milie, li pran li dan so lebra, apre li dir zot,"
Mark9:37 “Dimoun ki akey enn sa bann ti zanfan la, lor mo nom, li pe akeyir momem; e dimoun ki akeyir mwa, pa mwa li pe akeyir me seki finn avoy mwa la.”"
Mark9:38 Zan dir li, “Met, nou finn trouv kikenn servi to nom pou pous enn demon; nou finn sey anpes li parski li pa mars ar nou.”"
Mark9:39 Zezi dir, “Pa anpes li; dimoun ki servi mo nom pou fer enn mirak, pa kapav mal parl mwa apre;"
Mark9:40 Saki pa kont nou, ar nou."
Mark9:41 Dimoun ki donn zot enn ver dilo, lor mo nom, parski zot krwar dan Lekris, laverite, laverite mo dir zot, li pa pou perdi so rekonpans.”"
Mark9:42 “Dimoun ki fer enn sa bann ti zanfan ki krwar dan mwa la tonbe, ti a preferab atas enn gro ros otour so likou e zet li dan lamer."
Mark9:43 Si to lame fer twa tonbe, koup li; preferab to mank enn lame kan to rant dan lavi, ki to ena de lame dan lanfer, la kot dife napa tegn. [La,"
Mark9:44 lever ki detrir lekor pa mor, ek dife pa tegn zame ]"
Mark9:45 Si to lipie fer twa tonbe, koup li; preferab to mank enn lipie kan to rant dan lavi, ki to al avek to de lipie dan lanfer. [La,"
Mark9:46 lever ki detrir lekor pa mor, ek dife pa tegn zame ]"
Mark9:47 Si to lizie fer twa tonbe, aras li; preferab to mank enn lizie kan to rant dan Rwayom Bondie, ki to rant avek to de lizie dan lanfer,"
Mark9:48 la, kot lever pa mor e kot dife pa tegn."
Mark9:49 Nou tou, nou pou sale ar dife."
Mark9:50 Disel enn bon zafer, sa, selman si disel finn perdi so gou, ki ou pou servi pou asezone? Met disel dan zot lavi, viv dan lape avek tou dimoun.”"
Mark10:1 Zezi leve, li al dan paraz Lazide, lot kote larivier Zourdin. Ankor enn fwa, lafoul ti antour li. Kouma li abitie fer, li kontign ansegn zot."
Mark10:2 Bann Farizien koste ar li. Zot ti pe rod instal li, alor zot dimann li si lalwa permet enn mari ranvway so fam."
Mark10:3 Li reponn zot, “Ki komannman Moiz finn donn zot?”"
Mark10:4 Zot reponn, “Moiz permet nou servi enn papie avan met li deor.”"
Mark10:5 Zezi dir zot, “Moiz finn ekrir sa lalwa la akoz zot leker dir."
Mark10:6 Depi komansman kreasion, Bondie finn kre zot zom ek fam."
Mark10:7 Akoz samem enn dimoun pou kit so papa ek so mama.
Mark10:8 Toulede pou form enn sel lekor; koumsa zot nepli de, me enn sel."
Mark10:9 Fode pa dimoun separ seki Bondie finn met ansam.”
Mark10:10 Letan zot rant lakaz, bann disip dimann li enn leklersisman lor sa problem la."
Mark10:11 Li dir zot, “Zom ki ranvway so fam pou remarye avek enn lot, li komet adilter."
Mark10:12 Tou fam ki kit so mari pou remarye avek enn lot, li ousi, li komet adilter.”"
Mark10:13 Bann dimoun amenn bann tizanfan pouki Zezi poz lame lor zot me so bann disip farous zot.
Mark10:14 Zezi agase, li dir zot, “Les bann ti zanfan vinn ar mwa, napa anpes zot parski Rwayom Bondie pou dimoun ki parey kouma zot."
Mark10:15 Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, dimoun ki pa akeyir Rwayom Bondie parey kouma enn ti zanfan, napa pou rant dan so Rwayom.”"
Mark10:16 Li may zot dan so lebra, li poz lame lor zot, e li beni zot."
Mark10:17 Letan Zezi ti pe sorti pou ale, enn dimoun galoupe, vini, tom dan so lipie e dimann li, “Met, twa ki bon, ki mo bizin fer pou gagn lavi eternel aneritaz?”"
Mark10:18 Lerla Zezi reponn li, “Kifer to dir mwa bon? Personn pa bon, zis Bondie tousel ki bon."
Mark10:19 To konn bann komannman: pa touy dimoun, pa viv dan ladilter, pa kokin, pa fer fos temwagnaz, pa fer ditor to prosin, onor to papa ek to mama.”"
Mark10:20 Li dir Zezi, “Met, depi mo zenn mo viv dapre lalwa.”"
Mark10:21 Zezi get li bien, li finn bien apresie li; alor li reponn li, “To mank enn sel kiksoz: ale, vann tou to dibien, donn dimoun mizer, lerla to pou gagn enn gran trezor dan lesiel, apre sa vini, swiv mwa.”"
Mark10:22 Dimoun la so figir sanze letan li tann sa parol la, li ale leker lour parski li ti ena boukou dibien."
Mark10:23 Zezi vire, get partou, apre sa li dir so bann disip, “Bien difisil pou dimoun ki ena gran-gran dibien pou rant dan Rwayom Bondie.”"
Mark10:24 Bann disip ti inpe soke avek so parol; Zezi kontign koze, li dir, “Bann zanfan, li bien difisil pou dimoun ris rant dan Rwayom Bondie;"
Mark10:25 Li pli fasil pou enn samo pas par trou enn zegwi ki pou enn risar rant dan Rwayom Bondie.”
Mark10:26 Zot ankor plis soke, sakenn pe dir ar so kamarad, “Be alor, kisannla pou reysi sove?”"
Mark10:27 Zezi get zot fran dan zot lizie, li dir zot, “Pou dimoun li inposib me pa pou Bondie, parski pou Bondie tou kiksoz posib.”"
Mark10:28 Pier koumans dir, “Be nou, nou finn kit tou pou swiv twa.”"
Mark10:29 Zezi reponn, “Laverite, laverite mo pe dir zot, personn pa pou kit so lakaz, so frer, so ser, so mama, so papa, so zanfan, so later, akoz mwa ek Bonn Nouvel,"
Mark10:30 san ki li gagn, asterlamem, san fwa plis: lakaz, frer ek ser, mama ek zanfan, later, avek so persekision, e lavi eternel dan lot lemonn."
Mark10:31 Saki premie pou vinn dernie, saki dernie pou vinn premie.”"
Mark10:32 Zot ti lor sime pou mont Zerizalem; Zezi ti pe mars devan; zot ti boulverse e bann saki ti pe swiv li ti pe gagn per. Li pran Ledouz enn kote ankor enn fwa, li koumans rakont zot saki pou ariv li."
Mark10:33 “Gete! Nou pe mont Zerizalem, bannla pou livre Garson Limanite devan bann gran pret ek bann dokter lalwa, zot pou kondann li amor e zot pou les bann payin ziz li."
Mark10:34 Zot pou boufonn li, zot pou kras lor li, zot pou fwet li, zot pou touy li, me lor trwaziem zour li pou resisite.”"
Mark10:35 De garson Zebede, Zak ek Zan, koste ar li, zot dir li, “Met, nou ti pou bien kontan si to ti kapav fer nou enn faver.”"
Mark10:36 Li dimann zot, “Ki zot ti anvi mo fer pou zot?”"
Mark10:37 Zot reponn li, “Permet nou asiz enn dan to kote drwat, lot dan to kote gos kan to rant dan to laglwar.”"
Mark10:38 Zezi dir zot, “Zot pa kone ki zot pe dimande. Eski zot kapav bwar dan koup ki mo pou bwar, batiz dan batem ki mo pou batize?”"
Mark10:39 Zot dir li, “Wi nou kapav.” Zezi reponn zot, “Koup ki mo pou bwar, zot pou bwar ek batem ki mo pou batize, zot pou batize."
Mark10:40 Me pou kone kisannla pou asiz dan mo kote drwat ek mo kote gos, sa pa depann lor mwa me li finn deza prepare pou sertin dimoun.”"
Mark10:41 Letan sa dis la tann sa, zot agase avek Zak ek Zan."
Mark10:42 Zezi apel zot tou, li dir zot, “Zot kone tou seki finn gagn pozision otorite dan bann nasion, zot fer dominer e zot bann dirizan montre zot pouvwar."
Mark10:43 Li pa parey koumsa parmi zot. Seki anvi pran grander parmi zot, li bizin okip plas serviter"
Mark10:44 Seki anvi vinn premie, li bizin vinn esklav tou dimoun."
Mark10:45 Mazine ki Garson Limanite pa finn vini pouki dimoun servi li, me pou li servi dimoun e donn so lavi kouma enn ranson pou tou dimoun.”"
Mark10:46 Zot ariv dan Zeriko; zis kouma li ti pe kit Zeriko avek so bann disip ek enn gro lafoul, Bartime, garson Time, enn mandian aveg, ti pe asize dan bor sime."
Mark10:47 Letan li aprann ki Zezi ki sorti Nazaret la ti pe pase, li koumans kriye for-for, li dir, “Ayo, Zezi, Garson David, pitie mwa.”"
Mark10:48 Bannla donn li lord res trankil, me li kriye ankor pli for, “Garson David, pitie mwa.”"
Mark10:49 Zezi arete, li dir “Apel li.” Zot apel aveg la, zot dir li, “Kouraz, dibout, li pe apel twa.”"
Mark10:50 Li zet so palto, li fransi, li vinn devan Zezi."
Mark10:51 Zezi dir li, “Ki to oule mo fer pou twa?” Aveg la reponn, “Rabouni, fer mwa trouv kler.”"
Mark10:52 Zezi dir li, “Ale, to lafwa finn sov twa.” Deswit li trouv kler e li swiv Zezi."
Mark11:1 Kan zot ariv pre ar Zerizalem, parti Betfaze ek Betani, akote kolinn Pie Zoliv, Zezi avoy de disip e"
Mark11:2 li dir zot, “Al dan vilaz ki devan zot; kouma zot ariv laba, zot pou trouv enn ti-bourik ki atase; personn pa finn deza mont li, delarg li, amenn li isi."
Mark11:3 Si kikenn dimann zot, ‘Kifer zot pe fer sa?’ nek dir, ‘Lesegner bien bizin bourik la; kouma li fini, li pou retourn li.’ ”"
Mark11:4 Zot ale e zot trouv ti bourik atase, deor lor lari, pre ar enn laport. Kouma zot pe delarg li,"
Mark11:5 detrwa dimoun ki ti dan paraz dir zot, “Ki zot pe fer, kifer zot pe delarg sa ti bourik la?”"
Mark11:6 Zot reponn bannla parey kouma Zezi ti dir zot, lerla bannla les zot trankil."
Mark11:7 Zot amenn ti bourik la ar Zezi; zot zet zot linz lor li; Zezi asiz lor so ledo.
Mark11:8 Enn parti dimoun ti pe tal zot linz anba, enn lot bann ti pe tal ramo ki zot ti finn al koupe dan karo."
Mark11:9 Bann ki ti pe mars devan e bann ki ti pe swiv par deryer, ti pe kriye, “Ozana! Sa Dimoun ki pe vini lor nom nou Segner, finn beni."
Mark11:10 Regn nou papa David ki pe vini, finn beni, Ozana pli lao dan lesiel.”"
Mark11:11 Zezi rant dan Zerizalem, li pran direksion tanp, li get partou kote; me kouma ti deza tar, li sorti, li al Betani avek Ledouz."
Mark11:12 Landime, letan zot kit Betani, Zezi ti pe gagn fin."
Mark11:13 Depi lwin li trouv enn pie fig kouver ar fey; li aprose pou gete si li trouv kiksoz pou manze. Letan li vinn pre ar li, li pa trouv nanye, ti ena zis feyaz parski pa ti ankor sezon fig."
Mark11:14 Alor li dir sa pie fig la, “Zame ankor personn pou manz to fri!” So bann disip tann sa koze la."
Mark11:15 Letan zot ariv Zerizalem, Zezi al direk dan tanp. Li koumans farous tou bann marsan ek tou bann kliyan ki ti pe fer komers dan tanp, li devir latab bann sanzer-kas anbalao e li ranvers sez bann marsan pizon."
Mark11:16 Li pa les personn mars avek okenn lartik dan tanp.
Mark11:17 Lerla li ansegn zot, li dir, “Eski pa finn ekrir ki pou apel mo lakaz, lakaz lapriyer pou tou bann nasion? Me zot, zot finn fer li vinn enn kavern voler.”"
Mark11:18 Kan sef bann pret ek bann dokter lalwa finn konn sa, zot ti pe rode kouma pou touy li, me zot ti gagn per li parski lafoul ti apresie so lansegnman."
Mark11:19 Kouma koumans fer nwar, Zezi ek so bann disip sorti andeor lavil."
Mark11:20 Boner gramatin, letan zot pe marse dan bor sime, zot trouv pie fig la finn sek ziska so rasinn."
Mark11:21 Pier rapel saki ti finn pase e li dir, “Rabi, get pie fig ki to finn modi la; ala li finn sek.”"
Mark11:22 Zezi reponn zot, “Met to lafwa dan Bondie."
Mark11:23 Laverite mo dir zot, si kikenn dir sa montagn la, ‘Leve, al zet twa dan lamer,’ si li pena dout dan so leker, me lafwa dan saki li pe dir, samem pou arive."
Mark11:24 Akoz samem mo dir zot, tou saki zot dimande dan lapriyer, krwar ki zot finn fini gagn li, e zot pou gagn li."
Mark11:25 Kan zot vinn devan Bondie pou priye, si zot ena kiksoz kont enn dimoun, al pardonn li, pouki zot papa dan lesiel pardonn osi zot bann fot.”"
Mark11:26 [Me si zot pa pardonn lezot, zot Papa ki dan lesiel pa pou pardonn fot ki zot finn fer. ]"
Mark11:27 Ankor enn fwa Zezi ek so bann disip retourn Zerizalem. Zezi ti pe ale-vini dan tanp; sef bann gran pret, bann dokter lalwa ek bann ansien"
Mark11:28 dir li, “Saki to pe fer la, par ki lotorite to pe fer sa? Kisannla finn donn twa lotorite pou fer tousala?”"
Mark11:29 Zezi dir zot, “Mo pou poz zot enn sel kestion, reponn mwa, lerla mo pou dir zot kisannla finn donn mwa pouvwar pou fer tousala."
Mark11:30 Eski batem Zan sorti depi dan lesiel ou swa dimoun ki finn invant sa? Reponn mwa.”
Mark11:31 Zot fer enn korom, zot kalkile, “Si nou reponn ‘Depi dan lesiel,’ li pou dir, ‘Be ki fer alors zot pa finn krwar dan li?’"
Mark11:32 Me eski nou kapav reponn, ‘Dimoun’?” Zot ti gagn per lafoul parski tou dimoun ti konsider Zan kouma enn profet."
Mark11:33 Alor zot dir Zezi, “Nou pa kone.” Lerla Zezi reponn zot, “Mo osi mo pa pou dir zot kot mo pouvwar sorti.”"
Mark12:1 Li koumans koz ar zot an parabol. “Ti ena enn dimoun ki ti plant enn karo rezin; li ranz enn baraz pou antour so karo, li fouy enn trou pou instal so preswar, li ranz enn maray; apre li lwe so karo avek bann meteye e li parti, li ale."
Mark12:2 Letan sezon rekolt arive, li avoy enn serviter al get bann meteye pou rod so par dan karo rezin."
Mark12:3 Bannla trap serviter la, bat li e fer li retourn lame vid."
Mark12:4 Li avoy ankor enn lot serviter; sannla osi, zot kas-kas so latet ar bate e zot zour li."
Mark12:5 Li avoy enn lot serviter ankor; sannala, zot touy li. Apre zot kontign fer parey avek enn kantite lezot serviter. Ena finn gagn bate, ena finn gagn lamor."
Mark12:6 Ti res zis so garson ki li ti bien kontan; andernie li desid avoy li parski li ti pe dir, ‘Bannla pou respekte mo garson.’"
Mark12:7 Bann meteye la fer enn konplo, zot dir, ‘Limem eritie, anou touy li, lerla leritaz pou vinn pou nou.’"
Mark12:8 Zot trap garson la, zot touy li e zot zet li andeor karo."
Mark12:9 Dapre zot, ki propriyeter karo rezin pou fer? Li pou vini, li pou touy bann meteye e li pou donn so karo lezot dimoun."
Mark12:10 Zot pa finn lir dan Lekritir, ‘Ros ki bann mason finn rezete, samem finn vinn ros ki tini tou ros."
Mark12:11 Sa travay Bondie, sa, li enn gran mervey pou nou lizie.’?”"
Mark12:12 Bannla ti pe rod trap li me zot gagn per lafoul. Zot ti finn fini konpran ki Zezi ti pe koz pou zot, letan li ti pe koz an parabol. Apre sa, zot les li, zot ale."
Mark12:13 Zot avoy detrwa Farizien ek Erodien lor Zezi pou vir so koze anbalao.
Mark12:14 Zot vini e zot dir li, “Met, nou kone ki to koz fran, to pa les dimoun inflians twa, to pa ziz dimoun dapre so laparans me to montre sime Bondie dapre laverite; eski dapre lalwa nou bizin pey tax Sezar, wi ou non? Bizin peye, pa bizin peye?”"
Mark12:15 Li kone kouma bannla ipokrit; akoz samem li dir zot, “Pou ki fer zot rod instal mwa? Fer mwa gagn enn pies larzan mo gete.”"
Mark12:16 Zot donn li pies la; apre li dimann zot, “Ki figir ena lor la e ki finn ekrir?” Zot reponn li, “Sezar.”"
Mark12:17 Zezi dir zot, “Rann Sezar seki pou Sezar e rann Bondie seki pou Bondie.” Zot dekonserte."
Mark12:18 Bann Sadisein - enn group dimoun ki pa ti krwar dan rezireksion koste ar Zezi e dimann li,"
Mark12:19 “Met, ala lalwa ki Moiz finn ekrir: si frer enn dimoun mor san ki so madam finn gagn enn zanfan, dimoun la bizin marye ar vev la pou donn enn desandans so frer."
Mark12:20 Ti ena set frer. Premie la finn marye avek enn madam; finn arive li mor san les enn desandan.
Mark12:21 Deziem frer marye ar madam la; li ousi li mor san les desandan; parey pou trwaziem la.
Mark12:22 Okenn frer pa finn les enn desandans. Andernie, madam la mem mor."
Mark12:23 Ler larezireksion pou vini, kisannla pou vinn mari madam la? Touleset finn pran li kouma zot fam.”"
Mark12:24 Zezi dir zot, “Akoz samem zot dan lerer, zot pa konn ni Lekritir, ni pwisans Bondie."
Mark12:25 Kan bann dimoun pou resisite parmi bann mor, zom pa pou marye e pa pou bizin donn tifi an maryaz, zot pou kouma bann anz dan lesiel."
Mark12:26 Lor sa problem rezireksion bann mor la, zot pa finn lir saki finn ekrir dan liv Moiz? Zot pa finn tande kouma Bondie ti koz ar Moiz dan zistwar bwison ardan? Bondie limem pa ti dir, ‘Momem Bondie Abraam, momem Bondie Izaak, momem Bondie Zakob’?"
Mark12:27 Li pa Bondie bann mor me bann vivan, zot dan gran erer.”"
Mark12:28 Enn dokter lalwa ti pe tann zot diskite e li ti trouve kouma Zezi ti pe bien reponn zot; li aprose, li poz Zezi enn kestion, “Ki premie dan tou bann komannman?”"
Mark12:29 Zezi reponn li, “Ala ki premie komannman: Ekoute, Izrael! Lesegner nou Bondie li tousel Segner,"
Mark12:30 To pou kontan Lesegner to Bondie avek tou to leker, tou to lam, tou to lespri ek tou to lafors."
Mark12:31 Deziem, to pou kontan to prosin kouma tomem. Pena pli gran komannman ki sa.”"
Mark12:32 Dokter lalwa la dir li, “Sa enn zoli koze Met, samem laverite, ena enn sel Bondie, pena lot."
Mark12:33 Kontan li avek tou to leker, tou to lintelizans, tou to lafors ek kontan to prosin kouma to kontan tomem, samem pli inportan ki tou bann ofrand ek bann sakrifis.”"
Mark12:34 Letan Zezi trouve ki li finn reponn avek sazes, li dir li, “To pa lwin ar Rwayom Bondie.” Apre sa, personn pa oze poz li kestion."
Mark12:35 Kan Zezi ti pe ansegne dan tanp, li dir, “Kouma bann dokter lalwa kapav dir ki Lemesi, limem garson David?"
Mark12:36 Avek linspirasion Lespri Sin, David limem ti pe dir, ‘Lesegner finn dir ar mo Segner, asiz dan mo kote drwat, ziska mo fini met to bann ennmi anba to lipie.’"
Mark12:37 David limem apel li, Segner; alors kouma Lesegner kapav garson David?” Enn gro lafoul ti pe gagn lagam ekout li."
Mark12:38 Dan so lansegnman Zezi ti pe dir, “Fer atansion ar bann dokter lalwa. Zot kontan pavane avek zot gran-gran rob e zot kontan kan dimoun kourbe devan zot lor plas piblik."
Mark12:39 Zot kontan pran bann premie ban dan sinagog ek bann plas-doner dan bann resepsion,"
Mark12:40 Zot manz dibien bann vev e zot fer long-long lapriyer pou lizie dimoun, sa bannla, zot kondanasion pou pli lour.”"
Mark12:41 Zezi ti pe asize vizavi tron pou ofrand, e li ti pe obzerve kouma dimoun ti pe met zot kas ladan; boukou dimoun ris ti pe met gro-gro som larzan."
Mark12:42 Enn vev mizer-mizer koste, li met de kas ki pa ti ena gran valer."
Mark12:43 Zezi apel so bann disip, li dir zot, “Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, parmi tou sa bann dimoun ki finn met kas dan tron la, sa pov vev la, finn met plis ki zot tou."
Mark12:44 Zot tou zot finn met saki zot ti ena anplis, me li, vev la, li finn pran lor so rasion, lor saki li ti ena pou viv.”"
Mark13:1 Letan Zezi sorti andeor tanp, enn so bann disip dir li, “Met, gete kouma sa bann ros la zoli, get sa zoli batiman la, enn mervey!”"
Mark13:2 Zezi dir li, “To trouv sa bann gran-gran batiman la? Pa pou res ros lor ros; tou pou grene.”"
Mark13:3 Letan li finn fini asiz lor Kolinn Pie Zoliv, vizavi tanp, Pier, Zak, Zan ek Andre ris li dan enn kwin pou poz li enn kestion,"
Mark13:4 “Dir nou, kan tousala pou arive? Ki sign pou fer nou konpran ki tousala pre pou akonpli?”"
Mark13:5 Lerla Zezi koumans dir zot, “Get bien pouki personn pa anbet zot;"
Mark13:6 Boukou pou vini, zot pou servi mo nom, zot pou dir ‘Momem sa.’ Koumsamem zot pou anbet boukou dimoun."
Mark13:7 Kan zot pou tann lager ek tapaz lager, pa tranble; fode ki tousala arive, me li pankor lafin."
Mark13:8 Pou ena lager, pei kont pei, gouvernman kont gouvernman, pou ena tranblemandeter dan plizir landrwa, pou ena lafaminn; tousala kouma douler enn fam ki pre pou akouse."
Mark13:9 Me zot, fer atansion; bannla pou trenn zot devan tribinal ek dan sinagog e zot pou gagn bate; pou amenn zot devan bann gouverner ek bann lerwa akoz mwa, samem pou zot temwagnaz devan bannla."
Mark13:10 Premie dabor, fode ki Bonn Nouvel proklame dan tou bann nasion."
Mark13:11 Kan bannla pou aret zot, pou zot pas anzizman, pa trakase pou kone ki zot pou dir; me dan salerla dir saki vinn dan zot labous; parski napa zot ki pou koze me Lespri Sin."
Mark13:12 Frer pou trair frer ziska lamor, papa pou trair zanfan; zanfan pou revolte kont zot fami e pou fer touy zot."
Mark13:13 Tou dimoun pou air zot akoz mwa; me seki tini ferm ziska lafin, Bondie pou sov li."
Mark13:14 Kan zot pou trouv enn sakrilez abominab dan landrwa ki pa ti bizin (dimoun ki pe lir, konpran seki mo pe dir), bann ki dan Zide, sove, al dan montagn."
Mark13:15 Seki lao lor so lakaz, pa kalkil desann anba, ni rant dan lakaz pou pran kiksoz;"
Mark13:16 seki dan karo, pa kalkil retourn par deryer pou pran so linz."
Mark13:17 Bien malere bann fam ansint ek bann ki pe donn bwar zot tibaba sa lepok la.
Mark13:18 Priye pouki sa pa arive an-iver.
Mark13:19 Parski kan sa pou arive, pou ena enn gran detres, enn detres ki zame finn arive depi komansman kreasion, depi ki Bondie finn kre lemonn ziska aster, e ki zame pou trouve ankor."
Mark13:20 Si Lesegner pa ti finn rakoursi sa bann zour la, personn napa ti pou sove; me li finn rakoursi sa bann zour la, akoz bann dimoun ki li finn swazir."
Mark13:21 Si ninport kisannla dir zot dan salerla, ‘Gete, ala Lemesi isi! Gete ala li laba!’ Napa krwar li."
Mark13:22 Fos mesi ek fos profet pou leve; zot pou fer bann mirak pou fer dimoun tom dan lerer, e si posib, mem parmi bann saki finn swazir."
Mark13:23 Vey bien; mo finn bien prevenir zot.
Mark13:24 Kan sa pou arive, apre sa detres la, soley pou vinn som, lalinn pa pou donn so lekleraz,"
Mark13:25 zetwal pou koumans degringole e tou bann pwisans dan lesiel pou sakouye.
Mark13:26 Lerla zot pou trouv Garson Limanite desann depi dan niaz avek tou so pwisans ek tou so laglwar.
Mark13:27 Lerla li pou avoy so bann anz e li pou rasanble dimoun ki li finn swazir partou kote, depi enn bout later ziska lot bout lesiel."
Mark13:28 Konpran parabol pie fig: kan so bann brans vinn tann e ki so bann fey koumans sorti, zot kone ki lete pre pou vini."
Mark13:29 Parey pou zot osi, kan zot trouv sa bann zafer la arive; zot kone li pre, li deryer laport."
Mark13:30 Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, avan ki sa zenerasion la disparet, tousala pou arive."
Mark13:31 Lesiel ek later pou disparet me mo parol pa pou disparet.
Mark13:32 Personn napa kone ki zour, ki ler sa pou arive, ni bann anz, pa mem so Garson, me zis Bondie so Papa."
Mark13:33 Get bien, vey bien; parski zot pa kone kan tousala pou arive."
Mark13:34 Li parey kouma enn dimoun ki pe parti; avan li kit so lakaz, li donn bann serviter lotorite pou azir, sakenn so latas e li donn gardien lord pou veye."
Mark13:35 Akoz samem zot ousi, veye, parski zot pa kone kan propriyeter lakaz pou revini: aswar, damilie lanwit, letan kok sante, ouswa letan soley pe leve,"
Mark13:36 pangar, enn kout li vini e li trouv zot ape dormi."
Mark13:37 Saki mo pe dir zot, mo pe dir li pou zot tou: Veye.”"
Mark14:1 De zour avan fet Pak ek fet Dipin san levin, bann gran pret ek bann dokter lalwa ti pe fer tout sort manigans pou aret Zezi e fer touy li."
Mark14:2 Zot ti pe dir, “Pa fer sa pandan fet, sankwa lafoul kapav kre enn dezord.”"
Mark14:3 Zezi ti dan Betani, dan lakaz Simon, ki finn deza gagn lalep. Letan li pas atab, enn fam vini avek enn flakon albat, ranpli ar enn parfin aromatize ki bien-bien ser. Li kas flakon albat la e li vers parfin la lor latet Zezi."
Mark14:4 Detrwa dimoun ti pe revolte e zot ti pe dir ant zot mem, “Ki serti gaspiy sa parfin la koumsa?"
Mark14:5 Ti kapav vann sa pou valer trwasan zourne travay e ti pou kapav ed dimoun pov.” Alors zot kriy ar fam la.
Mark14:6 Zezi dir zot, “Les li trankil; ki fer zot koz brit ar li? Li finn fer enn gran kiksoz pou mwa."
Mark14:7 Pou ena touzour dimoun pov parmi zot; ninport ki ler zot anvi, zot kapav fer dibien pou bannla, me mwa, mo pa pou la toultan."
Mark14:8 Li, li finn fer seki li ti kapav fer; avan ler, li finn fini prepar mo lekor pou mo lanterman."
Mark14:9 Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, partou kote dan lemonn antie kot Bonn Nouvel pou anonse, pou rakont so zistwar e pou gard memwar saki sa fam la inn fer.”"
Mark14:10 Apre sa, Zida Iskaryot, enn parmi Ledouz, al get bann sef pret pou vann Zezi."
Mark14:11 Letan zot finn tann li, zot finn bien kontan e zot finn promet li larzan. Depi sa, Zida ti pe rod enn bon lokazion pou vann li."
Mark14:12 Premie zour fet Dipin san levin, kan fer sakrifis annyo pou fet Pak, bann disip dimann Zezi, “Kot to anvi nou ale pou fer bann preparasion pou manz repa paskal?”"
Mark14:13 Li avoy de so disip e li dir zot, “Al dan lavil; enn dimoun ki pe sarye enn seo dilo pou vinn zwenn zot; swiv li."
Mark14:14 La, kot li rantre, koz ar propriyeter lakaz la, dir li, ‘Lemet dimann twa, kot mo lasal pou mo manz repa paskal avek mo bann disip?’"
Mark14:15 Li pou montre zot enn gran lasal lao lor letaz ki finn deza pare avek tou so neseser. Prepar tou pou nou labamem.”
Mark14:16 Bann disip sorti, zot al dan lavil e zot trouv tou parey kouma li ti dir zot, e zot prepar fet Pak."
Mark14:17 Aswar, Zezi vini avek Ledouz."
Mark14:18 Kan zot finn fini asize atab e inn koumans manze, Zezi dir zot, “Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, enn parmi zot ki pe manz ansam ar mwa, pou vann mwa.”"
Mark14:19 Zot koumans resanti enn gran sagrin e enn apre lot demande, “Mwa sa?”"
Mark14:20 Li reponn zot, “Enn parmi Ledouz ki pe tranp so dipin avek mwa dan lasiet, limem sa."
Mark14:21 Garson Limanite pe ale parey kouma ti finn ekrir lor li; me bien malere dimoun ki pou trair Garson Limanite. Vomie li pa ti ne sa dimoun la.”
Mark14:22 Letan zot ti pe manze, Zezi pran dipin, li pronons enn benediksion, li kas dipin la, li donn zot, e li dir, “Pran, samem mo lekor.”"
Mark14:23 Apre sa, li pran enn koup, kan li fini rann gras, li donn zot e zot tou bwar."
Mark14:24 Li dir zot ankor, “Sa mem mo disan, disan lalians; mo pe vers li pou tou dimoun."
Mark14:25 Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, mo pa pou bwar ankor prodwi sa pie rezin la, ziska sa zour kot mo pou bwar divin nouvo dan Rwayom Bondie.”"
Mark14:26 Kan zot finn fini sant bann Psom, zot pran direksion Kolinn Pie Zoliv."
Mark14:27 Zezi dir zot, “Zot tou, zot pou tonbe; finn ekrir, ‘Mo pou bat berze la, tou mouton pou fane partou kote.’"
Mark14:28 Me apre mo rezireksion, mo pou atann zot Galile.”"
Mark14:29 Pier dir li, “Mem si zot tou tonbe, mwa, mo napa pou tonbe.”"
Mark14:30 Zezi dir li, “Laverite, laverite mo dir twa, zordi, aswar mem, avan ki kok sant de fwa to pou finn fini renie mwa trwa fwa.”"
Mark14:31 Pier reponn li, “Mem si bizin mor avek twa, mo pa pou renie twa.” Tou lezot dir mem zafer."
Mark14:32 Zot al dan enn landrwa ki ti apel Zetsemani e li dir so bann disip, “Asiz lamem, mwa, mo pe al priye.”"
Mark14:33 Li pran Pier, Zak ek Zan avek li; li koumans resanti enn gran detres ek enn gran freyer."
Mark14:34 Li dir zot, “Mo telman abat ki mo santi mo lavi pe ale; res la, veye.”"
Mark14:35 Li al inpe pli lwin, li tom anba e li priye pouki si posib, li pa pas par sa moman la."
Mark14:36 Li dir, “Abba! Pa! Pou twa tou posib; tir sa koup la devan mwa, me fer ki tou arive dapre to volonte, pa dapre mo volonte.”"
Mark14:37 Letan li revini, li trouv bannla pe asoupi. Li dir Pier, “Simon, to pe dormi? To pa finn gagn lafors pou vey enn er-tan ar mwa?"
Mark14:38 Veye, priye pou pa rant dan tantasion; lespri for, laser feb.”"
Mark14:39 Li reale, li al priye; li redir mem parol."
Mark14:40 Letan li revini, li trouv zot finn regagn somey ankor, parski zot lizie ti bien lour e zot pa ti kone ki pou dir li."
Mark14:41 Trwaziem fwa li revini, li dir zot, “Dormi asterla, repoz zot, tou saki ti bizin arive, inn arive. Ler finn vini pou Garson Limanite livre dan lame bann peser."
Mark14:42 Leve, anou ale. Gete, dimoun ki pou trair mwa pe aprose.”"
Mark14:43 Letan Zezi ti ankor pe koze, Zida, enn parmi Ledouz, vini avek enn lafoul, lepe ek baton dan lame. Bann sef pret, bann dokter lalwa ek bann ansien ti avoy zot."
Mark14:44 Sa tret ki ti pou vann Zezi la, finn donn zot enn signal, li finn dir zot, “Dimoun ki mo pou anbrase, trap li, pran li ale, sirvey li bien.”"
Mark14:45 Kouma li arive, toutswit li koste ar Zezi, li dir, “Rabi,” -e li anbras Zezi."
Mark14:46 Bannla tom lor li, blok li, trap li."
Mark14:47 Enn parmi bann ki ti la, tir so lepe e donn serviter gran pret enn kout. Li koup so zorey."
Mark14:48 Zezi dir zot, “Zot finn vinn avek lepe ek baton pou aret mwa koumadir mo enn vakabon?"
Mark14:49 Tou sa zour mo ti avek zot dan tanp, pe donn zot lansegnman, zot pa finn aret mwa. Me tousala pe arive pouki Lekritir akonpli.”"
Mark14:50 Zot tou kit li, zot sove."
Mark14:51 Enn zenn garson ki ti la, ti pe swiv li. Ti ena zis enn dra lor li; zot trap li."
Mark14:52 Me li larg dra, li galoup touni."
Mark14:53 Bannla amenn Zezi devan gran pret, kot zot tou finn rasanble: tou bann sef pret, bann ansien ek bann dokter lalwa."
Mark14:54 Pier ti pe swiv li delwin ziska li finn rant dan lakour andan, kot gran pret. Li finn asiz avek bann gard e li ti pe sof dife."
Mark14:55 Bann sef pret avek tou Sanedrin ti pe rod enn temwagnaz kont Zezi pou kondann li amor, me zot pa ti gagn nanye;"
Mark14:56 parski boukou finn donn fos temwagnaz lor li, me zot temwagnaz pa ti korbore."
Mark14:57 Detrwa met zot debout pou donn fos temwagnaz lor li. Zot ti pe dir,"
Mark14:58 “Nou finn tann li dir ‘Mo pou detrir sa tanp ki lame dimoun finn aranze la, e dan trwa zour mo pou konstrir enn lot san koudme personn.’ ”"
Mark14:59 Me mem lor sa pwin la, zot temwagnaz pa ti korbore."
Mark14:60 Gran pret met li dibout devan zot tou, li kestionn Zezi, “To pena nanye pou dir? Ki sa bann depozision ki dimoun inn fer kont twa la?”"
Mark14:61 Li res trankil, li pa dir nanye. Gran pret poz li kestion ankor enn fwa, li dir li, “Tomem Lemesi, Garson Bondie beni?”"
Mark14:62 Zezi reponn, “Momem sa; zot pou trouv Garson Limanite pe asize adrwat Toupwisan e pe desann dan niaz lesiel.”"
Mark14:63 Gran pret desir so linz, li dir, “Ki lot temwin nou bizin ankor?"
Mark14:64 Zot finn tann sa blasfem la? Ki zot dir asterla?” Zot tou kondann li, zot dir li merit lamor."
Mark14:65 Detrwa koumans kras lor li, zot bous so lizie, zot donn li koutpwin e zot dir li, “Fer to profet!” Bann serviter akeyir li ar kalot."
Mark14:66 Letan Pier ti anba dan lakour, enn parmi bann servant gran pret sorti e"
Mark14:67 trouv Pier pe sof dife. Li get li bien, li dir, “Twa osi to ti avek Zezi Nazaret.”"
Mark14:68 Li demanti, li dir, “Mo pa kone e mo pa konpran seki ou pe dir.” Li sorti li al dan lakour deor."
Mark14:69 Letan servant la retrouv li, li redir ar bann ki ti la, “Enn so bann sa.”"
Mark14:70 Ankor enn fwa li renie. Enn timama apre, zot redir Pier, “Vrememsa, to enn so bann, twa; parski twa osi to sorti Galile.”"
Mark14:71 Pier dimann malediksion lor li e li fer serman ki li pa konn sa dimoun ki zot pe koze la.
Mark14:72 Zis sa lerla, kok sante pou deziem fwa e Pier rapel parol ki Zezi ti dir li, ‘Avan kok sant de fwa to pou fini renie mwa trwa fwa.’ Lerla li krake, li plore."
Mark15:1 Boner gramatin, bann sef pret fer enn gran reynion avek bann ansien, bann dokter lalwa avek tou manm Sanedrin okonple. Zot atas Zezi, zot pran li e zot amenn li devan Pilat."
Mark15:2 Pilat dimann li, “Eski tomem lerwa Zwif?” Zezi reponn li, “Twa ki pe dir sa.”"
Mark15:3 Bann sef pret akiz li, zot met enn pake sarz lor li."
Mark15:4 Pilat redimann li “To pena nanye pou reponn? Gete ki kantite sarz bannla inn met lor twa.”
Mark15:5 Zezi pa reponn nanye. Sa ti fer Pilat res bet.
Mark15:6 Dapre koutim fet Pak, abitie larg enn prizonie ki dimoun demande."
Mark15:7 Ti ena enn prizonie ki ti apel Barabas. Li ti dan prizon avek bann lezot rebel ki ti finn komet enn krim dan emet.
Mark15:8 Lafoul monte pou dimann Pilat fer kouma li abitie fer.
Mark15:9 Pilat dimann zot, “Eski zot oule mo larg lerwa Zwif pou zot?”"
Mark15:10 Li ti realize ki bann sef pret finn livre li parski zot zalou.
Mark15:11 Alors bann sef pret exsit lafoul pouki zot dimann Pilat larg Barabas plito.
Mark15:12 Pilat redimann zot ankor enn fwa, “Be lerla, ki mo pou fer avek sa boug ki zot apel lerwa Zwif la?”"
Mark15:13 Zot kriye pli for, “Krisifie li!”"
Mark15:14 Pilat dir zot, “Ki li finn fer demal?” Zot kriye ankor pli for, “Krisifie li!”"
Mark15:15 Kouma Pilat ti anvi donn lafoul satisfaksion, li larg Barabas pou zot; letan zot finn fini fwet Zezi, Pilat livre li pouki bannla krisifie li."
Mark15:16 Bann solda sarye li dan lakour pale gouverner; lerla zot invit bann lezot gard vinn avek zot.
Mark15:17 Zot met enn manto rouz fonse lor li e zot anfons enn kouronn trese ar pikan lor so latet.
Mark15:18 Zot koumans salye li, “Bienveni, lerwa Zwif.”"
Mark15:19 Zot donn li enn kout zon lor so latet, zot kras lor li, zot azenou devan li e zot fer sanblan rann li omaz."
Mark15:20 Kan zot finn bien boufonn li, zot retir so manto rouz lor li e zot remet so linz; zot sarye li deor pou al koulout li lor lakrwa."
Mark15:21 Simon, papa Alexand ek Rifis, ti enn abitan Sirenn. Letan li sorti lakanpagn, li ti pe pas par la, kan bannla obliz li sarye lakrwa Zezi."
Mark15:22 Zot amenn Zezi dan enn landrwa ki ti apel Golgota, sakivedir Landrwa Krann dimoun mor."
Mark15:23 Zot sey donn li bwar enn melanz divin ek lamir me li refize.
Mark15:24 Zot koulout li lor lakrwa; zot tir lakourt-pay pou partaz so bann linz ant zot, pou gete ki sakenn pou gagne."
Mark15:25 Ti nev-er gramatin ler zot finn krisifie li.
Mark15:26 Ti ena enn plak ki explike pouki rezon li finn kondane e lor la ti ekrir “Lerwa Zwif.”
Mark15:27 Ti ena de bandi ki ti krisifie avek li, enn ti dan so drwat, lotla ti dan so gos. ["
Mark15:28 Koumsa ki Lekritir finn realize kot finn ekrir, “Li finn partaz sor bann kriminel.”]"
Mark15:29 Bann ki ti pe pase insilte li. Zot sakouy zot latet, zot dir, “Twa ki kraz tanp e rekonstrir li dan trwa zour"
Mark15:30 sov tomem, desann lor lakrwa!”"
Mark15:31 Bann sef pret ek bann dokter lalwa fer parey. Zot boufonn li ant zotmem e zot dir, “Li finn sov lezot me li pa kapav sov limem."
Mark15:32 Si vremem to Lemesi, lerwa Izrael, desann lor lakrwa, asterlamem, lerla nou pou krwar dan twa.” Bann ki ti krisifie ansam ar li, ti pe zour li zot osi."
Mark15:33 Ler finn ariv midi, teneb kouver later antie ziska trwa-zer tanto."
Mark15:34 Trwa-zer, Zezi kriy bien-bien for, “Eli, Eli, la-ma sabaktani?” - sakivedir, “Bondie, Bondie, kifer to finn abandonn mwa?”"
Mark15:35 Letan detrwa dimoun ki ti la, tann li, zot dir, “Tande! Li pe apel Eli.”"
Mark15:36 Enn parmi zot galoupe, inbib enn leponz ar vineg, met li dan bout enn banbou e donn Zezi sa pou bwar, e li dir, “Atann, anou gete si Eli pou vini, pou fer li desann.”"
Mark15:37 Apre sa Zezi kriye bien for e li rann so dernie soupir.
Mark15:38 Rido tanp desir an-de, depi lao ziska anba."
Mark15:39 Letan santiryon ki ti pe debout vizavi li, trouv manier li finn rann so dernie soupir, li dir, “Vremem, sa dimoun la ti Garson Bondie.”"
Mark15:40 Delwin, ti ena bann fam ki ti pe asiste seki ti pe pase; parmi zot ti ena Marie-Madlenn, Marie, mama ti-Zak, Zoze ek Salome,"
Mark15:41 Zot ti pe swiv Zezi e zot ti pe servi li depi Galile; ti ena ankor boukou lezot fam ki ti finn mont avek li ziska Zerizalem.
Mark15:42 Kan aswar vini, kouma ti zour Preparasion, savedir lavey saba,"
Mark15:43 Zozef ki sorti Arimate e ki ti enn konseye bien respekte, (li osi, li ti pe atann avek inpasians Rwayom Bondie), pran so kouraz, al get Pilat e dimann li lekor Zezi."
Mark15:44 Pilat ti etone ki li ti fini mor. Li ti fer apel santiryon e li dimann li si li ti finn mor depi lontan.
Mark15:45 Kan li ti finn gagn ransegnman avek santiryon, li donn Zozef permision pran so lekor."
Mark15:46 Zozef aste enn dra, desann Zezi anba, anvlop li dan dra la e met li dan enn tonbo ki ti finn taye dan ros; apre sa li ti roul enn gro ros devan so lantre."
Mark15:47 Marie-Madlenn ek Marie, mama Zoze ti pe bien gete kot ti finn met so lekor."
Mark16:1 Letan saba finn fini pase, Marie-Madlenn, Marie, mama Zak ek Salome aste bann aromat pou vinn anbom lekor Zezi."
Mark16:2 Gramatin boner, premie zour lasemenn, zis apre ki soley finn leve, zot vinn lor tom."
Mark16:3 Zot ti pe dir ant zotmem, “Kisannla pou roul sa ros ki devan lantre tom la?”"
Mark16:4 Kouma zot lev latet, zot gete, zot trouv sa gro ros la finn fini roule."
Mark16:5 Letan zot rant dan tonbo, zot trouv enn zennom ki ti pe asize adrwat. Li ti ena enn linz blan lor li. Zot gagn enn sok."
Mark16:6 Li dir zot, “Pa gagn per, zot ape rod Zezi Nazaret ki ti finn krisifie; li finn fini resisite, li pa isi. Get landrwa kot bannla ti met li."
Mark16:7 Aster, ale, al dir so bann disip ek Pier ki li pe atann zot Galile, parey kouma li ti dir zot. Zot pou trouv li laba.”"
Mark16:8 Zot sorti dan tonbo, zot sove. Zot tranble, zot boulverse e zot pa ti dir personn nanye parski zot ti gagn per. ["
Mark16:9 Letan li finn resisite boner gramatin, premie zour lasemenn, Zezi ti aparet dabor devan Marie-Madlenn; lor limem Zezi ti pous set demon."
Mark16:10 Marie-Madlenn ti al anons tou saki ti finn ariv li, ar bann dimoun ki ti avek Zezi; bannla ti andey e zot ti pe plore."
Mark16:11 Me letan zot finn aprann ki Zezi ti vivan e ki li ti finn aparet devan li, zot pa ti oule krwar."
Mark16:12 Apre sa, li finn aparet, dan enn lot manier, devan de parmi zot, letan zot ti pe marse dan lakanpagn."
Mark16:13 Zot ti retourne pou rakont lezot; me bannla pa ti oule krwar zot osi.
Mark16:14 Pli tar, li ti aparet devan Le-Onz, letan zot ti atab; li repros bannla ki zot pena lafwa e ki zot leker dir parski zot pa ti krwar dimoun ki ti finn trouv li apre so rezireksion."
Mark16:15 Li dir zot, “Al dan lemonn antie, al proklam Bonn Nouvel partou kote."
Mark16:16 Dimoun ki krwar ek resevwar batem pou sove, me dimoun ki pa krwar pou kondane."
Mark16:17 Ala bann sign ki pou fer dimoun rekonet bann ki krwar dan mwa: zot pou sas demon lor mo nom, zot pou koz bann nouvo langaz,"
Mark16:18 zot pou trap serpan dan zot lame e si zot arive bwar pwazon, zot pa pou gagn nanye; zot pou inpoz lame lor bann malad, bannla pou geri.”"
Mark16:19 Apre sa, Lesegner Zezi, letan li finn fini koz ar zot, li finn mont dan lesiel e li finn asiz kote drwat Bondie."
Mark16:20 So bann disip sorti e zot al proklam Bonn Nouvel partou kote; Lesegner ti pe travay avek zot e bann mirak ki ti pe arive ti pe montre ki zot predikasion ti vre. ]
Luke1:1 Onorab Teofil: Boukou dimoun finn pran lapenn pou ekrir enn liv lor bann evennman ki finn pase kot nou.
Luke1:2 Zot finn baz zot zistwar lor bann temwin ki finn trouv seki finn pase, e lor parol bann seki finn gagn lord transmet sa bann evennman la depi komansman."
Luke1:3 Akoz samem, mwa osi, mo finn deside pou bien pran ransegnman lor seki finn pase exakteman depi komansman. Dapre mwa, li bon ki mwa osi, mo ekrir enn liv pou twa, onorab Teofil."
Luke1:4 Mo pe fer sa pou to trouve ki sa bann lansegnman ki to finn gagne la, zot bien solid."
Luke1:5 Letan Erod ti lerwa Zide, ti ena enn pret ki ti apel Zakari, ki ti fer parti bann pret Abia; so fam Elizabet ti enn desandan gran pret Aaron."
Luke1:6 Toulede ti pe viv drwat devan Bondie, parski zot ti pe swiv lalwa ek so bann komannman kouma bizin."
Luke1:7 Me zot pa ti ena zanfan parski Elizabet ti steril, e zot toulede ti vie."
Luke1:8 Enn zour Zakari ti pe ofisie devan Bondie parski ti ariv tour so seksion pou servi dan tanp.
Luke1:9 Dapre koutim bann pret, finn swazir li par tiraz osor pou bril lansan lor lotel."
Luke1:10 Enn lafoul bann fidel ti pe priye deor letan ti pe bril lansan.
Luke1:11 Enn kout, enn anz Lesegner aparet devan li. Anz la ti pe dibout adrwat lotel kot lansan ti pe brile."
Luke1:12 Letan Zakari trouv li, li boulverse, li gagn per."
Luke1:13 Me anz la dir li, “Pa per, Zakari, parski Bondie finn tann to lapriyer. To fam Elizabet pou donn twa enn garson e to pou apel li Zan."
Luke1:14 To pou gagn enn gran lazwa akoz li, e boukou dimoun osi pou dan lazwa par so nesans."
Luke1:15 Li pou gran devan Lesegner. Li pa pou bwar divin ni okenn lalkol. Li pou ranpli ar Lespri Sin depi dan vant so mama.
Luke1:16 Li pou fer boukou zanfan Izrael retourn ar Lesegner zot Bondie.
Luke1:17 Li pou mars devan Bondie avek lafors ek lespri profet Eli. Li pou fer bann papa retourn ansam ek zot zanfan. Li pou fer bann rebel gagn lasazes bann zis. Li pou prepar enn lepep pou resevwar Bondie.”
Luke1:18 Me Zakari dir anz la, “Ki manier mo pou kone sa pou arive? Mo enn vie dimoun e mo fam osi vie.”"
Luke1:19 Anz la reponn li, “Mwa, mo Gabriel; mo devan Bondie pou servi li; li finn avoy mwa koz ar twa, pou anons twa sa bonn nouvel la."
Luke1:20 To pa finn krwar mwa, e pourtan tou seki mo pe dir pou realize, kan so ler pou vini. Akoz samem to pou perdi laparol e to pa pou kapav koze tanki sa pa arive.”"
Luke1:21 Deor, lepep ti pe atann Zakari. Zot ti etone parski Zakari ti pe tro tarde dan tanp."
Luke1:22 Kan Zakari sorti, li ti finn perdi laparol. Lerla zot ti konpran ki li ti gagn enn vizion dan tanp. Li ti pe koz ar zot ar bann sign."
Luke1:23 Zakari retourn kot li letan so tour servi dan tanp ti fini.
Luke1:24 Inpe plitar so fam, Elizabet, tom ansint e li ti res kasiet pandan sink mwa dan so lakaz. Li ti pe dir,"
Luke1:25 “Gete seki Bondie finn fer pou mwa, li finn tir laont ki ti lor mwa.”"
Luke1:26 Lor siziem mwa, Bondie avoy anz Gabriel dan lavil Nazaret dan Galile,"
Luke1:27 kot enn zennfi ki ti fianse avek Zozef, desandan David. Tifi la ti apel Marie."
Luke1:28 Anz la rant kot Marie, dir li, “Mo salye twa ki Bondie finn konble ar so lagras. Lesegner avek twa.”"
Luke1:29 Letan li tann sa bann parol la, li boulverse e li dimann dan so leker ki tousala oule dir."
Luke1:30 Anz la dir li, “Pa per, Marie, parski Bondie finn swazir twa."
Luke1:31 To pou ansint, to pou gagn enn garson, e to pou apel li Zezi."
Luke1:32 Li pou bien gran e pou apel li Garson Bondie Treo. Bondie Lesegner pou donn li tronn lerwa David, so anset,"
Luke1:33 e li pou regn toultan lor desandan Zakob; so regn pa pou fini zame.”
Luke1:34 Marie dir anz la, “Kouma sa pou arive, parski mo ankor vierz?”"
Luke1:35 Anz la reponn, “Lespri Sin pou vinn lor twa, e pwisans Bondie Treo pou kouver twa; akoz samem zanfan la pou Sin e pou apel li Garson Bondie."
Luke1:36 Get to kouzinn Elizabet, dan so vie zour, li pe atann enn garson. Sa fer sis mwa li ansint, alors ki dimoun ti pe dir ki li enn fam steril."
Luke1:37 Pou Bondie, nanye pa inposib.”"
Luke1:38 Lerla Marie dir, “Wi, mo servant Bondie. Ki tou seki to finn dir, samem arive pou mwa!” Apre sa, anz la kit li, ale."
Luke1:39 Samem lepok la, Marie leve e li degaze li al dan enn lavil Zida ki ti lao lor kolinn."
Luke1:40 Li rant dan lakaz Zakari e li salye Elizabet.
Luke1:41 Kan Elizabet tann lavwa Marie, tibaba la bouze dan so vant. Elizabet ti ranpli avek Lespri Sin"
Luke1:42 e li dir bien for, “To beni parmi tou bann fam e zanfan ki dan to vant osi, li beni."
Luke1:43 Ki mo ete pouki mama mo Segner vinn vizit mwa?
Luke1:44 Kan mo finn tann twa salye mwa, zanfan dan mo vant finn bouze avek enn gran lazwa."
Luke1:45 To bienerez parski to finn krwar ki parol Bondie pou realize.”
Luke1:46 Lerla Marie dir, “Mo lam glorifie Lesegner,"
Luke1:47 e mo leker ranpli ar lazwa akoz Bondie, mo Sover,"
Luke1:48 parski li finn oze poz so regar lor mwa, so pov servant. Depi zordi tou bann zenerasion pou dir mwa bienerez,"
Luke1:49 parski Bondie Toupwisan finn fer bann mervey pou mwa. So nom sin.
Luke1:50 Li montre so mizerikord pou dimoun ki onor li, zenerasion apre zenerasion."
Luke1:51 Li finn montre lafors so lebra; Li finn dispers bann ki ena lorgey dan zot leker.
Luke1:52 Li finn devir tronn bann gran sef anbalao. Li met dimoun ki gagn kraze dibout;
Luke1:53 Li ranpli vant bann seki gagn fin, li finn pous bann ris e zot finn ale lame vid."
Luke1:54 Li finn vinn tir so serviter Izrael dan difikilte; li pa bliye so lamour,"
Luke1:55 kouma li ti promet nou bann anset, Abraam ek so desandan ziska leternite.”"
Luke1:56 Marie res kot Elizabet anviron trwa mwa, apre li retourn so lakaz."
Luke1:57 Letan ariv ler pou Elizabet akouse, li donn nesans enn garson."
Luke1:58 Letan so bann vwazin ek so fami tann sa, zot vinn partaz so lazwa parski Lesegner finn montre li so lamour."
Luke1:59 Lor witiem zour, zot fer sirkonsizion zanfan la; zot ti pou apel li Zakari kouma so papa,"
Luke1:60 me so mama dir, “Non. Pou apel li Zan.”"
Luke1:61 Bannla dir li, “Personn pena sa nom la dan to fami.”"
Luke1:62 Alors zot fer bann sign ar so papa pou kone kouma li ti oule apel li.
Luke1:63 Zakari dimann enn lardwaz e li ekrir, “Li pou apel Zan.” Zot tou etone."
Luke1:64 Toutswit so lalang large, li koumans koze, ek li loue Bondie."
Luke1:65 Enn lafreyer trap tou bann vwazin, e dan tou bann kwin Zide dimoun ti pe koz samem."
Luke1:66 Tou seki finn tann sa nouvel la ti pe dimann zotmem, “Ki lavenir rezerve pou sa zanfan la?” Vremem lame Lesegner ti lor li."
Luke1:67 So papa Zakari ranpli ar Lespri Sin, profetize,"
Luke1:68 “Lesegner Bondie Izrael merit nou louanz parski li finn vizit so pep e li finn vinn delivre li.
Luke1:69 Pou nou, li finn lev enn Sover pwisan ki enn desandan David, so garson;"
Luke1:70 parey kouma li finn dir par labous so bann sin profet depi lontan.
Luke1:71 Li finn vinn delivre nou dan lame nou bann lennmi e li finn vinn tir nou dan lame bann ki fer nou ditor.
Luke1:72 Li finn montre nou anset so mizerikord, li finn rapel so lalians ki sin,"
Luke1:73 enn serman ki Bondie ti fer ar Abraam, nou anset,"
Luke1:74 pou liber nou depi lame nou lennmi, pouki nou servi li san freyer,"
Luke1:75 dan lasintete ek lazistis dan so prezans tou lezour nou lavi.
Luke1:76 E twa, tigarson, pou apel twa profet Bondie Treo, parski to pou mars devan Lesegner pou prepar so sime,"
Luke1:77 pou fer so lepep kone ki li pe vinn sov zot ler li pardonn zot pese.
Luke1:78 Par so tandres ek so mizerikord, nou Bondie pou avoy enn lalimier lor nou depi lao parey kouma soley pe leve."
Luke1:79 Li pou ekler bann seki dan teneb ek dan lonbraz lamor. Li pou gid nou pa lor sime lape.”
Luke1:80 Zanfan la ti pe grandi, so lespri ti pe fortifie. Li finn res dan dezer ziska zour ki li finn montre li anpiblik devan lepep Izrael."
Luke2:1 Sa lepok la Sezar Ogis donn lord fer resansman tou bann abitan Lanpir Romin.
Luke2:2 Ti fer sa premie resansman la letan Kirinyis ti gouverner provins Lasiri.
Luke2:3 Tou dimoun ti bizin al dan landrwa kot li ti ne, pou inskrir so nom."
Luke2:4 Zozef kit lavil Nazaret, an Galile, pou al Lazide dan lavil Betleem, la kot lerwa David ti ne, parski Zozef ti enn desandan David."
Luke2:5 Li ti al anrezistre so nom ansam ar Marie, so fianse, ki ti ansint."
Luke2:6 Letan zot ti laba, zour nesans tibaba la arive."
Luke2:7 Marie donn nesans enn garson, so premie zanfan e li anvlop li dan lanz e plas li dan enn manzwar, parski pa ti ena plas pou zot dan lasal pou vwayazer."
Luke2:8 Dan sa mem rezion la ti ena bann berze ki ti pe pas lanwit pou vey zot troupo.
Luke2:9 Enn anz Lesegner paret devan zot e laglwar Lesegner anvlop zot ar enn lalimier. Bannla gagn per.
Luke2:10 Me anz la dir zot, “Pa gagn per, mo pe anons zot enn gran nouvel ki pou fer lazwa boukou dimoun:"
Luke2:11 zordi dan lavil David, enn Sover, ki Lekris Lesegner, finn ne pou zot."
Luke2:12 Zot pou rekonet li par enn sign, zot pou trouv enn tibaba anvlope dan lanz e li dan enn manzwar.”"
Luke2:13 Enn sel kout enn larme bann anz arive pou zwenn ansam ar sa enn anz la, zot loue Bondie e zot dir:"
Luke2:14 “Laglwar pou Bondie lao e lape lor later ar tou seki li kontan.”
Luke2:15 Letan bann anz retourn dan lesiel, bann berze dir, “Anou al Betleem pou gete ki finn arive, ki Lesegner finn fer nou kone.”"
Luke2:16 Zot degaze ale, e zot trouv Marie, Zozef, e tibaba la ki ti dan manzwar."
Luke2:17 Apre ki bann berze finn trouv li, zot rakont seki anz ti dir zot lor zanfan la."
Luke2:18 E tou seki ti ekout zot koze ti etone ar zot dialog.
Luke2:19 Me Marie ti gard tou sa bann kiksoz la dan so leker.
Luke2:20 Lerla bann berze retourne; zot glorifie ek loue Bondie pou tou seki zot finn tande ek trouve parey kouma ti dir zot.
Luke2:21 Apre wit zour, letan pou sirkonsir li, zot ti apel li Zezi, sa nom lamem ki anz ti done, avan ki Marie ti ansint."
Luke2:22 Letan ariv ler pou Marie ek Zozef pirifie zotmem dapre lalwa Moiz, zot al Zerizalem pou prezant Zezi devan Lesegner,"
Luke2:23 parey kouma ekrir dan lalwa Lesegner: “Bizin konsakre sak garson premie-ne pou Lesegner.”
Luke2:24 Zot ti osi al ofer enn sakrifis kouma lalwa dimande: “Enn per tourtrel ou de ti pizon.”
Luke2:25 Dan Zerizalem ti ena enn dimoun apel Simeon. Li ti viv enn lavi bien drwat, li ti devoue pou Bondie e li ti pe atann seki pou vinn sov Izrael. Lespri Sin ti ar li."
Luke2:26 Lespri ti revel li ki li pa pou mor avan ki li trouv Lekris avoye par Lesegner.
Luke2:27 Simeon ti inspire par Lespri Sin pou vinn dan Tanp. Bann paran Zezi ti amenn zot zanfan pouki zot akonplir seki lalwa dimande.
Luke2:28 Simeon pran li dan so lebra e remersie Bondie, li dir,"
Luke2:29 “Asterla, Segner, les to serviter ale dan lape kouma to ti dir."
Luke2:30 Mo lizie finn trouv to delivrans,"
Luke2:31 Seki to finn prepare devan tou bann lepep;
Luke2:32 Enn lalimier ki amenn revelasion ar bann payin e laglwar pou to lepep Izrael.”
Luke2:33 So papa ek so mama ti etone ar tou seki ti dir lor li.
Luke2:34 Simeon beni zot, e li dir Marie, mama Zezi, “Sa garson la pou abes ouswa pou relev boukou dan Izrael, li enn sign Bondie, ki ena dimoun pou konteste."
Luke2:35 Bann panse ki kasiet dan leker boukou dimoun pou sorti okler, e tomem, enn lepe pou transpers to lam.”"
Luke2:36 Ti ena enn profetes osi, ki ti apel Ana, tifi Faniel, ki apartenir tribi Aser. Li ti bien vie, e ti viv set-an ar so mari."
Luke2:37 Apre sa li finn res vev ziska laz katrovin-kat-ran. Li pa ti kit tanp, me ti servi Bondie lanwit-lizour; li ti fer karem ek lapriyer."
Luke2:38 Li ti vinn dan tanp zis sa moman la e ti rann gras Bondie. Li ti koz sa zanfan la ar tou bann dimoun ki pe atann ki Bondie delivre Zerizalem.
Luke2:39 Letan zot fini fer tou seki lalwa Lesegner dimande, zot retourn Galile, dan zot prop lavil Nazaret."
Luke2:40 Zanfan la ti grandi e ti vinn for. Li ti ranpli ar sazes e lagras Bondie.
Luke2:41 Toulezan bann paran Zezi al Zerizalem pou fet Pak.
Luke2:42 Letan li ti ena douz-an zot ti al laba kouma zot abitie fer.
Luke2:43 Me letan fet fini, e zot retourne, garson la res Zerizalem, san ki so bann paran kone."
Luke2:44 Zot ti krwar li ansam dan group ki ti pe vwayaze, alor zot finn vwayaz toutenn zourne, lerla ki zot koumans rod li parmi bann fami e kamarad."
Luke2:45 Me letan zot pa trouv li zot retourn Zerizalem pou rod li.
Luke2:46 Apre trwa zour zot retrouv li dan tanp, pe asize parmi bann ki ansegn lalwa, li pe ekout zot e li pe poz zot kestion."
Luke2:47 Tou seki ti tann li ti etone ar so lintelizans e so repons.
Luke2:48 So bann paran ti etone letan zot trouv li, e so mama dir li, “Mo garson, kifer to fer sa ar nou? To papa ek momem nou finn gagn traka ar rod twa.”"
Luke2:49 Li dir zot, “Kifer zot ti bizin rod mwa? Zot pa kone ki mo bizin dan lakaz mo Papa?”"
Luke2:50 Zot pa ti konpran so repons.
Luke2:51 Zezi retourn Nazaret ar so bann paran. Li ti kontign obeir zot; e so mama ti gard tousala dan so leker.
Luke2:52 Zezi ti grandi dan sazes, ti grandi fizikman, e li ti trouv lagras devan Bondie e devan dimoun."
Luke3:1 Dan kinziem lane regn Tiber Sezar, letan Pons Pilat ti gouverner Zide, Erod ti sef Galile, so frer Filip ti sef rezion Itire ek Trakonitid, Lizias ti sef Abilenn;"
Luke3:2 letan Ann ek Kaif ti gran pret, Zan garson Zakari ti tann parol Bondie dan dezer."
Luke3:3 Zan ti al anons dan tou bann rezion Zourdin enn batem pouki dimoun sanz zot leker, pouki zot pese pardone."
Luke3:4 Kouma finn ekrir dan liv profet Izai, “Enn lavwa ape kriye dan dezer, prepar sime Lesegner, dres so santie drwat."
Luke3:5 Tou vale pou konble, sak montagn ek kolinn pou aplati, saki traver pou vinn drwat, sime kabose pou vinn plat"
Luke3:6 ek Bondie pou sov tou dimoun.”
Luke3:7 Alor li ti dir lafoul ki ti vini pou resevwar batem, “Bann espes serpan, kisannla finn montre zot ki zot pou sape devan koler Bondie ki pe aprose?"
Luke3:8 Prodwir bon fri ki montre ki zot finn sanz zot leker. Pa nek zis dir dan zotmem, ‘Abraam nou papa!’ Parski les mo dir zot, avek sa bann ros la, Bondie kapav fer bann desandan Abraam leve."
Luke3:9 Asterlamem laserp finn fini pare pou koup bann pie depi zot rasinn. Tou bann pie ki pa raport bon fri pou koupe e pou zet dan dife.”
Luke3:10 Lafoul dimann li, “Ki nou bizin fer alor?”"
Luke3:11 Li reponn zot, “Dimoun ki ena de palto bizin partaz ar seki pena, seki ena manze bizin fer parey.”"
Luke3:12 Bann komi tax ousi ti vini pou pran batem ek zot dir li, “Met, ki nou bizin fer?”"
Luke3:13 Li reponn zot, “Pa pran plis ki zot gagn drwa.”"
Luke3:14 Bann solda ousi dimann li, “Be nou, ki nou bizin fer?” Li reponn zot, “Pa kokin personn, pa fer fos akizasion; kontant zot ar zot lapey.”"
Luke3:15 Tou dimoun dan lepep ti pe atann kiksoz, ek tou dimoun ti pe poz kestion dan zot leker, sipa Zan mem ki Lemesi."
Luke3:16 Zan reponn zot tou, “Mwa, mo batiz zot ar dilo; me ena enn ki pli for ki mwa ki pe vini; mwa, mo mem pa dign pou larg so lase soulie; li pou batiz zot ar Lespri Sin ek dife."
Luke3:17 Li finn pran lapel dan so lame pou netway anba lor sali; li pou ramas lagrin dible dan so grenie, me li pou bril lapay dan enn dife ki zame pou tegn.”"
Luke3:18 Koumsamem e avek lezot parol ankor, Zan ti sakouy zot e li ti pe anons zot Bonn Nouvel."
Luke3:19 Me Zan ti repros Erod, gran sef Galile, parski li ti pran Erodiad, fam so frer, e parski li finn fer boukou move kiksoz ankor;"
Luke3:20 pa fini, lor la li finn fer kiksoz pir ankor, li ferm Zan dan prizon."
Luke3:21 Letan tou bann dimoun finn fini pran batem, e ki Zezi ousi finn fini batize, letan li pe priye,"
Luke3:22 lesiel ouver, e Lespri Sin desann lor li dan form enn vre kolonb, ek enn lavwa sorti dan lesiel, li dir, “Tomem mo Garson ki mo kontan, to fer mo boner.”"
Luke3:23 Letan Zezi ti koumans so minister li ti ena ape pre trant-an. Dapre bann dimoun, li"
Luke3:24 garson Zozef, ki ti garson Eli, garson Matat, garson Levi, garson Melki, garson Innai, garson Zozef,"
Luke3:25 garson Matatias, garson Amos, garson Nahoum, garson Esli, garson Nagai,"
Luke3:26 garson Maat, garson Matatias, garson Semein, garson Zozek, garson Yoda,"
Luke3:27 garson Yoanan, garson Reza, garson Zeroubabel, garson Sealtiel, garson Neri,"
Luke3:28 garson Melki, garson Adi, garson Kosam, garson Elmadan, garson Er,"
Luke3:29 garson Zezi, garson Eliezer, garson Yorim, garson Matat, garson Levi,"
Luke3:30 garson Simeon, garson Zida, garson Zozef, garson Yonam, garson Eliakim,"
Luke3:31 garson Melea, garson Mena, garson Matata, garson Natan, garson David,"
Luke3:32 garson Zese, garson Obed, garson Boaz, garson Sala, garson Nason,"
Luke3:33 garson Aminadab, garson Admin, garson Arni, garson Esron, garson Perez, garson Zida,"
Luke3:34 garson Zakob, garson Izaak, garson Abraam, garson Tara, garson Naor,"
Luke3:35 garson Serig, garson Reou, garson Peleg, garson Eber, garson Sela,"
Luke3:36 garson Kenan, garson Arfakzad, garson Sem, garson Noe, garson Lamek,"
Luke3:37 garson Metousalem, garson Enok, garson Yared, garson Malaleel, garson Kenan,"
Luke3:38 garson Enos, garson Set, garson Adam, garson Bondie."
Luke4:1 Zezi, ranpli ar Lespri Sin, kit Zourdin, e Lespri kondir li dan dezer."
Luke4:2 Laba diab ti tant li pandan karant zour. Pandan sa bann zour la, li pa ti manz nanye; apre sa, li ti gagn fin."
Luke4:3 Diab dir li, “Si tomem Garson Bondie donn lord sa ros la vinn dipin.”"
Luke4:4 Zezi reponn li, “Dan liv finn ekrir: ‘Dimoun pa viv zis ar dipin.’ ”"
Luke4:5 Diab amenn li pli lao e montre li enn sel kout tou bann rwayom lor later.
Luke4:6 Li dir Zezi, “Mo pou donn twa tou sa pouvwar la ek tou so rises, parski tousala mo finn resevwar e mo kapav donn sa ninport kisannla."
Luke4:7 Si to prostern twa devan mwa, tousala pou vinn pou twa.”"
Luke4:8 Zezi reponn li, “Dan liv finn ekrir: ‘To pou prostern twa devan Lesegner to Bondie, e to pou ador li tousel.’ ”"
Luke4:9 Diab amenn Zezi dan Zerizalem, li plas li net lao lor tanp, e li dir li, “Si tomem Garson Bondie, zet to lekor anba,"
Luke4:10 parski finn ekrir, ‘Li pou donn lord so bann anz vey lor twa,’"
Luke4:11 e ankor, ‘Zot pou sarye twa dan zot lame pouki to lipie pa kogn ar ros.’ ”"
Luke4:12 Zezi reponn li, “Finn dir: ‘Pa met Lesegner to Bondie dan enn sitiasion pou teste li.’ ”"
Luke4:13 Letan diab ti fini fer tou seki li kapav pou tant Zezi, li ti kit li ziska enn prosenn lokazion."
Luke4:14 Zezi retourn Galile avek pwisans Lespri e dimoun koumans koz li partou dan larezion.
Luke4:15 Li ti pe ansegn dan zot sinagog, e zot tou ti pe glorifie li."
Luke4:16 Li vinn Nazaret, la kot li ti grandi, e li al dan sinagog zour saba, kouma li ti abitie fer. Li dibout pou lir."
Luke4:17 Zot donn li liv Izai pou lir. Li ouver liv la e li tom lor paz kot finn ekrir:
Luke4:18 “Lespri Lesegner lor mwa, parski Li finn konsakre mwa par lonksion pou anons bann pov Bonn Nouvel. Li finn avoy mwa proklam delivrans bann seki an kaptivite, pouki bann aveg trouv kler, pouki bann oprime retrouv zot liberte,"
Luke4:19 e anons enn lane kot Lesegner pou fer zot enn gran faver.”
Luke4:20 Li ferm liv la, li donn li servan sinagog, e li asize. Tou dimoun ki ti dan sinagog fixe zot regar lor li."
Luke4:21 Alor li dir zot, “Azordi sa Parol ki zot finn tande la, li finn akonpli.”"
Luke4:22 Zot tou ti an admirasion; zot etone par bann zoli parol ki sorti dan so labous. Zot dir, “Pa garson Zozef sa?”"
Luke4:23 Lerla li dir zot, “Sirman zot pou sit mwa sa proverb ki dir, ‘Dokter, geri twa tomem. Nou okouran tou seki to finn fer dan Kafarnaom, fer parey isi dan to prop lavil.’ ”"
Luke4:24 Zezi dir zot, “Laverite mo dir zot: okenn profet pa gagn enn bon lakey dan so prop pei."
Luke4:25 Me laverite mo dir zot, dan lepok Eli ti ena boukou vev dan Izrael, kan lesiel ti ferme trwa-zan sis mwa, e kan enn gran lafaminn ti kouver pei antie;"
Luke4:26 pourtan Bondie pa ti avoy Eli kot okenn parmi zot me kot enn vev ki ti viv dan Sarepta, dan rezion Sidon."
Luke4:27 Dan lepok profet Elize ti ena boukou lepre dan Izrael, pourtan okenn parmi zot pa ti gagn gerizon, exsepte Naaman, enn Syrien.”"
Luke4:28 Tou seki dan sinagog ti ankoler letan zot tann sa koze la.
Luke4:29 Zot leve, zot trenn Zezi andeor lavil, zot amenn li lao lor kolinn kot zot lavil ti konstrir, e zot rod zet li anba."
Luke4:30 Me li pas omilie zot e li ale.
Luke4:31 Zezi desann Kafarnaom, enn lavil dan Galile, e li ti pe ansegne zour saba."
Luke4:32 Bannla ti inpresione par so lansegnman parski so parol ti ena pwa.
Luke4:33 Dan sinagog ti ena enn dimoun posede par enn move lespri ki ti pe kriye for-for,"
Luke4:34 “Ayo, Zezi Nazaret, ki to oule ar nou? Mo kone ki to ete; tomem Sin, tomem sorti kot Bondie.”"
Luke4:35 Zezi menas li, li dir, “Ferm to labous, sorti dan li, ale.” Move lespri zet posede la anba, omilie bannla, e kit li san fer li okenn ditor."
Luke4:36 Enn lafreyer trap zot tou e sakenn dir ar so kamarad, “Ala enn parol la! Li expilse avek otorite ek pwisans bann move lespri, e zot disparet.”"
Luke4:37 So renome fane partou kote.
Luke4:38 Zezi kit sinagog e li al lakaz Simon. Belmer Simon ti gagn enn move lafiev, e zot dimann Zezi fer kiksoz pou li."
Luke4:39 Zezi koste pre kot madam la e li menas lafiev la. Lafiev kit li, e li leve toutswit, li servi zot."
Luke4:40 Soley finn kouse, kan tou bann seki ti ena bann malad avek tou sort kalite maladi, ti amenn zot kot Zezi. Li poz lame lor sakenn e li geri zot."
Luke4:41 Bann move lespri osi sorti lor boukou dimoun malad, e zot kriye, “Tomem Garson Bondie!” Me Zezi ti menas zot e li ti anpes zot koze, parski zot ti kone ki limem Lemesi."
Luke4:42 Kouma fer lizour, Zezi sorti, li al dan enn landrwa izole. Enn lafoul dimoun rod li, e letan zot reysi zwenn li, zot fer tou pou gard li lamem, pouki li pa kit zot."
Luke4:43 Me Zezi dir zot, “Mo bizin anons Bonn Nouvel Rwayom Bondie dan lezot lavil osi; akoz samem Bondie finn avoy mwa.”"
Luke4:44 E alors li al proklam laparol dan bann sinagog dan Zide.
Luke5:1 Zezi ti pe dibout danbor lamer Zenezaret. Lafoul ti pe pouse pou vinn pli pre ar li, pou ekout parol Bondie."
Luke5:2 Li trouv de pirog danbor lak, me bann peser pa ti ladan, parski zot ti pe lav zot file."
Luke5:3 Li mont dan pirog Simon, e li dir li al inpe pli lwin. Lerla li asize e li ansegn lafoul."
Luke5:4 Letan li fini koze, li dir Simon, “Al inpe dan fon e zet zot file.”"
Luke5:5 Simon dir li, “Met, nou finn trime enn lanwit e nou pa finn gagn nanye! Me akoz to parol mo pou zet mo file.”"
Luke5:6 Zot zet zot file. Lerla zot ramas enn kantite pwason; ti ena telman boukou pwason ki zot file ti pre pou desire.
Luke5:7 Zot signal zot kamarad dan lot pirog pou vinn donn zot enn koudme. Bannla koste, zot ranpli toulede pirog. Ti ena telman pwason, ki pirog ti pe koumans koule."
Luke5:8 Letan Simon Pier trouv sa, li tom azenou devan Zezi e li dir, “Segner, res lwin ar mwa, parski mo enn dimoun ranpli ar pese.”"
Luke5:9 Simon ek tou bann ki ti ar li, ti etone ki finn may sa kantite pwason la."
Luke5:10 So bann asosie Zak ek Zan, de garson Zebede ti etone osi. Zezi dir ar Simon, “Pa bizin per. Asterla to pou al lapes dimoun.”"
Luke5:11 Letan zot fini ris pirog ater, zot kit tou, zot swiv Zezi."
Luke5:12 Zezi ti dan enn lavil, kan enn boug ki ti kouver ar lalep, trouv li. Boug la tom dan so lipie e so fron tous later. Li sipliy Zezi, “Segner, si to oule, to kapav pirifie mwa.”"
Luke5:13 Lerla Zezi avoy so lame, tous li, e li dir li, “Wi, mo oule, to pou pirifie.” Toutswit so lalep kit li."
Luke5:14 Zezi donn li lord pa dir personn. Li dir li, “Ale, al get bann pret, al ofer enn sakrifis pou to pirifikasion, parey kouma Moiz ti finn komande. Sa pou enn prev pou lezot.”"
Luke5:15 Lerla koze lor Zezi fann dan tou kwin lari plis ankor; lafoul dimoun ramase pou ekout li e pou gagn zot gerizon.
Luke5:16 Me li al dan bann landrwa retire pou priye.
Luke5:17 Enn zour, kan Zezi ti pe ansegne, bann Farizien ek bann dokter lalwa ti pe asize laba. Zot ti sorti dan bann vilaz Galile ek Zide e ena ki ti sorti Zerizalem. Pwisans Lesegner ti ar Zezi pou li fer gerizon."
Luke5:18 Zis lerla detrwa dimoun vini, zot ti pe sarye enn boug ki ti paralize lor enn brankar. Zot ti pe sey amenn li andan devan Zezi."
Luke5:19 Me pa ti ena sime pou pase akoz lafoul. Zot mont lao lor lakaz, zot fouy enn trou dan twa e zot desann li ar so brankar omilie lafoul devan Zezi."
Luke5:20 Kan Zezi trouv zot lafwa, li dir, “Kamarad, to pese finn pardone.”"
Luke5:21 Lerla bann dokter lalwa e bann Farizien koumans poz kestion, “Ki li krwar li ete? Li pe blasfeme. Kisannla kapav pardonn pese apar Bondie tousel?”"
Luke5:22 Zezi kone ki zot ti pe panse, li reponn zot, “Kifer zot ena bann panse koumsa dan zot leker?"
Luke5:23 Ki pli fasil pou dir, ‘To pese finn pardone,’ oubien, ‘Deboute marse’?"
Luke5:24 Me pouki zot kone ki Garson Limanite ena lotorite lor later pou pardonn pese” Zezi dir ar paralize la, “Mo dir twa, dibout, pran to brankar, al to lakaz.”"
Luke5:25 Toutswit li dibout devan zot, li pran so brankar e li al so lakaz e letan li pe ale, li glorifie Bondie."
Luke5:26 Zot tou emerveye, e zot glorifie Bondie osi, zot ti an adorasion e zot dir, “Nou finn trouv kiksoz extraordiner zordi!”"
Luke5:27 Apre sa li sorti deor e li trouv enn komi tax ki apel Levi, ki ti pe asiz dan biro tax; Zezi dir li, “Swiv mwa.”"
Luke5:28 Li leve, li kit tou, li swiv Zezi."
Luke5:29 Levi fer enn gran fet dan so lakaz; ti ena enn gran lafoul komi tax ek bann lezot ankor ki ti pe asiz atab.
Luke5:30 Bann Farizien ek bann dokter lalwa ti pe fer repros ar so bann disip. Zot ti pe dir, “Kifer zot pe manze-bwar avek bann komi tax ek bann peser?”"
Luke5:31 Zezi reponn, “Seki bien pa bizin dokter, me seki malad ki bizin;"
Luke5:32 mo pa finn vinn apel bann zis me bann peser pouki zot repanti.”
Luke5:33 Lerla zot dir Zezi, “Bann disip Zan parey kouma bann disip Farizien, souvan gard karem ek priye, me twa to bann disip nek manze-bwar.”"
Luke5:34 Zezi reponn zot, “Eski bann invite kapav res karem kan nouvo marye ankor ar zot?"
Luke5:35 Pou ariv enn zour kot nouvo marye pou nepli la, lerla zot ava gard karem.”"
Luke5:36 Li dir zot enn parabol, “Personn pa pran enn bout linz nef pou rakomod enn vie linz. Sinon nef la pou desire e lorla, bout nef la pa pou al ar vie la."
Luke5:37 Personn pa met divin nouvo dan vie barik; sinon divin nouvo pou eklat bann barik la, tou divin pou fane, e pou perdi bann barik la."
Luke5:38 Met divin nouvo dan barik nef.
Luke5:39 Personn pa pou anvi bwar divin nouvo, letan li finn gout vie divin parski zot dir, ‘Seki vie pli bon.’ ”"
Luke6:1 Enn zour saba, Zezi ti pe pas dan karo dible, so bann disip ti pe kas zepi dible, ki zot ti pe frot dan zot lame e zot ti pe manz lagrin la."
Luke6:2 Detrwa Farizien dir, “Kifer zour saba zot pe fer seki pa gagn drwa fer dapre lalwa?”"
Luke6:3 Zezi reponn, “Eski zot pa finn lir seki David ek so bann kamarad ti fer kan zot ti pe gagn fin?"
Luke6:4 Li ti rant dan lakaz Bondie, li ti pran dipin ki finn ofer Bondie, li finn manz li e li finn donn so bann kamarad osi. Dapre lalwa zis bann pret tousel gagn drwa manz sa dipin la.”"
Luke6:5 Zezi redir zot, “Garson Limanite limem propriyeter saba.”"
Luke6:6 Enn lot zour saba, letan li rant dan sinagog e ki li ti pe ansegne, ti ena enn boug prezan ki so lame drwat ti paralize."
Luke6:7 Bann dokter lalwa ek bann Farizien ti pe vey li, pou gete si pa li pou fer gerizon zour saba; koumsa zot ti pou gagn enn pwin pou met enn sarz lor li."
Luke6:8 Me Zezi ti konn zot panse, li dir sa dimoun ki ena lame paralize la, “Leve vinn dibout devan.” Lerla dimoun la leve, li vinn dibout devan zot."
Luke6:9 Apre sa Zezi dir ar bannla, “Mo poz zot enn kestion: ki lalwa permet zour saba? Fer dibien oubien fer dimal? Sov lavi ou detrir lavi?”"
Luke6:10 Li get bann ki ti otour li, e li dir paralize la, “Dres to lame.” Li fer seki dir li, e so lame revinn normal."
Luke6:11 Bannla irite e zot diskit ant zotmem pou kone ki kapav fer ar Zezi.
Luke6:12 Zezi mont lor montagn pou priye. Li pas lanwit priye Bondie.
Luke6:13 Letan barlizour leve, li apel so bann disip, e li swazir douz parmi zot, li donn zot nom apot."
Luke6:14 Ti ena Simon - li ti apel li Pier - ek so frer Andre, Zak ek Zan, Filip ek Bartelmi,"
Luke6:15 Matie ek Toma, Zak garson Alfe ek Simon ki ti apel Zelot,"
Luke6:16 Zida garson Zak ek Zida Iskaryot, ki ti trair Zezi."
Luke6:17 Zezi desann ansam ar zot e li aret dan enn landrwa plat. Enn kantite disip ek enn gran lafoul dimoun ki vinn depi Zide, Zerizalem ek danbor lakot Tir ek Sidon ti la osi."
Luke6:18 Zot ti vinn ekout li e pou gagn zot gerizon. Bann ki ti tourmante par lespri malsin ti geri.
Luke6:19 Tou dimoun ki dan lafoul ti pe sey tous li, parski enn lafors ti pe sorti dan li e ti pe geri zot tou."
Luke6:20 Apre sa Zezi get so bann disip e li dir, “Bienere zot ki bann pov, Rwayom Bondie pou zot."
Luke6:21 Bienere zot ki gagn fin asterla, zot pou rasazie. Bienere zot ki pe plore asterla, zot pou riye."
Luke6:22 Bienere kan dimoun air zot, e kan met zot deor, insilte zot, abes zot, mal parl zot akoz Garson Limanite."
Luke6:23 Rant dan lazwa sa zour la, sot anler, parski enn gran rekonpans pe atann zot dan lesiel; parski koumsamem zot bann gran dimoun ti maltret bann profet."
Luke6:24 Bienmalere zot ki bann ris parski zot finn deza resevwar zot konsolasion.
Luke6:25 Bienmalere zot ki viv dan labondans aster, parski zot pou gagn fin. Bienmalere zot ki pe riye aster, parski zot pou andey e zot pou plore."
Luke6:26 Bienmalere kan tou dimoun koz lor zot anbien, parski koumsamem zot gran dimoun ti fer ar bann fos profet."
Luke6:27 “Me mwa mo pe dir ar zot ki pe ekout mwa, kontan zot lennmi, fer dibien dimoun ki air zot,"
Luke6:28 beni dimoun ki modi zot, priye pou seki maltret zot."
Luke6:29 Si kikenn tap twa enn kalot lor to lazou, donn li lot kote lazou; si kikenn pran to palto, pa anpes li pran to simiz osi."
Luke6:30 Donn tou dimoun ki dimann twa sarite; e si kikenn pran to dibien, pa dir li rann twa."
Luke6:31 Seki to ti a kontan lezot fer pou twa, fer samem pou zot."
Luke6:32 Si to kontan zis bann seki kontan twa, ki rekonesans to merite ladan? Parski mem bann peser kontan seki kontan zot."
Luke6:33 Si to fer dibien zis pou dimoun ki fer dibien pou twa, ki to merite ladan? Mem bann peser fer parey."
Luke6:34 Si to pret zis dimoun ki to krwar pou rann twa, ki to merite ladan? Mem bann peser pret bann peser, pou ki zot resevwar mem som larzan."
Luke6:35 Me zot, kontan zot lennmi, fer dibien, e prete san atann nanye anretour. Zot rekonpans pou gran, e zot pou zanfan Bondie Treo parski li bon ar bann ingra ek bann move."
Luke6:36 Montre enn leker ranpli ar mizerikord parey kouma Bondie zot Papa.”
Luke6:37 “Pa port zizman e personn pa pou ziz zot; pa kondane e personn pa pou kondann zot. Pardone, zot pou gagn pardon."
Luke6:38 Done, zot pou resevwar dan pos zot tabliye enn mezir bien ranpli, bien dame e ki pe deborde; mezir ki to servi pou lezot, samem mezir ki pou servi pou twa.”"
Luke6:39 Zezi servi bann parabol ankor e li dir zot, “Eski enn aveg kapav gid enn lot aveg? Sinon eski toulede pa pou tom dan trou?"
Luke6:40 Enn disip pa pli gran ki so met, me tou seki gagn enn bon formasion pou kouma so met."
Luke6:41 Kifer to trouv lapay dan lizie to prosin, me to pa trouv poto ki dan to lizie?"
Luke6:42 Oubien, kouma to kapav dir to prosin, ‘Frer, les mo retir lapay ki dan to lizie,’ kan tomem to pa trouv poto dan to prop lizie? Twa ipokrit, tir poto ki dan to lizie avan, lerla to pou trouv kler pou tir lapay dan lizie to prosin."
Luke6:43 “Okenn bon zarb fritie kapav donn fri gate, ek enn move zarb pa kapav donn bon fri;"
Luke6:44 nou rekonet sak pie par so fri. Pa kapav ramas fig dan pikan, ni rezin lor raket."
Luke6:45 Enn bon dimoun prodwir dibien depi bon trezor ki dan so leker, e move dimoun prodwir lemal depi so move trezor; parski labous exprim seki debord dan leker."
Luke6:46 “Kifer zot apel mwa Segner, Segner, me zot pa fer seki mo dir?"
Luke6:47 Mo pou montre zot kouma li ete sa dimoun ki vinn ar mwa la, ki ekout mo parol e met li anpratik."
Luke6:48 Li parey kouma enn dimoun ki pe mont so lakaz. Li fouy enn transe bien fon, li poz fondasion la lor enn pavaz ros; letan inondasion vini, larivier deborde, bat ar lakaz la; lakaz la pa kraze parski li bien solid."
Luke6:49 Me dimoun ki ekout mo parol me pa met li anpratik, li kouma enn dimoun ki finn mont so lakaz san fouy fondasion. Kouma larivier desann, li balye lakaz la, nanye pa reste.”"
Luke7:1 Letan Zezi fini dir tou sa bann parol la devan lafoul, li rant dan Kafarnaom."
Luke7:2 Laba, enn santiryon ti ena enn serviter ki li ti estim boukou. Li ti malad e ti pre pou mor."
Luke7:3 Kan santiryon la finn tann koz Zezi, li avoy detrwa sef Zwif al get li pou dimann li vinn geri so serviter."
Luke7:4 Kan zot ariv devan Zezi, zot sipliy li e zot dir, “Li merit ki to fer sa pou li,"
Luke7:5 parski li kontan nou pep, e limem ki finn mont nou sinagog.”"
Luke7:6 Zezi al ar zot. Li pa ti tro lwin ar lakaz la kan santiryon la avoy bann kamarad pou dir li, “Segner, pa deranze; parski mo pa dign ki to vinn dan mo lakaz;"
Luke7:7 akoz samem mo pa finn oze vinn kot twa. Dir zis enn parol, lerla mo serviter pou geri."
Luke7:8 Parski momem mo enn dimoun ki anba lotorite mo bann sef, e mo ena solda anba mwa; e kan mo dir ar enn, ‘Ale,’ li ale; ar enn lot, ‘Vini,’ li vini; e ar mo serviter, ‘Fer sa,’ e li fer li.”"
Luke7:9 Kan Zezi tann sa li ti emerveye par so bann parol, e li tourn ar lafoul ki ti pe swiv li, e li dir, “Mo dir zot, mem dan Izrael mo pa finn trouv enn lafwa koumsa.”"
Luke7:10 Letan bann ki ti vinn get Zezi retourn lakaz, zot trouv serviter la an bonn sante."
Luke7:11 Enn zour, Zezi ti al dan enn lavil ki ti apel Nainn. So bann disip ek enn gran lafoul ti pe swiv li."
Luke7:12 Letan li ariv devan laport lavil, ala ki lanterman enn zennom ti pe sorti. Li ti sel garson pou so mama, e so mama ti enn vev. Enn gran lafoul ti pe mars ar mama la."
Luke7:13 Letan Lesegner trouv li, so leker fer mal, e li dir mama la, “Pa plore.”"
Luke7:14 Zezi koste ar serkey e tous li. Bann dimoun ki ti pe sarye serkey arete. Zezi dir, “Zennom, mo dir twa, leve.”"
Luke7:15 Mor la leve, li asize, li koumans koze. Zezi rann garson la so mama."
Luke7:16 Lafreyer sezi bann dimoun e zot glorifie Bondie; zot dir, “Enn gran profet finn leve parmi nou e Bondie finn vizit so pep.”"
Luke7:17 Sa nouvel la fane partou dan Zide ek dan lezanviron.
Luke7:18 Bann disip Zan rakont zot met tou sa bann kiksoz la. Alors Zan apel de disip
Luke7:19 e li avoy zot kot Lesegner pou dimann li, “Tomem ki sipoze vini la, oubien nou bizin atann enn lot?”"
Luke7:20 Letan bannla ariv kot Zezi, zot dir, “Zan Batis finn avoy nou dimann twa, ‘Eski tomem ki sipoze vini, oubien nou bizin atann enn lot?”"
Luke7:21 Dan sa ler la, Zezi ti pe geri boukou malad ki dan douler, ki ti ena lespri move; e bann aveg ti pe trouv kler."
Luke7:22 Alors li reponn zot, “Al dir Zan seki zot finn trouve ek seki zot finn tande: aveg trouv kler, paralize marse, bann lepre geri, bann sourd tande, bann mor leve, bann pov resevwar Bonn Nouvel."
Luke7:23 Bienere seki pa tonbe akoz mwa.”
Luke7:24 Letan bann mesaze Zan inn ale, Zezi koumans koz ar lafoul lor Zan: “Ki zot finn al gete dan dezer? Enn voun ki pe balote ar divan?"
Luke7:25 Ki zot finn al gete alor? Enn dimoun ki ti abiy ar kostim letof? Gete, bann ki met zoli linz, viv dan lix e res dan sato lerwa."
Luke7:26 Abe ki zot finn al gete? Enn profet? Laverite, mo dir zot, li plis ki enn profet."
Luke7:27 Lor limem Lekritir dir, ‘Mo pe avoy mo mesaze devan twa, li pou ouver enn sime devan twa.’"
Luke7:28 Mo dir zot, parmi tou seki sorti dan vant zot mama, pena personn ki pli gran ki Zan; pourtan seki pli piti dan Rwayom Bondie, pli gran ki li.”"
Luke7:29 Lafoul dimoun ek bann komi tax, ki ti tann sa, ti trouve ki Bondie zis parski zot ti deza resevwar batem Zan;"
Luke7:30 me bann Farizien e bann dokter lalwa ti rezet plan ki Bondie ti ena pou zot parski zot ti refiz batem Zan.
Luke7:31 “Ar ki mo pou konpar dimoun zordizour? Kouma zot ete?
Luke7:32 Zot parey kouma bann zanfan ki pe asize lor laplas piblik e zot pe kriye zot kamarad: ‘Nou ti zwe laflit pou zot, me zot pa ti danse; nou ti sant kantik lanterman, me zot pa ti plore.’"
Luke7:33 Zan Batis vini, li pa manz dipin, pa bwar divin, e zot dir, ‘Li ena enn demon lor li.’"
Luke7:34 Garson Limanite vini, li manze li bwar, e zot dir, ‘Get sa, li enn gourman, enn soular e li kamarad ar komi tax ek bann peser!’"
Luke7:35 Me tou seki finn aksepte lasazes Bondie finn rekonet ki Bondie zis.”
Luke7:36 Enn Farizien invit Zezi vinn manze kot li. Zezi ale e li asiz atab.
Luke7:37 Dan sa lavil la, ti ena enn fam ki ti pe amenn enn move lavi. Li ti tann dir ki Zezi ti pe manze dan lakaz Farizien la; alors, li amenn enn flakon an albat ranpli ar parfin."
Luke7:38 Li dibout deryer Zezi, kot so lipie, li ti pe plore, li ti pe mouy lipie Zezi avek so larm e li ti pe souy li avek so seve. Li ti pe anbras lipie Zezi e vers parfin lor so lipie."
Luke7:39 Letan Farizien ki ti invit Zezi trouv sa, li dir dan limem, “Si vremem li ti enn profet li ti pou kone ki kalite fam pe tous li e ki li enn fam move lavi.”"
Luke7:40 Zezi dir li, “Simon, mo ena enn kestion pou poz twa.” Li dir Zezi, “Koze Met.”"
Luke7:41 Zezi dir Simon, “Ti ena de dimoun ki ti dwa enn kaser; enn ti dwa sink-san pies larzan, lot ti dwa sinkant."
Luke7:42 Letan zot pa ti kapav ranbourse, li ti rey zot det. Dir mwa, kisannla pou plis kontan li?”"
Luke7:43 Simon reponn, “Mo sipoze seki ti ena pli gro det la.” Zezi dir li, “To ena rezon.”"
Luke7:44 Zezi vire get madam la, li dir Simon, “To trouv sa madam la? Mo finn rant kot twa, to pa finn donn mwa dilo pou lav mo lipie, me li, li finn tranp mo lipie ar so larm e li finn souy li ar so seve."
Luke7:45 To pa finn anbras mwa, me depi ki mo finn rantre, li pa finn aret anbras mo lipie."
Luke7:46 To pa finn vers delwil lor mo latet, me li finn frot mo lipie avek parfin."
Luke7:47 Ala mo dir twa, tou so pese finn pardone parski li finn montre boukou lamour. Dimoun ki gagn tigit pardon, montre tigit lamour”."
Luke7:48 Lerla Zezi dir madam la, “Tou to pese finn pardone.”"
Luke7:49 Bann ki ti la dir ant zotmem, “Ki li ete li pou li mem oze pardonn bann pese?”"
Luke7:50 Lerla Zezi dir ar madam la, “To lafwa finn sov twa, al anpe.”"
Luke8:1 Zis apre, Zezi travers bann lavil ek bann vilaz pou anons ek proklam Bonn Nouvel Rwayom Bondie. Ledouz ti avek li,"
Luke8:2 ek detrwa madam lor ki Zezi ti tir bann lespri move e ti geri zot bann maladi. Parmi ti ena Marie, ki ti apel Magdala lor ki ti ena set demon ki Zezi ti pouse,"
Luke8:3 Zann, fam Souza ki ti enn administrater kot Erod, ti ena osi Sizann, e boukou lezot ankor, ki ti servi zot dibien pou ed Zezi ek bann disip."
Luke8:4 Kan enn gran lafoul dimoun sorti dan bann lavil e vinn ar Zezi, li dir zot enn parabol,"
Luke8:5 “Enn planter sorti pou sem so bann lagrin; pandan li seme, inpe tom lor sime, dimoun mars lor la, e bann zwazo lesiel vinn manz tou."
Luke8:6 Inpe tom lor ros; letan zot grandi, zot sek parski ti mank limidite."
Luke8:7 Inpe tom dan pikan, e kan pikan la grandi ansam avek bann lagrin la, li touf zot."
Luke8:8 Inpe tom dan bon later, e kan zot grandi, zot prodwir san fwa plis.” Letan li fini dir sa, li dir avek otorite, “Seki ena zorey pou tande, li a tande!”"
Luke8:9 So bann disip dimann li ki sa vedir sa parabol la.
Luke8:10 Li dir, “Zot, finn donn zot konesans sekre Rwayom Bondie; me ar lezot mo koz an parabol, koumsa ‘zot pou gete san trouve, e zot pou tande san konpran.’"
Luke8:11 “Ala seki sa parabol la vedir: lagrin la, parol Bondie."
Luke8:12 Seki tom dan bor sime, sa bann ki finn tande me lerla diab vini, aras parol dan zot leker pouki zot pa krwar e zot pa sove."
Luke8:13 Seki tom lor ros, sa bann ki tann laparol e zot resevwar li dan lazwa; me zot pena rasinn, zot krwar pou enn letan e kan difikilte vini zot abandonn lafwa."
Luke8:14 Seki tom dan pikan, sa bann ki tande, me kan traka, larises ek plezir lavi vini, li touf zot; zot fri pa mir."
Luke8:15 Seki tom dan bon later, sa bann ki ekout laparol, gard li dan enn leker bon ek onet, e zot raport fri ar pasians ek perseverans."
Luke8:16 “Personn pa alim enn lalanp pou kouver li ar enn vaz, oubien met li anba lili, me li met li lor enn stenn, pouki seki rantre kapav trouv lalimier."
Luke8:17 Tou seki kasiet pou vinn dan lalimier e tou seki sekre pou devwale e pou vinn dan kler.
Luke8:18 Alor fer atansion manier ki zot ekoute parski seki ena pou gagn plis e seki pena, mem seki li krwar li ena, pou ras tou ar li.”"
Luke8:19 Lerla so mama ek so bann frer vinn zwenn li, me zot pa ti reysi koste ar li akoz lafoul."
Luke8:20 Bannla dir li, “To mama ek to bann frer pe dibout deor, zot anvi trouv twa.”"
Luke8:21 Me li reponn zot, “Seki ekout Parol Bondie ek met li anpratik samem mo mama ek mo bann frer.”"
Luke8:22 Enn zour li rant dan enn pirog ar so bann disip, e li dir zot, “Anou al lot kote lak.” E zot ale."
Luke8:23 Lor bato, Zezi gagn somey. Enn koudvan leve lor lak, pirog koumans pran dilo, lerla zot lavi andanze."
Luke8:24 Bannla al lev li, zot kriye, “Met, Met, nou pe mor!” Zezi leve, li menas divan ek gran laoul, lerla gagn enn akalmi."
Luke8:25 Li dir zot, “Kot zot lafwa ete?” Zot gagn per e zot sezi, e sakenn dir ar so kamarad, “Kisannla sa, li komann divan ek dilo, e bannla obeir li?”"
Luke8:26 Lerla zot ariv pei bann Zerazenien, ki vizavi ar Galile."
Luke8:27 Kouma li debarke, enn abitan lavil ki ti posede ar boukou demon vinn zwenn li. Depi lontan li ti finn aret met linz e li pa ti pe res dan lakaz me dan simitier."
Luke8:28 Kan li trouv Zezi, li zet so lekor devan Zezi e li kriye for-for, “Ki to oule ar mwa, Zezi, Garson Bondie Treo? Mo sipliy twa, pa tourmant mwa.”"
Luke8:29 Zezi donn move lespri lord pou sorti lor sa dimoun la. (Enn kantite fwa lespri la ti akapar li; lerla zot ti atas so lame ek so lipie ar lasenn pou tini li, me li ti kas lasenn e demon ti sarye li dan dezer.)"
Luke8:30 Lerla Zezi dimann li, “Ki to nom?” Li reponn, “Lezion,” - parski enn pake demon ti rant dan li."
Luke8:31 Zot sipliy Zezi pouki li pa avoy zot dan pwi-san-fon.
Luke8:32 Be ti ena enn gran troupo koson ki ti pe manze lor kolinn; bann demon la sipliy Zezi pou les zot rant dan bann koson la. Zezi donn zot permision.
Luke8:33 Lerla bann demon la sorti ar li, rant dan bann koson ki ti la, ek troupo la deval lapant, tom dan lak e zot nwaye."
Luke8:34 Letan bann gardien troupo trouv seki finn arive, zot sove zot al rakont sa dan lavil ek dan lakanpagn."
Luke8:35 Lerla bann dimoun vinn gete ki finn arive vremem; letan zot koste ar Zezi zot trouv sa dimoun ki ti posede par demon la, pe asiz kot lipie Zezi, so linz lor li e li sindespri. Lerla zot gagn per."
Luke8:36 Bann ki ti finn trouv sa, rakont lezot kouma posede la ti geri."
Luke8:37 Lerla tou bann abitan dan lezanviron ek bann Zerazenien dimann Zezi kit zot lavil ale parski zot ti gagn enn gran lafreyer. Alors Zezi rant dan pirog e li retourne.
