Luke8:38 Sa dimoun ki demon ti finn kit li la, sipliy Zezi pou res ar li; me Zezi ranvway li. Li dir,"
Luke8:39 “Retourn kot twa, e al rakonte seki Bondie finn fer pou twa.” Li ale, li proklam partou dan lavil seki Zezi inn fer pou li."
Luke8:40 Letan Zezi retourne, lafoul akeyir li parski zot tou ti pe atann li."
Luke8:41 Ala enn sef sinagog ki ti apel Zair vinn get Zezi. Sef la tom dan so lipie e li sipliy Zezi pou vinn kot li.
Luke8:42 Zair ti ena enn sel tifi ki ti ena ape pre douz-an, e li ti pe mor. Letan Zezi ale, lafoul antour li e dimoun ti pe pouse."
Luke8:43 Ti ena enn madam parmi, ki ti ena enn lemorazi ki ti pe minn li depi douz-an. Li ti finn depans tou seki li ti ena ar dokter. Personn pa finn kapav geri li."
Luke8:44 Li vinn deryer Zezi e li tous rebor so linz. Toutswit li aret segne anplas.
Luke8:45 Zezi dir, “Kisannla finn tous mwa?” Tou dimoun res trankil, lerla Pier dir li, “Met, enn gro lafoul pe antour twa e dimoun pe pouse.”"
Luke8:46 Zezi dir, “Kikenn finn tous mwa. Mo kone enn lafors finn sorti dan mwa.”"
Luke8:47 Letan madam la trouve ki finn dekouver li, li gagn tranbleman, li tom dan lipie Zezi e li dir devan tou dimoun kifer li ti finn tous Zezi e kouma li finn geri toutswit."
Luke8:48 Zezi dir li, “Mo tifi, to lafwa finn sov twa; al anpe.”"
Luke8:49 Letan Zezi pe dir sa, enn dimoun sorti lakaz sef sinagog e dir li, “To tifi finn mor, pa deranz Met plis ki sa.”"
Luke8:50 Me letan Zezi tann sa, li dir Zair, “Pa per, zis krwar e to tifi pou sove.”"
Luke8:51 Letan Zezi ariv lakaz Zair, li pa les personn rant ansam ar li, zis Pier, Zan, Zak, papa ek mama tifi la osi."
Luke8:52 Tou dimoun ti pe plore, e kriye, akoz tifi la. Me Zezi dir zot, “Pa plore. Tifi la pa finn mor, li zis pe dormi.”"
Luke8:53 Me zot riy li, parski zot kone ki tifi la finn fini mor."
Luke8:54 Zezi pran lame tifi la e dir li, “Zennfi, leve!”"
Luke8:55 Lespri tifi la retourne, e li leve deswit. Zezi dimann bannla donn li kiksoz pou manze."
Luke8:56 Bann fami tifi la ti etone; me Zezi donn zot lord pa dir personn ki finn arive.
Luke9:1 Zezi apel Ledouz e li donn zot pouvwar ek lotorite pou sas tou bann demon e pou geri tou bann maladi.
Luke9:2 Li avoy zot al proklam Rwayom Bondie e al geri bann malad.
Luke9:3 Li dir zot, “Pa pran nanye pou zot vwayaz, okenn baton, ni sak, ni dipin, ni larzan, mem pa enn semiz anplis."
Luke9:4 Kan zot rant dan enn lakaz, res lamem, ziska ki zot kit landrwa la."
Luke9:5 La kot pa akeyir zot, tap zot lipie, tir tou lapousier letan zot kit lavil la. Li pou enn temwagnaz kont bannla."
Luke9:6 Ledouz sorti ale; zot al dan bann vilaz, zot amenn Bonn Nouvel laba e zot geri bann malad partou kot zot pase."
Luke9:7 Erod, lerwa Galile, ti pe tann tou seki ti pe pase, e li pa ti pe konpran parski ena ti pe dir ki Zan finn resisite,"
Luke9:8 ena ti pe dir Eli finn aparet, e lezot ti pe dir, li enn parmi bann ansien profet ki finn releve."
Luke9:9 Erod dir, “Mo finn dekapit Zan; me ki sa dimoun lor ki mo pe tann tou sa bann koze la?” Alor li ti pe anvi zwenn Zezi."
Luke9:10 Letan bann apot retourne, zot rakont Zezi tou seki zot finn fer. Li pran zot, e li amenn zot apar dan lavil Betsaida."
Luke9:11 Kan lafoul ti konn sa, zot ti swiv li; li ti akeyir zot, li ti koz ar zot lor Rwayom Bondie, e li ti geri bann ki ti bizin geri."
Luke9:12 Lazourne ti pe al fini e Ledouz vinn ar Zezi, zot dir li, “Fer lafoul la ale, pouki zot al dan bann vilaz ek bann laferm dan landrwa, pou gagn enn plas pou manze ek dormi; parski nou lwin ar tou isi.”"
Luke9:13 Me li dir zot, “Donn bannla manze zotmem.” Zot reponn, “Nou ena zis sink dipin ek de pwason - amwin ki nou al aste manze pou tou sa bann dimoun la.”"
Luke9:14 Ti ena apepre sink mil zom. Li dir ar so bann disip, “Fer bannla asiz par group sinkant.”"
Luke9:15 Lerla zot fer tou dimoun asize.
Luke9:16 Zezi pran sink dipin ek de pwason la, li lev so lizie, li get lesiel, li beni zot, li kas zot, e li donn so bann disip pou distribie ar lafoul."
Luke9:17 Tou dimoun manze ziska vant plin. Zot ramas douz panie ranpli ar bout-bout dipin ki ti finn reste.
Luke9:18 Zezi ti pe priye tousel e ti ena zis so bann disip ki ti la; li dimann zot, “Ki dimoun dir mo ete?”"
Luke9:19 Zot reponn, “Zan Batis; me ena dir, Eli; e lezot dir ki to enn parmi bann ansien profet ki finn resisite.”"
Luke9:20 Li dir so bann disip, “Me zot, ki zot dir mo ete?” Pier reponn, “Tomem Mesi Bondie.”"
Luke9:21 Lerla li donn zot lord pa dir sa personn.
Luke9:22 Li dir, “Garson Limanite bizin soufer boukou, bann ansien, bann sef pret e bann dokter lalwa pou rezet li, zot pou touy li, lor trwaziem zour li pou resisite.”"
Luke9:23 Apre sa li dir zot tou, “Si kikenn anvi swiv mwa, li bizin aret pans zis limem, pran so lakrwa toulezour e swiv mwa."
Luke9:24 Seki anvi sov so lavi, pou perdi li; seki perdi so lavi akoz mwa, pou sov li."
Luke9:25 Kiserti enn dimoun gagn lemonn antie pouki apre li perdi limem oubien detrir so lavi?
Luke9:26 Seki gagn onte akoz mwa ek akoz mo parol, Garson Limanite pou ont li, kan li pou vinn dan so laglwar, dan laglwar so Papa ek bann anz ki sin."
Luke9:27 Me laverite mo dir zot, ena parmi zot ki pa pou konn lamor avan ki zot trouv Rwayom Bondie.”"
Luke9:28 Wit zour apre ki Zezi ti finn dir sa bann parol la, li ti pran Pier, Zan ek Zak e li ti mont lor montagn pou al priye."
Luke9:29 Letan li pe priye, so figir sanze e so linz vinn enn blan ki kas lizie."
Luke9:30 Ennselkout de dimoun ti pe koz ar li: Moiz ek Eli.
Luke9:31 Zot aparet dan laglwar, e zot pe koz lor so depar ki ti pre pou realize dan Zerizalem."
Luke9:32 Pier ek so bann kamarad ti dan enn profon somey; letan zot leve, zot trouv laglwar Zezi ek sa de ki ti ar li la."
Luke9:33 Letan sa de la kit Zezi, Pier dir li, “Met, li bon nou isi; anou dres trwa latant, enn pou twa, enn pou Moiz ek enn pou Eli.” Me li pa ti kone ki li ti pe dir."
Luke9:34 Kan li ti pe koze, enn niaz ti vinn kouver zot; zot ti gagn per letan niaz la anvlop zot."
Luke9:35 Enn lavwa sorti dan niaz, dir, “Samem mo Garson ki mo finn swazir. Ekout li!”"
Luke9:36 Letan lavwa la aret koze, zot nek trouv Zezi tousel. Sa lepok la, zot ti res trankil, zot pa ti rakont personn seki zot ti trouve."
Luke9:37 Landime, zot desann depi montagn, enn gran lafoul vinn zwenn Zezi."
Luke9:38 Ala ki enn boug dan lafoul kriye, “Met, mo sipliye twa vinn get mo garson, mo sel piti;"
Luke9:39 enn kout lespri sezi piti la; piti la irle, li gagn konvilsion, li kime e lespri la maltret li, sakouy li e larg li avek difikilte."
Luke9:40 Mo finn sipliy to bann disip pou sas sa lespri la, me zot pa finn kapav fer nanye.”"
Luke9:41 Zezi dir, “Ziska kan mo pou res ar zot, pou siport zot, zenerasion san lafwa ranpli ar mesanste? Amenn to garson isi.”"
Luke9:42 Letan garson la vini, demon la zet li ater, sakouy-sakouy li. Me Zezi menas lespri inpir la, geri garson la e retourn li so papa."
Luke9:43 Zot tou ti inpresione par grander inkonparab Bondie. Alor ki zot tou ti pe emerveye par tou seki li pe ti fer, li dir so bann disip,"
Luke9:44 “Les sa parol la rant bien dan zot zorey: Garson Limanite pou livre dan lame bann zom.”
Luke9:45 Me zot pa ti konpran sa parol la; li ti res flou dan zot latet pouki zot pa konpran. Zot ti gagn per pou poz li kestion lor sa size la.
Luke9:46 Bann disip koumans diskite kisannla pli gran parmi zot.
Luke9:47 Me Zezi ti konn zot panse. Alors li pran enn zanfan, li plas li pre ar li"
Luke9:48 e li dir zot, “Dimoun ki akeyir sa zanfan la lor mo nom, pe akeyir momem, e seki akeyir mwa pe akeyir Sa-Enn ki finn avoy mwa la; parski pli tipti parmi zot tou, limem pli gran.”"
Luke9:49 Zan pran laparol, “Met, nou finn trouv enn dimoun pe servi to nom pou pous demon, nou finn anpes li, parski li pa dan mem group ki nou.”"
Luke9:50 Me Zezi dir li, “Pa anpes li, parski seki pa kont twa, li ar twa.”"
Luke9:51 Letan ler ti pe arive kot Zezi pou kit lemonn, li ti met latet devan pou mont Zerizalem."
Luke9:52 Li avoy bann mesaze devan li. Bannla rant dan enn vilaz Samaritin pou prepar so larive.
Luke9:53 Me bann abitan sa vilaz la refiz akeyir li parski li ti pe monte pou al Zerizalem.
Luke9:54 Letan Zak ek Zan trouv sa, zot dir, “Segner, to oule nou fer dife sort dan lesiel tom lor zot pou detrir zot?”"
Luke9:55 Zezi vire get zot, e li menas zot."
Luke9:56 Lerla zot al dan enn lot vilaz.
Luke9:57 Lor larout enn dimoun dir Zezi, “Mo pou swiv twa partou kot to ale.”"
Luke9:58 Zezi dir li, “Renar ena lakaz pou reste, zwazo dan lesiel ena so nik, me Garson Limanite pena enn plas pou poz so latet.”"
Luke9:59 Zezi dir enn lot, “Swiv mwa.” Me li reponn, “Segner, les mwa anter mo papa avan.”"
Luke9:60 Me Zezi dir li, “Les bann mor anter bann mor; twa, al anons Rwayom Bondie.”"
Luke9:61 Enn lot dir li, “Mo pou swiv twa, Segner, me les mo al dir orevwar mo fami avan.”"
Luke9:62 Zezi dir li, “Seki pe labour later e get par deryer, li pa dign pou Rwayom Bondie.”"
Luke10:1 Apre sa Lesegner swazir swasann-dis lezot disip, e li avoy zot de par de devan li dan tou lavil e tou plas kot li ti ena lintansion pou ale."
Luke10:2 Li dir zot, “Rannman boukou dan karo me zouvrie tigit; priye Propriyeter karo pouki li avoy zouvrie dan so karo."
Luke10:3 Ale! Mo avoy zot parey kouma bann timouton parmi loulou.
Luke10:4 Pa pran ni kas, ni sak, ni soulie ar zot. E pa arete lor sime pou pran nouvel ar long-long konversasion."
Luke10:5 Kan zot rant dan enn lakaz, dir avan, ‘Shalom, lape dan sa lakaz la!’"
Luke10:6 Si lape res dan enn dimoun dan sa lakaz la, zot lape pou repoz lor li; sinon repran zot lape."
Luke10:7 Alor res dan sa lakaz la, manze e bwar seki donn zot, parski enn zouvrie merit so saler."
Luke10:8 Kan zot rant dan enn lavil ki akeyir zot, manz seki met devan zot;"
Luke10:9 geri bann malad sa lavil la e dir so bann abitan, ‘Rwayom Bondie finn vinn pre ar zot.’"
Luke10:10 Me si zot rant dan enn lavil ki pa akeyir zot, al partou lor gran sime e dir,"
Luke10:11 ‘Nou sakouy nou lipie pou tir tou lapousier zot lavil ki finn tas dan nou sandalet; me zot bizin kone ki Rwayom Bondie finn koste ar zot.’
Luke10:12 Mo dir zot, zour zizman pou mwin dir ar Sodom ki ar sa lavil la."
Luke10:13 Bienmalere Korazin! Bienmalere Betsaida! Si mirak ki finn fer kot zot, ti fer osi dan Tir ek Sidon, lontan so bann abitan ti pou repanti, ti pou met linz dey, e ti pou asiz dan lasann."
Luke10:14 Akoz sa, pou mwin dir ar Tir ek Sidon kan zour zizman pou vini."
Luke10:15 E twa Kafarnaom, to krwar to pou mont lao ziska dan lesiel? Non, pou desann twa ziska dan lanfer."
Luke10:16 Seki ekout zot, ekout mwa; seki rezet zot, rezet mwa, e seki rezet mwa, rezet Sa-Enn ki finn avoy mwa la.”"
Luke10:17 Bann swasann-dis disip retourne dan lazwa, e zot dir Zezi, “Segner, mem bann demon soumet kan nou servi to nom!”"
Luke10:18 Zezi reponn zot, “Mo finn trouv Satan tonbe kouma zekler depi lesiel."
Luke10:19 Ekoute, mo finn donn zot lotorite pou mars lor serpan, lor skorpion e lor lennmi ki bien for; nanye pa kapav fer zot dimal."
Luke10:20 Pa gagn lazwa akoz bann lespri soumet devan zot, me gagn lazwa parski zot nom finn anrezistre dan lesiel.”"
Luke10:21 Lerlamem, Zezi, ranpli dan lazwa Lespri Sin dir, “Papa, Segner lesiel ek later, mo remersie twa parski to finn fer bann tipti konn kiksoz ki to finn kasiet bann saz ek bann intelizan. Wi, papa, samem to volonte."
Luke10:22 Mo Papa finn remet tou kiksoz dan mo lame. Personn pa konn so Garson, exsepte Papa la, e personn pa konn Papa la exsepte so Garson e dimoun ar ki Garson la anvi revel so Papa."
Luke10:23 Lerla Zezi koz ar so disip anprive, “Bienere lizie ki trouv seki zot pe trouve!"
Luke10:24 Krwar mwa mo dir zot, boukou profet ek lerwa finn anvi trouv seki zot pe trouve, e zot pa finn trouve, e pou tann seki zot pe tande, e zot pa finn tande.”"
Luke10:25 Enn dokter lalwa vinn get Zezi pou may li dan enn piez, li dir, “Met, ki mo bizin fer pou gagn lavi eternel?”"
Luke10:26 Zezi dir li, “Ki finn ekrir dan lalwa? Ki to lir?”"
Luke10:27 Li reponn, “To bizin kontan Lesegner to Bondie ar tou to leker, tou to lam, tou to lafors, tou to lespri e to prosin kouma tomem.”"
Luke10:28 Alors Zezi dir li, “To finn bien reponn. Fer sa, e to pou gagn lavi.”"
Luke10:29 Me kouma dokter lalwa la ti anvi montre ki li enn dimoun drwat, li dimann Zezi, “Kisannla mo prosin?”"
Luke10:30 Zezi reponn, “Enn dimoun sorti Zerizalem e li ti pe desann Zeriko. Bann voler atak li, kokin tou seki li ena, zot bat li, zot sove, e zot les li demi-mor."
Luke10:31 Par sans, enn pret pas par la me letan li trouv li, li pas lot kote."
Luke10:32 Parey pou enn Levit; letan li trouv li, li pas lot kote."
Luke10:33 Me enn Samaritin ki ti anvwayaz, ler li ariv pre ar sa dimoun la e kan li trouv so leta, so leker fermal."
Luke10:34 Li al get blese la, li fer enn pansman e li vers delwil ek divin lor so dimal. Lerla li met blese la lor so bourik, li amenn li dan enn ti lotel e li kontigne swagn li."
Luke10:35 Landime, li tir larzan dan so pos, valer de zourne travay e li donn propriyeter lotel la. Li dir li, ‘Okip li bien, e ninport ki depans to fer anplis mo pou ranbours twa letan mo retourne.’"
Luke10:36 Dapre twa, kisannla parmi sa trwa la finn azir kouma enn prosin pou sa dimoun ki voler finn atake la?”"
Luke10:37 Dokter lalwa la reponn Zezi, “Be dimoun ki finn pran li kont la.” Zezi dir li, “Ale, al fer parey.”"
Luke10:38 Letan zot pe marse, zot rant dan enn vilaz, e enn fam ki apel Mart akeyir Zezi dan so lakaz."
Luke10:39 So ser ki ti apel Marie vinn asiz kot lipie Zezi pou ekout so parol.
Luke10:40 Me Mart ti pe ale-vini pou servi. Li al get Zezi, li dir, “Sa pa fer twa nanye ki mo ser les mwa tousel pou servi? Dir li vinn donn enn koudme.”"
Luke10:41 Lesegner reponn li, “Mart, Mart, to pran traka e to azite pou enn kantite kiksoz,"
Luke10:42 me enn sel neseser. Marie finn swazir meyer par, pa pou retir sa ar li.”"
Luke11:1 Zezi ti pe priye kikpar. Letan li fini, enn so bann disip dir, “Segner, montre nou kouma priye, parey kouma Zan finn montre so bann disip.”"
Luke11:2 Lerla li dir zot, “Kan zot priye, dir: Papa, ki to nom sanktifie; fer to regn vini."
Luke11:3 Donn nou sak zour dipin ki nou bizin.
Luke11:4 Pardonn nou nou pese, parey kouma nou pardonn bann seki ofans nou. Pa les nou tom dan tantasion.”"
Luke11:5 Zezi redir zot, “Si enn zot kamarad vinn kot zot omilie lanwit e dir zot, ‘Kamarad, pret mwa trwa dipin ar twa.’"
Luke11:6 Mo kamarad ki sorti an vwayaz inn vinn kot mwa e mo pena nanye pou ofer li.
Luke11:7 Si seki dan lakaz la reponn, ‘Pa deranz mwa, mo finn fini met lakle dan laport, mo bann zanfan ek mwa lor lili e mo pa kapav leve pou donn twa dipin.’"
Luke11:8 Mo dir zot, mem si li pa leve par amitie pou so kamarad, li pou leve pou donn so kamarad tou seki li bizin akoz toupe ki li ena pou insiste."
Luke11:9 Mwa, mo dir zot: dimande, zot pou gagne; rode, zot pou trouve; tape, laport pou ouver pou zot."
Luke11:10 Seki dimande pou gagne, seki rode pou trouve, e seki tape, laport pou ouver pou li."
Luke11:11 Ki papa parmi zot, si so zanfan dimann li enn pwason, pou donn li enn serpan?"
Luke11:12 Oubien si li dimann enn dizef, pou donn li enn skorpion?"
Luke11:13 Move kouma zot move, zot konn donn bon kiksoz zot zanfan; aster mazine komie plis ankor, zot Papa dan lesiel pou fer kado Lespri Sin seki dimann li.”"
Luke11:14 Zezi ti pe sas enn demon ki ti rann enn dimoun miye. Kan demon la kit li, miye la koze, e bann dimoun ti emerveye."
Luke11:15 Ena parmi zot ti pe dir, “Li sas demon par Belzeboul, prins demon.”"
Luke11:16 Me lezot pou teste li, dimann li enn sign ki vinn depi lesiel."
Luke11:17 Me kouma Zezi ti konn zot panse, li dir zot, “Si ena divizion dan enn rwayom, rwayom la pou tonbe; si ena divizion dan enn lakaz, lakaz la pou tonbe."
Luke11:18 Si Satan lager ar Satan, kouma so rwayom pou tini dibout? E zot, zot pe dir ki mo sas demon par Belzeboul."
Luke11:19 Me si mwa mo sas demon par Belzeboul, par kisannla zot disip sas demon? Bannla mem pou ziz zot."
Luke11:20 Me si mo sas demon par lame Bondie, savedir Rwayom Bondie finn vinn kot zot."
Luke11:21 Kan enn zom for e bien arme pe vey so prop lakaz, so dibien an sekirite."
Luke11:22 Me kan enn pli for vinn atak li e bat li, seki pli for la pran bann zarm dan ki lotla ti ena konfians, e li partaz so bann dibien."
Luke11:23 Seki pa ar mwa, kont mwa; seki pa rasanble ar mwa, kre divizion."
Luke11:24 Kan move lespri sorti dan enn dimoun, li travers bann landrwa kot pena dilo pou rod enn plas pou repoze; si li pa trouv nanye li dir, ‘Mo retourn lakaz kot mo finn sorti.’"
Luke11:25 Kan li retourne li trouv lakaz la bien balye e bann zafer bien ranze.
Luke11:26 Lerla li al rod set lespri pli move ki li, e zot rant dan lakaz la e zot instal zot. Leta dimoun la vinn pli pir ki avan.”"
Luke11:27 Kouma li fini dir sa, enn fam dan lafoul kriye, “Bienerez fam ki finn sarye twa e ki finn donn twa bwar!”"
Luke11:28 Me Zezi reponn li, “Bienere plito seki ekout laparol Bondie e obeir li!”"
Luke11:29 Letan lafoul ti pe grosi, Zezi koumans dir, “Sa zenerasion la, enn zenerasion move. Li dimann enn sign, me okenn sign li pa pou gagne, apar sign Zonas."
Luke11:30 Parey kouma Zonas ti enn sign pou bann abitan Niniv, parey Garson Limanite pou enn sign pou sa zenerasion la."
Luke11:31 Zour zizman, larenn Seba ki sorti lesid, pou lev devan dimoun sa zenerasion la e li pou kondann zot; parski li finn sorti bien-bien lwin pou vinn ekout sazes Salomon. E isi ena pli gran ki Salomon."
Luke11:32 Bann dimoun Niniv pou leve zour zizman devan sa zenerasion la e pou kondann li, parski bannla ti repanti letan zot ti tann predikasion Zonas. E isi ena pli gran ki Zonas."
Luke11:33 Personn pa alim enn lalanp pou kasiet li oubien pou met li anba enn seo; okontrer li met li lor enn stenn, pouki tou seki rantre trouv lalimier."
Luke11:34 To lizie lalimier to lekor; kan to lizie bon tou to lekor eklere; me si to lizie pa bon, tou to lekor dan marenwar."
Luke11:35 Alors, pran kont, tansion lalimier ki dan twa, anverite teneb sa."
Luke11:36 Si tou to lekor dan lalimier, san ki enn parti dan teneb, tou to lekor pou briye parey kouma enn lalanp ki ekler twa avek so lekleraz."
Luke11:37 Kan Zezi fini koze, enn Farizien invit li pou dezene. Zezi rant kot li e asiz atab."
Luke11:38 Farizien la ti soke parski Zezi pa ti lav so lame avan li manze.
Luke11:39 Lerla Lesegner dir li, “Ala kouma zot ete bann Farizien. Zot netway andeor zot koup ek zot lasiet bien prop, me andan zot ranpli ar lespri rapas ek mesanste."
Luke11:40 Bann tilespri! Eski Bondie ki finn fer andeor, li pa finn fer osi seki andan?"
Luke11:41 Donn bann pov rises ki ena dan zot koup; lerla, tou pou vinn prop."
Luke11:42 Maler lor zot bann Farizien! Zot donn enn diziem prodwi zot zardin kouma lamant, kotomili e tou kalite legim; me zot bliye lazistis ek lamour Bondie; pourtan samem ki zot ti bizin fer san bliye leres."
Luke11:43 Maler lor zot bann Farizien! Zot kontan bann premie plas dan sinagog e zot kontan loner lor laplas piblik.
Luke11:44 Maler lor zot! Zot parey kouma bann tom ki dimoun pa remarke, e lor ki zot marse san kone!”"
Luke11:45 Enn dokter lalwa dir li, “Met, kan to koz koumsa to pe ofans nou!”"
Luke11:46 Zezi reponn li, “Maler lor zot osi bann dokter lalwa! Zot dimann dimoun sarye bann fardo bien lour, me zot, zot mem pa lev zot ti ledwa pou donn enn koudme sarye sa pwa la."
Luke11:47 Maler lor zot! Zot konstrir tom pou bann profet ki zot anset finn touye.
Luke11:48 Savedir, zot pe montre ki zot dakor ar seki zot bann gran dimoun finn fer, parski bannla ti touy bann profet, e zot, zot konstrir tom pou bann profet la."
Luke11:49 Akoz samem Bondie dan so gran sazes finn dir, ‘Mo pou avoy bann profet ek bann apot kot zot; ena zot pou touye, ena zot pou persekite.’"
Luke11:50 Lakoz sa, zot pou pini pou disan bann profet ki finn koule depi kreasion lemonn ziska zordi -"
Luke11:51 depi lamor Abel ziska lamor Zakari ki finn perdi lavi ant lotel sakrifis ek sanktyer. Vremem, mo dir zot, sa zenerasion la pou pey tousala."
Luke11:52 Maler lor zot, dokter lalwa! Zot finn aras lakle konesans me zotmem zot pa rantre, e zot anpes lezot osi rantre."
Luke11:53 Kan Zezi sorti la ale, bann dokter lalwa e bann Farizien move ankoler e zot bonbard li ar kestion."
Luke11:54 Zot ti pe rod tou sort manier pou kwins li ar so prop parol.
Luke12:1 Ti ena telman enn gran lafoul ki dimoun ti pe mars lor lipie zot kamarad. Lerla Zezi koumans dir ar so bann disip, “Fer atansion levin bann Farizien, setadir, zot ipokrizi."
Luke12:2 Tou seki kasiet pou vinn dan kler e tou seki sekre pou devwale.
Luke12:3 Akoz samem tou seki zot dir dan nwar, dimoun pou tann li dan kler, seki zot mirmire dan zorey anprive, dimoun pou kriye li for-for lao lor lakaz."
Luke12:4 Ala mo dir zot, mo bann kamarad, pa per seki kapav detrir lekor, e pa kapav fer plis ki sa."
Luke12:5 Mo pou montre zot kisannla zot bizin per: gagn per Sa-Enn ki non selman kapav detrir zot me ena osi pouvwar pou zet zot dan lanfer. Wi, mo dir zot, Sennala ki zot bizin gagn per."
Luke12:6 Eski pa vann sink mwano pou de sou? Pourtan, Bondie pa bliye enn sel ladan."
Luke12:7 Me zot, tou brin seve lor zot latet inn konte. Pa per, zot ena plis valer ki tou mwano."
Luke12:8 Mo dir zot, tou seki rekonet mwa devan dimoun, Garson Limanite pou rekonet li devan bann anz Bondie."
Luke12:9 Me seki renie mwa devan dimoun, Garson Limanite pou renie li devan anz Bondie."
Luke12:10 Seki dir enn parol kont Garson Limanite pou gagn pardon; me seki blasfem kont Lespri Sin, pa pou gagn pardon."
Luke12:11 Kan amenn zot dan sinagog devan bann dirizan ek bann lotorite, pa trakase kouma zot pou defann zot e kouma zot pou reponn,"
Luke12:12 parski Lespri Sin pou montre zot dan sa ler la ki pou dir.
Luke12:13 Kikenn dan lafoul dir Zezi, “Met, dir mo frer donn mwa mo par leritaz.”"
Luke12:14 Me Zezi dir li, “Kamarad, kisannla finn nom mwa pou zize ek pou partaz zot dibien?”"
Luke12:15 Lerla li dir zot, “Fer atansion! Pa galoup deryer bann dibien materyel, parski lavi enn dimoun pa depann lor so dibien, mem si li bien ris.”"
Luke12:16 Zezi rakont enn parabol. “Enn dimoun ris ti ena enn plantasion ki ti raport boukou.
Luke12:17 Li dir ar limem, ‘Ki mo pou fer? Mo pena plas pou ramas mo rekolt."
Luke12:18 Be, ala seki mo pou fer: mo pou demoli mo bann grenie, mo pou mont bann pli gran kot mo pou ramas tou mo rekolt e tou mo lezot dibien."
Luke12:19 Lerla mo pou dir ar momem, Kamarad, to ena boukou dibien anrezerv pou boukou lane; repoz twa, manze, bwar, diverti.’"
Luke12:20 Me Bondie dir li, ‘Kouma to bet koumsa! Zordi swar mem to pou perdi to lavi; kisannla pou erit tou seki to finn ramase?’"
Luke12:21 Ala seki pou ariv dimoun ki ramas dibien zis pou li, me ki pa ramas rises kot Bondie.”"
Luke12:22 Li dir so bann disip, “Ala kifer mo dir zot, fode pa zot trakase ar seki bizin manze pou viv, oubien ar linz ki zot bizin pou zot lekor."
Luke12:23 Lavi pli inportan ki manze, e lekor pli inportan ki linz."
Luke12:24 Get bann korbo, zot pa seme e zot pa rekolte; zot pena ni stor ni grenie, e pourtan Bondie nouri zot. Zot, zot ena plis valer ki zwazo!"
Luke12:25 Eski traka ki to pran ar to lavi, pou fer li vinn pli long?"
Luke12:26 Si zot pena pouvwar lor enn ti kiksoz koumsa, kifer zot trakase pou tou leres?"
Luke12:27 Get kouma bann fler dan karo pouse; zot pa travay, zot pa koud linz. Pourtan, mem Salomon dan tou so laglwar pa ti ena zoli linz kouma sa bann fler la."
Luke12:28 Si Bondie abiy lerb ki zordi dan karo ek dime pe brile, kalkile komie li pou abiy zot. Zot lafwa vremem tipti."
Luke12:29 Pa kas latet pou rode ki pou manze, ki pou bwar."
Luke12:30 Se bann ki pa krwar dan Bondie ki rod sa bann kiksoz la; me zot, zot Papa kone ki zot bizin."
Luke12:31 Rod plito Rwayom Bondie, e zot pou resevwar tou leres."
Luke12:32 Pa gagn per, ti troupo, parski Bondie kontan pou donn zot so Rwayom."
Luke12:33 Vann zot dibien e donn bann pov; ranpli zot kof ar rises ki pa pou fini; ramas rises ki dan lesiel e ki pa pou disparet; parski kot sa ete, voler pa kapav koste e karya pa kapav manze."
Luke12:34 La kot leker ete, lamem zot rises pou ete."
Luke12:35 Pare e gard zot lalanp alime.
Luke12:36 Zot bizin kouma bann dimoun ki pe atann zot met retourne apre enn maryaz; kouma li tap laport, zot fini pare pou ouver."
Luke12:37 Bienere bann serviter ki zot met pou trouv dibout kan li rantre. Laverite mo dir zot, li pou tir so palto, fer zot asiz atab, e li pou servi zot."
Luke12:38 Si li vini damilie lanwit, oubien boner gramatin e li trouv zot lamem, bienere sa bann serviter la!"
Luke12:39 Ala seki zot bizin kone: si propriyeter lakaz ti kone ki ler voler ti pou vini, li pa ti pou les li rant dan so lakaz."
Luke12:40 Zot osi zot bizin pare, parski ler ki Garson Limanite pou vini personn pa pou atann.”"
Luke12:41 Pier dir, “Segner, to pe rakont sa parabol la pou nou tousel oubien pou tou dimoun?”"
Luke12:42 Lesegner reponn, “Ki sa administrater fidel ek bien serye ki finn gagn responsabilite ar so met pou vey lor so bann serviter e gete si zot gagn zot par manze dan ler?"
Luke12:43 Bienere serviter ki ankor pe travay ler so met retourne.
Luke12:44 Laverite mo dir zot, li pou donn li responsabilite lor tou so dibien."
Luke12:45 Me si serviter la dir, ‘Mo met pe tarde pou retourne,’ e li koumans bat bann servant ek bann serviter, li manze, li bwar e li sou, ki pou arive!"
Luke12:46 So met pou retourne zour ki li pa pe atann, ler ki li pa kone, pou koup-koup li e pou konsider li kouma enn dane."
Luke12:47 Serviter ki ti konn volonte so met, me ki pa finn prepar li, ni mem fer dapre volonte met la, pou gagn enn move bate."
Luke12:48 Me, seki pa ti kone, e finn fer kiksoz ki merit enn pinision, pou gagn enn ti pinision mem. Tou seki finn resevwar boukou, pou dimann li boukou; seki finn gagn boukou responsabilite, pou reklam li ankor plis."
Luke12:49 Mo finn vini pou aport enn dife lor later; mo ti a voudre ki li finn deza alime.
Luke12:50 Mo bizin plonz dan enn batem e mo resanti enn gran soufrans avan ki sa arive.
Luke12:51 Eski zot panse mo finn vinn lor later pou amenn lape? Non, mo dir zot; pa lape, me divizion."
Luke12:52 Depi asterla, dan enn lakaz kot ena sink dimoun zot pou ena divizion, trwa kont de e de kont trwa,"
Luke12:53 papa kont garson, garson kont papa; mama kont tifi, tifi kont mama; belmer kont belfi, belfi kont belmer."
Luke12:54 Zezi dir lafoul, “Kan zot trouv niaz leve dan lwes, deswit zot dir, ‘Lapli pou tonbe’; samem ki arive."
Luke12:55 Kan divan lesid soufle zot dir, ‘Pou fer so,’ samem ki arive."
Luke12:56 Ipokrit! Zot konpran ki pase lor later ek dan lesiel e zot konn dir ki letan pou fer me kifer zot pa konn interpret seki pe pase zordi?
Luke12:57 Kifer zot pa servi zot prop lespri pou fer enn zizman lor meyer fason azir?
Luke12:58 Letan to pe al kot mazistra avek dimoun ki pe akiz twa la, fer manier tom enn laranzman ar li lor sime mem; sinon li pou trenn twa devan ziz, ziz pou met twa dan lame lapolis, e lapolis pou zet twa dan prizon."
Luke12:59 Ala mo dir twa, to pa pou sorti ladan tanki to pa fini pey tou to det ziska dernie sou."
Luke13:1 Detrwa dimoun vinn rakont Zezi kouma Pilat finn masakre bann Galileen ki ti pe ofer sakrifis.
Luke13:2 Zezi reponn zot, “Eski zot panse ki sa bann Galileen la pli gran peser ki tou lezot Galileen parski zot finn soufer koumsa?"
Luke13:3 Mo dir zot, pa ditou! Me si zot pa repanti, zot pou mor parey."
Luke13:4 Ki zot panse lor latour Siloe ki finn kraz lor dizwit dimoun e finn touy zot tou? Eski zot krwar ki bannla ti pli koupab ki tou lezot abitan Zerizalem?
Luke13:5 Mo dir zot, pa ditou! Me si zot pa repanti, zot pou mor parey."
Luke13:6 Zezi rakont enn parabol, “Enn dimoun ti plant enn pie fig dan enn karo rezin. Li vinn rod fri lor so pie fig me li pa gagn nanye."
Luke13:7 Li dir ar planter rezin la, ‘Get sa, sa fer trwa-zan ki mo finn rod fri lor sa pie fig la me mo pa gagn nanye. Koup li. Kifer li bar plas pou nanye?’"
Luke13:8 Me li reponn propriyeter la, ‘Misie, donn li enn sans sa lane la ankor. Mo pou bim later la e mo pou met fimie ar li."
Luke13:9 Lerla li pou raporte lane prosenn. Sinon nou ava koup li.’ ”
Luke13:10 Zezi ti pe ansegne dan sinagog enn zour saba.
Luke13:11 Ti ena la, enn madam ki ti ena enn infirmite pandan dizwit-an akoz enn move lespri. Li ti kourbe e li pa ti kapav dres drwat."
Luke13:12 Letan Zezi trouv li, li apel madam la e li dir li, “Fam, to finn delivre depi to maladi.”"
Luke13:13 Zezi poz lame lor li, e toutswit madam la redrese e li glorifie Bondie."
Luke13:14 Me sef sinagog ti ankoler parski Zezi ti fer sa gerizon la enn zour saba. Alors li dir, “Ena sis zour pou travay; vinn rod gerizon dan sa bann zour la, me pa zour saba.”"
Luke13:15 Alor Zezi dir li, “Ipokrit! Eski zour saba, zot pa larg zot toro oubien zot bourik depi dan lekiri pou amenn li bwar dilo deor?"
Luke13:16 Eski zour saba, pa ti bizin liber sa madam la, ki enn tifi Abraam, e ki Satan finn atase pandan dizwit-an?”"
Luke13:17 Letan li dir sa, tou so bann adverser perdi lafas. Tou bann dimoun ti dan lazwa akoz bann mervey ki Zezi ti pe fer."
Luke13:18 Zezi dir, “Kouma Rwayom Bondie ete, ek ar ki mo kapav konpar li?"
Luke13:19 Li parey kouma enn lagrin moutard ki enn dimoun finn pran pou plant dan so zardin. Li grandi e li vinn gran kouma enn pie. Lerla bann zwazo dan lesiel vinn fer zot nik dan so brans.”
Luke13:20 Zezi rakont ankor, “Ar ki mo pou konpar Rwayom Bondie?"
Luke13:21 Li parey kouma levin ki enn fam inn pran e finn azout avek trwa goble lafarinn pou fer lapat la monte.”
Luke13:22 Zezi ti pe travers lavil ek vilaz e li ti pe al dan direksion Zerizalem. Lor larout li ti pe ansegne.
Luke13:23 Enn dimoun dimann li, “Segner eski pou ena enn tigit dimoun mem ki pou sove?” Li reponn zot,"
Luke13:24 “Fer tou zot posib pou rant par ti laport parski boukou pou rod rantre me zot pa pou kapav.
Luke13:25 Kan propriyeter lakaz leve e ferm laport, zot pou deor. Zot ava bon tape e zot ava bon dir, ‘Segner, ouver laport pou nou,’ li pou reponn zot, ‘Mo pa kone kot zot sorti.’"
Luke13:26 Alors, zot pou dir li, ‘Nou finn manze-bwar ar twa; to finn ansegn nou lor laplas piblik.’"
Luke13:27 Li pou redir zot, ‘Zot tou ki komet lemal, mo pa kone kot zot sorti. Sorti devan mwa ale.’"
Luke13:28 Laba pou ena plore, kriye, e ledan pou grinse, letan zot pou trouv Abraam, Izaak, Zakob ek tou bann profet dan Rwayom Bondie alor ki zot, pou zet zot deor."
Luke13:29 Dimoun pou sorti depi les ek lwes, depi lenor ek lesid, e zot pou asiz atab dan Rwayom Bondie."
Luke13:30 Marke garde, ena dernie pou vinn premie, ena premie pou vinn dernie.”"
Luke13:31 Sa moman la, detrwa Farizien vinn get Zezi pou dir li, “Ale pa res la, parski Erod pe rod touy twa.”"
Luke13:32 Zezi dir zot, “Al dir sa renar la, ‘Gete, mo pe pous demon e mo pe fer gerizon zordi ek dime, me lor trwaziem zour, mo ava finn fini mo mision."
Luke13:33 Selman mo bizin kontign mo sime zordi, dime ek apre dime, parski li pa posib ki enn profet mor andeor Zerizalem.’"
Luke13:34 Zerizalem, Zerizalem, twa ki touy bann profet e twa ki touy kout ros seki Bondie finn avoy ar twa, komie fwa mo ti anvi rasanble to bann zanfan kouma enn mama poul ramas so tipousin anba so lezel, me zot pa finn oule!"
Luke13:35 Krwar mwa, zot lakaz pou vid e mo pe dir zot, zot pa pou trouv mwa ankor ziska ler vini kot zot pou dir, ‘Sa-Enn ki vinn lor nom Lesegner la finn beni.’ ”"
Luke14:1 Enn zour saba, Zezi ti al manze dan lakaz enn sef Farizien. Bannla ti pe obzerv li."
Luke14:2 Ti ena la enn dimoun, so lekor ti gonfle partou."
Luke14:3 Zezi dir ar bann dokter lalwa ek bann Farizien, “Eski lalwa permet nou fer gerizon zour saba?”"
Luke14:4 Zot tou res trankil, zot pa dir nanye. Lerla Zezi tous malad la, geri li, e les li ale."
Luke14:5 Apre li dir zot, “Kisannla isi, si so garson oubien so bef tom dan enn pwi zour saba, li pa pou tir li?”"
Luke14:6 Zot res san parol.
Luke14:7 Letan Zezi trouv bann invite swazir bann plas doner, li rakont zot sa parabol la,"
Luke14:8 “Kan to invite dan enn maryaz, pa al asiz devan, tansion enn dimoun pli inportan finn gagn invitasion li osi;"
Luke14:9 lerla dimoun ki finn invit twa ek li, pou vinn dir twa, ‘Donn sa dimoun la to plas.’ Lerla to pou perdi pwin, to pou leve e to pou al asiz dan dernie ban."
Luke14:10 Me kan to invite kikpar, al asiz net par deryer; koumsa, kan dimoun ki finn invit twa la vini e dir twa, ‘Kamarad, al devan kot pli meyer.’ Lerla to pou gagn pwin devan tou bann invite ki atab ar twa."
Luke14:11 Seki rod grander pou abese, seki abese pou gagn grander.”"
Luke14:12 Lerla Zezi dir ar dimoun ki finn invit li, “Kan to fer enn dezene ou enn dine, pa invit to kamarad, to frer, to fami ou enn vwazin ki ris, parski zot kapav invit twa anretour e koumsa zot ava rann twa to invitasion."
Luke14:13 Me kan to fer enn fet invit bann pov, bann infirm, bann bwate ek bann aveg,"
Luke14:14 koumsa to pou beni, parski bannla pa kapav rann twa parey. To pou rekonpanse ler rezireksion bann zis vini.”"
Luke14:15 Enn invite ki ti atab avek Zezi finn tann sa e li dir Zezi, “Bienere seki pou pran so repa dan Rwayom Bondie.”"
Luke14:16 Lerla Zezi kontigne avek enn lot parabol, “Enn dimoun fer enn gran fet, e li invit enn kantite dimoun."
Luke14:17 Ler manze finn pare, li avoy so serviter al dir so bann invite, ‘Vini, manze finn pare.’"
Luke14:18 Me zot tou prezant exkiz. Premie la dir, ‘Mo fek aste enn karo, mo bizin al dan mo karo. Dir li exkiz mwa.’"
Luke14:19 Enn lot dir, ‘Mo fek aste sink per bef pou mo karo, e mo pe al gete si zot travay bien ansam. Dir li exkiz mwa.’"
Luke14:20 Enn lot dir, ‘Mo fek marye, akoz samem mo pa kapav vini.’"
Luke14:21 Serviter la retourn kot so met e li rakont li tou seki finn pase. Lerla propriyeter lakaz la pik enn koler e dir so serviter, ‘Degaze, al lor gran sime ek dan tou kwin lari e amenn bann pov, bann infirm, bann aveg ek bann paralize.’"
Luke14:22 Plitar serviter la vinn dir, ‘Met, mo finn fer tou seki to finn komande, ek ena ankor plas.’"
Luke14:23 Met la dir so serviter, ‘Al dan bann fobour, bann landrwa inpe bwa-bwa e fors dimoun vini pouki mo lakaz ranpli."
Luke14:24 Mo dir zot, okenn sa bann dimoun ki mo ti invite la pa pou dan mo fet.’ ”"
Luke14:25 Enn gran lafoul ti pe swiv Zezi. Zezi vire, dir zot,"
Luke14:26 “Si kikenn vinn ar mwa e li pa kontan mwa plis ki so papa ek so mama, so fam ek so zanfan, so frer, so ser, ek so prop lavi, li pa kapav vinn mo disip."
Luke14:27 Seki pa sarye so lakrwa e swiv mwa, pa kapav vinn mo disip."
Luke14:28 Si enn parmi zot anvi mont enn miray, eski dabor li pa asize pou kalkile komie sa pou kout li, ek apre li gete si li ena ase kas pou fini travay la?"
Luke14:29 Sinon, si li koul fondasion e apre li pa kapav fini, tou dimoun ki trouv sa pou riy li."
Luke14:30 Zot pou dir, ‘Sa dimoun la finn koumans enn travay me li pa finn kapav fini li.’"
Luke14:31 Kan enn lerwa al lager kont enn lot lerwa, eski li pa dabor asize, pran konsey pou gete si avek so dis mil zom li kapav al lager kont so lennmi ki ena vin-mil?"
Luke14:32 Si li pa kapav, letan lotla ankor lwin, li avoy enn delegasion pou fer lape."
Luke14:33 Alors, si zot pa renons tou seki zot posede, zot pa pou kapav vinn mo disip."
Luke14:34 Disel enn bon kiksoz; me si li perdi so gou, kouma pou kapav redonn li so gou?"
Luke14:35 Lerla li pa bon ni pou later, ni pou fimie e bizin zet li. Ekout bien, seki ena zorey pou tande."
Luke15:1 Boukou komi tax ek bann peser koste pre ar Zezi pou ekout li.
Luke15:2 Bann Farizien ek bann dokter lalwa mirmire e zot dir, “Li frekant bann peser, li manze-bwar ar zot.”"
Luke15:3 Lerla Zezi rakont sa parabol la,"
Luke15:4 “Kisannla parmi zot, si li ena san mouton, e ki li perdi enn ladan, li pa pou kit katrovin-diznef la dan dezer, pou al rod sa sel mouton ki finn perdi la, ziska ki li retrouv li?"
Luke15:5 E kan li finn trouv li, li met li lor so zepol avek enn gran kontantman."
Luke15:6 E letan li rant lakaz li apel tou so bann kamarad e so bann vwazin, li dir zot, ‘Vinn partaz mo lazwa parski mo finn retrouv mo mouton ki ti perdi.’"
Luke15:7 Mo dir zot, pou ena boukou plis lazwa dan lesiel pou enn sel peser ki finn repanti, ki pou katrovin-diznef dimoun ki zis, ki pa bizin repantir.”"
Luke15:8 “Si enn madam ki ena dis pies larzan perdi enn, eski li pa pou alim enn lalanp, balye lakaz e rode, rode mem, ziska ki li retrouv sa pies la?"
Luke15:9 Kan li finn retrouv li, li apel so bann kamarad ek bann vwazin, e li dir zot, ‘Vinn partaz mo lazwa parski mo finn retrouv pies ki mo ti finn perdi.’"
Luke15:10 Li pou parey pou bann anz Bondie ki pou dan lazwa akoz enn peser ki finn repanti.”
Luke15:11 Zezi dir, “Enn papa ti ena de garson."
Luke15:12 Pli zenn la dir ar so papa, ‘Papa, donn mwa mo par leritaz.’ Li partaz so dibien ant zot de."
Luke15:13 Pli zenn la pa perdi letan. Li ramas tou so bann zafer e li al bien-bien lwin dan enn lot pei. Laba li amenn enn lavi dezord e gaspiy tou so dibien.
Luke15:14 Letan li finn fini depans tou so kas, enn gran lafaminn tom lor pei la antie. Lerla li koumans santi lamizer."
Luke15:15 Li al rod travay kot enn abitan landrwa, ki ti avoy li nouri koson dan park."
Luke15:16 Li ti anvi manz gous ki bann koson ti pe manze, me sa osi personn pa ti donn li."
Luke15:17 Li koumans reflesi e li dir, ‘Ki kantite manze anplis bann travayer mo papa ena, e mwa mo pe mordefin isi!"
Luke15:18 Mo pou leve, mo pou al kot mo papa, mo pou dir li, ‘Papa, mo finn fer pese kont lesiel e kont twa;"
Luke15:19 mo nepli dign ki to apel mwa to garson; tret mwa kouma enn to bann travayer.’
Luke15:20 Li leve, li al kot so papa. Me letan li ti ankor bien lwin so papa trouv li pe vini. So leker fermal. Li galoupe, li ser so garson dan so lebra e li anbras li."
Luke15:21 Garson la dir li, ‘Papa, mo finn fer pese kont lesiel e kont twa; mo nepli dign ki to apel mwa to garson.’"
Luke15:22 Me papa la dir ar so bann serviter, ‘Degaze, amenn pli bon kostim, abiy li, met enn bag dan so ledwa, met soulie dan so lipie."
Luke15:23 Amenn enn ti toro bien gra, touy li; anou manze, anou fer fet,"
Luke15:24 parski mo garson ki ti mor finn regagn lavi; li ti perdi, mo finn retrouv li.’ Fet koumanse."
Luke15:25 Pli gran garson la ti dan karo. Letan li pe retourne e ki li finn ariv pre ar lakaz, li tann lamizik ek danse."
Luke15:26 Li apel enn serviter pou kone ki pe arive.
Luke15:27 Serviter la reponn, ‘To frer finn retourne e to papa finn touy sa vo bien gra la, parski li finn retourne anbonn sante.’"
Luke15:28 Garson la pik enn koler e li refiz rantre. So papa sorti vinn get li, e sipliy li,"
Luke15:29 me li reponn so papa, ‘Get sa, komie banane mo finn servi twa, zame mo finn dezobeir to lord; e zame to finn donn mwa enn tikabri pou mo fer fet ar mo bann kamarad."
Luke15:30 Me ler to garson retourne, apre ki li finn manz tou to dibien ar bann fam move lavi, to trouv mwayin touy sa vo bien gra la pou li.’"
Luke15:31 Alor papa la dir li, ‘Mo piti, twa, to touzour la ar mwa, e tou seki pou mwa, pou twa;"
Luke15:32 me nou ti bizin fer fet ek amize, parski to frer ki ti finn mor, li finn regagn lavi; li ti perdi, ala nou finn retrouv li.’ ”"
Luke16:1 Zezi dir ar so bann disip, “Enn boug ris ti anplway enn sef kontab. Li ti gagn bann informasion ki so sef kontab ti pe gaspiy so dibien."
Luke16:2 Li ti apel li e li ti dir li, ‘Ki mo pe tande lor twa? Fer mwa enn rapor lor to administrasion parski to nepli kapav kontign travay pou mwa.’"
Luke16:3 Sef la dir ar limem, ‘Ki mo pou fer aster? Mo patron pe donn mwa demision. Pou piose mo pena lafors, dimann sarite mo onte."
Luke16:4 Mo kone ki mo bizin fer pouki dimoun kontign get mwa kan mo perdi mo travay.’
Luke16:5 Enn par enn, li apel tou bann dimoun ki ti dwa so patron. Li dir ar premie la, ‘Komie to dwa mo patron?’"
Luke16:6 Li reponn, ‘San drom delwil zoliv.’ Kontab la dir li, ‘Degaze pran to karne, asize, mark sinkant.’"
Luke16:7 Apre li dir ar enn lot, ‘Twa, komie to dwa?’ Li reponn, ‘San bal dible.’ Li dir ar sannla, ‘Pran to karne, mark katrovin.’"
Luke16:8 Patron la felisit sef kontab malonet la parski li ti debrouyar. Bann zanfan lemonn pli debrouyar ki zanfan lalimier kan ena pou dres papie pou tras zot lavi.
Luke16:9 Mo dir zot, fer kamarad ar dibien ki ena lor later, koumsa kan dibien la pou nepli existe, zot pou gagn plas dan lakaz eternel."
Luke16:10 Seki fidel dan ti kiksoz, pou fidel dan seki gran; e seki malonet dan ti kiksoz, pou malonet dan seki gran."
Luke16:11 Si to pa finn fidel ar dibien ki ena lor later, kisannla pou konfie twa dibien ki dan lesiel?"
Luke16:12 E si to pa finn fidel ar dibien ki pa pou twa, kisannla pou konfie twa to prop dibien?"
Luke16:13 Enn serviter pa kapav servi de met; swa li air enn e li kontan lotla, swa li devoue pou enn e li mepriz lotla. To pa kapav servi Bondie ek dibien lor later.”"
Luke16:14 Letan bann Farizien ki ti bien kontan larzan tann sa, zot boufonn Zezi."
Luke16:15 Zezi dir zot, “Zot fer krwar ki zot ena lazistis zis pou lizie dimoun, me Bondie konn zot leker. Seki ena valer pou dimoun, enn abominasion pou Bondie."
Luke16:16 Lalwa ek profet finn fer lotorite ziska Zan; apre sa, pe proklam Bonn Nouvel Rwayom Bondie e sakenn pe fors limem pou rant ladan."
Luke16:17 Me li pli fasil ki later ek lesiel disparet, ki enn ti pwin dan lalwa disparet."
Luke16:18 Enn zom ki divors ar so fam e marye ar enn lot, komet adilter e seki marye ar enn fam ki finn kit so mari, komet adilter osi."
Luke16:19 Ti ena enn zom ris, ki ti met bel-bel kostim, bien-bien ser. Li ti pe viv dan lix e toulezour li ti pe fer gran-gran fet."
Luke16:20 Ti ena enn pov malere ki ti apel Lazar. Li ti pe asize devan laport ris la, e so lekor ti kouver ar lagal."
Luke16:21 Li ti pou bien kontan manz bann restan ki tom anba latab. Pli terib ankor, bann lisien ti vinn lis so lagal."
Luke16:22 Arive ki pov malere la mor e bann anz amenn li pre kot Abraam. Ris la osi mor e zot anter li.
Luke16:23 Dan lemonn bann mor letan li ti pe soufer, li lev so lizie, li trouv Abraam delwin e pre ar li, ti ena Lazar."
Luke16:24 Li kriye, ‘Papa Abraam, papa Abraam, pitie mwa. Avoy Lazar tranp so bout ledwa dan dilo pou rafresi mo lalang parski mo pe soufer lagoni dan sa laflam la.’"
Luke16:25 Me Abraam dir, ‘Mo garson, rapel bien ki dan to lavi lor later to ti dan bien, alor ki Lazar ti gagn boukou maler; me asterla li dan bien isi, e twa to dan soufrans."
Luke16:26 Anplis, ant nou finn met enn gran separasion pou anpes zot vinn kot nou e nou al kot zot.’"
Luke16:27 Ris la dir li, ‘Mo sipliy twa, papa Abraam, avoy Lazar lakaz mo papa,"
Luke16:28 parski mo ena sink frer laba. Averti zot pouki zot osi, zot pa vinn dan sa dife la.’"
Luke16:29 Me Abraam reponn li, ‘Zot ena Moiz e bann profet, les zot ekout bannla.’"
Luke16:30 Li reponn, ‘Non, papa Abraam, me si enn parmi bann mor al get zot, zot pou repanti.’"
Luke16:31 Abraam dir li, ‘Si zot pa ekout Moiz e bann profet, zot pa pou sanze, mem si enn mor ki finn resisite al get zot.’ ”"
Luke17:1 Zezi dir ar so bann disip, “Li normal ki ena obstak ki fer dimoun tonbe, me li bien malere pou sa dimoun ki fer lezot tonbe la!"
Luke17:2 Li preferab li atas enn gro ros dan so likou e li zet li dan lamer olie ki li fer enn sel tipti tonbe.
Luke17:3 Alor, fer bien atansion. Si to frer fer pese, koriz li, e si li repanti, pardonn li."
Luke17:4 Si set fwa dan enn zourne, li finn fer pese kont twa e set fwa li revinn get twa, e li dir twa, ‘Mo rekonet mo tor’, to bizin pardonn li.”"
Luke17:5 Bann apot dir Lesegner, “Ogmant nou lafwa.”"
Luke17:6 Lesegner reponn, “Si zot ena lafwa groser enn lagrin moutard, zot nek ena pou dir sa pie la, ‘Bouze, al plant twa dan lamer,’ li pou obeir zot.”"
Luke17:7 “Si enn parmi zot ena enn serviter ki pe travay dan karo oubien ki pe gardien troupo, eski kan li sorti dan karo li revini, zot pou dir li, ‘Degaze vinn atab’?"
Luke17:8 Plito zot pou dir li, ‘Prepar kiksoz pou mo manze, sanz to linz, vinn servi mwa ziska ki mo fini manze; apre sa, twa, to ava manze.’"
Luke17:9 Eski nou pou remersie enn serviter parski li finn fer seki li bizin fer?
Luke17:10 Zot osi parey. Letan zot fini fer seki finn komann zot, dir, ‘Nou bann sinp serviter, nou nek finn fer seki ti bizin fer.’ ”"
Luke17:11 Letan Zezi ti lor larout pou al Zerizalem, li ti pas ant Samari ek Galile."
Luke17:12 Kouma li ti rant dan enn vilaz li ti zwenn dis lepre. Zot res lwin ar li
Luke17:13 e zot kriye for-for, “Zezi! Met! Pitie nou.”"
Luke17:14 Ler li trouv zot, li dir zot, “Al montre zot devan bann pret.” Zot ti ankor dan sime, ler zot finn gagn zot pirifikasion."
Luke17:15 Letan enn parmi zot finn remarke ki li finn geri, li retourne e li glorifie Bondie avek tou so leker."
Luke17:16 Li tom azenou dan lipie Zezi e li remersie li. Li ti enn Samaritin.
Luke17:17 Lerla Zezi dir, “Pa dis ki finn pirifie? Lezot nef la kote?"
Luke17:18 Apar sa etranze la, personn pa ti pans retourne pou glorifie Bondie?”"
Luke17:19 Lerla Zezi dir li, “Leve, kontign to sime, to lafwa finn sov twa.”"
Luke17:20 Bann Farizien dimann Zezi, “Kan Rwayom Bondie pou vini?” Li reponn zot, “Rwayom Bondie pa pou vinn dan enn fason kler."
Luke17:21 Pa pou kapav dir, ‘Gete, ala li la!’ oubien, ‘Ala li laba!’ Krwar mwa, Rwayom Bondie parmi zot.”"
Luke17:22 Lerla li dir so bann disip, “Zour pe vini kot zot pou anvi trouv Garson Limanite, e zot pa pou trouv li."
Luke17:23 Dimoun pou dir zot, ‘Isi sa! Laba sa!’ Pa ale, pa swiv zot."
Luke17:24 Parey kouma zekler eklat enn kout dan lesiel e ekler lesiel depi enn kote ziska enn lot kote, koumsamem zour Garson Limanite pou ete."
Luke17:25 Me avan, li bizin soufer boukou e sa zenerasion la pou rezet li."
Luke17:26 Zour Garson Limanite pou parey kouma dan lepok Noe.
Luke17:27 Dimoun ti pe manze-bwar, ti pe marye, ti pe donn zot tifi an maryaz, ziska zour ki Noe rant dan so bato; lerla inondasion vini, detrir partou kote."
Luke17:28 Mem zafer ti pase lepok Lot. Zot ti pe manze, bwar, aste, vande, plante, konstrir;"
Luke17:29 me zour Lot sorti Sodom li ale, dife ek souf tom depi lesiel e detrir zot tou."
Luke17:30 Koumsamem pou ete zour Garson Limanite pou revel limem.
Luke17:31 Sa zour la, seki lor so teras, fode pa li desann dan so lakaz pou repran so bann zafer; parey pou seki dan karo, fode pa li retourn par deryer."
Luke17:32 Rapel seki ti ariv fam Lot.
Luke17:33 Seki rod sov so lavi pou perdi li, seki perdi so lavi pou sov li."
Luke17:34 Mo dir zot, sa lanwit la pou ena de lor mem lili; pou pran enn, pou kit enn."
Luke17:35 Pou ena de fam ki pe travay ansam; pou pran enn, pou kit enn."
Luke17:36 Pou ena de zom dan karo; pou pran enn, pou kit enn.”"
Luke17:37 Zot dir li, “Kot sa pou arive?” Li dir zot, “Kot ena kadav, lamem votour rasanble.”"
Luke18:1 Zezi rakont enn parabol pou montre ki bizin toultan priye san dekouraze.
Luke18:2 Li dir, “Dan enn lavil ti ena enn ziz ki pa ti per Bondie e ki pa ti ena respe pou personn."
Luke18:3 Ti ena enn vev dan sa lavil la ki ti vinn get ziz la souvan pou dimann li, ‘Donn mwa enn zizman favorab kont mo adverser.’"
Luke18:4 Pandan enn bon letan ziz la refize; me apre li dir ar limem, ‘Mem si mo pa per Bondie e mo pa ena respe pou personn,"
Luke18:5 mo pou donn sa vev la rezon parski li fatig mo latet; sinon li pou minn mo lavi afors li vinn devan mo laport toulezour.’ ”
Luke18:6 Lesegner dir, “Ekout bien ki sa move ziz la finn dir."
Luke18:7 Eski Bondie pa pou rann lazistis bann ki li finn swazir e ki pe sipliy li lanwit-lizour? Eski li pou tarde pou sekour zot?
Luke18:8 Mo dir zot, li pou donn zot lazistis san tarde. Kan Garson Limanite vini, eski li pou trouv lafwa lor later?”"
Luke18:9 Zezi ti rakont sa parabol la pou dimoun ki krwar zot drwat e ki ena mepri pou lezot.
Luke18:10 “De dimoun rant dan tanp pou priye; enn ladan ti enn Farizien, lotla ti enn komi tax."
Luke18:11 Farizien la ti pe dibout enn kote, apar, e li ti pe priye dan so leker, ‘Bondie, mo remersie twa ki mo pa kouma bann lezot dimoun, voler, explwater, adilter, e sirtou pa kouma sa komi tax la."
Luke18:12 Mo gard karem de fwa par semenn, mo donn enn diziem reveni ki mo gagne.’"
Luke18:13 Me komi tax la, ti pe dibout net par deryer e li pa ti mem oze lev so lizie pou get lesiel. Li ti pe tap so lapwatrinn e li ti pe dir, ‘Bondie, pitie mwa parski mo enn peser!’"
Luke18:14 Mo dir zot, kan sa dimoun la rant so lakaz li pou gagn pardon Bondie, me pa lotla. Seki rod grander pou abese, e seki abese pou gagn grander.”"
Luke18:15 Dimoun ti pe amenn bann tibaba pouki Zezi beni zot. Kan bann disip trouv sa, zot koz brit ar sa bann dimoun la."
Luke18:16 Me Zezi apel zot e li dir, “Les bann zanfan vinn ar mwa. Pa anpes zot, parski Rwayom Bondie pou tou dimoun ki parey kouma zot."
Luke18:17 Laverite, mo dir zot, seki pa resevwar Rwayom Bondie kouma enn zanfan pa pou kapav rant ladan.”"
Luke18:18 Enn sef Zwif dimann Zezi, “Bon Met, ki mo bizin fer pou gagn lavi eternel?”"
Luke18:19 Zezi dir li, “Kifer to apel mwa bon? Personn pa bon, zis Bondie tousel ki bon."
Luke18:20 To bien konn bann komannman: Pa komet ladilter, pa touye, pa kokin, pa fer fos temwagnaz, onor to papa ek to mama.”"
Luke18:21 Sef Zwif la dir, “Depi mo zenes mo finn gard tousala.”"
Luke18:22 Letan Zezi tann sa, li dir li, “To mank enn kiksoz. Vann tou seki to ena, donn bann pov, e to pou ena enn trezor dan lesiel; apre sa vini, swiv mwa.”"
Luke18:23 Me letan li tann sa, so figir sanze, parski li ti ena boukou rises."
Luke18:24 Zezi trouv li bien tris, alor li dir, “Pa fasil pou bann ris rant dan Rwayom Bondie!"
Luke18:25 Li pli fasil pou enn samo pas par trou zegwi ki enn ris rant dan Rwayom Bondie.”
Luke18:26 Bann ki ti pe tann sa demande, “Abe kisannla kapav sove?”"
Luke18:27 Me li dir zot, “Seki inposib pou bann imin, li posib pou Bondie.”"
Luke18:28 Lerla Pier dir li, “Nou finn kit tou seki nou posede pou swiv twa.”"
Luke18:29 Zezi dir zot, “Laverite, laverite, mo dir zot, si pou Rwayom Bondie enn dimoun kit so lakaz, so fam, so bann frer, so fami, so zanfan,"
Luke18:30 li pou gagn boukou plis dan sa lavi la, dan lot lavi e li pou gagn lavi eternel.”"
Luke18:31 Zezi pran Ledouz avek li e li dir zot, “Ekout mwa, nou pe al Zerizalem, e tou seki finn profetize lor Garson Limanite pou realize."
Luke18:32 Pou livre li ar bann payin, dimoun pou boufonn li, pou insilte li ek pou kras lor li."
Luke18:33 Zot pou fwet li, ek touy li, e lor trwaziem zour li pou resisite.”"
Luke18:34 Me bann disip pa konpran seki li ti pe dir. So parol ti enn mister pou zot; zot pa ti pe reysi kapte seki li ti pe dir.
Luke18:35 Letan li koste pre ar Zeriko, ti ena enn aveg ki ti pe asiz dan bor sime, ti pe dimann sarite."
Luke18:36 Letan li tann lafoul pe pase, li dimann ki pe arive."
Luke18:37 Zot dir li, “Zezi Nazaret pe pase.”"
Luke18:38 Li kriye bien for, “Zezi, Garson David, pitie mwa!”"
Luke18:39 Bann ki devan kriy ar li pouki li res trankil, me li kriye ankor pli for, “Garson David, pitie mwa!”"
Luke18:40 Zezi arete, li donn lord pou amenn aveg la; kan li finn koste, Zezi dimann li,"
Luke18:41 “Ki to oule mo fer pou twa?” Li reponn, “Segner, fer mwa trouv kler.”"
Luke18:42 Zezi dir li, “Trouv kler. To lafwa finn sov twa.”"
Luke18:43 Toutswit li trouv kler, li swiv Zezi, e li glorifie Bondie. Tou dimoun ki ti trouv sa, ti glorifie Bondie."
Luke19:1 Zezi rant dan Zeriko e li travers lavil la.
Luke19:2 Ti ena enn dimoun ki ti apel Zase; li ti enn sef komi tax e li ti bien ris.
Luke19:3 Li ti anvi trouv Zezi, me akoz lafoul li pa ti kapav parski li ti tro kourt."
Luke19:4 Alors li ti galoup devan, li ti mont lor enn gran pie sikomor pou trouv Zezi parski li ti pre pou pas par la."
Luke19:5 Letan Zezi ariv pre sa plas la, li lev lizie, li get Zase, e li dir li, “Zase, degaze desann; mo bizin vinn res kot twa zordi.”"
Luke19:6 Zase degaze desann e resevwar Zezi dan lazwa.
Luke19:7 Tou bann ki ti trouv sa mirmire e zot dir, “Ala li finn al res kot enn dimoun ki fer pese.”"
Luke19:8 Zase leve e li dir ar Lesegner, “Ekout mwa, Segner. Mo pou donn lamwatie mo dibien bann pov; e si mo finn kokin dimoun, mo pou rann zot kat fwa plis.”"
Luke19:9 Lerla Zezi dir li, “Azordi mem, delivrans finn rant dan sa lakaz la parski li osi, li enn zanfan Abraam."
Luke19:10 Parski Garson Limanite inn vinn rod seki finn perdi pou sov zot.”
Luke19:11 Letan Zezi ti koste ar Zerizalem, li rakont enn lot parabol pou bann ki ti pe ekout li parski zot ti panse ki Rwayom Bondie ti pre pou manifeste limem."
Luke19:12 Alors Zezi dir zot, “Enn zom ki sorti dan enn gran fami al dan enn lot pei pou gagn tit lerwa e li ti pou retourne apre sa."
Luke19:13 Li apel dis so bann serviter, e li donn zot dis pies an-or, ki ena gran valer. Li dir zot, ‘Fer roulman ar sa ziska mo revini.’"
Luke19:14 Me bann dimoun dan so prop pei ti deteste li. Zot avoy enn delegasion dir, ‘Nou pale li vinn nou lerwa.’"
Luke19:15 Me apre ki li finn gagn so tit lerwa, li retourne. Li fer apel so bann serviter pou li kone ki profi zot ti finn fer ar larzan ki li ti finn donn zot."
Luke19:16 Premie la vinn devan li, e li dir, ‘Segner, to pies lor finn raport dis fwa plis.’"
Luke19:17 Lerwa dir li, ‘Felisitasion, bon serviter! Parski to finn serye dan enn ti zafer, mo pou donn twa lotorite lor dis lavil.’"
Luke19:18 Deziem la koste, li dir, ‘Segner, to pies lor finn raport sink fwa plis.’"
Luke19:19 Lerwa la dir li osi, ‘Twa, mo pou donn twa sink lavil pou okipe.’"
Luke19:20 Enn lot vini ankor e li dir, ‘Segner, ala ou pies lor, ki mo finn kasiet dan mouswar."
Luke19:21 Mo ti per ou parski ou enn dimoun sever; ou pran la kot ou pa finn met nanye ek ou rekolte kot ou pa finn seme.’
Luke19:22 Lerwa la dir li, ‘Serviter move, mo pou kondann twa par to prop parol. To ti kone mo sever, mo pran kot mo pa finn met nanye e mo rekolte kot mo pa finn seme."
Luke19:23 Alors kifer to pa finn met mo larzan labank; letan mo retourne mo ti a repran li ar so lintere?’
Luke19:24 Apre sa li dir dimoun ki ti la, ‘Aras so larzan, donn sa lot la ki ena dis pies lor.’"
Luke19:25 Zot dir li, ‘Segner, abe li ena deza dis pies!’"
Luke19:26 ‘Ala mo dir zot, seki ena pou gagn plis ankor, me seki pena, pou perdi tigit ki li ena."
Luke19:27 Asterla, mo bann ennmi, ki pa ti oule mo vinn zot lerwa, amenn zot isi e eliminn zot devan mwa.’ ”"
Luke19:28 Letan li fini koze, Zezi mars devan zot pou mont Zerizalem."
Luke19:29 Letan li ariv pre ar vilaz Betfaze ek Betani, kot enn kolinn ki ti apel kolinn Pie Zoliv, li avoy de disip e"
Luke19:30 li dir zot, “Al dan vilaz ki lot kote. Letan zot rant laba, zot pou trouv enn ti bourik atase e ki zame personn pa finn monte. Larg li, amenn li isi."
Luke19:31 Si kikenn dimann zot, ‘Kifer zot finn larg sa ti bourik la?’, zot va reponn, ‘Lesegner bizin li.’ ”"
Luke19:32 Toulede disip ale e zot trouv tou parey kouma Zezi finn dir zot.
Luke19:33 Letan zot pe larg ti bourik la, so bann propriyeter vinn dimande, “Kifer zot pe larg sa ti bourik la?”"
Luke19:34 Zot reponn, “Lesegner bizin li.”"
Luke19:35 Zot amenn bourik la ar Zezi; zot zet zot linz lor li e zot fer Zezi mont lor li.
Luke19:36 Lor sime, dimoun tal zot linz devan li."
Luke19:37 Letan Zezi pe koste ar Zerizalem, dan ladesant kolinn Pie Zoliv, lafoul bann disip ti ranpli ar lazwa; zot koumans sante, loue Bondie, pou bann mirak ki zot ti finn trouve."
Luke19:38 Zot ti pe dir, “Li finn beni Lerwa ki pe vinn lor nom Lesegner! Lape dan lesiel e laglwar pou Bondie Treo!”"
Luke19:39 Detrwa Farizien ki ti dan lafoul dir Zezi, “Met, dir to bann disip res trankil.”"
Luke19:40 Zezi reponn, “Ala mo dir zot, si bannla res trankil, ros ki pou kriye.”"
Luke19:41 Kan Zezi ariv pre ar Zerizalem, li plore kan li trouv lavil la."
Luke19:42 Li dir, “Si selma zordizour to ti kone ki kapav donn twa lape; me asterla, tou kasiet devan to lizie."
Luke19:43 Me bann zour pou vini kot to bann ennmi pou antour twa ar enn miray, pou anserkle twa e pou atak twa partou kote."
Luke19:44 Zot pou kraz twa ek tou to zanfan, e pa pou les enn sel ros dibout, parski to pa finn rekonet Bondie kan li ti vinn vizit twa.”"
Luke19:45 Zezi rant dan tanp e pous bann marsan.
Luke19:46 Li dir zot, “Dan liv finn ekrir, ‘Mo lakaz enn lakaz lapriyer.’ Me zot, zot finn fer li vinn enn kavern voler.”"
Luke19:47 Toulezour Zezi ti pe ansegne dan tanp. Bann sef pret, bann dokter lalwa ek dimoun bien inflian ti pe rod touy li."
Luke19:48 Me zot pa ti kone kouma pou fer sa, parski tou lepep ti pe ekout li avek boukou atansion."
Luke20:1 Enn zour, Zezi ti pe ansegn lepep dan tanp e li ti pe anons Bonn Nouvel. Bann sef pret, bann dokter lalwa ek bann ansien vini tom lor li."
Luke20:2 Zot dimann li, “Dir nou, dapre ki lord to pe fer seki to pe fer la, kisannla finn donn twa sa lotorite la?"
Luke20:3 Zezi reponn zot, “Mo pou poz zot enn kestion mwa osi. Dir mwa,"
Luke20:4 eski batem Zan sorti depi lesiel ou bien ar bann imin?”
Luke20:5 Zot koumans diskite e zot dir ant zotmem, “Si nou dir depi lesiel, li pou dir nou, abe kifer nou pa finn krwar dan li?"
Luke20:6 Me si nou dir ar bann imin, tou lepep pou avoy nou kout ros, parski zot krwar ki Zan ti enn profet.”"
Luke20:7 Alor zot reponn, “Nou pa kone kot li sorti.”"
Luke20:8 Zezi dir zot, “Mwa osi mo pa pou dir zot kot mo finn gagn lotorite pou fer seki mo pe fer.”"
Luke20:9 Zezi rakont lepep sa parabol la: “Enn dimoun ti plant enn karo rezin, li ti lwe li ar bann planter e li parti pou enn bon bout letan."
Luke20:10 Kan ler finn vini, li avoy so serviter al get bann planter la pou pran so par lor seki karo rezin la ti raporte. Bann planter la bat li, pous li e li retourn lame vid."
Luke20:11 Propriyeter karo avoy enn lot serviter; bann planter la bat li osi, insilte li e li retourn san nanye."
Luke20:12 Li kontigne mem, li avoy enn trwaziem. Sannla osi zot bien bles li e zot zet li deor."
Luke20:13 Lerla propriyeter karo dir, ‘Ki mo pou fer? Mo pou avoy mo garson ki mo bien kontan; mo espere zot pou respekte li.’"
Luke20:14 Letan bann planter la trouv garson la vini, zot konplote e zot dir ant zotmem, ‘Limem eritie; anou touy li e so leritaz pou vinn pou nou.’"
Luke20:15 Zot pous li andeor karo e zot touy li. Ki propriyeter karo la pou fer ar zot?
Luke20:16 Limem pou vini, li pou touy zot enn par enn e li pou donn so karo lot dimoun.” Letan zot tann sa, zot dir, “Pena sime!”"
Luke20:17 Li get zot, li dir zot, “Ki vedir sa parol Lekritir la: ‘Ros ki bann mason finn rezete, Samem finn vinn lakle prinsipal’?"
Luke20:18 Tou dimoun ki tom lor sa ros la pou kas an morso e kan ros la tom lor kikenn, ros la pou kraz li.”"
Luke20:19 Bann dokter lalwa, bann sef pret ti pe rod trap li lerlamem parski zot ti kone ki li ti finn rakont sa parabol la kont zot; me zot pa oze akoz lafoul."
Luke20:20 Alors bannla vey tou so mouvman; zot avoy bann espion ki deklar onet, pou trap Zezi kan li pou dir enn kiksoz ki pa korek. Koumsa zot pou kapav aret li e met li dan lame gouverner."
Luke20:21 Alors zot poz li enn kestion, “Met, nou kone ki to parol e to lansegnman zot bien drwat; to pa get dapre figir dimoun, me to ansegn sime Bondie dapre laverite."
Luke20:22 Dapre lalwa, eski nou bizin pey tax Sezar ou non?”"
Luke20:23 Zezi ti konn zot lespri rize. Li dir zot,"
Luke20:24 “Montre mwa enn pies larzan. Ki figir ena lor la e ki finn ekrir?” Zot reponn, “Sezar.”"
Luke20:25 Zezi dir zot, “Abe rann Sezar seki pou Sezar, e Bondie seki pou Bondie.”"
Luke20:26 Kouma zot pa ti kapav may li dan lak ar so prop parol devan lepep, zot ti res trankil. So bann parol ti inpresionn zot."
Luke20:27 Enn de Sadisein vinn get Zezi. (Zot ti dir ki pena rezireksion.) Alors zot poz Zezi enn kestion.
Luke20:28 Zot dir li, “Met, Moiz finn ekrir, ‘Si frer enn boug mor e pa les okenn zanfan e ki so fam ankor vivan, sa boug la bizin pran fam so frer pou donn so frer enn desandans.’"
Luke20:29 Ti ena set frer. Premie la marye. Li mor san ena okenn zanfan.
Luke20:30 Li parey pou deziem la.
Luke20:31 Trwaziem la osi marye ar li, e touleset ti marye ar li enn apre lot e zot inn mor san gagn zanfan."
Luke20:32 Alafin fam la osi ti mor.
Luke20:33 Zour larezireksion, kisannla so mari parski touleset ti marye ar li?”"
Luke20:34 Zezi reponn zot, “Lor later dimoun marye e donn zot tifi an maryaz."
Luke20:35 Tou seki finn zize dign pou larezireksion bann mor, e pou viv dan lemonn ki pou vini, pa pou marye e pa pou donn zot tifi anmaryaz."
Luke20:36 Zot pa kapav mor ankor parski zot kouma bann anz e zot finn vinn bann zanfan Bondie parski zot bann zanfan larezireksion.
Luke20:37 Moiz limem finn fer kone ki bann mor pou leve parski dan sa pasaz lor bwison ardan la, li dir, ‘Lesegner Bondie Abraam, Bondie Izaak, Bondie Zakob’."
Luke20:38 Bondie, pa Bondie bann mor me Bondie bann vivan. Pou li, tou dimoun vivan.”"
Luke20:39 Detrwa dokter lalwa ki ti la dir, “Met, to finn bien koze.”"
Luke20:40 Lerla zot pa oze poz li okenn kestion ankor.
Luke20:41 Zezi dir zot, “Kouma li posib ki zot dir ki Lekris Garson David?"
Luke20:42 Parski David limem dir dan Liv Psom, ‘Lesegner dir ar mo Segner, asiz adrwat mo tronn,"
Luke20:43 ziska ki mo servi to bann lennmi kouma enn eskabo anba to lipie.’
Luke20:44 Si David apel Lekris Segner, kouma Lekris kapav so garson?”"
Luke20:45 Letan tou lepep pe ekout li, Zezi dir so bann disip,"
Luke20:46 “Mefie zot bann dokter lalwa ki kontan pavane avek gran-gran rob e ki kontan kan dimoun salye zot dan bann plas piblik; dan sinagog, zot swazir bann plas kot tou dimoun pou trouv zot e dan bann dine, zot rod bann plas doner."
Luke20:47 Zot devor tikas ki bann vev finn ramase e zot fer long-long lapriyer pouki tou dimoun trouv zot. Zot pou gagn pli gran kondanasion.
Luke21:1 Zezi get partou e li trouv bann dimoun ris ki ti pe met larzan dan tron.
Luke21:2 Anmemtan, li trouv enn pov vev ki met de pies larzan."
Luke21:3 Lerla li dir zot, “Laverite, mo dir zot, sa pov vev la finn met plis ki zot tou."
Luke21:4 Zot tou zot finn met seki zot ti ena anplis me li, li finn donn tou seki li ti ena pou viv.”"
Luke21:5 Devan bann dimoun ki ti pe admir bote tanp ek so bann ros,"
Luke21:6 Zezi dir, “Enn zour pou vini, kot tou seki zot pe trouve la, pou devir anbalao. Pa pou res enn sel ros poze lor enn lot.”"
Luke21:7 Lerla zot dimann Zezi, “Met, kan tousala pou arive? Ki sign pou fer nou kone ki sa pe vini?”"
Luke21:8 “Pran kont, pa les dimoun anbet zot. Parski boukou dimoun pou vinn lor mo nom e zot pou dir, ‘Momem sa.’ ‘Ler finn arive’. Pa swiv zot."
Luke21:9 Kan zot pou tann bann lager ek bann revolision, pa gagn per; fodre ki tousala arive dabor, me lafin pa pou toutswit.”"
Luke21:10 Apre Zezi dir, “Pei pou lev kont pei, rwayom kont rwayom."
Luke21:11 Pou ena bann tranblemandeter terib ek lafaminn dan boukou landrwa ek bann lepidemi; pou ena osi bann gran sign terifian dan lesiel.
Luke21:12 Me avan tousala arive, bannla pou trap zot, pou persekit zot, pou livre zot dan sinagog e pou met zot dan prizon; zot pou pas anzizman devan bann lerwa ek bann gouverner akoz mo nom."
Luke21:13 Sa pou enn lokazion pou zot donn zot temwagnaz.
Luke21:14 Met dan zot latet ki zot pena pou prepar zot defans.
Luke21:15 Parski mo pou donn zot bann parol e enn sazes ki okenn adverser pa pou kapav reponn ek kontredir.
Luke21:16 Zot prop papa, zot prop mama, zot prop frer, zot bann konesans ek zot bann kamarad pou livre zot, e plizir parmi zot pou kondane amor."
Luke21:17 Tou dimoun pou air zot akoz mo nom.
Luke21:18 Me pa enn sel brin seve lor zot latet pou perdi.
Luke21:19 Tini ferm par zot perseverans, zot pou gagn lavi.”"
Luke21:20 “Kan zot pou trouv bann larme anserkle Zerizalem, lerla zot pou kone ki so lafin finn arive."
Luke21:21 Lerla dimoun Zide pou bizin sove al lor montagn, dimoun dan lavil pou bizin al lwin, e seki dan lakanpagn fode pa rant dan lavil."
Luke21:22 Parski samem bann zour zizman, e tou seki deklare dan lekritir pou realize."
Luke21:23 Maler pou bann fam ansint e pou bann seki pe donn baba bwar dan sa peryod la; pou ena enn gran detres lor later e lakoler Bondie pou abat lor lepep.
Luke21:24 Bannla pou transpers zot ar pwint lepe, pou fer zot prizonie parmi bann lezot pep; sa bann pep la pou pil lor Zerizalem ziska ki letan ki finn akord zot termine."
Luke21:25 Pou ena bann sign dan soley, lalinn ek zetwal; lor later bann pei pou viv dan langwas; zot pa pou kone ki pou fer letan zot tann tapaz violan lamer e fraka bann vag."
Luke21:26 Dimoun pou tom sek telman zot gagn per letan zot mazinn seki pe vinn lor later; bann pwisans dan lesiel pou tranble.
Luke21:27 Lerla zot pou trouv Garson Limanite sorti dan niaz, desann avek pwisans ek tou so laglwar."
Luke21:28 Kan tousala pou arive, drese, lev latet parski zot delivrans pe aprose.”"
Luke21:29 Zezi rakont zot enn parabol, “Get enn pie fig ek lezot pie;"
Luke21:30 letan so bann fey pe sorti, zot kone ki lete pe vini."
Luke21:31 Li parey kan zot pou trouv sa bann evennman la arive; zot kone ki Rwayom Bondie pe aprose.
Luke21:32 Laverite, laverite mo dir zot, sa zenerasion la pa pou disparet avan ki tousala arive."
Luke21:33 Lesiel ek later pou disparet me mo parol pa pou disparet.”
Luke21:34 “Pran kont pouki zot leker pa angourdi par tousort kalite kiksoz, par labwason ek bann difikilte lavi, sinon Gran Zour la pou tom lor zot san ki zot atann,"
Luke21:35 parey kouma enn piez; li pou tom lor tou dimoun ki lor later.
Luke21:36 Gard zot lizie ouver, priye pouki zot gagn ase lafors pou sap dan bann maler ki pou arive, pou zot kapav dibout e prezant zot devan Garson Limanite.”"
Luke21:37 Dan lazourne, Zezi ti pe ansegn dan tanp me aswar, li kit lavil e li pas lanwit lor kolinn ki ti apel Kolinn Pie Zoliv."
Luke21:38 Antie lepep ti vinn dan tanp boner gramatin pou ekout li koze.
Luke22:1 Fet dipin san levin, ki ti apel osi fet Pak, ti pe aprose."
Luke22:2 Bann sef pret ek bann dokter lalwa ti pe rod enn sime pou touy Zezi me zot ti per lepep.
Luke22:3 Letansa, Satan ti rant dan Zida ki ti apel Iskaryot, ki ti enn parmi Ledouz."
Luke22:4 Zida sorti pou al zwenn bann sef pret ek bann sef gard pou dir zot ki manier li pou kapav livre zot Zezi.
Luke22:5 Zot ti bien kontan e zot ti promet li enn som larzan.
Luke22:6 Zida tom dakor e li rod enn bon lokazion pou livre zot Zezi san ki lafoul kone.
Luke22:7 Fet Pak arive e sa zour la bizin fer sakrifis annyo.
Luke22:8 Alor Zezi avoy Pier ek Zan e li rekomann zot, “Al prepar nou repa Pak pouki nou kapav manze.”"
Luke22:9 Zot dir li, “Kot to ti anvi nou al prepar sa?”"
Luke22:10 Li dir zot, “Get sa, kan zot pou rant dan lavil, enn boug ki pe sarye enn damzann dilo pou vinn zwenn zot. Swiv li ziska kot li pou rantre."
Luke22:11 Dir propriyeter lakaz la, ‘Nou Met dir twa, kot lasal kot mo pou kapav manz repa Pak avek mo bann disip?’"
Luke22:12 Li pou montre zot lor letaz enn gran lasal ki finn fini meble. Fer bann preparasion laba.”
Luke22:13 Zot ale e zot trouv tou dapre seki li ti finn dir e zot koumans prepar repa Pak.
Luke22:14 Kan ler ti finn arive, Zezi asiz atab avek so bann apot."
Luke22:15 Li dir zot, “Mo finn vremem souete manz sa repa Pak la avek zot avan mo al konn lasoufrans."
Luke22:16 Mo dir zot sa parski mo pa pou pran sa repa la ankor ziska ki tou so vre sans akonpli dan Rwayom Bondie.”
Luke22:17 Zezi pran enn koup, li rann gras e li dir, “Pran sa e partaz ant zot."
Luke22:18 Mo pe dir zot depi asterlamem, mo pa pou bwar ankor fri karo rezin ziska ki Rwayom Bondie vini.”"
Luke22:19 Apre li pran dipin, li rann gras, li kas li e li donn zot. Li dir, “Samem mo lekor, ki mo donn pou zot. Fer sa, an mo memwar.”"
Luke22:20 Li fer parey ar koup la apre ki finn fini manze, li dir, “Samem koup nouvo lalians ki mo fer par mo disan. Mo vers sa pou zot."
Luke22:21 Me gete, lame sa dimoun ki pou trair mwa la lor latab avek mwa."
Luke22:22 Wi, Garson Limanite pe ale parey kouma finn dir, me maler sa dimoun ki pe livre li la."
Luke22:23 Lerla zot koumans poz kestion kisannla parmi zot pou kapav fer sa.
Luke22:24 Diskision leve ant zot pou gete kisannla pli gran parmi zot.
Luke22:25 Alors Zezi dir zot, “Lerwa bann pei diriz zot sitwayin e montre zot lotorite. Apel zot ‘bienfeter’."
Luke22:26 Pou zot, fode pa li koumsa. Pli gran parmi zot bizin azir kouma enn pli zenn, e seki komande bizin azir kouma enn serviter."
Luke22:27 Parski kisannla pli gran? Seki atab oubien seki pe servi? Pa plito seki atab la? Me mwa mo parmi zot kouma sa kikenn ki pe servi la.
Luke22:28 Zot finn toultan ar mwa dan mo bann difikilte,"
Luke22:29 akoz samem mo pou donn zot pouvwar lor Rwayom parey kouma mo Papa finn donn mwa,"
Luke22:30 pouki zot manze ek bwar lor mem latab ar mwa dan mo Rwayom e ki zot siez lor tronn pou ziz douz tribi Izrael.”
Luke22:31 Simon, Simon, gete, Satan finn demande pou pas zot tou dan tami parey kouma fer ar dible."
Luke22:32 Mo finn priye pou twa pouki to pa perdi lafwa. Twa, kan to pou retourn ar mwa, fortifie to bann frer."
Luke22:33 Pier dir li, “Segner, mo finn pare pou al dan prizon ar twa e mor pou twa.”"
Luke22:34 Zezi reponn li, “Mo dir twa, Pier, avan ki kok fini sante azordi, to pou finn renie mwa trwa fwa.”"
Luke22:35 Li dir zot, “Kan mo ti avoy zot anmision san portmone, san sak e san sandalet, eski zot ti mank kiksoz?” Zot reponn, “Nanye”."
Luke22:36 Li dir zot, “Aster, seki ena enn portmone pran li e seki ena enn sak, fer parey; seki pena lepe, vann so manto pou aste enn."
Luke22:37 Parski mo dir zot, fodre ki seki finn ekrir lor mwa realize: ‘Finn kont li parmi bann malfeter’. Anfet seki finn ekrir lor mwa pou arive.”"
Luke22:38 Zot dir li, “Segner, nou ena de lepe.” Li reponn zot, “Li pou ase.”"
Luke22:39 Zezi sorti pou al lor kolinn Pie Zoliv kouma li abitie. So bann disip swiv li.
Luke22:40 Letan li ariv laba, li dir zot, “Priye pou pa rant dan lak tantasion.”"
Luke22:41 Apre sa, li al inpe pli lwin, distans enn kout ros, li tom azenou e li koumans priye."
Luke22:42 Li dir, “Papa, si to kapav, tir sa koup la devan mwa; me pa fer mo volonte, me to volonte.”"
Luke22:43 Enn anz paret devan li pou donn li lafors.
Luke22:44 Dan so lagoni, Zezi priye avek plis ferver. So transpirasion parey kouma gout disan tom lor later."
Luke22:45 Ler li fini priye, li leve e li al get so bann disip. Li trouv zot pe dormi parski zot ti dan sagrin."
Luke22:46 Li dir zot, “Kifer zot pe dormi? Leve, priye pouki zot pa rant dan piez tantasion.”"
Luke22:47 Li ti pe ankor koze, kan enn lafoul aparet avek Zida ki ti enn parmi Ledouz e limem ti antet. Li vinn pre ar Zezi e li anbras li."
Luke22:48 Zezi dir li, “Zida, to anbras Garson Limanite pou trair li?”"
Luke22:49 Letan bann ki ti ar Zezi trouv seki pe deroule, zot dir, “Segner, eski nou donn zot enn kout lepe?”"
Luke22:50 Enn parmi donn serviter gran pret enn kout lepe e li koup so zorey drwat.
Luke22:51 Zezi dir li, “Pa fer sa.” Lerla li tous zorey serviter la, e li geri li."
Luke22:52 Apre sa, Zezi dir bann sef pret, bann sef gard dan tanp, bann ansien ki finn vinn rod li, “Eski ti bizin lepe ek baton pou aret mwa koumadir mo enn voler?"
Luke22:53 Toulezour mo ti avek zot dan tanp e zot pa finn trap mwa pou aret mwa. Me zot ler ek ler pwisans teneb finn vini.”
Luke22:54 Alors zot trap Zezi e zot amenn li dan lakaz gran pret. Pier ti pe swiv depi enn distans.
Luke22:55 Ti ena enn dife ki ti alime dan lakour e Pier ti pe asiz avek bann ki ti la.
Luke22:56 Enn servant trouv Pier pe asiz dan bor dife; li get li bien e li dir, “Sa boug la osi ti avek li!”"
Luke22:57 Me li renie e li dir, “Fam, mo pa konn li.”"
Luke22:58 Inpe letan apre, enn lot dimoun trouv li e li insiste, “Twa osi, to dan so bann.” Pier reponn, “Kamarad, pa mwa sa.”"
Luke22:59 Enn-ertan apre, enn lot ankor persiste ar li e li dir, “Pena okenn dout, sa dimoun la ti avek li parski li enn Galileen.”"
Luke22:60 Pier reponn, “Kamarad, mo pa kone ki to pe dir. Avan li fini koze, kok sante."
Luke22:61 Lesegner tourne e get li dan so lizie. Lerla Pier rapel seki Lesegner finn dir li, “Avan ki kok sante zordi, to pou finn renie mwa trwa fwa.”"
Luke22:62 Li sorti deor e gro-gro larm koule dan so lizie.
Luke22:63 Bann zom ki ti pe vey Zezi, ti pe boufonn li e ti pe bat li."
Luke22:64 Zot kouver so figir e zot ti dimann li, “Fer to profet, kisannla finn bat twa?”"
Luke22:65 Zot ti pe zour li tousort kalite.
Luke22:66 Kouma fer lizour, bann ansien dan pep Zwif, bann sef pret ek bann dokter lalwa zwenn e zot amenn li devan Gran Tribinal."
Luke22:67 Zot dimann li, “Si tomem Lemesi, dir nou.” Li dir zot, “Si mo dir zot, zot pa pou krwar."
Luke22:68 E si mwa, mo poz enn kestion, zot pa pou reponn."
Luke22:69 Me asterla, ala seki pou arive - Garson Limanite pou asiz adrwat pwisans Bondie.”"
Luke22:70 Zot tou dir, “Alors to Garson Bondie?” E li reponn zot, “Zotmem pe dir ki mwa sa.”"
Luke22:71 Lerla zot dir, “Ki lot temwin ankor nou bizin? Nou finn tande noumem saki li finn dir ar so prop labous.”"
Luke23:1 Lasanble ki ti prezan leve e amenn Zezi devan Pilat.
Luke23:2 Zot koumans akiz li. Zot dir, “Nou finn trouv li pe met lepep dan trou, anpes nou pey tax Sezar, e lorla li pe dir ki limem Lemesi ek lerwa.”"
Luke23:3 Lerla Pilat poz li enn kestion, “Eski tomem Lerwa bann Zwif?” Zezi reponn li, “Twa ki pe dir.”"
Luke23:4 Pilat dir ar bann sef pret ek lafoul, “Mo pa trouv okenn sarz kont sa boug la.”"
Luke23:5 Zot kriy pli for, “So lansegnman exsit lepep pou revolte partou dan Zide; li finn koumanse depi Galile e li finn ariv ziska isi.”"
Luke23:6 Letan Pilat finn tann sa, li demande si sa boug la sorti Galile."
Luke23:7 Kouma li aprann ki Zezi sorti sa landrwa ki Erod ti pe administre la, li avoy li ar Erod ki ti dan Zerizalem pandan sa peryod la."
Luke23:8 Letan Erod trouv Zezi, li ti bien kontan. Depi lontan Erod ti pe anvi zwenn Zezi parski li ti finn tann koz li e li ti espere ki li pou trouv Zezi fer detrwa mirak."
Luke23:9 Li poz li boukou kestion me Zezi pa reponn nanye.
Luke23:10 Bann sef pret ek bann dokter lalwa ki ti pe dibout lamem akiz Zezi avek violans.
Luke23:11 Erod ek so bann solda boufonn li, maltret li koumadir li enn pouritir. Zot abiy li kouma enn lerwa e zot reanvway li ar Pilat."
Luke23:12 Sa zour la Erod ek Pilat ti vinn de bon kamarad; avan zot pa ti kapav santi zot kamarad.
Luke23:13 Pilat reyni bann sef pret, bann dirizan ek lepep."
Luke23:14 Li dir zot, “Zot finn amenn devan mwa sa boug la e zot finn akiz li kouma kikenn ki pe met lepep dan trou. Mwa mo finn interoz li, e mo pa pe trouv okenn sarz ki zot finn met lor li."
Luke23:15 Erod osi pa finn trouv nanye e li finn reanvway li ar nou parski li pa finn komet enn fot ki merit lamor.
Luke23:16 Mo pou dir bannla fwet li apre sa mo pou larg li.”
Luke23:17 Pou sak fet Pak, Pilat ti abitie larg enn prizonie."
Luke23:18 Me zot tou kriye bien for, “Fini li enn fwa, larg Barabas.”"
Luke23:19 Barabas ti dan prizon parski li ti finn diriz enn emet dan lavil e li ti finn komet enn krim.
Luke23:20 Pilat ti ankor anvi liber Zezi, alors li kontigne diskit ar zot."
Luke23:21 Me zot revolte, zot kriye pli for, “Krisifie li! Krisifie li!”"
Luke23:22 Trwaziem fwa, li redir zot, “Ki krim li finn fer? Mo pa trouv okenn sarz ki dir ki li merit lamor. Mo pou dimann bannla fwet li apre sa mo pou relarg li.”"
Luke23:23 Me zot kriye ankor pli for e zot dimann koulout li lor lakrwa. Zot lavwa dominn partou.
Luke23:24 Lerla Pilat desid donn zot seki zot pe dimande.
Luke23:25 Li larg sa boug ki zot ti dimann pou grasie la, e ki ti dan prizon akoz enn emet ek enn krim, e li livre zot Zezi dapre ki zot ti pe rode."
Luke23:26 Letan bannla ti pe amenn Zezi, zot zwenn Simon ki enn abitan lavil Sirenn. Li ti sorti dan karo, li pe ale. Zot aret li pou li sarye lakrwa deryer Zezi."
Luke23:27 Enn gran lafoul ti pe swiv li; bann fam ti pe kriye, plore e zot ti pe sagrin li."
Luke23:28 Zezi vire, get par deryer e li dir zot, “Fam, zot ki tifi Zerizalem, pa plor pou mwa. Plor plito pou zotmem e pou zot bann zanfan."
Luke23:29 Parski zour pou vini kot zot pou dir, ‘Bienerez bann fam ki pa kapav gagn zanfan, bann seki zame finn akouse, bann ki zame finn donn bwar.’"
Luke23:30 Alor dimoun pou dir bann montagn, Tom lor nou, ek kolinn Kasiet nou,"
Luke23:31 Parski si zot fer koumsa ar dibwa ver, ki zot pou fer ar dibwa sek?”"
Luke23:32 Ti amenn osi ansam avek li de malfeter ki ti finn kondane amor.
Luke23:33 Ler zot ariv landrwa ki ti apel Krann, zot koulout li lor lakrwa e zot met bann malfeter la, enn dan so drwat ek lotla dan so gos."
Luke23:34 Zezi dir, “Papa pardonn zot parski zot pa kone ki zot pe fer.” Zot fer enn tiraz osor pou partaz so linz."
Luke23:35 Lepep ti pe dibout e ti pe gete. Bann sef Zwif ti pe kontigne boufonn li. Zot ti pe dir, “Li finn sov lezot; les li sov limem si vremem li Lekris ki Bondie finn swazir.”"
Luke23:36 Bann solda boufonn li. Zot koste pre ar li e zot donn li vineg.
Luke23:37 Zot dir li, “Si to Lerwa Zwif, sov twa tomem.”"
Luke23:38 Lao lor lakrwa ti finn ekrir, “Limem Lerwa Zwif.”"
Luke23:39 Enn sa de kriminel ki ti lor lakrwa la insilte li. Li dir li, “Eski to pa Lekris? Sov twa tomem ek sov nou.”"
Luke23:40 Lotla repros li, “To pa gagn per Bondie, twa ki finn kondane parey kouma li?"
Luke23:41 Nou, nou pe gagn seki nou merite parski nou pe pey pou seki nou finn fer, me li, li pa finn fer nanye de mal.”"
Luke23:42 E li dir Zezi, “Zezi pa bliye mwa kan to vini kouma Lerwa.”"
Luke23:43 Zezi reponn li, “Laverite, laverite mo dir twa, azordi mem to pou avek mwa dan paradi.”"
Luke23:44 Ti apepre midi, letan teneb tom lor antie later ziska trwa-zer tanto."
Luke23:45 Letan soley aret briye, rido tanp desire damilie."
Luke23:46 Zezi kriye bien for, “Papa, mo met mo lespri dan to lame.” Letan li fini dir sa, li rann so dernie soupir."
Luke23:47 Letan santiryon Romin trouv seki ti finn arive, li rann laglwar Bondie, li dir, “Vremem sa dimoun la ti inosan.”"
Luke23:48 Kan sa gran lafoul ki ti finn vini pou get spektak la trouv seki ti finn arive, zot rant kot zot latet bese."
Luke23:49 Tou bann kamarad Zezi ek bann fam ki ti akonpagn li depi Galile ti pe dibout lwin e zot ti pe get seki ti pe pase.
Luke23:50 Ti ena enn dimoun ki ti apel Zozef ki ti sorti Arimate, enn lavil Zwif. Li ti bon ek bien drwat e li ti enn manm Gran Tribinal bann Zwif. Li pa ti dakor ar zot desizion e zot aksion, e li ti pe atann Rwayom Bondie."
Luke23:51 Zozef al get Pilat e li dimann li lekor Zezi.
Luke23:52 Li desann so lekor e li anvlop li dan enn dra an lin e li met li dan enn tom ki ti finn kreze dan ros kot personn pa ti ankor antere.
Luke23:53 Ti vandredi, zour Preparasion, e saba ti pre pou koumanse."
Luke23:54 Bann fam ki ti pe swiv Zezi depi Galile vinn avek Zozef e zot trouv tom kot ti met so lekor.
Luke23:55 Apre sa zot retourne e zot prepar bann delwil ek bann parfin. Zour saba, zot repoze dapre seki lalwa dir."
Luke24:1 Premie zour lasemenn, boner dimans gramatin, detrwa fam vinn lor tonbo avek delwil parfime ki zot ti finn prepare."
Luke24:2 Me zot trouv ros lantre tonbo ti finn avanse.
Luke24:3 Zot rantre me zot pa trouv lekor Segner Zezi.
Luke24:4 Zot pa pe konpran seki finn arive e anmemtan de zom paret devan zot. Zot linz ti pe briye.
Luke24:5 Kouma zot ti pe gagn per e zot ti pe bes zot latet anba, sa de zom la dir zot, “Kifer zot pe rod enn dimoun vivan parmi bann mor;"
Luke24:6 li pa isi, li finn resisite. Rapel seki li ti dir zot kan li ti dan Galile."
Luke24:7 ‘Fode ki Garson Limanite livre dan lame bann peser, ki li kouloute lor lakrwa avan ki li resisite lor so trwaziem zour.’ ”"
Luke24:8 Lerla zot rapel sa bann parol la.
Luke24:9 Zot kit tonbo pou rakont sa onz disip ek bann lezot.
Luke24:10 Ti ena Marie Madlenn, Zann ek Marie, mama Zak ek detrwa ankor ki ti avek zot. Zot rakont sa bann apot."
Luke24:11 Me bannla panse ki zot ti pe divage e zot pa ti krwar parol bann fam la.
Luke24:12 Pier leve e galoupe, al dan tonbo. Li bese e li trouv zis bann bandaz an lin; apre sa li retourn kot li. Li ti res bet par seki ti finn pase."
Luke24:13 Sa zour la, de parmi zot, ti pe al dan zot vilaz Emais ki ti apepre de zer-tan marse depi Zerizalem."
Luke24:14 Zot ti pe koz lor tou seki ti finn deroule.
Luke24:15 Kan zot ti pe koze ek diskite, Zezi koste ar zot e mars ar zot."
Luke24:16 Zot trouv li me zot lizie pa rekonet li.
Luke24:17 Li dir zot, “Ki zot pe dialoge letan zot pe marse? “ Zot arete, figir tipti."
Luke24:18 Seki ti apel Kleopas dir li, “To tousel dan Zerizalem pa kone seki finn arive sa detrwa zour la isi?”"
