John16:22 Asterla zot dan lapenn me kan mo pou retrouv zot ankor, zot leker pou dan lazwa e personn pa pou kapav retir sa lazwa la ar zot."
John16:23 Kan sa zour la vini, zot nepli pou poz mwa okenn kestion; vremem, laverite mo dir zot, tou seki zot demann mo Papa lor mo nom, li pou donn zot."
John16:24 Ziska asterla, zot pa finn demann nanye lor mo nom; demande, zot pou resevwar, lerla zot pou ranpli ar lazwa."
John16:25 Mo finn koz ar zot an parabol; me ler pe vini kot mo nepli pou koz an parabol me mo pou direk ar zot, ler mo koz lor mo Papa"
John16:26 Sa zour la, zot pou demann kiksoz mo Papa lor mo nom, san ki mo ena pou koz pou zot."
John16:27 Mo Papa bien kontan zot parski zot finn kontan mwa e zot finn krwar ki mo sorti kot Bondie.
John16:28 Mo sorti kot mo Papa e mo finn vinn dan lemonn; mo pe kit lemonn e mo pe retourn kot mo Papa.”
John16:29 So disip dir, “Aster to direk ar nou e to nepli koz an parabol."
John16:30 Aster nou kone ki to konn tou kiksoz e ki pa bizin poz twa kestion; akoz samem nou krwar to sorti kot Bondie.”
John16:31 Zezi dir, “Eski zot krwar asterla?"
John16:32 Gete, ler pe vini, ler inn fini vini, kot zot pou disperse e kot sakenn pou retourn kot li. Zot pou les mwa tousel, me mo pa tousel parski mo Papa touzour avek mwa."
John16:33 Mo finn dir zot tousala pou zot gagn lape an mwa. Lemonn pou fer zot soufer; me gard kouraz, mo finn sorti vinker lor lemonn.”"
John17:1 Letan Zezi finn fini dir tousala, li lev so lizie, li get lesiel e li dir, “Papa, ler finn vini; glorifie to Garson, pouki to Garson glorifie twa."
John17:2 Vremem, to finn donn li pouvwar lor tou dimoun e li finn donn lavi eternel tou seki to finn konfie li."
John17:3 Ki ete lavi eternel? Se dekouver ki tomem vre Bondie e ki Zezi Kris, limem ki to finn avoye."
John17:4 Mo finn glorifie twa lor later par tou seki mo finn fer; mo finn terminn louvraz ki to ti donn mwa pou fer.
John17:5 Papa, glorifie mwa aster; donn mwa laglwar ki mo ti ena kot twa depi komansman, avan ki later ti kre."
John17:6 Mo finn fer tou dimoun ki to finn donn mwa lor later, konn to nom; zot ti pou twa, to finn donn mwa zot tou e zot finn gard to parol."
John17:7 Asterla zot finn konpran ki tou seki to finn donn mwa sorti kot twa.
John17:8 Mo finn donn zot parol ki to finn konfie mwa, e zot finn resevwar li. Zot finn rekonet ki vremem mo finn sorti kot twa, e zot krwar ki to finn avoy mwa."
John17:9 Mo priye pou zot; mo pa pe priye pou lemonn me mo priye pou tou seki to finn konfie mwa, parski zot tou pou twa."
John17:10 Tou seki pou mwa, pou twa e tou seki pou twa, pou mwa; mo laglwar reflekte lor zot figir."
John17:11 Mo nepli dan lemonn alors ki zot ankor dan lemonn; mwa mo pe vinn kot twa. Bondie sin, mo Papa! Protez zot par pouvwar ki to finn donn mwa. Lerla zot pou vinn enn sel kouma nou."
John17:12 Kan mo ti avek zot, mo ti gard zot tou par pouvwar to nom ki to finn donn mwa; mo finn vey lor zot, e personn pa finn perdi exsepte sa dimoun ki ti bizin perdi la pouki Lekritir akonpli."
John17:13 Asterla mo pe vinn kot twa e mo pe dir tousa dan lemonn pouki zot leker deborde ar mo lazwa.
John17:14 Mo finn konfie zot to parol me lemonn deteste zot parski zot pa dan lemonn parey kouma mwa, mo pa dan lemonn."
John17:15 Mo pa pe dimann twa, tir zot dan lemonn me protez zot kont lemal."
John17:16 Zot pa dan lemonn parey kouma mwa, mo pa dan lemonn."
John17:17 Sanktifie zot dan laverite parski to parol laverite.
John17:18 Parey kouma to finn avoy mwa dan lemonn, mwa osi mo finn avoy zot dan lemonn."
John17:19 Mo finn konsakre mwa antierman pou zot; asterla, zot osi, zot pou konsakre zot dan laverite."
John17:20 Mo pa priye zis pou zot me mo priye pou tou seki pou krwar dan mwa, par parol ki mo disip pou anonse."
John17:21 Mo priye pouki zot tou vinn enn sel e ki zot res ar nou parey kouma twa Papa, to dan mwa e mwa mo dan twa. Lerla lemonn pou krwar ki to finn avoy mwa."
John17:22 Mo finn donn zot laglwar ki to finn donn mwa pouki zot vinn enn sel parey kouma nou, nou enn sel."
John17:23 Mwa dan zot, twa dan mwa pouki zot vinn enn sel. Lerla lemonn pou kone ki to finn avoy mwa, ki mo kontan zot kouma to kontan mwa."
John17:24 Papa, seki to finn konfie mwa, mo anvi ki la kot mo ete zot avek mwa; koumsa zot kontanp laglwar ki to finn donn mwa e zot pou kone ki to kontan mwa depi avan komansman kreasion."
John17:25 Twa Papa ki zis, lemonn pa konn twa; mwa mo finn konn twa e zot kone ki to finn avoy mwa."
John17:26 Mo finn fer zot konn to nom e mo pe fer li ankor pouki lamour ki to ena pou mwa res dan zot, kouma mwa mo dan zot.”"
John18:1 Apre sa bann parol la, Zezi sorti avek so bann disip. Li sot larivier Sedron, li rant dan enn zardin avek so bann disip."
John18:2 Zida, ki pou trayir Zezi, ti konn osi sa landrwa la parski Zezi ti vinn la souvan avek so bann disip."
John18:3 Zida vinn avek enn larme solda ek bann gard ki bann gran pret ek bann Farizien finn donn li; zot ti ena lalanp ek flanbo e zot ti arme ar gourdin.
John18:4 Zezi ti konn tou seki ti pou ariv li; li vinn devan zot e li demann zot, “Kisannla zot pe rode?”"
John18:5 Zot reponn, “Zezi Nazaret.” Li dir zot, “Mwa sa.” Zida, ki pou trayir Zezi, ti pe debout la avek zot."
John18:6 Kouma li dir zot, “Mwa sa”, bannla kil deryer e zot tom anba."
John18:7 Zezi redemann zot ankor, “Kisannla zot pe rode?” Zot dir, “Zezi Nazaret.”"
John18:8 Zezi reponn zot, “Mo finn dir zot, mwa sa; si momem ki zot pe rode, les bannla, ale.”"
John18:9 Lerla Parol ki finn dir realize, “Mo pa finn perdi personn ki to finn konfie mwa.”"
John18:10 Simon Pier pran lepe ki ti ar li, donn serviter gran pret enn kout lepe e koup so zorey drwat. Serviter la ti apel Malkis."
John18:11 Zezi dir Pier, “Remet to lepe dan so fouro; eski mo pa pou bwar koup ki mo Papa finn donn mwa?”"
John18:12 Alors enn larme solda ek so komandan ek gard Zwif aret Zezi. Zot atas li.
John18:13 Zot amenn li devan Ann premie kout. Ann ti bo-per Kaif ki ti gran pret sa lane la.
John18:14 Kaif mem ki finn konsey bann Zwif, “Li preferab pou zot ki enn sel dimoun mor pou tou lepep.”"
John18:15 Simon Pier ek enn lot disip ti pe swiv Zezi. Gran Pret ti konn disip la, akoz samem li finn les li rant avek Zezi dan lakour."
John18:16 Me Pier ti pe debout deor devan laport. Disip ki gran pret ti kone, sorti deor, koz ar fam ki ti pe vey laport la e disip la fer Pier rantre."
John18:17 Fam la dir ar Pier, “Eski twa osi to pa enn disip sa boug la?” Li reponn, “Mwa? Non.”"
John18:18 Bann serviter ek bann gard ti pe debout. Zot finn alim enn dife parski ti pe fer fre. Pier ti la ar zot e li osi ti pe sof dife.
John18:19 Alors gran pret poz Zezi kestion lor so bann disip e lor so lansegnman.
John18:20 Zezi reponn li, “Mo finn koz devan tou dimoun lor later; mo finn ansegn toultan dan sinagog e dan tanp, la kot tou bann Zwif rasanble; zame mo finn kasiet pou koze."
John18:21 Kifer to poz mwa sa bann kestion la? Al demann bann dimoun ki finn vinn ekout mwa; zot va dir twa ki mo finn dir zot; zot konn bien seki mo finn dir.”
John18:22 Letan bannla tann sa parol la, enn gard ki ti la donn Zezi enn kalot. Li dir Zezi, “Enn manier pou koz ar gran pret sa?”"
John18:23 Zezi reponn li, “Si mo koze pa bon, montre mwa seki pa bon me si mo koze bon, ki fer to bat mwa?”"
John18:24 Alors Ann avoy Zezi devan Kaif ki ti gran pret. Zezi ti touzour atase.
John18:25 Letan sa, Simon Pier ti pe debout e li ti pe sof dife. Bannla demann li, “Eski twa osi to pa enn so bann disip?” Li renie Zezi e li dir, “Mwa? Non.”"
John18:26 Enn serviter gran pret, fami boug ki Pier ti koup so zorey la, dir, “Eski mo pa finn trouv twa dan zardin avek li?”"
John18:27 Ankor enn fwa, Pier renie. Lerla mem kok sante."
John18:28 Boner gramatin, zot pran Zezi kot Kaif e zot amenn li devan pale gouverner. Zot pa rant dan pale pouki zot pa vinn inpir e pouki zot kapav manz repa Paskal."
John18:29 Akoz samem Pilat sorti deor e vinn get zot. Li demande, “Ki sarz zot ena kont sa boug la?”"
John18:30 Zot dir, “Nou pa ti pou amenn li devan twa, si li pa ti enn malfeter.”"
John18:31 Pilat reponn, “Pran li zotmem, ziz li dapre zot lalwa.” Bann Zwif dir, “Dapre nou lalwa nou pa gagn drwat tir lavi dimoun.”"
John18:32 Lerla parol Zezi realize kan li ti pe dir ki manier li ti pou mor.
John18:33 Ankor enn fwa, Pilat rant dan so pale, li apel Zezi e li dir, “Eski to lerwa Zwif, twa?”"
John18:34 Zezi reponn, “Seki to pe dir lor mwa, eski to pe dir sa par to prop lide ou bien lot dimoun finn dir twa?”"
John18:35 Pilat dir, “Eski mo enn Zwif mwa? To prop dimoun ek bann gran pret finn livre twa ar mwa; ki to finn fer koumsa?”"
John18:36 Zezi reponn, “Mo Rwayom pa lor later; si mo Rwayom ti lor later, mo bann gard ti pou lager pou mwa, pouki bannla pa livre mwa ar bann Zwif. Me vremem, mo Rwayom pa la isi.”"
John18:37 Lerla Pilat dir, “Alors to enn lerwa?” Zezi reponn, “Twa ki pe dir. Mo finn ne, mo finn vinn dan lemonn pou enn sel rezon: rann temwagnaz laverite. Tou dimoun ki dan laverite, ekout mo lavwa.”"
John18:38 Pilat demann Zezi, “Ki ete laverite?” Apre sa dialog la, Pilat sorti deor ankor enn fwa; li al get bann Zwif e li dir zot, “Mo pa trouv okenn rezon pou kondann li."
John18:39 Dapre zot koutim, mo abitie larg enn prizonie pou Pak; eski zot oule mo larg lerwa Zwif?”"
John18:40 Zot tou kriye, “Non, pa li! Larg Barabas.” Barabas la ti enn bandi."
John19:1 Apre sa Pilat pran Zezi e li donn lord pou fwet li.
John19:2 Bann solda tres enn kouronn pikan e fons sa lor so latet; zot met enn manto rouz fonse lor li.
John19:3 Zot vinn devan li e zot salye li, “Me respe lerwa Zwif!” Lerla zot donn li kalot."
John19:4 Pilat sorti deor ankor enn fwa e li dir bannla, “Gete, mo amenn li devan zot pouki zot kone ki mo pa trouv nanye de mal ar li.”"
John19:5 Lerla Zezi vinn deor avek so kouronn pikan lor so latet ek so manto rouz fonse lor li. Pilat dir zot, “Ala zom la.”"
John19:6 Kan bann gran pret ek bann gard trouv li, zot kriye bien-bien for, “Krisifie li, krisifie li.” Pilat dir, “Pran li, krisifie li zotmem parski mwa, mo pa trouv okenn rezon fer sa.”"
John19:7 Bann Zwif reponn, “Nou ena enn lalwa e dapre sa lalwa la, li bizin mor parski li deklar li Garson Bondie.”"
John19:8 Ler Pilat tann sa bann parol la, li gagn plis per ankor."
John19:9 Li rerant dan so pale e li demann Zezi, “Kot to sorti?” Me Zezi pa reponn."
John19:10 Lerla Pilat dir, “To pale reponn mwa? To pa kone mo ena pouvwar pou larg twa ek pouvwar pou krisifie twa?”"
John19:11 Zezi reponn, “To pena pouvwar lor mwa exsepte seki to finn resevwar depi lao. Akoz samem sa dimoun ki finn livre mwa la, so pese pli gran ki pou twa.”"
John19:12 Lerla Pilat ti pe rod tou mwayin pou larg li me bann Zwif kontigne kriye e zot dir, “Si to larg li, to pa kamarad lanperer; dimoun ki deklar li lerwa pe kont lanperer.”"
John19:13 Letan Pilat finn tann sa bann parol la, li amenn Zezi deor. Pilat asiz dan fotey kot ziz rann zizman, dan enn landrwa ki ti apel ‘Pavaz’ ki vedir ‘Gabata’ an Ebre."
John19:14 Ti lavey Pak e ti pre pou midi. Pilat dir ar bann Zwif, “Ala zot lerwa.”"
John19:15 Me zot tou kriye, “Touy li, koulout li lor lakrwa.” Pilat dir zot, “Eski mo pou krisifie zot lerwa?” Bann gran pret reponn, “Nou pena lot lerwa apart lanperer.”"
John19:16 Alors Pilat livre Zezi pouki bannla krisifie li. Zot pran Zezi.
John19:17 Li sorti, li ale e limem sarye so lakrwa; li ariv dan enn landrwa ki ti apel ‘Krann’, an Ebre: Golgota."
John19:18 Zot krisifie li lamem; ti ena de lot dimoun avek li, enn sak kote, Zezi dan milie."
John19:19 Pilat finn ekrir lor enn plak pou met lor lakrwa, “Zezi Nazaret Lerwa Zwif.”"
John19:20 Boukou Zwif finn lir plak la parski Zezi finn krisifie pre ar lavil; ti ekrir li an Ebre, Latin ek Grek."
John19:21 Bann gran pret dir Pilat, “Pa ekrir, ‘Lerwa Zwif’, me ‘Li finn dir mo lerwa Zwif’.”"
John19:22 Pilat reponn, “Seki mo finn ekrir, mo finn ekrir.”"
John19:23 Kan bann solda inn fini krisifie Zezi, zot pran so manto, zot diviz li an-kat e sak solda gagn enn par. Zot inn pran osi so rob ki ti fer avek enn sel bout latwal, san okenn koutir."
John19:24 Zot dir ant zot, “Pa bizin desir so rob me anou fer enn tiraz osor, seki gagne, pran li.” Tou sa la finn pase pouki sa parol Lekritir la realize, ‘Zot finn partaz mo manto ant zot Zot finn fer enn tiraz osor lor mo linz.’ Ala seki bann solda inn fer."
John19:25 Kot lakrwa Zezi, ti ena so mama, ser so mama, Marie, fam Klopa ek Marie Madlenn ki ti pe debout."
John19:26 Letan Zezi trouv so mama ek pre ar li, disip ki li ti kontan la, li dir ar so mama, “Fam, ala to garson.”"
John19:27 Apre li dir ar disip la, “Ala to mama.” Depi sa, disip la pran so mama kot li."
John19:28 Apre tousala, letan Zezi trouve ki tou asterla finn akonpli, e pouki Lekritir realiz ziska dan bout, li dir, “Mo swaf.”"
John19:29 Ti ena la enn bol plin ar vineg; alors bann solda met enn leponz dan vineg, zot fons leponz la dan enn bout baton e zot met li kot labous Zezi."
John19:30 Zezi pran vineg la, apre li dir, “Tou inn fini.” Li bes so latet e li rann so dernie soupir."
John19:31 Kouma ti zour preparasion avan Pak, bann Zwif pa ti oule ki bann lekor res lor lakrwa zour saba, (parski sa saba la ti enn zour espesial); alors zot demann Pilat, kas lipie bannla pouki kapav desann zot."
John19:32 Bann solda vini. Zot kas lipie premie boug la, answit deziem la, e"
John19:33 kan zot vinn devan Zezi, zot konstate ki li finn fini mor. Alors zot pa kas so lipie."
John19:34 Enn parmi bann solda pik so lans dan kot Zezi; lerla disan ek dilo koule.
John19:35 Dimoun ki finn trouv sa pe donn so temwagnaz pouki zot osi, zot kapav krwar; li kone ki li pe dir laverite."
John19:36 Tousala finn arive pouki Lekritir realize, “Pa pou kas okenn so lezo.”"
John19:37 Enn lot pasaz dir ankor, “Zot pou fixe zot regar lor Sa-Enn ki zot finn transperse la.”"
John19:38 Apre sa, Zozef ki sorti Arimate, demann Pilat si li kapav pran lekor Zezi. (Zozef finn swiv Zezi me san ki personn kone, parski li ti gagn per bann Zwif). Pilat donn li permision pran so lekor. Alors li ale e li pran lekor Zezi."
John19:39 Nikodem, ki ti vinn zwenn Zezi dan nwar premie fwa ki li ti vinn get li, finn amenn enn melanz lamir ek lalwes, anviron san liv pou anbom so lekor."
John19:40 Zot pran lekor Zezi, zot anvlop li avek bann bandaz an lin; dan sa bandaz la zot met melanz la dapre koutim Zwif kan met enn lekor dan tonbo."
John19:41 Dan landrwa kot Zezi ti krisifie, ti ena enn zardin e dan sa zardin la, ti ena enn nouvo tonbo ki pa ti ankor servi."
John19:42 Kouma ti lavey saba e ki tonbo la ti pre, zot met Zezi ladan."
John20:1 Premie zour lasemenn, boner gramatin kan ti ankor fer nwar, Marie Madlenn al dan tonbo e li konstate ki ros ki ti devan lantre tonbo, finn avanse."
John20:2 Lerla li galoupe, li al get Simon Pier e lot disip ki Zezi ti kontan la e li dir zot, “Zot finn kokin Lesegner dan tonbo e nou pa kone kot zot finn al met li.”"
John20:3 Lerla Pier ek lot disip la sorti pou al dan tonbo.
John20:4 Toulede galoupe ale me lot disip la galoup pli vit ki Pier e li ariv avan li dan tonbo.
John20:5 Li bese pou gete e li trouv bann bandaz an lin anba me li pa rantre.
John20:6 Ler Simon Pier, ki ti pe vinn deryer li, arive, li rant dan tonbo e li trouv bann bandaz an lin."
John20:7 Linz ki ti servi pou rekouver so latet, ti nepli avek bann bandaz me finn anroule apar dan enn lot plas."
John20:8 Apre sa, lot disip ki finn ariv premie dan tonbo, rantre li osi. Ler li trouve, li krwar."
John20:9 Tou sa letan la, zot pa finn konpran ki li ti bizin resisite parmi bann mor parey kouma finn ekrir dan liv."
John20:10 Apre sa, bann disip la retourn kot zot."
John20:11 Marie ti pe asize deor, pre ar tonbo e li ti pe plore. Letan li ti pe plore, li bese pou get dan tonbo."
John20:12 Li trouv de anz abiye anblan ki ti pe asize; zot ti la, kot ti met lekor Zezi, enn kot latet, lot kot lipie."
John20:13 Zot dir, “Fam, ki fer to pe plore?” Li dir zot, “Zot finn kokin mo Segner e mo pa kone kot zot finn al met li.”"
John20:14 Letan li finn fini dir sa, li vir deryer e li trouv Zezi ki ti pe debout, me li pa ti rekonet li."
John20:15 Zezi dir li, “Fam, ki fer to pe plore? Kisannla to pe rode?” Li ti krwar zardinie e li dir, “Misie, si twa ki finn pran li, dir mwa kot to finn met li, mo pou al sers li.”"
John20:16 Zezi dir, “Marie.” Marie vire e dir an Ebre, “Rabouni!” (Seki vedir Met)."
John20:17 Zezi dir, “Pa tous mwa, parski mo pankor mont kot mo Papa. Al kot mo bann frer e dir zot, ‘Mo pe al kot mo Papa ek zot Papa, kot mo Bondie ek zot Bondie.’ ”"
John20:18 Marie Madlenn sorti e al anons bann disip, “Mo finn trouv Lesegner!” E li rakont zot seki Zezi finn dir."
John20:19 Aswar premie zour lasemenn, bann disip ti ansam dan enn lakaz. Zot inn met lakle dan laport parski zot ti gagn per bann Zwif. Zezi vini, li debout devan zot e li dir, “Shalom”."
John20:20 Kan li fini salye zot, li montre zot so lame ek so kot. Bann disip ti dan enn gran lazwa kan zot finn trouv Lesegner."
John20:21 Zezi dir zot ankor, “Lape avek zot; parey kouma mo Papa finn avoy mwa, mo osi mo avoy zot.”"
John20:22 Apre sa, Zezi soufle lor zot e dir zot, “Ala Lespri Sin."
John20:23 Si zot pardonn pese dimoun, pese la pou pardone, si zot tini pese dimoun, pese la pou tini.”"
John20:24 Toma, enn parmi Ledouz, (so nom gate Didim, ki vedir Zimo), pa ti avek zot kan Zezi ti vini."
John20:25 Bann lezot disip inn dir li, “Nou finn trouv Lesegner.” Me li dir zot, “Si mo pa trouv ar mo lizie bann mark koulou dan so lame, si mo pa met mo ledwa dan so ple e si mo pa met mo lame dan so kot, mo pa pou krwar.”"
John20:26 Wit zour apre, bann disip ti ansam dan lakaz e Toma ti avek zot. Ti ena lakle dan laport e Zezi vini, li debout devan zot e li dir, “Shalom.”"
John20:27 Apre li dir ar Toma, “Met to le dwa isi, ala mo lame; pran to lame, met li dan mo kot. Pa doute me krwar.”"
John20:28 Toma dir, “Mo Segner, mo Bondie.”"
John20:29 Zezi dir, “Akoz to trouve, to finn krwar? Bienere seki krwar san trouve.”"
John20:30 Zezi finn fer devan so bann disip boukou lot sign ki pa finn ekrir dan sa liv la.
John20:31 Tousala finn ekrir pouki zot krwar ki Zezi-mem Lekris, Garson Bondie e pouki bann seki krwar gagn lavi par so nom."
John21:1 Apre sa, Zezi re-aparet devan so bann disip dan borlamer Tiberiad. Ala kouma sa finn pase."
John21:2 Ti ena Simon Pier, Toma, (so nom gate Didim), Natanael (limem sorti Kana, enn vilaz dan Galile), de garson Zebede ek de disip ankor."
John21:3 Simon Pier dir zot, “Mo pe al lapes.” Zot dir li, “Nou osi, nou vinn ar twa.” Zot mont lor bato, zot ale, enn nwit zot pa may nanye."
John21:4 Kan lizour ti pe koumans paret, Zezi ti pe debout dan bor dilo, me bann disip pa ti kone si li sa."
John21:5 Zezi dir zot, “Mo bann zanfan, pena pwason?” Zot reponn li, “Non, pena.”"
John21:6 Li dir zot, “Zet zot file kote drwat zot pou trouve.” Lerla zot zete. Telman file ti ranpli ar pwason ki zot ti nepli ena lafors pou ris li."
John21:7 Disip ki Zezi ti kontan la dir Pier, “Lesegner sa.” Letan Simon Pier tande ki ti Lesegner sa, li pas so linz lor li, parski li ti touni, e li zete, li naze."
John21:8 Lezot disip vinn ater dan bato. Kouma zot pa ti lwin ar laplaz, apepre san met, zot ris zot file ranpli ar pwason deryer zot."
John21:9 Letan zot finn fini desann ater, zot trouv enn ti dife; lor dife la pwason ti pe griye e ti ena dipin osi."
John21:10 Zezi dir zot, “Amenn inpe pwason ki zot finn lapes zordi.”"
John21:11 Lerla Simon Pier mont lor bato e li ris ater file ki ti ranpli ar gro-gro pwason. Ti ena san sinkann-trwa e zot tou tini dan file la san ki li defonse.
John21:12 Zezi dir zot, “Vinn manze.” Personn parmi bann disip pa oze demann li, “Ki to ete?” Zot ti kone se Lesegner."
John21:13 Zezi vini, pran dipin e donn zot e li fer parey ar pwason."
John21:14 Sa fer trwaziem fwa ki Zezi aparet ar so bann disip depi ki li finn resisite parmi lemor.
John21:15 Kan zot finn fini manze, Zezi demann Simon Pier, “Simon garson Zan eski to kontan mwa plis ki bannla kontan mwa?” Li reponn, “Wi Segner, to kone ki mo kontan twa.” Zezi dir li, “Donn mo bann timouton manze.”"
John21:16 Li demann li enn deziem fwa, “Simon garson Zan, eski to kontan mwa?” Simon reponn li, “Wi Segner, to kone mo kontan twa.” Zezi dir li, “Pran swin mo bann brebi.”"
John21:17 Zezi demann li enn trwaziem fwa, “Simon garson Zan, eski to kontan mwa?” Pier sagrin ki Zezi demann li enn trwaziem fwa, “Eski to kontan mwa?” Lerla Pier reponn, “Segner, to konn tou, to kone ki mo kontan twa.” Zezi dir li, “Donn manze mo bann mouton."
John21:18 Vremem, laverite mo dir twa, kan to ti zenn, to ti met to sang par tomem e to ti al kot to kontan; me kan to pou vinn vie, to pou lev to lame lao e enn lot ki pou atas to sang e pou amenn twa kot to pa anvi ale.”"
John21:19 (Li finn dir sa pou montre par ki kalite lamor Pier pou glorifie Bondie). Apre sa Zezi dir li, “Swiv mwa.”"
John21:20 Pier vir deryer e li trouv disip ki Zezi ti kontan. Li ti pe swiv zot. Limem ti met so latet lor lestoma Zezi pandan repa e ti dir, ‘Segner, kisannla pou vann twa?’"
John21:21 Letan Pier trouv disip la, li dir Zezi, “E li, Segner, ki pou ariv li?”"
John21:22 Zezi dir li, “Si mo le ki li res ziska mo revini, eski to problem sa? Twa, swiv mwa.”"
John21:23 Sa parol la finn sirkile parmi bann frer e zot ti krwar ki sa disip la pa pou mor; me Zezi pa ti pe dir ki li pa pou mor me, “Si mo le ki li res ziska mo revini, eski to problem sa?”"
John21:24 Sa disip la pe donn so temwagnaz lor tousala e limem finn ekrir tou sa e nou kone seki li finn rakonte, li vre."
John21:25 Zezi inn fer boukou kiksoz ankor. Si ti ena pou ekrir tousala, mo panse ki lemonn antie pa pou ase gran pou gard tou sa bann liv la."
Acts1:1 Dan mo premie liv, Teofil, mo finn ekrir lor tou seki Zezi ti koumans fer ek ansegne"
Acts1:2 ziska ki li mont dan lesiel. Avan sa, li ti donn instriksion, par Lespri Sin, bann apot ki li ti swazir."
Acts1:3 Apre so lamor, li ti donn zot boukou prev ki li ankor vivan. Li ti aparet ar zot pandan karant zour e li ti koz ar zot lor Rwayom Bondie."
Acts1:4 Letan li ti pe manze ansam ar zot, li ti donn zot lord napa kit Zerizalem, me atann ki promes so Papa realize kouma li ti dir,"
Acts1:5 “Zan finn batiz ar dilo, me zot, dan enn de zour zot pou resevwar batem dan Lespri Sin.”"
Acts1:6 Alor ler zot ti zwenn ansam, zot dimann Zezi, “Segner, eski asterlamem ki to pou remet Rwayom Izrael dibout?”"
Acts1:7 Zezi reponn, “Zot pena pou kone ki ler ki moman, mo Papa limem finn deside."
Acts1:8 Me zot pou gagn enn lafors kan Lespri Sin pou desann lor zot - lerla zot pou vinn mo temwin dan Zerizalem, dan Zide ek Samari e partou lor later.”"
Acts1:9 Kouma Zezi ti fini koze, li ti mont dan ler e li disparet dan enn niaz."
Acts1:10 Zot ti ankor pe get li monte dan lesiel kan zot trouv de zom anblan kot zot
Acts1:11 ki dir zot, “Bann abitan Galile, kifer zot pe kontign get lao dan lesiel koumsa? Sa Zezi la ki finn separe ar zot pou al dan lesiel, pou retourne parey kouma zot finn trouv li ale.”"
Acts1:12 Lerla zot ti retourn Zerizalem depi Kolinn Pie Zoliv, enn distans ki ti permet pou marse zour saba, setadir enn kilomet."
Acts1:13 Kan zot ti ariv Zerizalem, zot ti mont dan lasam dan lakaz kot zot ti pe reste; la ti ena Pier, Zan, Zak ek Andre, Filip ek Toma, Bartelmy ek Matie; Zak garson Alfe, Simon Zelot e Zid, garson Zak."
Acts1:14 Zot tou ti plonze dan lapriyer ansam avek detrwa fam. Parmi ti ena Marie, mama Zezi ek so bann frer."
Acts1:15 Detrwa zour apre, Pier debout dan milie bann frer ki ti la; ti ena anviron san-vin e li ti dir,"
Acts1:16 “Mo bann frer, Lekritir ti bizin akonpli, la kot Lespri Sin ti predir par labous David konsernan Zida ki ti servi kouma gid letan bannla ti vinn aret Zezi."
Acts1:17 Li ti parmi nou e li ti ena so par dan nou mision.”
Acts1:18 (Sa zom la finn aste enn terin avek kas ki li ti finn resevwar pou so traizon - li finn tom tou so grander, so vant finn ouver e tou so trip finn sorti deor."
Acts1:19 Tou dimoun Zerizalem finn konn sa e zot finn apel sa terin la ‘Akeldama’, seki vedir, ‘Karo disan.’)"
Acts1:20 “Koumsamem finn ekrir dan liv Psom: ‘Ki so Lakaz vinn dezer, ki personn pa res ladan.’ Finn osi ekrir: ‘Ki enn lot pran so plas.’"
Acts1:21 Parmi bann dimoun ki ti mars avek nou depi batem Zan letan Lesegner Zezi ti ale-vini parmi nou ziska ki li ti remont dan lesiel,"
Acts1:22 omwin enn bizin zwenn ar nou pou fer temwagnaz lor rezireksion Zezi.”
Acts1:23 Zot ti propoz de nom: Zozef ki ti apel Barsabas (li osi apel Zistis) ek enn lot ki ti apel Matias.
Acts1:24 Lerla zot ti priye e dir, “Segner, twa ki konn leker tou dimoun, dir nou kisannla ant sa de la to finn swazir pou ranplas"
Acts1:25 Zida ki finn abandonn so plas apot pou al kot li finn ale.”
Acts1:26 Zot tir lakourt-pay e nom Matias sorti. Li ti vinn zwenn avek lezot onz apot.
Acts2:1 Kan zour Lapantkot ti arive, tou bann krwayan ti reyni ansam dan mem landrwa."
Acts2:2 Enn sel kout enn son terib ti sorti depi lesiel parey kouma enn divan violan ki pe soufle, e sa ti ranpli lakaz kot zot ti reyni."
Acts2:3 Lerla zot ti trouv seki paret kouma bann ti laflam dan form lalang, ki separe ek repoz lor sakenn parmi bann krwayan."
Acts2:4 Zot tou ti ranpli ar Lespri Sin e zot koumans koz dan lezot langaz dapre seki Lespri ti pe donn zot pou exprime.
Acts2:5 Dan Zerizalem ti ena bann Zwif ki ti bien devoue pou Bondie, e ki ti sorti partou lor later."
Acts2:6 Enn gran lafoul ti rasanble letan ti finn tann sa tapaz la. Zot ti res bet parski sakenn ti tann bann krwayan pe koz dan langaz zot pei.
Acts2:7 Dan zot etonnman ek admirasion zot koumans dimande, “Tou sa bann dimoun ki pe koze la, pa bann Galileen?"
Acts2:8 Abe kouma sakenn parmi nou pe tann zot koz dan langaz nou prop pei?
Acts2:9 Nou sorti pei Part, Medi ek Elam. Ena bann abitan Mezopotami, Zide e Kapados, ena sorti Pon ek provins Lazi,"
Acts2:10 Frizi e Panfili, Lezip ek rezion Sirenn dan Libi, ek ena ki vinn depi Rom,"
Acts2:11 Kret ek Arabi; ena ki finn ne Zwif, ena ki finn konverti dan relizion Zwif - me pourtan nou tou tann zot pe rakont mervey Bondie sakenn dan nou bann langaz!”"
Acts2:12 Zot ti telman etone e dan konfizion, ki zot ti pe dir ant zot, “Kisavedir, sa?”"
Acts2:13 Me lezot ti pe boufonn bann krwayan; zot ti pe dir, “Divin ki pe koze.”"
Acts2:14 Pier ti diboute avek lezot onz apot e avek enn lavwa bien-bien for li ti koz ar lafoul, “Mo bann kamarad Zwif e zot tou ki abitan Zerizalem, les mo explik zot, ekout mo parol avek atansion."
Acts2:15 Non, sa bann dimoun la pa finn soule zot, li zis nev-er gramatin la."
Acts2:16 Me seki profet Zoel ti anonse, samem ki pe realize asterla:"
Acts2:17 ‘Ala seki pou arive dan dernie zour, Bondie dir, Mo pou repann mo Lespri lor tou dimoun. Zot garson, zot tifi pou anons mo mesaz; zot bann zenes pou trouv vizion, zot bann vie dimoun pou fer bann rev."
Acts2:18 Wi, lor mo bann serviter, ki li zom ki li fam, mo pou vers mo Lespri sa zour la; e zot pou profetize."
Acts2:19 Mo pou fer bann mervey dan lesiel lao e bann sign mirak anba lor later, pou ena disan, dife, ek niaz lafime,"
Acts2:20 soley pou rant dan fernwar, lalinn vinn disan avan ki zour Lesegner arive dan grander, dan laglwar."
Acts2:21 Lerla, ninport ki dimoun ki kriye sekour Lesegner, li pou sove.’"
Acts2:22 Mo bann kamarad Izraelit, ekout seki mo ena pou dir zot: Zezi ki sorti Nazaret, ti enn dimoun ki ena lotorite Bondie, ki finn prouve devan zot par mirak, mervey ek sign, kouma zotmem zot kone."
Acts2:23 Dapre konesans ki Bondie ena davans, ek dapre so plan, sa zom la finn livre dan zot lame, e zot finn touy li avek led bann move dimoun; zot finn krisifie li."
Acts2:24 Me Bondie finn resisit li, finn tir li dan douler lamor, parski li ti inposib ki lamor tini li dan so pouvwar."
Acts2:25 Ala seki David dir lor li: ‘Mo toultan trouv Lesegner devan mwa; Li pre ar mwa, koumsa mo pa tranble."
Acts2:26 Akoz sa mo ranpli ar boner, mo parol ranpli ar lazwa. Mo lekor pou repoz dan lesperans"
Acts2:27 parski to pa pou abandonn mwa dan landrwa kot bann mor ale to pa pou les to serviter pouri dan tonbo.
Acts2:28 To finn montre mwa sime ki donn lavi, e to prezans ranpli mwa ar lazwa.’."
Acts2:29 Mo bann kamarad Izraelit, mo kapav dir zot avek lasirans ki nou anset David ti mor e ti anter li. So tom ankor la avek nou zordi."
Acts2:30 Parski li ti enn profet, li ti kone ki Bondie ti promet li par enn serman ki enn zour enn so desandan pou asiz lor so tronn."
Acts2:31 David ti trouve anavans seki Bondie pou fer enn zour, alor li ti koz lor rezireksion Lemesi letan li ti dir: ‘Pa ti abandonn li dan landrwa kot bann mor ale, e so lekor pa ti pouri dan tonbo.’"
Acts2:32 Bondie ti resisit Zezi depi lamor e nou bann temwin ki sa ti arive.
Acts2:33 Bondie ti plas li dan so kote drwat, e li finn resevwar promes Lespri Sin par so Papa; e Zezi finn repann saki zot pe trouve ek tande."
Acts2:34 David pa ti mont dan lesiel, me pourtan li ti dir: ‘Lesegner Bondie finn dir mo Segner: asiz la lor mo drwat,"
Acts2:35 ziska ki mo fer to bann lennmi to marspie.’
Acts2:36 Tou lepep Izrael bizin kone avek lasirans: sa Zezi ki zot finn krisifie la, limem ki Bondie finn fer Segner e Mesi!”"
Acts2:37 Letan bann dimoun tann sa zot ti boulverse dan zot leker, zot dir Pier e lezot apot, “Frer, ki nou bizin fer?”"
Acts2:38 Pier reponn, “Repanti, e resevwar batem dan nom Zezi Kris pou zot gagn pardon pou zot pese; e zot pou resevwar don ki Bondie done, Lespri Sin."
Acts2:39 Sa promes la li pou zot e zot zanfan, e pou tou seki lwin - pou tou seki Lesegner nou Bondie pou apele.”"
Acts2:40 Pier kontign ankouraz bannla ar boukou lezot temwagnaz pou konvink zot; li dir zot, “Sov zotmem depi pinision ki pe vinn lor sa bann move dimoun ki dan perdision.”"
Acts2:41 Boukou seki finn krwar sa mesaz la ti pran batem, e sa zour la anviron trwa-mil dimoun ti azoute ar group bann krwayan."
Acts2:42 Zot ti devoue zot letan pou ekout lansegnman bann apot e kominion fraternel, zot ti partaz repa lakominion e lapriyer."
Acts2:43 Boukou mirak ek sign ti pe akonpli par bann apot, e tou dimoun ti inpresione."
Acts2:44 Tou bann krwayan ti ini e ti pe partaz tou zot dibien ansam.
Acts2:45 Zot ti vann zot dibien e seki zot posede, pou zot distribie li dapre seki sakenn ti bizin."
Acts2:46 Zour apre zour zot ti rasanble kouma enn group dan Tanp, zot ti kas dipin ansam dan lakaz, e ti pran zot repa ansam avek enn leker sinser e ranpli ar lazwa."
Acts2:47 Zot ti loue Bondie e ti gagn lestim tou bann dimoun. Toulezour Lesegner ti pe sov dimoun ki li ti pe azout dan zot group.
Acts3:1 Enn zour ver trwa-zer tanto, letan Pier ek Zan ti pe al dan tanp dan ler lapriyer,"
Acts3:2 bann dimoun ti pe amenn enn zom ki ti paralize depi so nesans. Toulezour zot ti vinn depoz li dan lantre tanp ki ti apel ‘Zoli Laport’ pouki li dimann sarite tou bann ki rant dan tanp.
Acts3:3 Kouma li ti trouv Pier ek Zan pe rant dan tanp, li ti dimann zot sarite."
Acts3:4 Pier ek Zan ti fixe li e zot ti dir li, “Get nou.”"
Acts3:5 Zom la ti get zot, li ti atann pou gagn kiksoz ar zot."
Acts3:6 Me Pier ti dir, “Mo pena ni larzan ni lor, me seki mo ena mo donn twa, lor nom Zezi Kris ki sorti Nazaret, mo donn twa lord marse.”"
Acts3:7 Pier trap li par so lame drwat e fer li leve. Toutswit so lipie ek so sevi ti gagn lafors.
Acts3:8 Enn sel kout li ti diboute, li ti koumans marse, e ansam avek zot, li ti rant dan tanp, li ti sot-sote, li ti loue Bondie."
Acts3:9 Tou dimoun ti trouv li marse e rann gras Bondie.
Acts3:10 Zot ti rekonet ki limem sa dimoun ki ti touzour pe asiz kot Zoli Laport tanp pou dimann sarite. E zot tou ti bien emerveye e ti res bet lor saki finn ariv li.
Acts3:11 Ler sa zom la pa ti le kit Pier ek Zan, bann dimoun dan zot etonnman ti swiv zot dan sa galri ki ti apel Galri Salomon."
Acts3:12 Kan Pier ti trouv sa, li ti dir bann dimoun la, “Zot, bann Izraelit, ki fer zot etone ar saki finn arive; kifer zot get nou koumsa, koumadir par nou prop lafors ek nou lafwa ki nou finn fer sa zom la marse."
Acts3:13 Bondie Abraam, Bondie Izaak, ek Bondie Zakob, Bondie nou bann anset finn glorifie so serviter Zezi. Limem zot ti livre ek rezete alor ki Pilat ti anvi liber li."
Acts3:14 Me zot ti rezet Sa-Enn ki Sin ek Drwat e zot ti fer Pilat larg enn kriminel
Acts3:15 Zot finn touy Sa-Enn ki donn lavi, me Bondie finn resisit li. Nou tou nou temwin sa."
Acts3:16 Sa zom ki zot trouve e ki zot kone la finn retrouv so lafors par lafwa dan nom Zezi Kris. Par sa nom lamem e so lafwa dan Zezi ki li finn regagn so lasante, kouma zot tou zot inn trouve."
Acts3:17 Asterla, mo bann frer, mo kone zot ti azir dan lignorans parey kouma zot bann sef."
Acts3:18 Dan sa fason la Bondie finn akonpli seki li ti anonse par bann profet, ki so Mesi pou soufer."
Acts3:19 Alors, sanz zot leker e tourn ver Bondie pouki li efas zot pese,"
Acts3:20 koumsa Lesegner pou donn enn letan rekonfor, e li pou kapav avoy Zezi, Lemesi ki li finn swazire pou zot."
Acts3:21 Asterla li bizin res dan lesiel ziska ki seki Bondie finn anonse bien-bien lontan par so bann sin profet, realize."
Acts3:22 Moiz ti dir, ‘Lesegner zot Bondie pou lev enn profet kouma mwa parmi zot pep. Zot bizin ekout seki li dir zot."
Acts3:23 Seki pa ekout sa profet la pou nepli trouv li parmi lepep Bondie.’
Acts3:24 Tou bann profet ki finn koze depi Samiel, enn apre lot, ti osi predir ki seki pe arive pou arive."
Acts3:25 Zot desandan bann profet ek eritie lalians ki Bondie ti fer avek zot anset, kan li ti dir Abraam, ‘Mo pou beni tou bann fami lor later atraver to bann desandan.’"
Acts3:26 Bondie finn avoy so serviter, pou zot dabor, pou beni zot e fer zot sanz zot bann move manier.”"
Acts4:1 Pier ek Zan ti ankor pe koz ar lepep, kan responsab tanp, bann pret ek Sadisein ti vinn ver zot,"
Acts4:2 bien ankoler parski Pier ek Zan ti pe ansegn lepep lor Zezi ek rezireksion bann mor.
Acts4:3 Zot aret Pier ek Zan e ferm zot dan prizon ziska landime parski ti fini aswar.
Acts4:4 Boukou ki ti tann laparol ti krwar, e ti ena anviron sink mil dimoun."
Acts4:5 Landime matin, bann sef, bann ansien ek profeser lalwa ti zwenn dan Zerizalem."
Acts4:6 Gran Pret Ann ti prezan, ansam ar Kaif, Zan, Alexand e tou bann manm lafami gran pret."
Acts4:7 Ler ti amenn Pier ek Zan devan zot, zot kestionn sa de la, “Par ki pouvwar ek ki nom zot servi pou fer sa gerizon la?”"
Acts4:8 Alor, Pier ranpli ar Lespri Sin dir zot, “Sef lepep ek ansien,"
Acts4:9 si nou bizin rann kont parski nou finn fer dibien enn paralize e bizin reponn kouma li finn geri,"
Acts4:10 fodre zot tou kone, e osi tou lepep Izrael, ki sa dimoun la pe dibout devan zot anbonn sante grasa pouvwar nom Zezi Kris ki sorti Nazaret, ki zot finn krisifie e ki Bondie finn resisite depi bann mor."
Acts4:11 Zezi ‘Limem ros ki zot, bann mason, zot ti rezete me li finn vinn ros prinsipal.’"
Acts4:12 Pena personn kapav sov nou apar Zezi, parski pena okenn lot nom dan lemonn antie ki kapav sov nou.”"
Acts4:13 Kan zot trouv kouraz ki Pier ek Zan ena, zot etone parski zot kone ki sa de la ti bann dimoun sinp e san ledikasion. Zot rekonet ki bannla ti mars ar Zezi."
Acts4:14 Me letan zot trouv sa dimoun ki finn geri la pe dibout akote bannla, zot pa ti kapav dir nanye."
Acts4:15 Alors zot donn lord pou bannla sorti deor, pouki zot kapav diskit ant zot."
Acts4:16 Zot dir, “Ki nou kapav fer ar sa bann zom la? Tou dimoun dan Zerizalem kone ki zot finn fer enn gran mirak. Nou pa kapav dir lekontrer."
Acts4:17 Fode pa ki sa nouvel la kontign fane parmi plis dimoun. Nou bizin anpes zot koz dan nom Zezi.”
Acts4:18 Alors zot reapel Pier ek Zan pou defann zot koze ek ansegne dan nom Zezi.
Acts4:19 Me Pier ek Zan reponn, “Zize zotmem, eski li korek devan Bondie ki nou obeir zot olie obeir Bondie?"
Acts4:20 Me nou, nou nek kapav koz zis lor seki nou finn trouve ek tande.”"
Acts4:21 Bann manm konsey menas Pier ek Zan ankor; lerla ti les zot ale. Pa ti ena okenn mwayin pou pini zot, parski lepep ti pe loue Bondie pou seki finn arive."
Acts4:22 Sa dimoun ki ti geri par mirak la ti ena plis ki karant-an.
Acts4:23 Kouma larg zot, zot ti al kot bann kamarad e ti rakont tou seki sef pret e bann ansien ti dir zot."
Acts4:24 Letan bann krwayan ti tann sa, avek enn sel leker zot tou ti priye Bondie, “Segner, Kreater lesiel, later, ek lamer e tou seki viv lor later ek dan lamer,"
Acts4:25 tomem ki, par Lespri Sin, finn met dan labous David, nou anset, to serviter, ‘Kifer bann nasion azite? Kifer bann pep ena panse bet?"
Acts4:26 Bann lerwa lor later finn prepar zot, bann sef finn vinn ansam kont Lesegner e kont so Mesi.’"
Acts4:27 Li bien vre ki Erod e Pons Pilat finn marye pike, ansam ar bann nasion ek Izrael, kont Zezi, to serviter sin, ki to finn konsakre."
Acts4:28 Koumsa, zot finn realiz seki to lame ek to plan ti deside depi komansman."
Acts4:29 Asterla, Segner, get enn kout zot menas, e donn to bann serviter boukou kouraz pou anons to parol."
Acts4:30 Fer dimoun trouv to pwisans par bann gerizon, bann mirak, ek bann sign, ki pou akonpli dan nom Zezi to serviter.”"
Acts4:31 Letan zot fini priye, landrwa kot zot ti reyni ansam ti tranble. Zot ti ranpli ar Lespri Sin ek zot ti anons laparol Bondie avek lasirans."
Acts4:32 Sa group krwayan la ti ena enn sel leker, enn sel lespri; personn pa ti dir ki so dibien pou li tousel sa, me zot ti met tou ansam ankominote."
Acts4:33 Bann apot ti rann temwagnaz lor rezireksion Zezi par enn gran pwisans, ek zot ti ranpli ar lagras Bondie."
Acts4:34 Personn parmi zot pa ti res dan lamizer. Tou seki ti propriyeter enn bout terin ou enn lakaz ti vann li, ti amenn larzan la"
Acts4:35 e ti remet li bann apot, ki ti distribie resours la selon bezwin sakenn."
Acts4:36 Zozef ti enn Levit ki ti ne an Sip, bann apot ti donn li enn nom gate Barnabas, ki vedir ‘Garson ki ankouraz lezot.’"
Acts4:37 Zozef ti vann so karo e li ti remet tou larzan la bann apot.
Acts5:1 Me enn zom ki ti apel Ananias avek so fam Safira ti vann zot terin.
Acts5:2 Li ti tom dakor avek so fam pou gard enn parti larzan la pou zot, e li ti remet leres bann apot."
Acts5:3 Pier dimann li, “Ananias, kifer to les Satan ranpli to leker? To finn koz manti ar Lespri Sin e to finn gard enn parti larzan pou twa."
Acts5:4 Kan pa ti ankor vann terin la, eski li pa ti pou twa? E letan to ti vann li, eski tou larzan pa ti dan to lame? Kouma to finn kapav fer enn plan koumsa dan to leker? Pa ar nou ki to finn koz manti, me ar Bondie.”"
Acts5:5 Letan Ananias tann sa bann parol la, li tonbe, li mor sek. Enn gran lafreyer ti vinn lor tou seki ti tann sa."
Acts5:6 Bann zenes vini, zot anvlop so lekor, zot al anter li."
Acts5:7 Apre trwa zer-tan, so fam rantre; li pa ti kone ki ti finn arive."
Acts5:8 Pier dimann li, “Dir mwa, twa ek to mari finn vann sa later la pou sa kantite kas la?” Li reponn, “Wi, pou sa pri la mem.”"
Acts5:9 Lerla Pier dir li, “Kouma zot finn tom dakor pou tronp Lespri Bondie? Bann ki finn anter to mari pe dibout deryer laport, zot pare pou sarye twa ale.”"
Acts5:10 Toutswit li tom devan Pier e li mor. Ler bann zenes rantre, zot trouv li finn mor. Zot pran li, zot al anter li koste ar so mari."
Acts5:11 Legliz antie e tou bann ki ti tann seki finn arive ti gagn enn gran lafreyer.
Acts5:12 Bann apot ti fer enn kantite mirak ek mervey parmi lepep. Zot tou ti ansam anba galri Salomon kot ti ena bann kolonn.
Acts5:13 Leres dimoun pa ti oze zwenn ar zot, me lepep ti ena gran respe pou zot."
Acts5:14 Plis letan pase, enn lafoul dimoun, zom ek fam, ti pe krwar e ti pe swiv Lesegner."
Acts5:15 Zot ti pe mem sarye bann malad lor brankar, lor nat, e ti plas zot lor sime pouki letan Pier pase so lonbraz kapav kouver detrwa parmi zot."
Acts5:16 Mem dan bann lavil otour Zerizalem ti ena lafoul ki ti pe vini e ti pe sarye bann malad ek bann ki ti posede par move lespri, e zot tou ti pe geri."
Acts5:17 Lerla gran pret ek tou seki ti avek li, setadir bann manm parti Sadisein, ti ranpli ar zalouzi."
Acts5:18 Zot ti aret bann apot e ti zet zot dan prizon.
Acts5:19 Me dan lanwit enn anz Lesegner ti ouver laport prizon, fer zot sorti e dir zot,"
Acts5:20 “Al dan tanp e anons lepep tou sa bann parol ki donn nouvo lavi la.”
Acts5:21 Ler bann apot tann sa, zot al dan tanp kouma soley leve ek zot koumans ansegne. Gran pret ansam avek tou so konpagnon ti rasanble tou bann manm konsey. Zot donn lord pou al sers bann apot dan prizon, e amenn devan zot."
Acts5:22 Letan solda tanp ti al laba, zot pa ti trouv bann apot dan kaso. Alors zot ti retourne pou fer zot rapor:"
Acts5:23 “Nou finn trouv prizon bien ferme, bann gard dan zot plas devan laport. Me letan nou ouver laport, nou pa finn trouv personn andan.”"
Acts5:24 Kan sef tanp ek bann sef pret tann sa, zot res bet, zot kas zot latet pou sey konpran ki ti pe arive."
Acts5:25 Lerlamem enn zom rantre e li dir zot, “Sa bann dimoun ki zot ti zet dan prizon la, zot dan tanp zot pe ansegn lepep.”"
Acts5:26 Lerla sef la ek so bann solda ti al sers bann apot san okenn violans, parski zot ti per ki lepep lapid zot."
Acts5:27 Kan zot ti amenn bannla, ti pas zot devan konsey. Lerla gran pret ti kestionn zot."
Acts5:28 “Nou ti anpes zot ansegn dan sa nom la; me ala ki zot finn ranpli Zerizalem avek zot lansegnman; e lorla zot pe rann nou responsab so lamor!”
Acts5:29 Pier avek lezot apot reponn, “Nou bizin obeir Bondie plito ki obeir dimoun."
Acts5:30 Bondie nou bann anset finn resisit Zezi, limem ki zot finn touye kan zot finn koulout li lor lakrwa."
Acts5:31 Bondie, par so pwisans, finn lev li lao kouma Sef ek Sover pouki li donn Izrael lokazion repanti, e ki li pardonn zot pese."
Acts5:32 Nou temwin tou seki finn arive, nou ansam avek Lespri Sin ki Bondie finn donn bann dimoun ki obeir li.”"
Acts5:33 Kan bannla ti tann sa zot ti bien ankoler e zot ti anvi touy bann apot.
Acts5:34 Ti ena enn Farizien parmi manm konsey, ki ti apel Gamaliel. Li ti enn dokter lalwa ki lepep ti bien respekte. Li ti diboute e li ti donn lord amenn bann apot deor enn ti mama."
Acts5:35 Lerla li ti dir zot, “Mo bann frer Izraelit, get bien ki zot pe rod fer ar bann zom la."
Acts5:36 Parski pa tro lontan enn kikenn ki ti apel Teodas ti deklar li enn terib; kat san zom ti mars ar li. Me li ti trouv lamor, e tou seki ti pe swiv li ti disperse, e mouvman la ti tegn."
Acts5:37 Apre li, ti ena enn lot ki ti apel Zida. Li ti Galile, lepok resansman; li osi ti rasanble enn lafoul ki ti swiv li, me li ti trouv lamor, e tou bann ki ti swiv li ti disperse."
Acts5:38 Asterla, les mo dir zot, pa fer bannla nanye, les zot ale. Si zot lintansion ek zot plan finn ne dan lespri zom, li pa pou marse;"
Acts5:39 me si li sorti kot Bondie, zot pa pou kapav ranvers plan bannla; lerla zot riske trouv zotmem pe lager kont Bondie!” Bannla ti aksepte so konsey."
Acts5:40 Zot apel bann apot, fwet zot, e donn zot lord aret koz dan nom Zezi; lerla ti les zot ale."
Acts5:41 Bann apot ti kit lasal konsey leker kontan parski ti konsider zot dign pou gagn maltrete akoz nom Zezi.
Acts5:42 Toulezour dan tanp e dan bann lakaz, zot ti kontign ansegne e proklam Bonn Nouvel Zezi Kris."
Acts6:1 Sa lepok la, letan nonb bann disip ti pe ogmante, bann krwayan ki ti koz Grek ti pe grogne kont bann ki ti koz Ebre parski zot bann vev ti santi zot neglize letan ti ena distribision manze."
Acts6:2 Ledouz ti rasanble tou bann disip e ti dir zot, “Li pa korek ki nou negliz laparol Bondie pou nou servi repa."
Acts6:3 Alors, bann frer, swazir set zom parmi zot ki ena bon repitasion, ki ranpli avek Lespri Sin ek sazes pou fer sa travay la."
Acts6:4 Koumsa nou kapav kontign lapriyer ek predikasion.”
Acts6:5 Sa parol la ti fer kominote la plezir. Zot ti swazir Etienn ki ti ranpli avek lafwa ek Lespri Sin, ansam avek Filip, Prokor, Nikanor, Timon, Parmenas, ek Nikola ki ti sorti Antios, ki lontan ti konverti pou vinn enn Zwif."
Acts6:6 Group disip prezant sa set la bann apot, ki ti priye e ti inpoz lame lor zot."
Acts6:7 Parol Bondie ti pe kontign repann; nonb disip ti ogmante dan Zerizalem, e mem enn lafoul pret ti aksepte lafwa."
Acts6:8 Etienn ki ti ranpli ar lagras ek pwisans, ti fer bann gran mervey ek mirak parmi lepep."
Acts6:9 Enn parti bann manm sinagog Esklav Libere, ki ti bann Zwif ki ti sorti Sirenn, Aleksandri, ek osi bann ki ti sorti Silisi e Lazi, ti diskit ar Etienn."
Acts6:10 Me zot ti perdi pwin parski Lespri ti donn Etienn enn gran sazes.
Acts6:11 Lerla zot ti mont latet detrwa dimoun ankasiet pouki bannla dir, “Nou finn tann li blasfeme kont Moiz ek Bondie.”"
Acts6:12 Zot ti eksit lepep, bann ansien ek bann dokter lalwa; lerla bannla ti vinn aret Etienn, e ti trenn li devan konsey."
Acts6:13 Zot amenn fos temwin ki ti dir, “Sa zom la pe toultan koz kont tanp ek lalwa Moiz."
Acts6:14 Nou finn tann li dir ki sa Zezi ki sorti Nazaret la, pou detrir sa plas la e pou sanz koutim ki Moiz finn donn nou.”"
Acts6:15 Tou seki ti pe asiz dan konsey e ti pe fixe Etienn, ti trouv so figir parey kouma figir enn anz."
Acts7:1 Gran pret dimann li, “Vremem sa?”"
Acts7:2 Etienn reponn, “Bann frer, bann gran dimoun, ekout mwa. Bondie dan so laglwar ti revel li ar nou anset Abraam letan li ti dan Mezopotami, avan ki li ti al res Aran."
Acts7:3 Li ti dir Abraam, ‘Kit to pei ek to fami, al dan pei ki mo pou montre twa.’"
Acts7:4 Lerla li kit so pei Kalde, li al res Aran. Apre lamor so papa, Bondie tir Abraam depi Aran e amenn li dan pei kot zot pe viv asterla."
Acts7:5 Bondie pa ti donn li okenn eritaz, pa mem enn pie kare later; me ti promet ki li ti pou erit pei la antie ek so bann desandan apre li, mem si li pa ti ankor ena zanfan."
Acts7:6 Bondie ti dir ki bann desandan Abraam pou viv dan enn pei etranze, kouma esklav, e zot pou gagn maltrete pandan kat san banane."
Acts7:7 Bondie ti dir, “Me mwa mo pou ziz sa nasion ki pou tret zot kouma esklav. Apre sa zot pou sorti laba, pou vinn ador mwa isi mem.”"
Acts7:8 Bondie ti fer lalians avek Abraam. Sirkonsizion sinbol sa lalians la. Abraam fer sirkonsizion ar so garson Izaak, wit zour apre so nesans; Izaak ti fer parey avek so garson Zakob, e Zakob osi ar so douz garson, bann patriars."
Acts7:9 Bann patriars ki ti zalou Zozef ti vann li kouma enn esklav dan pei Lezip,"
Acts7:10 me Bondie ki ti ar li, ti delivre li dan so lapenn, e ti donn li lasazes ek faver Faraon, lerwa Lezip, ki ti fer li vinn gouverner Lezip ek tou so rwayom."
Acts7:11 Apre ti ena lafaminn dan antie Lezip e Kanaan; lafaminn la ti telman for ki nou bann anset ti soufer boukou.
Acts7:12 Me kan Zakob ti tann dir ki ena manze dan Lezip, li ti avoy nou bann anset enn premie fwa laba."
Acts7:13 Lor zot deziem vizit Zozef ti fer so bann frer rekonet li, e Faraon ti fer konesans fami Zozef."
Acts7:14 Alors Zozef ti fer so papa ek tou so bann fami vinn Lezip. Ti ena swasann-kinz antou.
Acts7:15 Zakob ti desann Lezip. Li ti mor laba, ek nou bann anset osi."
Acts7:16 Ti retourn zot lekor Sikem e ti met zot dan tonbo ki Abraam ti aste pou enn som larzan ar bann garson Emor dan Sikem.
Acts7:17 Kouma letan ti pe aprose pouki Bondie akonplir so promes ki li ti fer Abraam, nou lepep dan Lezip ti grandi e miltipliye."
Acts7:18 Lerla ti ena enn lot lerwa ki pa ti konn Zozef ki ti regne lor Lezip.
Acts7:19 Li ti maltret nou ras e fors nou bann anset anpes zot tibaba viv.
Acts7:20 Sa lepok la Moiz ti ne e Bondie ti trouv li enn zoli baba. Pandan so trwa premie mwa li ti grandi dan lakaz so papa.
Acts7:21 Kan zot ti abandonn li, tifi Faraon ti ramas li e ti grandi li kouma so prop garson."
Acts7:22 Alor Moiz ti gagn sazes bann Ezipsien e li ti vinn pwisan dan so parol ek so bann aksion.
Acts7:23 Letan li gagn karant-an, enn dezir vinn dan li pou vizit so bann frer Izraelit."
Acts7:24 Letan li trouv enn Ezipsien maltret enn dan so bann, li ti defann li e li ti touy Ezipsien la."
Acts7:25 Li ti panse ki so bann frer ti pou konpran ki Bondie pe delivre zot par so lame, me zot pa finn konpran sa."
Acts7:26 Landime li finn trouv detrwa Izraelit ki ti pe lager ant zot. Moiz ti sey rekonsilie zot. Li ti dir zot, ‘Bann frer, kifer zot lager?’"
Acts7:27 Me sa zom ki ti pe maltret so prosin la ti pous Moiz e ti dir li, ‘Kisannla finn fer twa sef pou ziz nou?"
Acts7:28 Eski to anvi touy mwa kouma yer to finn touy sa Ezipsien la?’
Acts7:29 Kouma Moiz tann sa, li sove; li al viv dan Madian kouma enn etranze. Laba li ti vinn papa de garson."
Acts7:30 Apre ki karant-an ti pase, enn anz ti paret devan Moiz dan laflam enn bwison ki ti pe brile dan dezer."
Acts7:31 Moiz ti etone par seki li ti trouve; alor li ti koste pli pre pou trouv pli bien. Li tann lavwa Lesegner ki dir,"
Acts7:32 ‘Momem Bondie to bann anset, Bondie Abraam, Izaak ek Zakob.’ Moiz koumans tranble e li pa oze gete."
Acts7:33 Lesegner dir li, ‘Tir to sandalet; la kot to pe deboute, enn landrwa konsakre."
Acts7:34 Mo finn trouv kouma pe maltret mo pep dan Lezip, mo finn tann zot plegne, mo finn desann pou liber zot. Ekout mwa, mo pe avoy twa Lezip.’"
Acts7:35 Ar Moiz mem ki bann Izraelit ti poz enn kestion, letan zot ti rezet li, zot ti dir, ‘Kisannla finn fer twa sef ek ziz lor nou?’ Samem Moiz ki Bondie finn avoye kouma sef ek liberater so lepep avek led anz ki ti paret dan bwison ardan."
Acts7:36 Li finn sorti lepep Bondie depi Lezip par bann mervey ek bann mirak ki li ti fer laba, ek osi dan lamer rouz ek dan dezer pandan karant-an."
Acts7:37 Moiz mem ankor ki dir bann Izraelit, ‘Bondie pou avoy zot enn profet kouma mwa ki pou enn manm zot pep.’"
Acts7:38 Letan lepep ti rasanble dan dezer, Moiz ti dibout ant lepep ek anz ki ti pe koz ar li lor Mon Sinai. Li ti resevwar mesaz vivan ki sorti kot Bondie, pou partaz sa ar nou."
Acts7:39 Me nou bann gran dimoun ti refiz obeir li, e zot ti rezet li. Dan zot leker zot ti pe repans Lezip. Zot dir Aaron,"
Acts7:40 ‘Fer bann idol bondie ki pou al devan nou. Nou pa kone ki finn ariv sa Moiz ki finn tir nou dan Lezip la.’
Acts7:41 Lerla zot fabrik enn idol dan form enn vo, e zot ofer li sakrifis. Zot ti fier saki zot finn fabrike ar zot lame."
Acts7:42 Me Bondie vir ledo ar zot ek li abandonn zot pouki zot ador bann pwisans dan lesiel, kouma finn ekrir dan liv bann profet: ‘Eski zot finn ofer mwa bann zanimo ek bann sakrifis, karant lane dan dezer, lepep Izrael?"
Acts7:43 Non, zot finn sarye latant Molok, ek zimaz Refan, zot bondie zetwal, sa bann idol ki zot finn fer pou zot adore. Akoz sa mo pou deport zot pli lwin ki Babilonn.’"
Acts7:44 Nou bann gran dimoun ti ena latant temwagnaz dan dezer, ki Moiz ti fer parey kouma linstriksion ki li ti gagne, parey kouma model li ti trouve."
Acts7:45 Lerla nou bann gran dimoun ti erit li; zot finn sarye li ar zot letan zot ti al ansam ar Zozwe pou pran later bann nasion ki Bondie ti deplase devan zot. Bann zafer ti roul koumsa ziska lepok David
Acts7:46 ki ti gagn faver Bondie ek ti dimann permision pou fer enn lakaz pou Bondie Zakob.
Acts7:47 Me Salomon ki ti mont enn lakaz pou Bondie.
Acts7:48 Pourtan Gran Bondie napa res dan lakaz ki fer ar lame; kouma profet dir,"
Acts7:49 ‘Lesiel mo tronn, later mo marspie. Bondie dir: Ki lakaz to pou fer pou mwa? Oubien dan ki landrwa mo pou repoze?"
Acts7:50 Pa mo lame ki finn fer tousala?’
Acts7:51 Zot, bann dimoun ki ena latet dir, zot leker ek zot zorey pa ekout Bondie, zot touzour reziste Lespri Sin. Zot fer parey kouma zot bann anset."
Acts7:52 Dan tou bann profet, lekel zot gran dimoun napa finn persekite? Zot finn mem touy bann ki ti pe anonse anavans ki Lemesi pou vini. Asterla zot ki la, ki finn trayir Lemesi ek zot finn asasinn li."
Acts7:53 Zot finn resevwar lalwa par bann anz me zot pa finn obeir li.”
Acts7:54 Letan zot tann sa bann koze la zot araze ek zot grins zot ledan kont Etienn.
Acts7:55 Me Etienn, ranpli ar Lespri Sin, get ver lesiel ek li trouv laglwar Bondie, ek Zezi pe dibout lor so kote drwat."
Acts7:56 Etienn dir, “Gete, mo trouv lesiel ouver ek Garson Bondie pe dibout lor so kote drwat.”"
Acts7:57 Me zot bous zot zorey, zot kriye for, ek zot fons lor li."
Acts7:58 Lerla zot sarye li andeor lavil ek zot pil ros lor li; ek bann temwin donn enn zennom ki apel Sol pou vey zot linz.
Acts7:59 Letan zot pe pil ros lor Etienn, li priye, “Segner Zezi, pran mo lespri.”"
Acts7:60 Li tom azenou ek li kriye for, “Segner, napa pini zot pou sa pese la.” Letan li finn fini dir sa, li mor."
Acts8:1 Sol ti dakor ar zot krim lor Etienn.
Acts8:2 Sa zour lamem enn gran persekision ti koumanse kont legliz Zerizalem. Tou dimoun, apart bann apot, finn fane dan rezion Zide ek Samari. Bann zom relizie ti anter Etienn e zot ti plor boukou lor so lamor."
Acts8:3 Me Sol ti pe persekit legliz; li ti rant dan lakaz apre lakaz, li tir bann krwayan - ki li zom ki li fam - e li ti al zet zot dan prizon."
Acts8:4 Bann ki ti finn fane partou kote, finn al proklam Bonn Nouvel."
Acts8:5 Filip desann dan enn lavil Samari e li proklam Lemesi.
Acts8:6 Tou bann abitan sa lavil la ti ekout mesaz Filip avek boukou latansion parski zot ti temwin bann mirak ki li ti pe fer.
Acts8:7 Bann move lespri ti pe kriye kan zot ti pe sorti depi bann posede, bann paralize ek bann andikape ti geri."
Acts8:8 Ti ena enn gran lazwa dan lavil.
Acts8:9 Me ti ena enn zom ki ti apel Simon ki avan ti pe fer mazik; li ti etonn boukou dimoun dan sa lavil la; li ti deklar li enn gran dimoun.
Acts8:10 Bann abitan, tipti kouma gran, ti ekout li, zot ti pe dir, “Sa zom la, li pe montre pwisans Bondie ki apel ‘Gran pouvwar.’ ”"
Acts8:11 Zot ti ekout li avek boukou lintere parski depi lontan li finn fer zot res bet avek so mazik.
Acts8:12 Me kan zot finn krwar dan Bonn Nouvel rwayom Bondie ek Zezi Kris ki Filip ti pe proklame, zom kouma fam, ti batize."
Acts8:13 Mem Simon ti krwar. Apre so batem li ti res avek Filip e li ti etone kan li ti trouv bann sign ek mirak ki ti pe arive.
Acts8:14 Kan bann apot dan Zerizalem tann dir ki Samari finn aksepte parol Bondie, zot avoy Pier ek Zan laba."
Acts8:15 Toulede desann e priye pou bannla resevwar Lespri Sin.
Acts8:16 Lespri Sin pa ti ankor desann lor personn parmi zot; zot ti finn zis batize dan nom Segner Zezi.
Acts8:17 Lerla Pier ek Zan poz lame lor zot e zot resevwar Lespri Sin.
Acts8:18 Letan Simon trouve ki Lespri Sin inn desann lor bann krwayan kan bann apot inn poz lame lor zot, li ofer Pier ek Zan enn som larzan."
Acts8:19 Li dir, “Donn mwa osi sa pouvwar la, pouki ler mo poz lame lor enn dimoun, li kapav resevwar Lespri Sin.”"
Acts8:20 Me Pier reponn, “Twa ek to kas pou fini ansam! To panse to kapav aste sa don la ar Bondie?"
Acts8:21 To pena nanye pou gagne parski to leker pa drwat devan Bondie.
Acts8:22 Sanz to move lintansion e priy Lesegner; kikfwa li va pardonn move lintansion to leker.
Acts8:23 Parski mo trouve ki to leker amer e to prizonie to pese.”
Acts8:24 Simon reponn, “Priy Bondie pou mwa tomem pouki tou seki to pe dir la pa ariv mwa.”"
Acts8:25 Apre ki Pier ek Zan finn rann temwagnaz e proklam parol Bondie, zot retourn Zerizalem. Lor zot sime, zot ti anons Bonn Nouvel dan enn kantite vilaz Samari."
Acts8:26 Apre sa, enn anz Lesegner dir Filip, “Leve, al dan direksion lesid, lor sime ki desann depi Zerizalem ziska Gaza. Enn sime ki pa frekante sa.”"
Acts8:27 Li leve, li ale. Lor so sime ti ena enn gran ofisie Etiopien ki ti ansarz trezor larenn Kandas; li ti vinn Zerizalem pou ador Bondie."
Acts8:28 Li ti pe retourn dan so pei dan enn kales, e li ti pe lir enn pasaz liv profet Izai."
Acts8:29 Lespri Lesegner dir Filip, “Koste ar sa kales la.”"
Acts8:30 Filip galoup kot kales la e li tann ofisie la pe lir enn pasaz liv profet Izai. Filip dimann li, “Eski to konpran saki to pe lir?”"
Acts8:31 Li reponn, “Kouma mo pou konpran, si personn pa explik mwa?” Lerla li invit Filip pou mont dan kales e asiz kot li."
Acts8:32 Ala pasaz Lekritir ki li ti pe lir: “Parey kouma enn mouton ki zot pe amenn labatwar kouma enn annyo bien trankil devan bann ki pe koup so lalenn, li pa ouver so labous."
Acts8:33 Zot finn abes li e pa finn ena lazistis; kisannla kapav dekrir so desandan? Parski zot finn pran so lavi lor later.”
Acts8:34 Ofisie Etiopien la dimann Filip, “Dir mwa, lor kisannla profet la pe dir sa, lor limem oubien lor enn lot?”"
Acts8:35 Alors Filip koumans explike. Li koumans par sa pasaz Lekritir la pou anons li Bonn Nouvel lor Zezi.
Acts8:36 Letan zot pe kontign zot sime, zot ariv kot ena dilo; lerla ofisie la dir Filip, “Ala dilo, ki anpes mwa resevwar batem?” ["
Acts8:37 Filip dir, “Si to krwar avek tou to leker, li posib.” Li reponn, “Mo krwar ki Zezi Kris limem Garson Bondie.” ]"
Acts8:38 Li donn lord pou aret kales, e toulede, Filip ek ofisie la, desann dan dilo, lerla Filip batiz li."
Acts8:39 Letan zot sorti dan dilo, Lespri Lesegner anlev Filip; ofisie la nepli trouv Filip ankor, e li ale ranpli ar lazwa."
Acts8:40 Filip retrouv limem dan enn landrwa ki ti apel Azot, e li ti anons Bonn Nouvel dan tou bann lavil ki li finn traverse ziska li ariv Sezare."
Acts9:1 Sa lepok la, Sol ti ankor ranpli avek menas lamor kont bann disip Lesegner. Li ti al kot gran pret"
Acts9:2 pou dimann li papie arestasion pou bann sinagog dan Damas. Koumsa si li trouv ninport ki zom ou fam ki pe swiv Sime Bondie li pou aret zot ek amenn zot Zerizalem.
Acts9:3 Li ti dan sime pre ar Damas ler enn sel kout enn lalimier sorti dan lesiel, briye otour li."
Acts9:4 Li tonbe, e li tann enn lavwa ki dir li, “Sol, Sol, kifer to persekit mwa?”"
Acts9:5 Li reponn, “Kisannla to ete, Segner?” “Mwa, momem Zezi ki to pe persekite."
Acts9:6 Lev twa, rant dan lavil e zot pou dir twa seki to bizin fer.”"
Acts9:7 Bann ki ti pe vwayaz ar Sol ti res san parol parski zot ti tann enn lavwa me zot pa ti trouv personn.
Acts9:8 Sol leve, me letan li ouver so lizie, li pa trouv nanye. Zot trap so lame e zot amenn li Damas."
Acts9:9 Li res trwa zour pa trouv kler. Pandan sa letan la li pa ni manze ni bwar.
Acts9:10 Ti ena enn disip dan Damas ki ti apel Ananias. Lesegner dir li dan enn vizion, “Ananias!” Li reponn, “Ala mo la, Segner.”"
Acts9:11 Lesegner dir li, “Leve, al dan lari Drwat, dan lakaz Zida, rod enn zom ki sorti Tars ki apel Sol. Li pe fer lapriyer,"
Acts9:12 e dan enn vizion li finn trouv enn dimoun apel Ananias rantre e poz lame lor so latet pou li retrouv kler.”
Acts9:13 Ananias reponn, “Segner, mo finn tann enn kantite koze lor sa zom la, ki kantite ditor li finn fer to bann fidel dan Zerizalem."
Acts9:14 E isi mem, li finn gagn lotorite avek bann gran pret pou aret tou bann ki priye twa.”"
Acts9:15 Lesegner dir li, “Ale, parski limem sa instriman ki mo finn swazir pou amenn Bonn Nouvel kot bann payin e zot lerwa, e osi kot lepep Izrael."
Acts9:16 Momem mo pou montre li ki kantite li bizin soufer pou mwa.”
Acts9:17 Ananias ale, li rant dan lakaz kot Sol ti ete, li poz lame lor li e li dir li, “Frer Sol, Lesegner Zezi ki ti aparet devan twa lor sime ler to ti pe vinn isi, finn avoy mwa pouki to retrouv kler e ki to ranpli ar Lespri Sin.”"
Acts9:18 Zis lerla, enn kiksoz kouma lekay tonbe depi so lizie. Li leve e li resevwar batem."
Acts9:19 Lerla li manze e li repran lafors. Li pas detrwa zour ar bann disip dan Damas.
Acts9:20 Toutswit apre li koumans proklam Zezi dan sinagog, li dir, “Limem Garson Bondie.”"
Acts9:21 Tou dimoun ki ti tann li ti res bet. Zot ti pe dir, “Pa limem ki dan Zerizalem ti pe persekit tou dimoun ki priye Zezi? Pa limem ki finn vinn isi pou aret zot e amenn zot prizonie devan sef pret?”"
Acts9:22 Me predikasion Sol vinn pli for ankor e li fer bann Zwif dan Damas perdi pwin letan li prouve ki Zezi limem Lemesi.
Acts9:23 Apre inpe letan bann Zwif fer konplo pou touy li,"
Acts9:24 me Sol ti dekouver zot plan. Lanwit-lizour zot ti pe vey lantre lavil pou zot touy li.
Acts9:25 Me so bann disip finn pran li lanwit e finn desann li par enn trou miray dan enn panie.
Acts9:26 Letan li ti ariv Zerizalem li finn sey zwenn li ar group bann disip me zot tou ti per li. Zot pa ti le krwar ki li vremem enn disip.
Acts9:27 Me Barnabas ti pran li e ti amenn li kot bann apot. Li rakont zot kouma lor sime vwayaz Sol ti trouv Lesegner, ki finn koz ar li. Li osi rakont bannla kouma Sol ti servi nom Lesegner pou koz avek lasirans dan Damas."
Acts9:28 Alor Sol ti res ar zot e li ti ale-vini dan Zerizalem. Li ti koz avek boukou konviksion dan nom Lesegner.
Acts9:29 Li ti osi koze ek diskite ar bann Zwif ki koz Grek, me zot ti rod touy li."
Acts9:30 Kan bann frer finn dekouver sa, zot finn amenn li Sezare e depi laba zot finn avoy li Tars."
Acts9:31 Legliz dan Zide, Galile ek Samari ti viv enn letan lape. Legliz ti vinn for e ti ena gran respe pou Lesegner e par led Lespri Sin legliz ti pe ogmante."
Acts9:32 Dan bann vizit ki Pier ti pe fer inpe partou, li ti al get bann krwayan dan Lida."
Acts9:33 Laba li ti trouv enn dimoun ki ti apel Ene ki ti paralize depi wit-an.
Acts9:34 Pier dir li, “Ene, Zezi Kris geri twa. Leve, aranz to lili.” Toutswit Ene leve."
Acts9:35 Tou bann abitan Lida e Saron ki ti trouv sa finn met zot lafwa dan Lesegner.
Acts9:36 Dan lavil Zope ti ena parmi bann disip enn fam ki ti apel Tabita, dan langaz Grek so nom vedir Dorkas, ki vedir gazel. Li ti touzour fer dibien pou ed bann pov."
Acts9:37 Sa lepok la li finn tom malad e li finn mor. Kan zot finn fini begn li, zot met so lekor dan enn lasam aletaz."
Acts9:38 Lida ti pre ar Zope. Letan bann disip ti kone ki Pier laba, zot avoy de zom pou sipliy li ar enn mesaz, “Vinn kot nou toutswit.”"
Acts9:39 Lerla Pier al ar zot. Kan li ariv laba zot amenn li dan lasam lao. Tou bann vev antour li, zot ti pe plore. Zot montre li bann semiz e lezot linz ki Dorkas ti koud letan li ti ankor vivan."
Acts9:40 Pier fer tou dimoun sorti, li azenou e li fer lapriyer. Lerla, li tourn ar lekor la e li dir, “Tabita, leve.” Tabita ouver so lizie, e letan li trouv Pier, li asize."
Acts9:41 Pier atrap so lame ek ed li diboute. Pier apel bann krwayan e bann vev e li prezant zot Dorkas ki ti vivan.
Acts9:42 Sa nouvel la finn fane dan Zope, boukou dimoun finn krwar dan Lesegner."
Acts9:43 Pier ti res ase lontan dan Zope kot kikenn ki apel Simon, enn zouvrie ki travay lapo."
Acts10:1 Dan Sezare ti ena enn zom ki ti apel Korney. Li ti kapitenn enn divizion larme ki ti apel ‘Batayon Italien.’
Acts10:2 Li ti bien relizie; li ansam ar tou so fami ti ador Bondie. Li ti bien ed bann pov e toultan li ti priye Bondie.
Acts10:3 Enn zour ver trwa-zer tanto, li fer enn vizion. Li trouv enn anz Bondie ki rant kot li e ki dir li, “Korney!”"
Acts10:4 Li get anz la avek freyer e li dir, “Ki ena, Segner?” Anz la dir li, “Bondie finn pran kont to lapriyer ek led ki to donn bann pov."
Acts10:5 Asterla, avoy dimoun Zope pou amenn Simon, ki zot apel Pier."
Acts10:6 Li pe res kot Simon, enn zouvrie ki travay lapo e ki res dan borlamer.”"
Acts10:7 Kan anz la finn ale, Korney apel de serviter ek enn solda ki ti bien relizie e ki ti servi li."
Acts10:8 Li rakont zot tou saki finn arive, e li avoy zot Zope."
Acts10:9 Landime ver midi letan zot ti pe vwayaze e ti pe apros Zope, Pier al lao lor twa lakaz pou priye."
Acts10:10 Li koumans gagn fin e li ti pe anvi manze. Pandan ki ti pe prepar enn repa pou li, li gagn enn vizion."
Acts10:11 Li trouv lesiel ouver ek enn kiksoz ki resanble enn nap ki pe desann par so kat kwin.
Acts10:12 Ladan ti ena tousort kalite zanimo, reptil ek zwazo."
Acts10:13 Enn lavwa dir li, “Pier, leve; touye, manze.”"
Acts10:14 Me Pier reponn, “Non, zame, Segner. Mo pa finn zame manz kiksoz ki interdi e pa finn pirifie.”"
Acts10:15 Lavwa enn deziem fwa dir li, “Pa konsider kiksoz inpir si Bondie finn deklar li prop pou manze.”"
Acts10:16 Sa ti arive trwa fwa, lerla lobze la retourn dan lesiel lao."
Acts10:17 Letan Pier pe reflesi lor kisavedir sa vizion la, bann dimoun ki sorti kot Korney ti reysi trouve kikote lakaz Pier ete. Zot finn aret devan laport lantouraz."
Acts10:18 Zot kriye pou dimande si Pier ti res dan sa lakaz la.
Acts10:19 Pier ti ankor pe sey konpran vizion la letan Lespri dir li, “Gete, ena trwa zom ki pe rod twa."
Acts10:20 Leve e desann. Pa ezite pou swiv zot parski mwa ki finn avoy zot.”
Acts10:21 Pier desann e li dir bannla, “Momem ki zot pe rode. Kifer zot finn vinn isi?”"
Acts10:22 Zot reponn li, “Kapitenn Korney ki finn avoy nou isi. Li enn dimoun drwat ki ena bel respe pou Bondie, e bann Zwif bien estim li. Enn anz Bondie ki finn dir li invit twa dan so lakaz pou li ekout seki to ena pou dir.”"
Acts10:23 Pier invit zot rantre pou pas lanwit kot li. Landime li prepar limem pou al ar zot. Detrwa bann frer dan Zope ti akonpagn li.
Acts10:24 Se nek zour apre ki zot ariv Sezare. Korney ti pe atann ki zot vini, alor li finn reyni so bann fami e kamarad pros."
Acts10:25 Zis letan Pier pou rantre, Korney vinn zwenn li e li tom dan so lipie, li kourb devan li pou montre so respe."
Acts10:26 Me Pier fer li leve. Pier dir li, “Leve. Mo nek enn zom parey kouma twa.”"
Acts10:27 Li kontign koz ar Korney pandan ki zot rant dan lakaz, e la li trouv enn kantite dimoun ki finn vinn ansam."
Acts10:28 Li dir zot, “Zot tou bien kone ki dapre lalwa, enn Zwif pa asosie limem ar enn etranze, e li pa frekant lezot ki pa Zwif. Me Bondie finn montre mwa ki fode pa mo konsider okenn dimoun inpir oubien indign pou mo frekant li."
Acts10:29 Akoz sa, kouma zot finn apel mwa pou vini, mo pa finn ena okenn obzeksion. Asterla, mo kapav dimann zot kifer finn apel mwa isi?”"
Acts10:30 Korney reponn, “Ena trwa zour letan mo ti dan mo lakaz mo pe priye, apepre sa lerlamem, trwa-zer lapre-midi, enn sel kout enn dimoun avek enn linz bien briyan, paret devan mwa."
Acts10:31 Li dir mwa, ‘Korney, Bondie finn pran kont to lapriyer ek led ki to donn bann pov."
Acts10:32 Avoy dimoun Zope pou amenn Simon, ki zot apel Pier. Li pe res kot Simon, enn zouvrie ki travay lapo e ki res danbor lamer.’"
Acts10:33 Alor mo finn fer apel twa toutswit, e to finn vremem bon pou aksepte vini. Nou tou la, dan prezans Bondie pou ekout seki Bondie finn komann twa pou dir nou.”"
Acts10:34 Pier pran laparol, li dir, “Asterla mo realize ki Bondie tret tou dimoun parey lor mem baz."
Acts10:35 Bondie aksepte ninport ki dimoun dan ninport ki nasion si li ador li e fer seki drwat.
Acts10:36 Zot konn mesaz ki li finn avoy lepep Izrael, enn Bonn Nouvel ki ena lape par Zezi Kris ki Lesegner tou dimoun."
Acts10:37 Zot kone ki finn arive premie dabor dan Galile, ek answit partou dan Zide, apre batem ki Zan ti anonse."
Acts10:38 Zot kone kouma Bondie ti vers pwisans Lespri Sin lor Zezi ki sorti Nazaret. Li ti al partou, li fer dibien e ti geri tou dimoun ki ti may dan pouvwar diab, parski Bondie ti avek li."
Acts10:39 E nou, nou temwin tou seki li finn fer dan pei Izrael ek dan Zerizalem. Bannla finn koulout li lor lakrwa pou touy li."
Acts10:40 Me lor trwaziem zour Bondie finn relev li parmi bann mor, e fer li aparet."
Acts10:41 Pa tou dimoun ki finn trouv li, me bann temwin ki Bondie ti finn fini swazir, setadir nou ki finn manze-bwar ar li apre ki li ti regagn lavi."
Acts10:42 Li finn komann nou anons Bonn Nouvel e rann temwagnaz ki limem ki Bondie finn swazire kouma ziz lor bann vivan ek bann mor.
Acts10:43 Tou bann profet ti koz lor li. Zot ti dir seki krwar dan li pou resevwar pardon zot pese par pwisans so nom.”
Acts10:44 Letan Pier ti ankor pe dir sa bann parol la, Lespri Sin ti desann lor tou seki ti pe ekout so mesaz."
Acts10:45 Bann krwayan ki lorizinn Zwif e ki ti akonpagn Pier, ti etone ki don Lespri Sin ti osi verse lor bann dimoun ki pa Zwif."
Acts10:46 Zot tann bannla koz anlang etranz e zot pe loue grander Bondie. Lerla Pier dir,"
Acts10:47 “Sa bann dimoun la finn resevwar Lespri Sin parey kouma nou, eski zot krwar nou kapav anpes zot batize dan dilo?”"
Acts10:48 Alor li donn lord ki batiz zot dan nom Lesegner Zezi Kris. Bannla dimann Pier res kot zot ankor detrwa zour.
Acts11:1 Bann apot ek bann frer ki ti dan Zide ti tann dir ki bann non-Zwif osi finn resevwar parol Bondie.
Acts11:2 Lerla, letan Pier retourn Zerizalem, bann krwayan ki anfaver sirkonsizion dir,"
Acts11:3 “To finn al kot bann ki pa fer sirkonsizion ek to finn mem manz avek zot.”
Acts11:4 Lerla Pier koumans explik zot andetay seki finn arive. Li dir zot,"
Acts11:5 “Mo ti pe priye dan lavil Zope e mo finn gagn enn vizion. Enn kiksoz ki resanble enn gran dra ti pe desann par so kat kwin depi lesiel ziska devan mwa.
Acts11:6 Ler mo get pli pre ladan mo trouv bann zanimo, bann bebet sovaz, bann reptil e bann zwazo."
Acts11:7 Mo tann enn lavwa ki dir mwa, ‘Pier, diboute; touye manze.’"
Acts11:8 Me mo reponn, ‘Non Segner, zame mo met kiksoz ki defann ou ki inpir dan mo labous.’"
Acts11:9 Me depi lesiel lavwa la redir mwa, ‘Pa apel inpir seki Bondie finn deklar pir.’"
Acts11:10 Sa finn arive trwa fwa, apre tou kiksoz finn remont dan lesiel."
Acts11:11 Lerlamem trwa zom ki sorti Sezare ti ariv dan lakaz kot nou ti ete.
Acts11:12 Lespri Sin dir mwa al ar zot san okenn ezitasion. Sa sis frer la finn al ar mwa kot Korney e nou finn rant dan so lakaz.
Acts11:13 Korney rakont nou kouma li ti trouv enn anz pe dibout dan so lakaz, e ti dir li, ‘Avoy dimoun Zope pou al sers Simon ki apel Pier."
Acts11:14 Li pou donn twa enn mesaz ki pou sov twa ek to fami.’
Acts11:15 Kouma mo koumans koze, Lespri Sin desann lor zot parey kouma ti desann lor nou dan komansman."
Acts11:16 Mo finn rapel parol Bondie ki dir, ‘Zan ti batiz ar dilo, me zot, zot pou resevwar batem dan Lespri Sin.’"
Acts11:17 Si Bondie finn donn bannla mem don ki li finn donn nou kan nou ti krwar dan Zezi Kris, mwa ki mo ete pou reziste Bondie?”"
Acts11:18 Kan bannla tann sa zot res trankil. Zot ti glorifie Bondie. Zot dir, “Alor Bondie finn donn bann ki pa Zwif repantans ki donn vre lavi.”"
Acts11:19 Bann ki ti disperse akoz persekision ki ti koumanse par lamor Etienn ti al ziska Fenisi, Sip ek Antios. Zot ti pe partaz laparol zis ar bann Zwif."
Acts11:20 Me ti ena parmi zot ki ti sorti Sip ek Sirenn. Kan zot ti vinn Antios zot finn koz ar bann Grek pou anons zot Bonn Nouvel lor Zezi Kris.
Acts11:21 Lame Bondie ti lor zot ek enn kantite ti krwar e ti tourn ver Lesegner.
Acts11:22 Sa nouvel la ti ariv dan zorey bann ki ti dan Legliz Zerizalem. Lerla zot avoy Barnabas Antios.
Acts11:23 Letan li ariv laba li trouv lagras Bondie, li ti bien-bien kontan. Li ti ankouraz zot tou pou res fidel ar Lesegner ar tou zot leker."
Acts11:24 Barnabas ti enn bon dimoun ranpli ar Lespri Sin ek lafwa. Ti gagn enn kantite dimoun pou Lesegner.
Acts11:25 Lerla Barnabas ti al Tars pou rod Sol.
Acts11:26 Kan li finn trouv li, li finn amenn li Antios. Zot finn pas enn lane dan legliz pou ansegn enn kantite dimoun. Dan Antios mem ki premie fwa ti apel bann disip Kretien."
Acts11:27 Sa lepok la detrwa profet sorti Zerizalem finn vinn Antios.
Acts11:28 Enn parmi zot, Agabis, met li dibout e par pwisans Lespri Sin li koumans anonse ki pou ena enn faminn lor later. (Sa ti arive lepok Klod ti anperer.)"
Acts11:29 Bann disip deside pou avoy otan led ki zot kapav bann krwayan ki abit dan Zide.
Acts11:30 Zot finn fer samem, e finn avoy zot don kot bann ansien dan legliz Zide par Barnabas ek Sol."
Acts12:1 Sa lepok la lerwa Erod ti pe persekit detrwa manm Legliz.
Acts12:2 Li fer touy Zak, frer Zan, par lepe."
Acts12:3 Letan li trouve ki sa ti fer plezir bann Zwif li fer aret Pier osi. Sa ti pase pandan fet dipin san levin.
Acts12:4 Erod fer aret Pier e met li dan prizon. Li fer kat lekip ki ena kat solda sakenn vey li, parski li ti ena lintansion ziz Pier anpiblik apre fet Pak."
Acts12:5 Pandan ki Pier ti dan prizon Legliz ti priye Bondie boukou pou li.
Acts12:6 Lavey ki Erod ti pou amenn li devan lepep, Pier ti pe dormi aswar ant de solda. Zot ti finn atas li ar lasenn. Ti ena bann gard ki ti pe veye devan laport prizon."
Acts12:7 Ala ki enn selkout enn anz Bondie paret ek enn lalimier briye dan kaso. Anz la bouz Pier, li kas so somey, e li dir li, “Degaze-leve!” Lerla lasenn ki ti otour so lame tonbe."
Acts12:8 Anz la dir li, “Met to sintir ek to sandalet.” Pier obeir. Li dir Pier, “Met to manto, swiv mwa.”"
Acts12:9 Pier sorti swiv li. Li pa ti kone sipa saki anz la ti pe fer, ti vre. Li ti krwar ki li pe fer enn vizion."
Acts12:10 Letan zot finn pas premie ek deziem lekip solda, zot ariv devan enn laport an feray ki tom lor lavil. Laport la ouver tousel. Zot sorti e zot mars ziska danbout sime; lerlamem anz la kit li."
Acts12:11 Lerla Pier rann li kont ki finn arive. Li dir, “Aster mo sir ki Lesegner finn avoy so anz pou tir mwa dan lame Erod. Li finn protez mwa kont tou dimal ki lepep Zwif ti pe anvi ariv mwa.”"
Acts12:12 Kan li finn realize ki ti pe arive, li pran direksion lakaz Marie, mama Zan, ki ti osi apel Mark. Boukou dimoun ti reyni laba pou priye."
Acts12:13 Kan Pier tap laport lantouraz, enn servant ki ti apel Roda ti vini pou ouver."
Acts12:14 Li rekonet lavwa Pier. Dan so lazwa li bliye ouver laport, li galoupe li al dir bann ki andan ki Pier pe dibout devan laport."
Acts12:15 Zot dir li, “To fol.” Me li persiste. Zot dir, “So anz sa.”"
Acts12:16 Pandan sa letan la, Pier kontign tape mem. Zot ouver, e zot res bet ler zot trouv li."
Acts12:17 Pier fer enn sign ar so lame pou dir zot res trankil. Li rakont zot kouma Lesegner finn tir li dan prizon. Li dir bannla, “Al rakont sa Zak ek bann lezot frer.” Apre sa li sorti li al dan enn lot landrwa."
Acts12:18 Ler gramatin arive, bann solda ti bien trakase ek azite. Zot ti anvi kone kot Pier ete."
Acts12:19 Erod fer rod Pier, me pa trouv li. Li kestionn bann solda la e li donn lord pou touy zot. Apre sa, li sorti Zide pou li al Sezare."
Acts12:20 Erod ti bien ankoler ar bann abitan Tir ek Sidon. Alor bannla tom dakor pou al zwenn li. Zot reysi negosie ar Blastis ki ti responsab pale lerwa, pou zot dimann lape, parski zot pei ti pe depann lor lerwa Erod pou gagn manze."
Acts12:21 Zour randevou, Erod met so linz lerwa, mont lor tronn ek fer enn diskour anpiblik."
Acts12:22 Lepep kriye, “Lavwa enn bondie sa, pa lavwa enn zom.”"
Acts12:23 Anplas enn anz Lesegner zet Erod anba parski li pa finn glorifie Bondie, me finn pran loner la pou li. Lever manz li e li mor."
Acts12:24 Me laparol Bondie ti kontign repann ek miltipliye.
Acts12:25 Kan Barnabas ek Sol ti fini fer zot mision dan Zerizalem, zot ti retourne e zot ti amenn ar zot Zan ki ti osi apel Mark."
Acts13:1 Dan Legliz Antios ti ena bann profet ek profeser kouma Barnabas, Simeon ki ti apel Nizer, Lisyis ki sorti Sirenn, Manaen ki ti grandi ansam ar Erod, ek Sol."
Acts13:2 Letan zot ti pe ador Lesegner e zot ti pe gard karem, Lespri Sin dir zot, “Met Barnabas ek Sol enn kote pou enn mision ki mo ena pou zot.”"
Acts13:3 Alor apre ki zot fini priye ek fer karem, zot inpoz lame lor bannla e les zot ale."
Acts13:4 Sa de la, ki Lespri Sin ti avoye, ti al Selesi e depi laba zot ti pran bato pou al Sip."
Acts13:5 Ler zot ariv Salamis, zot anons parol Bondie dan bann sinagog Zwif. Zan Mark ti vini pou donn zot enn koudme."
Acts13:6 Ler zot ti fini travers lil ziska Pafos, zot zwenn enn longanis ki enn fos profet Zwif ki ti apel Barzezi."
Acts13:7 Li ti enn kamarad gouverner Serz Polis, ki ti enn dimoun bien intelizan. Li ti donn lord al rod Barnabas ek Sol parski li ti anvi tann parol Bondie."
Acts13:8 Me longanis Elimas - samem so nom dan langaz Grek - ti kont zot e li ti sey detourn gouverner pou anpes li vinn enn krwayan.
Acts13:9 Sol, ki ti osi apel Pol, ti ranpli ar Lespri Sin. Li get Elimas drwat dan so lizie e li dir li,"
Acts13:10 “Twa ki rize e ranpli ar mesanste, zanfan diab e lennmi lazistis, to pa pou aret detourn sime drwat Lesegner?"
Acts13:11 Get sa! Lame Lesegner kont twa. To pou vinn aveg e to pa pou trouv lalimier soley pandan enn bon bout letan.” Enn selkout Elimas trouv li dan marenwar, e li tourn partou-kote, pou gagn kikenn pou kondir li."
Acts13:12 Letan gouverner trouv seki finn arive, li vinn enn krwayan. Li ti bien inpresione par lansegnman Lesegner."
Acts13:13 Pol ek so bann kamarad ti pran bato depi Pafos pou al Perz dan Panfili. La, Zan Mark kit zot pou retourn Zerizalem."
Acts13:14 Apre Perz zot kontign zot sime ziska Antios dan Pisidi. Zot rant dan sinagog enn zour saba e zot asize.
Acts13:15 Kouma fini lir liv Lalwa ek liv Profet, bann sef sinagog fer dir zot, “Mo bann frer, si zot ena kik mesaz pou ankouraz bann dimoun ki la, zot kapav koze.”"
Acts13:16 Pol leve, li fer enn sign ar so lame, li dir, “Mo bann frer, ek zot tou ki ena gran respe pou Bondie, ekout mwa."
Acts13:17 Bondie lepep Izrael finn swazir nou bann anset, e li finn fer zot vinn enn gran nasion pandan lepok ki zot ti res Lezip. Apre li finn fer zot sorti laba par so aksion pwisan."
Acts13:18 Pandan karant banane li finn siport zot dan dezer.
Acts13:19 Li finn detrir set nasion dan pei Kanaan e li finn donn so lepep later bannla kouma enn leritaz
Acts13:20 pandan katsan-sinkant banane. Apre sa li finn donn zot bann ziz ziska profet Samiel.
Acts13:21 Lerla lepep ti dimann pou gagn enn lerwa. Bondie ti donn zot Sail, garson Kis depi tribi Benzamin, pandan karant banane."
Acts13:22 Kan Bondie ti finn rezet Sail, li ti elev David pou vinn zot lerwa. Ala temwagnaz ki li ti rann lor David: ‘Mo finn trouv dan David, garson Zese, kikenn ki mo leker bien kontan e ki pou fer mo volonte.’"
Acts13:23 Bondie finn azir dapre so promes e li finn lev enn Sover, Zezi, enn desandan David."
Acts13:24 Avan larive Zezi, Zan ti proklam enn batem repantans pou tou bann dimoun dan Izrael."
Acts13:25 Kan lepok Zan pe al fini, li dir, ‘Kisannla zot panse mo ete? Mwa, mo pa Lemesi. Non, me Sa-Enn ki pe vini apre mwa la, mo mem pa vo pou larg so lase soulie.’"
Acts13:26 Bann frer, desandan Abraam ek zot bann non-Zwif ki ena respe pou Bondie, sa mesaz liberasion la, finn avoye pou nou sa."
Acts13:27 Bann abitan Zerizalem ek zot bann sef pa finn rekonet Zezi; letan zot finn kondann li, zot finn fer parol bann profet ki nou lir sak saba vinn vre."
Acts13:28 Zot pa finn trouv nanye kont li pouki li merit lamor, pourtan zot finn dir Pilat touy li."
Acts13:29 Letan zot finn fer tou seki ti deza ekrir lor li, zot desann li depi lor lakrwa e zot met li dan enn tonbo."
Acts13:30 Me Bondie finn resisit li.
Acts13:31 Pandan boukou zour apre sa, li finn aparet ar dimoun ki ti mars ansam ar li depi Galile ziska Zerizalem, e ki azordi pe rann temwagnaz pou li ar lepep Izrael."
Acts13:32 E nou, nou pe anons zot sa Bonn Nouvel ki Bondie limem ti promet nou bann anset."
Acts13:33 Li fer sa vinn vre pou nou, ki zot bann desandan, letan li finn resisit Zezi; parey kouma ti ekrir dan deziem Psom: ‘Tomem mo Garson, Azordi mo finn vinn to Papa.’"
Acts13:34 Li finn resisit Zezi pouki zame li retourn ankor dan lamor ek pouri laba, e samem ki fer sa bann parol la vinn vre: ‘Mo pou donn zot benediksion ki sakre ki mo ti promet David.’"
Acts13:35 E dan enn lot pasaz finn ekrir: ‘To pa pou les to serviter fidel pouri dan tom.’
Acts13:36 Me David, apre ki li finn akonpli plan Bondie dan so lepok, li finn mor e finn anter li ansam ar so bann anset. So lekor finn pouri dan tom."
Acts13:37 Me Sa-Enn ki Bondie finn resisite la, li pa finn konn sa mem sor la."
Acts13:38 Bann frer, mo anvi ki zot kone ki atraver Zezi ki pe proklam pardon zot bann pese."
Acts13:39 Par Zezi tou dimoun ki krwar pe gagn liberasion so bann pese ki lalwa Moiz pa ti kapav fer.
Acts13:40 Pran kont ki seki bann profet finn dir pa ariv twa:
Acts13:41 ‘Gete, zot ki ranpli ar mepri, ki aster zot ranpli ar etonnman e ki zot disparet! Saki mo pe fer zordi zour enn kiksoz ki zot pa pou krwar mem si kikenn rakont zot sa.’ ”"
Acts13:42 Letan Pol e Barnabas ti pe sorti sinagog, bann ki ti rasanble dimann zot retourne lot saba pou koz lor sa mem size la."
Acts13:43 Ler reynion termine, enn kantite Zwif ek bann konverti Zwif ti swiv Pol ek Barnabas. Sa de la ti koz ar zot e ti exort zot res fidel ar lagras Bondie."
Acts13:44 Kouma lot saba arive preske tou dimoun dan lavil ti rasanble pou ekout parol Lesegner.
Acts13:45 Me bann Zwif ti ranpli ar zalouzi letan zot trouv sa lafoul la. Zot insilte Pol e kontredir saki li ti pe dir.
Acts13:46 Lerla avek boukou kouraz Pol ek Barnabas dir bannla, “Li ti neseser ki anons parol Bondie ar zot premie dabor. Me akoz zot finn repous li e zot pa konsider zot dign lavi eternel, abe asterla nou pou al kot bann non-Zwif."
Acts13:47 Ala saki Lesegner finn komann nou: ‘Mo finn etablir twa kouma enn lalimier pou bann nasion, pou sov lemonn antie.’ ”"
